解 作变量代换 $x = u + t, y = v + t$ （ $t$ 固定），则

$$
F (t) = \iint_ {u ^ {2} + v ^ {2} \leqslant 1} \sqrt {(u + t) ^ {2} + (v + t) ^ {2}} d u d v. \tag {1}
$$

今在积分号下求导数，得

$$
F ^ {\prime} (t) = \iint_ {u ^ {2} + v ^ {2} \leqslant 1} \frac {u + t + v + t}{\sqrt {(u + t) ^ {2} + (v + t) ^ {2}}} d u d v = \iint_ {(x - t) ^ {2} + (y - t) ^ {2} \leqslant 1} \frac {x + y}{\sqrt {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}}} d x d y (- \infty <   t <   + \infty).
$$

\*）积分号下求导数的合理性，证明如下：令

$$
f (u, v, t) = \sqrt {(u + t) ^ {2} + (v + t) ^ {2}},
$$

则 $f_{t}^{\prime}(u,v,t) = \frac{u + t + v + t}{\sqrt{(u + t)^{2} + (v + t)^{2}}}\quad ((u,v)\neq (-t, - t)).$

当 $(u, v) = (-t, -t)$ 时，易知 $f_{t}^{\prime}(u, v, t)$ 不存在，但右导数存在且等于 $\sqrt{2}$ ，左导数也存在且等于 $-\sqrt{2}$ 。由于对任何数 $a, b$ ，有 $a^{2} + b^{2} \geqslant 2ab$ ，故 $2(a^{2} + b^{2}) \geqslant (a + b)^{2}$ ，从而， $\frac{|a + b|}{\sqrt{a^{2} + b^{2}}} \leqslant \sqrt{2}$ 。于是，

$$
\left| f _ {t} ^ {\prime} (u, v, t) \right| \leqslant \sqrt {2} \quad ((u, v) \neq (- t, - t)). \tag {2}
$$

如果 $|t| > \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}$ ，这时 $f(u, v, t), f_{t}^{\prime}(u, v, t) (t$ 固定）都是区域 $u^{2} + v^{2} \leqslant 1$ 上的连续函数，当然可在积分号下求导数，得

$$
F ^ {\prime} (t) = \iint_ {u ^ {2} - v ^ {2} \leqslant 1} f _ {t} ^ {\prime} (u, v, t) d u d v. \tag {3}
$$

但如果 $|t|\leqslant \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}$ ，则(3)式右端积分的被积函数 $f_{t}^{\prime}(u,v,t)$ 在积分域 $u^{2} + v^{2}\leqslant 1$ 中的点 $(u,v) = (-t, - t)$ 不

连续. 因此, 不能立即断定 (3) 式的正确性. 下面不论 $t$ 为何值 $(- \infty < t < +\infty)$ , 直接证明 (3) 式成立. 令

$$
g (t) = \iint_ {u ^ {2} + v ^ {2} \leqslant 1} f _ {t} ^ {\prime} (u, v, t) d u d v (- \infty <   t <   + \infty). \tag {4}
$$

由(2)式知 $f_{t}^{\prime}(u, v, t)$ 是有界的，且在区域 $u^{2} + v^{2} \leqslant 1$ 上至多有一个不连续点（ $t$ 固定），故(4)式右端的积分存在。实际上，利用(2)式以及 $f_{t}^{\prime}(u, v, t)$ 当 $(u, v) \neq (-t, -t)$ 时的连续性，用（必要时，即 $|t| \leqslant \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}$ 时）挖掉以点 $(-t, -t)$ 为中心的小圆域的方法，不难证明 $g(t)$ 是 $-\infty < t < +\infty$ 上的连续函数（详细证明留给读者）。令

$$
G (t) = \int_ {0} ^ {t} g (s) d s \quad (- \infty <   t <   + \infty),
$$

则 $G^{\prime}(t) = g(t)\quad (-\infty <  t <   + \infty),$ (5）

但

$$
G (t) = \int_ {0} ^ {\prime} d s \iint_ {u ^ {2} + v ^ {2} \leqslant 1} f _ {t} ^ {\prime} (u, v, s) d u d v = \iiint_ {u ^ {2} + v ^ {2} \leqslant 1} f _ {t} ^ {\prime} (u, v, s) d u d v d s = \iint_ {u ^ {2} + v ^ {2} \leqslant 1} d u d v \int_ {0} ^ {\prime} f _ {t} ^ {\prime} (u, v, s) d s. \tag {6}
$$

注意，(6)式中的运算是合理的，因为三维区域 $u^2 + v^2 \leqslant 1, 0 \leqslant s \leqslant t$ （ $t$ 固定）中，三元函数 $f_{i}^{\prime}(u, v, s)$ 有界且只在直线 $u = v = -s$ 的一段上不连续，从而，(6)式中的三重积分及两个累次积分都存在，故它们相等.

下证恒有

$$
\int_ {0} ^ {t} f _ {t} ^ {\prime} (u, v, s) \mathrm {d} s = f (u, v, t) - f (u, v, 0). \tag {7}
$$

事实上，若 $(u,v)\neq (-t_1, - t_1)(t_1\in [0,t])$ ，则 $f_{t}^{\prime}(u,v,t)$ 是 $0\leqslant s\leqslant t$ 上的连续函数 $(u,v$ 固定），从而，（7）式成立；若 $(u,v) = (-t_{1}, - t_{1})(t_{1}$ 是属于[0,t]的某数)，则由 $f(u,v,s)$ 对任何 $u,v,s$ 的连续性，有

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int_ {0} ^ {t} f _ {t} ^ {\prime} (u, v, s) \mathrm {d} s = \lim  _ {\epsilon \rightarrow + 0} \int_ {0} ^ {t _ {1} - \epsilon} f _ {t} ^ {\prime} (u, v, s) \mathrm {d} s + \lim  _ {\epsilon^ {\prime} \rightarrow 0} \int_ {t _ {1} + \epsilon^ {\prime}} ^ {t} f _ {t} ^ {\prime} (u, v, s) \mathrm {d} s \\ = \lim  _ {\varepsilon \rightarrow + 0} [ f (u, v, t _ {1} - \varepsilon) - f (u, v, 0) ] + \lim  _ {\varepsilon^ {\prime} \rightarrow 0} [ f (u, v, t) - f (u, v, t _ {1} + \varepsilon^ {\prime}) ] \\ = f (u, v, t _ {1}) - f (u, v, 0) + f (u, v, t) - f (u, v, t _ {1}) \\ = f (u, v, t) - f (u, v, 0), \\ \end{array}
$$

故(7)式恒成立.代入(6)式，得 $G(t) = \iint_{u^2 + v^2 \leqslant 1} [f(u, v, t) - f(u, v, 0)] \mathrm{d}u \mathrm{d}v = F(t) - F(0) (-\infty < t < +\infty)$ .

由此，再注意到（5）式，即知 $F^{\prime}(t)$ 存在，且

$$
F ^ {\prime} (t) = G ^ {\prime} (t) = g (t) = \iint_ {u ^ {2} - v ^ {2} \leqslant 1} f _ {t} ^ {\prime} (u, v, t) d u d v (- \infty <   t <   + \infty),
$$

即（3）式成立.

【3981】设 $F(t) = \iint_{x^2 + y^2 \leqslant t^2} f(x, y) \, \mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y \quad (t > 0)$ ，求 $F'(t)$ .

解题思路 令 $x = r\cos \varphi, y = r\sin \varphi$ ，则积分域 $x^2 + y^2 \leqslant t^2$ 变为

$$
\Omega^ {\prime} = \left\{0 \leqslant r \leqslant t, 0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant 2 \pi \right\} \quad \text {且} \quad F (t) = \int_ {0} ^ {t}   \mathrm {d} r \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} f (r \cos \varphi , r \sin \varphi) r \mathrm {d} \varphi ,
$$

利用2302题的结果即易获解.

解 令 $x = r\cos \varphi, y = r\sin \varphi$ ，则

$$
F (t) = \int_ {0} ^ {t} d r \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} f (r \cos \varphi , r \sin \varphi) r d \varphi ,
$$

故得 $F^{\prime}(t) = \int_{0}^{2\pi}f(t\cos \varphi ,t\sin \varphi)t\mathrm{d}\varphi .$

注意，此题中应假定 $f(x,y)$ 是连续函数.

【3982】证明：若 $f(x,y)$ 连续，则函数

$$
u (x, y) = \frac {1}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {x} d \xi \int_ {\xi - x + y} ^ {x + y - \xi} f (\xi , \eta) d \eta
$$

满足方程 $\frac{\partial^2 u}{\partial x^2} - \frac{\partial^2 u}{\partial y^2} = f(x, y)$ .

证明思路 利用含参变量的常义积分求导数的公式，可得

$$
\frac {\partial u}{\partial x} = \frac {1}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {x} [ f (\xi , x + y - \xi) + f (\xi , \xi - x + y) ] d \xi
$$

及 $\frac{\partial^2u}{\partial x^2} = \frac{1}{2}\int_0^x\left[f'_y(\xi ,x + y - \xi) - f'_y(\xi ,\xi -x + y)\right]\mathrm{d}\xi +f(x,y).$

同法可求得 $\frac{\partial u}{\partial y} = \frac{1}{2}\int_{0}^{x}[f(\xi ,x + y - \xi) - f(\xi ,\xi -x + y)]\mathrm{d}\xi ,$

及 $\frac{\partial^2 u}{\partial y^2} = \frac{1}{2} \int_{0}^{x} [f_y'(\xi, x + y - \xi) - f_y'(\xi, \xi - x + y)] \mathrm{d}\xi.$

于是，命题易获证

证 利用含参变量的常义积分求导数的公式，得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \frac {\partial u}{\partial x} = \frac {1}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {x} [ f (\xi , x + y - \xi) - (- 1) f (\xi , \xi - x + y) ] d \xi + \frac {1}{2} \int_ {x - x + y} ^ {x + y - x} f (x, \eta) d \eta \\ = \frac {1}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {r} [ f (\xi , x + y - \xi) + f (\xi , \xi - x + y) ] d \xi , \\ \end{array}
$$

$$
\begin{array}{l} \frac {\partial^ {2} u}{\partial x ^ {2}} = \frac {1}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {x} \left[ f _ {y} ^ {\prime} (\xi , x + y - \xi) - f _ {y} ^ {\prime} (\xi , \xi - x + y) \right] d \xi + \frac {1}{2} \left[ f (x, x + y - x) + f (x, x - x + y) \right] \\ = \frac {1}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {x} \left[ f _ {y} ^ {\prime} (\xi , x + y - \xi) - f _ {y} ^ {\prime} (\xi , \xi - x + y) \right] d \xi + f (x, y). \\ \end{array}
$$

同理，有

$$
\frac {\partial u}{\partial y} = \frac {1}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {x} [ f (\xi , x + y - \xi) - f (\xi , \xi - x + y) ] d \xi , \quad \frac {\partial^ {2} u}{\partial y ^ {2}} = \frac {1}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {x} [ f _ {y} ^ {\prime} (\xi , x + y - \xi) - f _ {y} ^ {\prime} (\xi , \xi - x + y) ] d \xi .
$$

于是，得 $\frac{\partial^2 u}{\partial x^2} - \frac{\partial^2 u}{\partial y^2} = f(x, y)$ ，证毕.

注意 显然本题还应假定 $f_{y}^{\prime}(x,y)$ 存在且连续.

【3983】设函数 $f(x,y)$ 的等值线是简单封闭曲线，区域 $S(v_{1},v_{2})$ 由曲线 $f(x,y) = v_{1}$ 及 $f(x,y) = v_{2}$ 围成.证明：

$$
\iint_ {S (v _ {1}, v _ {2})} f (x, y) \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y = \int_ {v _ {1}} ^ {v _ {2}} v F ^ {\prime} (v) \mathrm {d} v,
$$

其中 $F(v)$ 为曲线 $f(x,y) = v_{1}$ 与 $f(x,y) = v_{2}$ 所包围的面积.

提示 用函数的无限接近的等值线把积分域 $S(v_{1}, v_{2})$ 分为许多子域，并利用积分中值定理及微分中值定理，即可获证.

证 作 $[v_1, v_2]$ 的任一分划 $T$ ： $v_1 = v_0' < v_1' < \dots < v_i' < \dots < v_n' = v_2$ 。令 $\mathrm{d}(T) = \max_{1 \leq i \leq n} \Delta v_i$ ，这里 $\Delta v_i = v_i' - v_{i-1}' (i = 1, 2, \dots, n)$ 。于是，由积分中值定理（这里假定了 $f(x, y)$ 在 $S(v_1, v_2)$ 上连续）知，

$$
\iint_ {S \left(v _ {1}, v _ {2}\right)} f (x, y) d x d y = \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {n} \iint_ {S \left(v _ {i - 1} ^ {\prime}, v _ {i} ^ {\prime}\right)} f (x, y) d x d y = \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {n} f \left(\bar {x} _ {i}, \bar {y} _ {i}\right) \Delta S _ {i},
$$

其中 $\Delta S_{i}$ 表小环形域 $S(v_{i-1}', v_i')$ （如图8.33阴影部分所示）的面积， $\overline{P}(\overline{x}_i, \overline{y}_i) \in S(v_{i-1}', v_i')$

令 $v_{i}^{*} = f(\overline{x}_{i}, \overline{y}_{i})$ ，则 $v_{i-1}^{\prime} \leqslant v_{i}^{*} \leqslant v_{i}^{\prime}$ 。又显然（利用微分中值定理）有 $\Delta S_{i} = F(v_{i}^{\prime}) - F(v_{i-1}^{\prime}) = F^{\prime}(\overline{v}_{i})(v_{i}^{\prime} - v_{i-1}^{\prime}) = F^{\prime}(\overline{v}_{i})\Delta v_{i} \quad (i = 1,2,\dots,n)$ ，其中 $v_{i}^{\prime} \leqslant \overline{v}_{i} \leqslant v_{i}^{\prime}$ 。这里我们假定了 $F^{\prime}(v)$ 在 $[v_{1}, v_{2}]$ 上存在且可积，于是它有界，即

![](images/400d48d036499e2c2443025ce3b8f17d70d582b72b1bf69b5d897c74de4a67be.jpg)  
图8.33

$$
| F ^ {\prime} (v) | \leqslant M = \text {常 数} \quad (v _ {1} \leqslant v \leqslant v _ {2}). \tag {1}
$$

我们有 $\iint_{S(v_1, v_2)} f(x, y) \, \mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y = \sum_{i=1}^{n} v_i^* F'(v_i) \Delta v_i = I_1 + I_2,$ (2)

其中 $I_{1} = \sum_{i = 1}^{n}\overline{v}_{i}F^{\prime}(\overline{v}_{i})\Delta v_{i},\quad I_{2} = \sum_{i = 1}^{n}(v_{i}^{*} - \overline{v}_{i})F^{\prime}(\overline{v}_{i})\Delta v_{i}.$

由于 $F^{\prime}(v)$ 在 $[v_1, v_2]$ 上可积，故 $vF^{\prime}(v)$ 也在 $[v_1, v_2]$ 上可积。因此，

$$
\lim  _ {d (T) \rightarrow 0} I _ {1} = \lim  _ {d (T) \rightarrow 0} \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {n} \bar {v} _ {i} F ^ {\prime} (\bar {v} _ {i}) \Delta v _ {i} = \int_ {v _ {1}} ^ {v _ {2}} v F ^ {\prime} (v) d v. \tag {3}
$$

另一方面，由(1)式知 $|I_2|\leqslant M\mathrm{d}(T)\sum_{i = 1}^{n}\Delta v_i = M(v_2 - v_1)\mathrm{d}(T),$

故 $\lim_{\mathrm{d}(T)\to 0}I_2 = 0.$ (4）

现在(2)式两端令 $\mathrm{d}(T)\rightarrow 0$ 取极限（注意(2)式左端是常数），并注意到(3)式与(4)式，即得

$$
\iint_ {S \left(v _ {1}, v _ {2}\right)} f (x, y) d x d y = \int_ {v _ {1}} ^ {v _ {2}} v F ^ {\prime} (v) d v.
$$

证毕.

应当指出，正如上面所说的，本题应假定 $f(x,y)$ 在 $S(v_{1},v_{2})$ 上连续，而 $F^{\prime}(v)$ 在 $[v_1,v_2]$ 上存在并且可积.

# § 2. 面积的计算法

$Oxy$ 平面上区域 $S$ 的面积由以下公式给出： $S = \iint_{S} \mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y$ .

求下列曲线所界的面积：

【3984】 $xy = a^2, x + y = \frac{5a}{2} (a > 0)$

解 两曲线的交点为 $A\left(\frac{a}{2}, 2a\right)$ 和 $B\left(2a, \frac{a}{2}\right)$ （图8.34），故所求面积为

$$
S = \int_ {\frac {a}{2}} ^ {2 a} d x \int_ {\frac {a ^ {2}}{x}} ^ {\frac {3 a}{2} - x} d y = \frac {1 5}{8} a ^ {2} - 2 a ^ {2} \ln 2.
$$

【3985】 $y^{2} = 2px + p^{2}, y^{2} = -2qx + q^{2}$ （ $p > 0, q > 0$ ）.

解曲线的交点为 $A\left(\frac{q - p}{2}, \sqrt{pq}\right)$ 和 $B\left(\frac{q - p}{2}, -\sqrt{pq}\right)$ （图8.35），

故所求面积为 $S = 2\int_{0}^{\sqrt{pq}} \mathrm{d}y \int_{\frac{y^2 - p^2}{2p}}^{\frac{q^2 - y^2}{2q}} \mathrm{d}x = \frac{2}{3} (p + q) \sqrt{pq}$ .

![](images/b2b94c797022dc9a92f94dd355af16c8d2fff168e1f39e425424648e91b44bf0.jpg)  
图8.35

![](images/7a45d7e7296e7182dff80a0b009e43f4c796f4082790a82d358e684b927f7047.jpg)  
图8.34

![](images/7528811cc2db3863951234ff3814e64e9919d79563f9e1cb7b0c16e65ddf5802.jpg)  
图8.36

【3986】 $(x - y)^2 + x^2 = a^2 \quad (a > 0)$

解如图8.36所示，所求面积的区域为：

$$
- a \leqslant x \leqslant a, \quad x - \sqrt {a ^ {2} - x ^ {2}} \leqslant y \leqslant x + \sqrt {a ^ {2} - x ^ {2}}.
$$

于是，所求的面积为

$$
S = \int_ {- a} ^ {a} d x \int_ {r - \sqrt {a ^ {2} - x ^ {2}}} ^ {x + \sqrt {a ^ {2} - x ^ {2}}} d y = 4 \int_ {0} ^ {a} \sqrt {a ^ {2} - x ^ {2}} d x = \pi a ^ {2}.
$$

变换为极坐标，计算下列曲线所围的面积：

【3987】 $(x^{2} + y^{2})^{2} = 2a^{2}(x^{2} - y^{2});\quad x^{2} + y^{2}\geqslant a^{2}.$

解曲线的极坐标方程为 $r^2 = 2a^2\cos 2\varphi ;r\geqslant a.$

它们的交点在第一象限内为 $(a, \frac{\pi}{6})$ ，如图8.37所示。利用对称性，得所求面积为

$$
S = 4 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{6}} d \varphi \int_ {a} ^ {\sqrt {2 a ^ {2} \cos 2 \varphi}} r d r = 2 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{6}} (2 a ^ {2} \cos 2 \varphi - a ^ {2}) d \varphi = \frac {3 \sqrt {3} - \pi}{3} a ^ {2}.
$$

【3988】 $(x^{3} + y^{3})^{2} = x^{2} + y^{2};x\geqslant 0,y\geqslant 0.$

解 将方程化为极坐标方程，得 $(r^3\cos^3\theta + r^3\sin^3\theta)^2 = r^2$

即 $r^2 = \frac{1}{\cos^3\theta + \sin^3\theta} (0\leqslant \theta \leqslant \frac{\pi}{2}).$

曲线所围的面积为 $S = \iint_{S} r \, \mathrm{d}r \, \mathrm{d}\theta = \frac{1}{2} \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} r^{2} \, \mathrm{d}\theta = \frac{1}{2} \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} \frac{\mathrm{d}\theta}{\cos^{3}\theta + \sin^{3}\theta},$

由于 $\frac{1}{\cos^3\theta + \sin^3\theta} = \frac{1}{3}\left(\frac{2}{\sin\theta + \cos\theta} +\frac{\sin\theta + \cos\theta}{1 - \sin\theta\cos\theta}\right),$

又

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \frac {\mathrm {d} \theta}{\sin \theta + \cos \theta} = \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \frac {\mathrm {d} \theta}{\sin \left(\theta + \frac {\pi}{4}\right)} = \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \ln \tan \frac {\theta + \frac {\pi}{4}}{2} \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} = \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \left(\ln \tan \frac {3 \pi}{8} - \ln \tan \frac {\pi}{8}\right) \\ = \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \left(\ln \sqrt {\frac {\sqrt {2} + 1}{\sqrt {2} - 1}} - \ln \sqrt {\frac {\sqrt {2} - 1}{\sqrt {2} + 1}}\right) = \sqrt {2} \ln (1 + \sqrt {2}), \\ \end{array}
$$

$$
\int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \frac {\sin \theta + \cos \theta}{1 - \sin \theta \cos \theta} d \theta = 2 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \frac {d \left(\frac {1}{2} \sin \theta - \frac {1}{2} \cos \theta\right) ^ {*}}{2 \left(\frac {1}{2} \sin \theta - \frac {1}{2} \cos \theta\right) ^ {2} + \frac {1}{2}} = 2 \arctan (\sin \theta - \cos \theta) \Big | _ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} = \pi .
$$

于是，所求的面积为 $S = \frac{1}{3}\int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}\frac{\mathrm{d}\theta}{\sin\theta + \cos\theta} +\frac{1}{6}\int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}\frac{\sin\theta + \cos\theta}{1 - \sin\theta\cos\theta}\mathrm{d}\theta = \frac{\sqrt{2}}{3}\ln (1 + \sqrt{2}) + \frac{\pi}{6}.$

\*）利用2053题的结果，其中 $\lambda_1 = \frac{1}{2},\lambda_2 = \frac{3}{2},A = 2,B = 0.$

【3989】 $(x^{2} + y^{2})^{2} = a(x^{3} - 3xy^{2})$ （ $a > 0)$

解 显然曲线关于 $Ox$ 轴对称，故只要求出 $y \geq 0$ 的部分.化为极坐标，方程为

$$
r = a \cos \theta (4 \cos^ {2} \theta - 3).
$$

由于必须 $x^{3} - 3xy \geqslant 0$ ，故 $\cos \theta (4\cos^2\theta - 3) \geqslant 0$ 。因此， $\cos \theta \geqslant 0$ 且 $\cos \theta \geqslant \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}$ 或 $\cos \theta \leqslant 0$ 且 $\cos \theta \geqslant -\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}$ ，故 $-\frac{\pi}{6} \leqslant \theta \leqslant \frac{\pi}{6}, \frac{\pi}{2} \leqslant \theta \leqslant \pi - \frac{\pi}{6}, -\pi + \frac{\pi}{6} \leqslant \theta \leqslant -\frac{\pi}{2}$ 。于是，在 $Ox$ 轴的上方部分（ $y \geqslant 0$ ）为

$$
0 \leqslant \theta \leqslant \frac {\pi}{6} \quad \text {和} \quad \frac {\pi}{2} \leqslant \theta \leqslant \pi - \frac {\pi}{6}.
$$

由此可知

![](images/ce3f455c68d33574a18e0f4510a75873399aabea78c25c1bb912c6a6a1877d24.jpg)  
图8.37

$$
S = \iint_ {S} r \mathrm {d} r \mathrm {d} \theta = 2 \left(\frac {1}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{6}} r ^ {2} \mathrm {d} \theta + \frac {1}{2} \int_ {\frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\pi - \frac {\pi}{6}} r ^ {2} \mathrm {d} \theta\right) = \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{6}} a ^ {2} \cos^ {2} \theta (4 \cos^ {2} \theta - 3) ^ {2} \mathrm {d} \theta + \int_ {\frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {5 \pi}{6}} a ^ {2} \cos^ {2} \theta (4 \cos^ {2} \theta - 3) ^ {2} \mathrm {d} \theta .
$$

在上式右端第二个积分中作代换 $\theta = \pi -\varphi$ ，则

$$
\int_ {\frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{6}} a ^ {2} \cos^ {2} \theta (4 \cos^ {2} \theta - 3) ^ {2} d \theta = \int_ {\frac {\pi}{6}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} a ^ {2} \cos^ {2} \theta (4 \cos^ {2} \theta - 3) ^ {2} d \theta ,
$$

故 $S = \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} a^{2} \cos^{2} \theta (4 \cos^{2} \theta - 3)^{2} \mathrm{d}\theta = a^{2} \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} (16 \cos^{6} \theta - 24 \cos^{4} \theta + 9 \cos^{2} \theta) \mathrm{d}\theta$

$$
= a ^ {2} \left(1 6 \cdot \frac {5 \cdot 3 \cdot 1}{6 \cdot 4 \cdot 2} \cdot \frac {\pi}{2} - 2 4 \cdot \frac {3 \cdot 1}{4 \cdot 2} \cdot \frac {\pi}{2} + 9 \cdot \frac {1}{2} \cdot \frac {\pi}{2}\right) = \frac {\pi a ^ {2}}{4}.
$$

【3990】 $(x^{2} + y^{2})^{2} = 8a^{2}xy;$ $(x - a)^{2} + (y - a)^{2}\leqslant a^{2}(a > 0).$

解 将方程化为极坐标方程，得（双纽线）

$$
r ^ {4} = 8 a ^ {2} r ^ {2} \cos \theta \sin \theta , \quad \text {即} \quad r = 2 a \sqrt {\sin 2 \theta};
$$

与圆周 $(r\cos \theta - a)^2 + (r\sin \theta - a)^2 = a^2$ ，即 $r = a(\cos \theta + \sin \theta) \pm a\sqrt{\sin 2\theta}$ .

显然，两条曲线关于射线 $\theta = \frac{\pi}{4}$ 是对称的. 令

$$
2 a \sqrt {\sin 2 \theta} = a (\cos \theta + \sin \theta) - a \sqrt {\sin 2 \theta},
$$

解得交点的极角 $\theta = \frac{1}{2}\arcsin \frac{1}{8}$ . 于是，所求的面积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} S = \iint_ {S} r \mathrm {d} r \mathrm {d} \theta = \int_ {\frac {1}{2} \arcsin \frac {1}{8}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} \left\{\left(2 a \sqrt {\sin 2 \theta}\right) ^ {2} - \left[ a (\cos \theta + \sin \theta) - a \sqrt {\sin 2 \theta} \right] ^ {2} \right\} \mathrm {d} \theta \\ = \int_ {\frac {1}{2} \arcsin \frac {1}{8}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} \left[ 2 a ^ {2} \sin 2 \theta + 2 a ^ {2} (\sin \theta + \cos \theta) \sqrt {\sin 2 \theta} - a ^ {2} \right] d \theta . \\ \end{array}
$$

注意到 $\int (\sin \theta +\cos \theta)\sqrt{\sin 2\theta}\mathrm{d}\theta = \frac{1}{2} (\sin \theta -\cos \theta)\sqrt{\sin 2\theta} +\frac{1}{2}\arcsin (\sin \theta -\cos \theta) + C^{*})$ ，即得

$$
\begin{array}{l} S = a ^ {2} \left[ - \cos 2 \theta + (\sin \theta - \cos \theta) \sqrt {\sin 2 \theta} + \arcsin (\sin \theta - \cos \theta) - \theta \right] \left| \begin{array}{l} \frac {\pi}{4} \\ \frac {1}{2} \arcsin \frac {1}{8} \end{array} \right. \\ = a ^ {2} \left[ - \frac {\pi}{4} + \frac {3 \sqrt {7}}{8} + \frac {\sqrt {1 4}}{4} \sqrt {\frac {1}{8}} + \arcsin \frac {\sqrt {1 4}}{4} + \frac {1}{2} \arcsin \frac {1}{8} \right] = a ^ {2} \left(\frac {\sqrt {7}}{2} + \arcsin \frac {\sqrt {1 4}}{4} - \frac {1}{2} \arccos  \frac {1}{8}\right) \\ = a ^ {2} \left(\frac {\sqrt {7}}{2} + \arcsin \frac {\sqrt {1 4}}{8}\right) ^ {* *}). \\ \end{array}
$$

\*）利用三角恒等式

$$
\sqrt {\sin 2 x} \sin x = \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \left(\frac {2 \tan x}{1 + \tan^ {2} x}\right) \sqrt {\tan x}, \quad \sqrt {\sin 2 x} \cos x = \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \left(\frac {2 \tan x}{1 + \tan^ {2} x}\right) \sqrt {\cot x}
$$

化为二项微分式的积分,参看A.Φ.THMOΦeeB《HHTEPHPOBAHNE ΦYHKUHN》第五章§15.

$\star \star$ ) 容易证明: $\arcsin \frac{\sqrt{14}}{4} - \frac{1}{2} \arccos \frac{1}{8} = \arcsin \frac{\sqrt{14}}{8}$ . 事实上, 我们有

$$
\sin \left(\arcsin \frac {\sqrt {1 4}}{8} + \frac {1}{2} \arccos  \frac {1}{8}\right) = \frac {3 \sqrt {1 4}}{3 2} + \frac {5 \sqrt {1 4}}{3 2} = \frac {\sqrt {1 4}}{4}.
$$

根据以下公式引入广义极坐标 $r$ 和 $\varphi$

$$
x = a r \cos^ {a} \varphi , \quad y = b r \sin^ {a} \varphi \quad (r \geqslant 0),
$$

其中 $a, b$ 和 $\alpha$ 为以适当的方法选出的常数，且考虑到 $\frac{D(x, y)}{D(r, \varphi)} = \alpha abr\cos^{\alpha - 1}\varphi \sin^{\alpha - 1}\varphi$ ，求由下列曲线所围的面积（假定参数是正的）：

【3991】 $\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2} = \frac{x}{h} +\frac{y}{k}.$

解不失一般性，设 $k > 0,h > 0.$ 令 $x = \arccos \varphi ,y = br\sin \varphi$ ，则方程化为

$$
r = \frac {a}{h} \cos \varphi + \frac {b}{k} \sin \varphi .
$$

由于 $r\geqslant 0$ ，故有 $\frac{a}{h}\cos \varphi +\frac{b}{k}\sin \varphi \geqslant 0,$

因此，首先必须 $-\frac{\pi}{2} \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \pi$ 。同时，应有 $\cos \varphi \geqslant 0$ 且 $\tan \varphi \geqslant -\frac{ak}{bh}$ 或者 $\cos \varphi < 0$ 且 $\tan \varphi \leqslant -\frac{ak}{bh}$ 。

从而，极角 $\varphi$ 应满足不等式 $-\arctan{\frac{ak}{bh}}\leqslant \varphi \leqslant \pi -\arctan{\frac{ak}{bh}}.$ 于是，曲线所围的面积为

$$
S = \iint_ {S} a b r d r d \varphi = \frac {a b}{2} \int_ {- \arctan \frac {a k}{b h}} ^ {\pi - \arctan \frac {a k}{b h}} \left(\frac {a}{h} \cos \varphi + \frac {b}{k} \sin \varphi\right) ^ {2} d \varphi = \frac {a b}{2} \left(\frac {a ^ {2}}{h ^ {2}} + \frac {b ^ {2}}{k ^ {2}}\right) \int_ {- \arctan \frac {a k}{b h}} ^ {\pi - \arctan \frac {a k}{b h}} \sin^ {2} (\varphi + \alpha_ {0}) d \varphi ,
$$

其中 $\alpha_{1} = \arctan{\frac{ak}{bh}}$ 从而，我们有

$$
S = \frac {a b}{2} \left(\frac {a ^ {2}}{h ^ {2}} + \frac {b ^ {2}}{k ^ {2}}\right) \left[ \frac {\varphi + \alpha_ {0}}{2} - \frac {1}{4} \sin 2 (\varphi + \alpha_ {0}) \right] \Bigg | _ {- \arctan \frac {a k}{b h}} ^ {\pi - \arctan \frac {a k}{b h}} = \frac {a b}{2} \left(\frac {a ^ {2}}{h ^ {2}} + \frac {b ^ {2}}{k ^ {2}}\right) \frac {\pi}{2} = \frac {\pi a b}{4} \left(\frac {a ^ {2}}{h ^ {2}} + \frac {b ^ {2}}{k ^ {2}}\right).
$$

【3992】 $\frac{x^3}{a^3} +\frac{y^3}{b^3} = \frac{x^2}{h^2} +\frac{y^2}{k^2};x = 0,y = 0.$

解 令 $x = \arccos \varphi, y = b r \sin \varphi$ ，则方程化为

$$
r = \frac {\left(\frac {a}{h}\right) ^ {2} \cos^ {2} \varphi + \left(\frac {b}{k}\right) ^ {2} \sin^ {2} \varphi}{\cos^ {3} \varphi + \sin^ {3} \varphi}.
$$

于是，曲线所围的面积为

$$
S = \iint_ {S} a b r d r d \theta = \frac {a b}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} r ^ {2} d \varphi = \frac {a b}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \frac {\left(\frac {a}{h}\right) ^ {4} \cos^ {4} \varphi + \left(\frac {b}{k}\right) ^ {4} \sin^ {4} \varphi + 2 \left(\frac {a}{h}\right) ^ {2} \left(\frac {b}{k}\right) ^ {2} \cos^ {2} \varphi \sin^ {2} \varphi}{\left(\cos^ {3} \varphi + \sin^ {3} \varphi\right) ^ {2}} d \varphi .
$$

根据H.M.雷日克、H.C.格拉德什坦编著的《函数表与积分表》2.125、2.126知：

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {\cos^ {4} \varphi \mathrm {d} \varphi}{(\cos^ {3} \varphi + \sin^ {3} \varphi) ^ {2}} = \int \frac {1}{(1 + \tan^ {3} \varphi)} \mathrm {d} (\tan \varphi) \\ = \frac {\tan \varphi}{3 \left(1 + \tan^ {3} \varphi\right)} + \frac {2}{9} \left[ \frac {1}{2} \ln \frac {(\tan \varphi + 1) ^ {2}}{\tan^ {2} \varphi - \tan \varphi + 1} + \sqrt {3} \arctan \frac {2 \tan \varphi - 1}{\sqrt {3}} \right] + C. \\ \end{array}
$$

从而，

$$
\begin{array}{l} \frac {a b}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \frac {\left(\frac {a}{h}\right) ^ {4} \cos^ {4} \varphi}{\left(\cos^ {3} \varphi + \sin^ {3} \varphi\right) ^ {2}} d \varphi \\ = \frac {a b}{2} \left(\frac {a}{h}\right) ^ {4} \left\{\frac {\tan \varphi}{3 \left(1 + \tan^ {3} \varphi\right)} + \frac {2}{9} \left[ \frac {1}{2} \ln \frac {(\tan \varphi + 1) ^ {2}}{\tan^ {2} \varphi - \tan \varphi + 1} + \sqrt {3} \arctan \frac {2 \tan \varphi - 1}{\sqrt {3}} \right] \right\} \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2} - 0} \\ = \frac {a b}{2} \left(\frac {a}{h}\right) ^ {4} \cdot \frac {2 \sqrt {3}}{9} \left(\frac {\pi}{2} + \frac {\pi}{6}\right) = \frac {2 \pi a b}{9 \sqrt {3}} \left(\frac {a}{h}\right) ^ {4}; \\ \end{array}
$$

又 $\int \frac{\sin^4\varphi\mathrm{d}\varphi}{(\cos^3\varphi + \sin^3\varphi)^2} = \int \frac{\tan^4\varphi}{(1 + \tan^3\varphi)^2}\mathrm{d}(\tan \varphi) = \frac{\tan^5\varphi}{3(1 + \tan^3\varphi)} -\frac{2}{3}\int \frac{\tan^4\varphi}{1 + \tan^3\varphi}\mathrm{d}(\tan \varphi)$

$$
= \frac {\tan^ {5} \varphi}{3 (1 + \tan^ {3} \varphi)} - \frac {2}{3} \left\{\frac {\tan^ {2} \varphi}{2} + \frac {1}{3} \left[ \frac {1}{2} \ln \frac {(\tan \varphi + 1) ^ {2}}{\tan^ {2} \varphi - \tan \varphi + 1} - \sqrt {3} \arctan \frac {2 \tan \varphi - 1}{\sqrt {3}} \right] \right\} + C,
$$

从而， $\frac{ab}{2}\int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}\frac{\left(\frac{b}{k}\right)^{4}\sin^{3}\varphi}{(\cos^{3}\varphi + \sin^{3}\varphi)^{2}}\mathrm{d}\varphi$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {a b}{2} \left(\frac {b}{k}\right) ^ {4} \left\{\frac {\tan^ {5} \varphi}{3 \left(1 + \tan^ {3} \varphi\right)} - \frac {\tan^ {2} \varphi}{3} - \frac {2}{9} \left[ \frac {1}{2} \ln \frac {(\tan \varphi + 1) ^ {2}}{\tan^ {2} \varphi - \tan \varphi + 1} - \sqrt {3} \arctan \frac {2 \tan \varphi - 1}{\sqrt {3}} \right] \right\} \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2} - 0} \\ = \frac {a b}{2} \left(\frac {b}{k}\right) ^ {1} \cdot \frac {2 \sqrt {3}}{9} \left(\frac {\pi}{2} + \frac {\pi}{6}\right) = \frac {2 \pi a b}{9 \sqrt {3}} \left(\frac {b}{k}\right) ^ {4}; \\ \end{array}
$$

此外，还有

$$
\int \frac {\cos^ {2} \varphi \sin^ {2} \varphi d \varphi}{(\cos^ {3} \varphi + \sin^ {3} \varphi) ^ {2}} = \int \frac {\tan^ {2} \varphi}{(1 + \tan^ {3} \varphi) ^ {2}} d (\tan \varphi) = - \frac {1}{3 (1 + \tan^ {3} \varphi)} + C,
$$

从而，

$$
\frac {a b}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \frac {2 \left(\frac {a}{h}\right) ^ {2} \left(\frac {b}{k}\right) ^ {2} \cos^ {2} \varphi \sin^ {2} \varphi}{(\cos^ {3} \varphi + \sin^ {3} \varphi) ^ {2}} d \varphi = a b \left(\frac {a}{h}\right) ^ {2} \left(\frac {b}{k}\right) ^ {2} \left[ - \frac {1}{3 (1 + \tan^ {3} \varphi)} \right] \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2} - n} = \frac {a b}{3} \left(\frac {a}{h}\right) ^ {2} \left(\frac {b}{k}\right) ^ {2}.
$$

于是，曲线所围的面积为

$$
S = \frac {2 \pi a b}{9 \sqrt {3}} \left(\frac {a}{h}\right) ^ {4} + \frac {2 \pi a b}{9 \sqrt {3}} \left(\frac {b}{k}\right) ^ {4} + \frac {a b}{3} \left(\frac {a}{h}\right) ^ {2} \left(\frac {b}{k}\right) ^ {2} = \frac {a b}{3} \left[ \frac {2 \pi}{3 \sqrt {3}} \left(\frac {a ^ {4}}{h ^ {4}} + \frac {b ^ {4}}{k ^ {4}}\right) + \frac {a ^ {2} b ^ {2}}{h ^ {2} k ^ {2}} \right].
$$

【3993】 $\left(\frac{x}{a} +\frac{y}{b}\right)^4 = \frac{x^2}{h^2} +\frac{y^2}{k^2}\quad (x > 0,y > 0).$

解解法1：

令 $x = \arccos \varphi, y = brs\sin \varphi$ ，则方程化为

$$
r ^ {2} = \frac {\left(\frac {a}{h}\right) ^ {2} \cos^ {2} \varphi + \left(\frac {b}{k}\right) ^ {2} \sin^ {2} \varphi}{(\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi) ^ {4}} \quad (0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}).
$$

于是，曲线所围的面积为 $S = \iint_{S} ab r \, \mathrm{d}r \, \mathrm{d}\varphi = \frac{ab}{2} \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} \frac{\left(\frac{a}{h}\right)^{2} \cos^{2}\varphi + \left(\frac{b}{k}\right)^{2} \sin^{2}\varphi}{(\cos\varphi + \sin\varphi)^{4}} \, \mathrm{d}\varphi.$

注意到

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int \frac {\cos^ {2} \varphi}{(\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi) ^ {4}} d \varphi = \int \frac {1}{(1 + \tan \varphi) ^ {4}} d (\tan \varphi) = - \frac {1}{3 (1 + \tan \varphi) ^ {3}} + C, \\ \int \frac {\sin^ {2} \varphi}{(\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi) ^ {4}} d \varphi = \int \frac {\tan^ {2} \varphi}{(1 + \tan \varphi) ^ {4}} d (\tan \varphi) = \int \frac {(\tan \varphi - 1) (\tan \varphi + 1) + 1}{(1 + \tan \varphi) ^ {4}} d (\tan \varphi) \\ = \int \frac {1}{(1 + \tan \varphi) ^ {2}} d (\tan \varphi) - 2 \int \frac {1}{(1 + \tan \varphi) ^ {3}} d (\tan \varphi) + \int \frac {1}{(1 + \tan \varphi) ^ {4}} d (\tan \varphi) \\ = - \frac {1}{1 + \tan \varphi} + \frac {1}{(1 + \tan \varphi) ^ {2}} - \frac {1}{3} \frac {1}{(1 + \tan \varphi) ^ {3}} + C, \\ \end{array}
$$

于是，所求的面积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} S = \frac {a b}{2} \left(\frac {a}{h}\right) ^ {2} \left[ - \frac {1}{3 (1 + \tan \varphi) ^ {3}} \right] \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2} - 0} + \frac {a b}{2} \left(\frac {b}{k}\right) ^ {2} \left[ - \frac {1}{1 + \tan \varphi} + \frac {1}{(1 + \tan \varphi) ^ {2}} - \frac {1}{3 (1 + \tan \varphi) ^ {3}} \right] \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2} - 0} \\ = \frac {a b}{6} \left(\frac {a ^ {2}}{h ^ {2}} + \frac {b ^ {2}}{k ^ {2}}\right). \\ \end{array}
$$

解法2：

令 $x = h r\cos \varphi, y = k r\sin \varphi$ ，则方程化为

$$
r ^ {2} = \frac {1}{\left(\frac {h}{a} \cos \varphi + \frac {k}{b} \sin \varphi\right) ^ {4}} = \left[ \frac {a ^ {2} b ^ {2}}{(h b) ^ {2} + (k a) ^ {2}} \right] ^ {2} \frac {1}{\sin^ {4} (\varphi + \alpha)} \quad (0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}),
$$

其中 $\tan \alpha = \frac{hb}{ka}$ 于是，曲线所围的面积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} S = \iint_ {S} h k r d r d \varphi = \frac {h k a ^ {4} b ^ {4}}{\left[ (h b) ^ {2} + (k a) ^ {2} \right] ^ {2}} \cdot \frac {1}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \frac {d \varphi}{\sin^ {4} (\varphi + \alpha)} \\ = \frac {h k a ^ {4} b ^ {4}}{\left[ (h b) ^ {2} + (k a) ^ {2} \right] ^ {2}} \left[ - \frac {1}{6} \frac {\cos (\varphi + \alpha)}{\sin (\varphi + \alpha)} - \frac {1}{3} \frac {\cos (\varphi + \alpha)}{\sin (\varphi + \alpha)} \right] \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2} *} \\ = \frac {h k a ^ {4} b ^ {4}}{\left[ (h b) ^ {2} + (k a) ^ {2} \right] ^ {2}} \left[ \frac {1}{6} \left(\frac {\sin \alpha}{\cos^ {3} \alpha} + \frac {\cos \alpha}{\sin^ {3} \alpha}\right) + \frac {1}{3} (\tan \alpha + \cot \alpha) \right] \\ = \frac {h k a ^ {4} b ^ {4}}{\left[ (h b) ^ {2} + (k a) ^ {2} \right] ^ {2}} \cdot \frac {1}{6} \frac {\left[ (h b) ^ {2} + (k a) ^ {2} \right] ^ {3}}{(h b k a) ^ {3}} = \frac {a b}{6} \left(\frac {a ^ {2}}{h ^ {2}} + \frac {b ^ {2}}{k ^ {2}}\right). \\ \end{array}
$$

\*）利用2012题的结果.

$\text{串}$ ）由 $\tan \alpha = \frac{hb}{ka}$ 知： $\cot \alpha = \frac{ka}{hb},$ $\sin \alpha = \frac{hb}{\sqrt{(hb)^2 + (ka)^2}},\quad \cos \alpha = \frac{ka}{\sqrt{(hb)^2 + (ka)^2}}.$

【3994】 $\left(\frac{x}{a} +\frac{y}{b}\right)^4 = \frac{x^2}{h^2} -\frac{y^2}{k^2}\quad (x > 0,y > 0).$

解 令 $x = \arccos \varphi, y = b r \sin \varphi$ ，则方程化为

$$
r ^ {2} = \frac {\left(\frac {a}{h}\right) ^ {2} \cos^ {2} \varphi - \left(\frac {b}{k}\right) ^ {2} \sin^ {2} \varphi}{\left(\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi\right) ^ {i}}.
$$

由于 $\left(\frac{a}{h}\right)^2\cos^2\varphi -\left(\frac{b}{k}\right)^2\sin^2\varphi \geqslant 0,\quad \left(\frac{ak}{bh}\right)^2\geqslant \tan^2\varphi ,$

注意到 $0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac{\pi}{2}$ , 可知极角的变化区间为 $0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \arctan \frac{ak}{bh}$ .

于是，注意利用上题中两个不定积分的结果，即得曲线所围的面积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} S = \iint_ {S} a b r d r d \varphi = \frac {a b}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {\arctan \frac {a b}{b h}} r ^ {2} d \varphi = \frac {a b}{2} \left(\frac {a}{h}\right) ^ {2} \int_ {0} ^ {\arctan \frac {a b}{b h}} \frac {\cos^ {2} \varphi}{\left(\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi\right) ^ {4}} d \varphi - \frac {a b}{2} \left(\frac {b}{k}\right) ^ {2} \int_ {0} ^ {\arctan \frac {a b}{b h}} \frac {\sin^ {2} \varphi}{\left(\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi\right) ^ {4}} d \varphi \\ = \frac {a b}{2} \left(\frac {a}{h}\right) ^ {2} \left[ - \frac {1}{3 (1 + \tan \varphi) ^ {3}} \right] \left| _ {0} ^ {\arctan \frac {a k}{b h}} - \frac {a b}{2} \left(\frac {b}{k}\right) ^ {2} \left[ - \frac {3 \tan^ {2} \varphi + 3 \tan \varphi + 1}{3 (1 + \tan \varphi) ^ {3}} \right] \right| _ {0} ^ {\arctan \frac {a k}{b h}} \\ = \frac {a b}{6} \left(\frac {a}{h}\right) ^ {2} \left[ \frac {- 1}{\left(1 + \frac {a k}{b h}\right) ^ {3}} + 1 \right] + \frac {a b}{6} \left(\frac {b}{k}\right) ^ {2} \left[ \frac {3 \left(\frac {a k}{b h}\right) ^ {2} + 3 \left(\frac {a k}{b h}\right) + 1}{\left(1 + \frac {a k}{b h}\right) ^ {3}} - 1 \right] \\ = \frac {a b}{6} \left(\frac {a}{h}\right) ^ {2} \frac {(a k) ^ {3} + 3 (a k) ^ {2} b h + 3 a k (b h) ^ {2}}{(a k + b h) ^ {3}} + \frac {a b}{6} \left(\frac {b}{k}\right) ^ {2} \frac {- (a k) ^ {3}}{(a k + b h) ^ {3}} \\ = \frac {a ^ {4} b k}{6 h ^ {2} (a k + b h) ^ {3}} \left(a ^ {2} k ^ {2} + 3 a k b h + 2 b ^ {2} h ^ {2}\right) = \frac {a ^ {4} b k (a k + 2 b h)}{6 h ^ {2} (a k + b h) ^ {2}}. \\ \end{array}
$$

【3995】 $\sqrt[4]{\frac{x}{a}} + \sqrt[4]{\frac{y}{b}} = 1; x = 0, y = 0.$

提示 作变换 $x = a r \cos^8 \varphi, y = b r \sin^8 \varphi$ ，则方程化为 $r = 1 (0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac{\pi}{2})$ .

解 令 $x = \arccos^8\varphi, y = br\sin^8\varphi$ ，则方程化为

$$
r = 1 \quad (0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}).
$$

于是，曲线所围的面积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} S = \iint_ {S} 8 a b r \cos^ {7} \varphi \sin^ {7} \varphi d \varphi = 4 a b \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {7} \varphi \sin^ {7} \varphi d \varphi = 4 a b \int_ {0} ^ {1} u ^ {7} (1 - u ^ {2}) ^ {3} d u \\ = 4 a b \int^ {1} \left(u ^ {7} - 3 u ^ {9} + 3 u ^ {1 1} - u ^ {1 3}\right) d u = 4 a b \left(\frac {1}{8} - \frac {3}{1 0} + \frac {1}{4} - \frac {1}{1 4}\right) = \frac {a b}{7 0}. \\ \end{array}
$$

进行适当的变量代换，求下列曲线所围的面积：

【3996】 $x + y = a, x + y = b, y = \alpha x, y = \beta x (0 < a < b; 0 < \alpha < \beta)$ .

提示 作变换 $x + y = u, \frac{y}{x} = v$ ，则 $a \leqslant u \leqslant b, \alpha \leqslant v \leqslant \beta$ ，且有 $|I| = \frac{u}{(1 + v)^2}$ 。

解 作变换 $x + y = u, \frac{y}{x} = v$ ，则 $a \leqslant u \leqslant b, a \leqslant v \leqslant \beta$ ，且有 $|I| = \frac{u}{(1 + v)^2}$ 。

于是，所求的面积为 $S = \int_{a}^{b} u \, \mathrm{d}u \int_{a}^{\beta} \frac{\mathrm{d}v}{(1 + v)^2} = \frac{1}{2} \cdot \frac{(\beta - \alpha)(b^2 - a^2)}{(1 + \alpha)(1 + \beta)}.$

【3997】 $xy = a^2$ ， $xy = 2a^2$ ， $y = x$ ， $y = 2x$ （ $x > 0;y > 0)$

提示 作变换 $xy = u$ ， $\frac{y}{x} = v$ ，则 $a^2 \leqslant u \leqslant 2a^2, 1 \leqslant v \leqslant 2$ ，且有 $|I| = \frac{1}{2v}$

解 作变换 $xy = u, \frac{y}{x} = v$ ，则 $a^2 \leqslant u \leqslant 2a^2, 1 \leqslant v \leqslant 2$ ，且有 $|I| = \frac{1}{2v}$ 。

于是，所求的面积为 $S = \frac{1}{2}\int_{a^2}^{2a^2}\mathrm{d}u\int_1^2\frac{\mathrm{d}v}{v} = \frac{1}{2} a^2\ln 2.$

【3998】 $y^{2} = 2px,y^{2} = 2qx,x^{2} = 2ry,x^{2} = 2sy(0 <   p <   q;0 <   r <   s).$

提示 作变换 $\frac{y^2}{x} = u, \frac{x^2}{y} = v$ ，则 $2p \leqslant u \leqslant 2q, 2r \leqslant v \leqslant 2s$ ，且有 $|I| = \frac{1}{3}$ 。

解 作变换 $\frac{y^2}{x} = u, \frac{x^2}{y} = v$ ，则 $2p \leqslant u \leqslant 2q, 2r \leqslant v \leqslant 2s$ ，且有 $|I| = \frac{1}{3}$ 。

于是，所求的面积为 $S = \frac{1}{3}\int_{2p}^{2q}\mathrm{d}u\int_{2r}^{2s}\mathrm{d}v = \frac{4}{3} (q - p)(s - r).$

【3999】 $\sqrt{\frac{x}{a}} +\sqrt{\frac{y}{b}} = 1,\sqrt{\frac{x}{a}} +\sqrt{\frac{y}{b}} = 2,\frac{x}{a} = \frac{y}{b},\frac{4x}{a} = \frac{y}{b}$ （ $a > 0,b > 0)$

提示 作变换 $\sqrt{\frac{x}{a}} +\sqrt{\frac{y}{b}} = u,\frac{x}{y} = v$ ，即

$$
x = \frac {u ^ {2} v}{\left(\sqrt {\frac {v}{a}} + \frac {1}{\sqrt {b}}\right) ^ {2}}, \quad y = \frac {u ^ {2}}{\left(\sqrt {\frac {v}{a}} + \frac {1}{\sqrt {b}}\right) ^ {2}},
$$

则 $1 \leqslant u \leqslant 2, \frac{a}{4b} \leqslant v \leqslant \frac{a}{b}$ , 且有 $|I| = \frac{2u^3}{\left(\sqrt{\frac{v}{a}} + \frac{1}{\sqrt{b}}\right)^4}$ .

解 作变换 $\sqrt{\frac{x}{a}} +\sqrt{\frac{y}{b}} = u,\frac{x}{y} = v$ ，即

$$
x = \frac {u ^ {2} v}{\left(\sqrt {\frac {v}{a}} + \frac {1}{\sqrt {b}}\right) ^ {2}}, \quad y = \frac {u ^ {2}}{\left(\sqrt {\frac {v}{a}} + \frac {1}{\sqrt {b}}\right) ^ {2}},
$$

则 $1 \leqslant u \leqslant 2, \frac{a}{4b} \leqslant v \leqslant \frac{a}{b}$ , 且有

$$
| I | = \frac {2 u ^ {3}}{\left(\sqrt {\frac {v}{a}} + \frac {1}{\sqrt {b}}\right) ^ {4}}.
$$

于是，所求的面积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} S = \int_ {1} ^ {2} 2 u ^ {3} \mathrm {d} u \int_ {\frac {a}{4 b}} ^ {\frac {a}{b}} \frac {\mathrm {d} v}{\left(\sqrt {\frac {v}{a}} + \frac {1}{\sqrt {b}}\right) ^ {4}} = \frac {1 5}{2} \int_ {\frac {1}{2 \sqrt {b}}} ^ {\frac {1}{\sqrt {b}}} \frac {2 a t \mathrm {d} t}{\left(\iota + \frac {1}{\sqrt {b}}\right) ^ {4}} \\ = 1 5 a \int_ {\frac {1}{2 \sqrt {b}}} ^ {\frac {1}{\sqrt {b}}} \left[ \frac {1}{\left(t + \frac {1}{\sqrt {b}}\right) ^ {3}} - \frac {1}{\sqrt {b}} \cdot \frac {1}{\left(\sqrt {\frac {1}{b}} + t\right) ^ {4}} \right] d t = 1 5 a \left(\frac {7 b}{7 2} - \frac {3 7 b}{6 4 8}\right) = \frac {6 5 a b}{1 0 8}. \\ \end{array}
$$

\*) 作代换 $v = at^2$

【4000】 $\frac{x^2}{\lambda} + \frac{y^2}{\lambda - c^2} = 1$ ，其中 $\lambda$ 取下列各值：

$$
\frac {1}{3} c ^ {2}, \quad \frac {2}{3} c ^ {2}, \quad \frac {4}{3} c ^ {2}, \quad \frac {5}{3} c ^ {2} \quad (x > 0, y > 0).
$$

解方程 $\frac{x^2}{\lambda} + \frac{y^2}{\lambda - c^2} = 1$ 可变为 $\lambda^2 - (x^2 + y^2 + c^2)\lambda + c^2 x^2 = 0.$

将 $\lambda$ 作为未知量解方程，不妨记方程的两个解为 $\lambda$ 及 $\mu$ ，则

$$
\lambda = \frac {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} + c ^ {2} + \sqrt {\left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} + c ^ {2}\right) ^ {2} - 4 c ^ {2} x ^ {2}}}{2}, \quad \mu = \frac {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} + c ^ {2} - \sqrt {\left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} + c ^ {2}\right) ^ {2} - 4 c ^ {2} x ^ {2}}}{2},
$$

今设按上式作变量代换，将 $(x,y)$ 变为 $(\lambda ,\mu)$ 易知

$$
\left| \frac {D (\lambda , \mu)}{D (x , y)} \right| = \frac {4 c ^ {2} x y}{\sqrt {(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} + c ^ {2}) ^ {2} - 4 c ^ {2} x ^ {2}}} = \frac {4 \sqrt {\lambda \mu (c ^ {2} - \mu) (\lambda - c ^ {2})}}{\lambda - \mu},
$$

从而， $\frac{D(x,y)}{D(\lambda,\mu)} = \frac{1}{\frac{D(\lambda,\mu)}{D(x,y)}} = \frac{\lambda - \mu}{4\sqrt{\lambda\mu(c^2 - \mu)(\lambda - c^2)}}.$

于是，所求的面积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} S = \iint_ {\Omega} \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y = \iint_ {\substack {\frac {4 c ^ {2}}{3} \leqslant \lambda \leqslant \frac {5 c ^ {2}}{3} \\ \frac {c ^ {2}}{3} \leqslant \mu \leqslant \frac {2 c ^ {2}}{3}}} \frac {\lambda - \mu}{4 \sqrt {\lambda \mu (c ^ {2} - \mu) (\lambda - c ^ {2})}} \mathrm {d} \lambda \mathrm {d} \mu = \frac {c ^ {2}}{4} \int_ {\frac {4}{3}} ^ {\frac {5}{3}} \int_ {\frac {1}{3}} ^ {\frac {2}{3}} \frac {u - v}{\sqrt {u v (1 - v) (u - 1)}} \mathrm {d} u \mathrm {d} v \\ = \frac {c ^ {2}}{4} \int_ {\frac {4}{3}} ^ {\frac {5}{3}} \frac {\sqrt {u} d u}{\sqrt {u - 1}} \int_ {\frac {1}{3}} ^ {\frac {2}{3}} \frac {d v}{\sqrt {v (1 - v)}} - \frac {c ^ {2}}{4} \int_ {\frac {4}{3}} ^ {\frac {5}{3}} \frac {d u}{\sqrt {u (u - 1)}} \int_ {\frac {1}{3}} ^ {\frac {2}{3}} \frac {\sqrt {v} d v}{\sqrt {1 - v}}. \\ \end{array}
$$

由于 $\int_{\frac{4}{3}}^{\frac{5}{3}} \frac{\sqrt{u}}{\sqrt{u - 1}} \mathrm{d}u = \frac{\sqrt{10}}{3} - \frac{2}{3} + \lg \frac{\sqrt{5} - \sqrt{2}}{2 - \sqrt{2}}, \quad \int_{\frac{4}{3}}^{\frac{5}{3}} \frac{\mathrm{d}u}{\sqrt{u(u - 1)}} = 2 \lg \frac{\sqrt{5} - \sqrt{2}}{2 - \sqrt{2}},$

$$
\int_ {\frac {1}{3}} ^ {\frac {2}{3}} \frac {\mathrm {d} v}{\sqrt {v (1 - v)}} = 2 \arcsin \sqrt {\frac {2}{3}} - 2 \arcsin \sqrt {\frac {1}{3}}, \quad \int_ {\frac {1}{3}} ^ {\frac {2}{3}} \frac {\sqrt {v}}{\sqrt {1 - v}} \mathrm {d} v = \arcsin \sqrt {\frac {2}{3}} - \arcsin \sqrt {\frac {1}{3}},
$$

故最后得

$$
\begin{array}{l} S = \frac {c ^ {2}}{4} \left[ \left(\frac {\sqrt {1 0}}{3} - \frac {2}{3} + \lg \frac {\sqrt {5} - \sqrt {2}}{2 - \sqrt {2}}\right) \left(2 \arcsin \sqrt {\frac {2}{3}} - 2 \arcsin \sqrt {\frac {1}{3}}\right) \right] - \frac {c ^ {2}}{4} \left[ \left(2 \lg \frac {\sqrt {5} - \sqrt {2}}{2 - \sqrt {2}}\right) \right. \\ \left. \cdot \left(\arcsin \sqrt {\frac {2}{3}} - \arcsin \sqrt {\frac {1}{3}}\right) \right] \\ = \frac {c ^ {2}}{6} (\sqrt {1 0} - 2) \arcsin \frac {1}{3}. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4001】求椭圆 $(a_{1}x + b_{1}y + c_{1})^{2} + (a_{2}x + b_{2}y + c_{2})^{2} = 1$ （其中 $\delta = a_1b_2 - a_2b_1\neq 0)$ 的面积.

提示 作变换 $a_1x + b_1y + c_1 = u$ ， $a_2x + b_2y + c_2 = v$ ，则椭圆所围区域变为 $u^2 + v^2 \leqslant 1$ ，且有 $|I| = \frac{1}{|\delta|}$

解 作变换 $a_1x + b_1y + c_1 = u, a_2x + b_2y + c_2 = v$ ，则椭圆所围区域变为 $u^2 + v^2 \leqslant 1$ ，且有 $|I| = \frac{1}{|\delta|}$ 。

于是，所求的面积为 $S = \frac{1}{|\delta|}\iint_{u^2 +v^2\leqslant 1}du\mathrm{d}v = \frac{\pi}{|\delta|}.$

【4002】 求椭圆 $\frac{x^2}{\mathrm{ch}^2u} +\frac{y^2}{\mathrm{sh}^2u} = c^2 (u = u_1,u_2)$

和双曲线 $\frac{x^2}{\cos^2 v} - \frac{y^2}{\sin^2 v} = c^2 \quad (v = v_1, v_2) \quad (0 < u_1 < u_2; 0 < v_1 < v_2; x > 0, y > 0)$

所围的面积.

提示 作变换 $x = c \operatorname{ch} u \cos v, y = c \operatorname{sh} u \sin v$ ，则有 $|I| = |c^2 \operatorname{ch}^2 u - c^2 \cos^2 v|$ 。

解 作变换 $x = c\mathrm{ch}u\mathrm{cos}v$ ， $y = c\mathrm{sh}u\mathrm{sin}v$ ，则有 $\left|I\right| = \left|c^{2}\mathrm{ch}^{2}u - c^{2}\mathrm{cos}^{2}v\right|$

因为 $\mathrm{ch}^2 u\geqslant 1\geqslant \cos^2 v$ ，故所求的面积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} S = c ^ {2} \int_ {u _ {1}} ^ {u _ {2}} \int_ {v _ {1}} ^ {v _ {2}} \left(\operatorname {c h} ^ {2} u - \cos^ {2} v\right) \mathrm {d} u \mathrm {d} v = c ^ {2} \left[ \left(v _ {2} - v _ {1}\right) \int_ {u _ {1}} ^ {u _ {2}} \frac {1 + \operatorname {c h} 2 u}{2} \mathrm {d} u - \left(u _ {2} - u _ {1}\right) \int_ {v _ {1}} ^ {v _ {2}} \cos^ {2} v \mathrm {d} v \right] \\ = \frac {c ^ {2}}{4} \left[ \left(v _ {2} - v _ {1}\right) \left(\operatorname {s h} 2 u _ {2} - \operatorname {s h} 2 u _ {1}\right) - \left(u _ {2} - u _ {1}\right) \left(\sin 2 v _ {2} - \sin 2 v _ {1}\right) \right]. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4003】求平面 $x + y + z = b$ 与曲面 $x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2} - xy - xz - yz = a^{2}$ 相截所得截断面之面积.

解 为简化平面和曲面的方程，作变量代换

$$
x ^ {\prime} = \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} x - \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} z, \quad y ^ {\prime} = \frac {1}{\sqrt {6}} x - \frac {2}{\sqrt {6}} y + \frac {1}{\sqrt {6}} z, \quad z ^ {\prime} = \frac {1}{\sqrt {3}} x + \frac {1}{\sqrt {3}} y + \frac {1}{\sqrt {3}} z,
$$

这是一个正交变换，故 $Ox'y'z'$ 成为一新的直角坐标系.在新的坐标系下，平面方程为

$$
z ^ {\prime} = \frac {1}{\sqrt {3}} (x + y + z) = \frac {b}{\sqrt {3}}.
$$

由于 $x = \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} x' + \frac{1}{\sqrt{6}} y' + \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}} z'$ , $y = \frac{-\sqrt{6}}{3} y' + \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}} z'$ , $z = -\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} x' + \frac{1}{\sqrt{6}} y' + \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}} z'$ ,  
故有 $x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2} - xy - xz - yz = \frac{1}{2} [(x - y)^{2} + (y - z)^{2} + (z - x)^{2}] = \frac{3}{2} (x'^{2} + y'^{2}).$

从而，曲面方程变为 $x^{\prime 2} + y^{\prime 2} = \frac{2}{3} a^{2}$ .于是，所求的面积为

$$
S = \iint_ {x ^ {\prime 2} + y ^ {\prime 2} \leqslant \frac {2}{3} a ^ {2}} d x ^ {\prime} d y ^ {\prime} = \frac {2}{3} \pi a ^ {2}.
$$

【4004】求平面 $z = 1 - 2(x + y)$ 与曲面 $\frac{1}{x} +\frac{1}{y} +\frac{1}{z} = 0$ 相截所得截断面之面积.

解 平面被曲面所截部分记为 $S$ , 它在 $Oxy$ 平面上的投影记为 $D$ . 由于平面 $z = 1 - 2(x + y)$ 的法线之方向余弦为 $\cos \alpha = \cos \beta = \frac{2}{3}$ , $\cos \gamma = \frac{1}{3}$ , 故 $D = S\cos \gamma = \frac{1}{3} S$ , 从而, $S = 3D$ , 显然 $D$ 为 $Oxy$ 平面上由曲线 $\frac{1}{x} + \frac{1}{y} + \frac{1}{1 - 2(x + y)} = 0$ (也即 $2x^2 + 2y^2 + 3xy - x - y = 0$ ) 所围的区域. 作变量代换

$$
x = u + v + \frac {1}{7}, \quad y = u - v + \frac {1}{7}.
$$

于是， $\frac{D(x,y)}{D(u,v)} = -2$ ，且曲线 $2x^{2} + 2y^{2} + 3xy - x - y = 0$ 变为 $7u^{2} + v^{2} - \frac{1}{7} = 0$ ，这是一个椭圆（在 $uv$ 平面上）。从而，即得

$$
D = \iint_ {D} \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y = 2 \iint_ {4 9 u ^ {2} - 7 v ^ {2} \leqslant 1} \mathrm {d} u \mathrm {d} v = 2 \pi \left(\frac {1}{7}\right) \left(\frac {1}{\sqrt {7}}\right) = \frac {2 \pi}{7 \sqrt {7}}.
$$

由此，最后得 $S = 3D = \frac{6\pi}{7\sqrt{7}}.$

# § 3. 体积的计算法

如图8.38所示，设柱体顶面位于连续曲面 $z = f(x,y)$ ，底面位于平面 $z = 0$ ，侧面垂直于底面，且底面在平面 $Oxy$ 上所占区域 $\Omega$ 是可求积的，则.柱体的体积等于

$$
V = \iint_ {\Omega} f (x, y) d x d y.
$$

![](images/d64a1682da02df2bd164dc316518dfffd1c8e705d71f2b5b9d22920d50e7bc85.jpg)  
图8.38

![](images/32541a2515a945c5a592290588ee24cf324b1b3bc53b59710e7c4a0623ce0b7e.jpg)  
图8.39

【4005】试绘出一物体，其体积等于积分

$$
V = \int_ {0} ^ {1} d x \int_ {0} ^ {1 - x} (x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}) d y.
$$

解 积分域为三角形 $0 \leqslant x \leqslant 1, 0 \leqslant y \leqslant 1 - x$ .

柱体上顶为旋转抛物面 $z = x^{2} + y^{2}$ .物体的形状如图8.39所示

【4006】 绘出下列二重积分所表示的体积：

(1) $\iint_{\substack{0 \leq x + y \leq 1 \\ x \geq 0, y \geq 0}} (x + y) \mathrm{d}x \mathrm{d}y;$

(2) $\iint_{\substack{\frac{x^2}{4} + \frac{y^2}{9} \leqslant 1}} \sqrt{1 - \frac{x^2}{4} - \frac{y^2}{9}} \, \mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y;$

(3) $\iint_{|x| + |y| \leqslant 1} (x^2 + y^2) \, \mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y;$

(4) $\iint_{x^2 + y^2 \leqslant x} \sqrt{x^2 + y^2} \, \mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y;$

（5） $\iint_{\substack{1\leqslant x\leqslant 2\\ r\leqslant y\leqslant 2r}}\sqrt{xy}\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y;$

(6) $\iint_{x^2 + y^2 \leq 1} \sin \pi \sqrt{x^2 + y^2} \, \mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y.$

解（1）积分域为三角形 $0 \leqslant x + y \leqslant 1, x \geqslant 0, y \geqslant 0.$ 柱体的上顶为平面 $z = x + y$ （图8.40）

![](images/b5bd451c7fd8826fda3e95ddcae6770465724d8e9dd7efcaa4915eff23176a3e.jpg)  
图8.40

![](images/6e0424e5ceb117aa3864a7d33d065d254c62a88b8f90efe002817ffbd0cf9eb8.jpg)  
图8.41

（2）积分域为椭圆 $\frac{x^2}{4} +\frac{y^2}{9}\leqslant 1$ ，即立体的底面，顶面为椭球面 $z = \sqrt{1 - \frac{x^2}{4} - \frac{y^2}{9}}$ （图8.41).

（3）积分域为由直线 $x + y = 1, x + y = -1, x - y = 1, y - x = 1$ 围成的正方形. 柱体的顶面为旋转抛物面 $z = x^2 + y^2$ . 图8.42仅画了第一卦限部分的体积.

![](images/010dddfc2d1347a11ecc268c18bdb9b5f5b8b57789231787bcc592475ec620aa.jpg)  
图8.42

![](images/f07754eaf1b32c763a92ca906c703ec35a44d538e78ee0e459df58cbb058aabf.jpg)  
图8.43

（4）积分域为圆 $\left(x - \frac{1}{2}\right)^2 + y^2 \leqslant \frac{1}{4}$ . 柱体的顶面为圆锥面 $z = \sqrt{x^2 + y^2}$ （图8.43）.  
（5）积分域为梯形 $1 \leqslant x \leqslant 2, x \leqslant y \leqslant 2x.$ 柱体的顶面为双曲抛物面 $z = \sqrt{xy}$ （图8.44）

![](images/d2e3d7cb1ca820b984ee5f4a476ae5e698b32b7dcd4b12ff963a06f50430416b.jpg)  
图8.44

![](images/f690b28edd08251c300273f036cbb0bf7e1c72e12ed18a9e7bca5feb36bbd1e1.jpg)  
图8.45

（6）积分域为圆 $x^{2} + y^{2}\leqslant 1.$ 即立体的底面，顶面是由正弦曲线 $z = \sin \pi x$ 绕 $Oz$ 轴旋转一周而得的旋转曲面(图8.45).

求下列曲面所围区域的体积：

【4007】 $z = 1 + x + y, z = 0, x + y = 1, x = 0, y = 0.$

解 $V = \int_{0}^{1}\mathrm{d}x\int_{0}^{1 - x}(1 + x + y)\mathrm{d}y = \int_{0}^{1}\left(\frac{3}{2} -x - \frac{x^2}{2}\right)dx = \frac{5}{6}.$

【4008】 $x + y + z = a, x^2 + y^2 = R^2, x = 0, y = 0, z = 0 (a \geqslant R\sqrt{2})$

解 $V = \int_{0}^{R}\mathrm{d}x\int_{0}^{\sqrt{R^2 - x^2}}(a - x - y)\mathrm{d}y = \int_{0}^{R}\left[(a - x)\sqrt{R^2 - x^2} -\frac{R^2 - x^2}{2}\right]\mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \int_ {0} ^ {R} a \sqrt {R ^ {2} - x ^ {2}} d x - \int_ {0} ^ {R} \left(x \sqrt {R ^ {2} - x ^ {2}} + \frac {R ^ {2} - x ^ {2}}{2}\right) d x = \frac {\pi a R ^ {2}}{4} - \frac {2 R ^ {3}}{3}.
$$

【4009】 $z = x^{2} + y^{2},y = x^{2},y = 1,z = 0.$

解 $V = \int_{-1}^{1}\mathrm{d}x\int_{x^2}^{1}(x^2 +y^2)\mathrm{d}y = \frac{88}{105}.$

【4010】 $z = \cos x\cos y, z = 0, |x + y| \leqslant \frac{\pi}{2}, |x - y| \leqslant \frac{\pi}{2}.$

提示 注意函数 $z = \cos x\cos y$ 的图像关于 $Oyz$ 平面对称，而积分域关于 $Oy$ 轴对称.

解 因函数 $z = \cos x\cos y$ 的图像关于 $Oyz$ 平面对称，而积分域(图8.46)关于 $Oy$ 轴对称，故所求的体积为

$$
V = 2 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d x \int_ {x - \frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2} - r} \cos x \cos y d y = 4 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {2} x d x = 4 \left(\frac {x}{2} + \frac {\sin 2 x}{4}\right) \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} = \pi .
$$

【4011】 $z = \sin \frac{\pi y}{2x}, z = 0, y = x, y = 0, x = \pi.$

解 $V = \int_{0}^{\pi}\mathrm{d}x\int_{0}^{x}\sin \frac{\pi y}{2x}\mathrm{d}y = \frac{2}{\pi}\int_{0}^{\pi}x\mathrm{d}x = \pi .$

【4012】 $z = xy, x + y + z = 1, z = 0.$

提示 注意所求的体积 $V$ 由两部分组成：

$$
V _ {1}: 0 \leqslant x \leqslant 1, 0 \leqslant y \leqslant \frac {1 - x}{1 + x}, z = x y.
$$

$$
V _ {2}: 0 \leqslant x \leqslant 1, \frac {1 - x}{1 + x} \leqslant y \leqslant 1 - x, z = 1 - x - y.
$$

解体积 $V$ 由两部分组成：

$$
V _ {1}: 0 \leqslant x \leqslant 1, 0 \leqslant y \leqslant \frac {1 - x}{1 + x}, z = x y.
$$

$$
V _ {2}: 0 \leqslant x \leqslant 1, \frac {1 - x}{1 + x} \leqslant y \leqslant 1 - x, z = 1 - x - y.
$$

![](images/e17d2e7b17145b863a8897c642c7505acde310a19e7d0db98767ea92358b76e6.jpg)  
图8.46

它们在 $Oxy$ 平面上的投影域 $\Omega_{1}$ 及 $\Omega_{2}$ 如图8.47所示.于是，所求的体积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = V _ {1} + V _ {2} \\ = \int_ {0} ^ {1} x \mathrm {d} x \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {1 - x}{1 + x}} y \mathrm {d} y + \int_ {0} ^ {1} \mathrm {d} x \int_ {\frac {1 - x}{1 + x}} ^ {1 - x} (1 - x - y) \mathrm {d} y = \left(- \frac {1 1}{4} + 4 \ln 2\right) + \left(\frac {2 5}{6} - 6 \ln 2\right) = \frac {1 7}{1 2} - 2 \ln 2. \\ \end{array}
$$

![](images/bb9165a4f27a003c9bacd6799457a7766ddb9d9ed84059554c9d922e20bffabd.jpg)  
图8.47

变换成极坐标，求下列曲面所围区域的体积：

【4013】 $z^2 = xy, x^2 + y^2 = a^2.$

提示 注意对称性，令 $x = r\cos \varphi, y = r\sin \varphi$ ，并利用3856题的结果.

解 因为 $z = \sqrt{xy}$ ，故所求的体积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = 4 \iint_ {\substack {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} \leqslant a ^ {2} \\ x \geqslant 0, y \geqslant 0}} \sqrt {x y} \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y = 4 \int_ {0} ^ {a} \mathrm {d} r \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \sqrt {\cos \varphi \sin \varphi} r ^ {2} \mathrm {d} \varphi = \frac {4}{3} a ^ {3} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {\frac {1}{2}} \varphi \sin^ {\frac {1}{2}} \varphi \mathrm {d} \varphi \\ = \frac {4}{3} a ^ {3} \frac {1}{2} B \left(\frac {3}{4}, \frac {3}{4}\right) ^ {*}) = \frac {2}{3} a ^ {3} \frac {\Gamma^ {2} \left(\frac {3}{4}\right)}{\Gamma \left(\frac {3}{2}\right)} = \frac {2}{3} a ^ {3} \frac {\Gamma^ {2} \left(\frac {3}{4}\right)}{\frac {1}{2} \Gamma \left(\frac {1}{2}\right)} = \frac {4}{3} a ^ {3} \frac {\Gamma^ {2} \left(\frac {3}{4}\right)}{\sqrt {\pi}}. \\ \end{array}
$$

\*) 利用3856题的结果.

【4014】 $z = x + y, (x^2 + y^2)^2 = 2xy, z = 0 (x > 0, y > 0)$

提示 令 $x = r\cos \varphi, y = r\sin \varphi$ ，并利用3856题的结果.

解 令 $x = r\cos \varphi, y = r\sin \varphi$ ，则方程 $(x^2 + y^2)^2 = 2xy$ 及 $z = x + y$ 变为

$$
r ^ {2} = 2 \sin \varphi \cos \varphi = \sin 2 \varphi \quad \text {及} \quad z = r (\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi).
$$

于是，所求的体积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = \iint_ {\Omega} (x + y) d x d y = \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt {\sin 2 \varphi}} r ^ {2} (\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi) d r = \frac {2 \sqrt {2}}{3} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \left(\sin^ {\frac {5}{2}} \varphi \cos^ {\frac {3}{2}} \varphi + \cos^ {\frac {5}{2}} \varphi \sin^ {\frac {3}{2}} \varphi\right) d \varphi \\ = \frac {2 \sqrt {2}}{3} B \left(\frac {5}{4}, \frac {7}{4}\right) ^ {\prime \prime} = \frac {2 \sqrt {2}}{3} \frac {\Gamma \left(\frac {5}{4}\right) \Gamma \left(\frac {7}{4}\right)}{\Gamma (3)} = \frac {2 \sqrt {2}}{3} \frac {\frac {1}{4} \cdot \frac {3}{4} \Gamma \left(\frac {1}{4}\right) \Gamma \left(\frac {3}{4}\right)}{2 !} \\ = \frac {\sqrt {2}}{1 6} \frac {\pi}{\sin \frac {\pi}{4}} = \frac {\pi}{8}. \\ \end{array}
$$

\*) 利用3856题的结果.

【4015】 $z = x^{2} + y^{2},x^{2} + y^{2} = x,x^{2} + y^{2} = 2x,z = 0,$

解令 $x = r\cos \varphi$ ， $y = r\sin \varphi$ ，则方程 $x^{2} + y^{2} = x$ ， $x^{2} + y^{2} = 2x$ 及 $z = x^{2} + y^{2}$ 变为

$$
r = \cos \varphi , \quad r = 2 \cos \varphi \quad \text {及} \quad z = r ^ {2}.
$$

于是，所求的体积为

$$
V = \iint_ {\Omega} (x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}) d x d y = \int_ {- \frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {\cos \varphi} ^ {2 \cos \varphi} r ^ {3} d r = \frac {2}{4} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} (1 6 \cos^ {4} \varphi - \cos^ {4} \varphi) d \varphi = \frac {1 5}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {4} \varphi d \varphi
$$

$$
= \frac {1 5}{2} \cdot \frac {3}{4} \cdot \frac {1}{2} \cdot \frac {\pi}{2} = \frac {4 5}{3 2} \pi .
$$

【4016】 $x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2} = a^{2}, x^{2} + y^{2} \geqslant a|x| (a > 0)$

解只需计算由下列曲面所围区域的体积：

$$
x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} + z ^ {2} = a ^ {2}, \quad x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} \leqslant a | x |.
$$

若引用极坐标，则 $r^2 + z^2 = a^2$ ， $r^2 \leqslant a |r \cos \varphi|$ ，其体积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} V _ {1} = 8 \iint_ {\substack {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} \leqslant a r \\ x \geqslant 0, y \geqslant 0}} \sqrt {a ^ {2} - (x ^ {2} + y ^ {2})} \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y = 8 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \mathrm {d} \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {a \cos \varphi} r \sqrt {a ^ {2} - r ^ {2}} \mathrm {d} r = - \frac {8}{3} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} (a ^ {2} - r ^ {2}) ^ {\frac {3}{2}} \left| \begin{array}{c} a \cos \varphi \\ 0 \end{array} \right. \mathrm {d} \varphi \\ = \frac {8 a ^ {3}}{3} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} (1 - \sin^ {3} \varphi) d \varphi = \frac {4 \pi a ^ {3}}{3} - \frac {1 6 a ^ {3}}{9}. \\ \end{array}
$$

于是，所求的体积为 $V = \frac{4\pi a^3}{3} -\left(\frac{4\pi a^3}{3} -\frac{16a^3}{9}\right) = \frac{16a^3}{9}.$

【4017】 $x^{2} + y^{2} - az = 0, (x^{2} + y^{2})^{2} = a^{2}(x^{2} - y^{2}), z = 0 (a > 0)$

解 若引用极坐标，则有 $z = \frac{r^2}{a},\qquad r^2 = a^2\cos 2\varphi \quad (a > 0).$

于是，利用对称性知，所求的体积为

$$
V = 4 \iint_ {\Omega} \frac {1}{a} (x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}) d x d y = 4 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {a \sqrt {\cos 2 \varphi}} \frac {r ^ {2}}{a} r d r = a ^ {3} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} \cos^ {2} 2 \varphi d \varphi = \frac {\pi a ^ {3}}{8}.
$$

【4018】 $z = \mathrm{e}^{-(x^2 -y^2)}$ ， $z = 0$ ， $x^{2} + y^{2} = R^{2}$

解利用对称性，得所求的体积为

$$
V = 4 \iint_ {\substack {x ^ {2} - y ^ {2} \leqslant R ^ {2} \\ x \geqslant 0, y \geqslant 0}} \mathrm {e} ^ {- (x ^ {2} - y ^ {2})} \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y = 4 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \mathrm {d} \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {R} \mathrm {e} ^ {- r ^ {2}} r \mathrm {d} r = \pi (1 - \mathrm {e} ^ {R ^ {2}}).
$$

【4019】 $z = c\cos \frac{\pi\sqrt{x^2 + y^2}}{2a},x^2 +y^2 = a^2,y = x\tan \alpha ,y = x\tan \beta (a > 0,c > 0,0\leqslant a <   \beta \leqslant 2\pi).$

解 所求的体积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = \iint_ {a} c \cos \frac {\pi \sqrt {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}}}{2 a} d x d y = \int_ {a} ^ {\beta} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {a} c r \cos \frac {\pi r}{2 a} d r = c (\beta - \alpha) \left[ \frac {2 a r}{\pi} \sin \frac {\pi r}{2 a} + \frac {4 a ^ {2}}{\pi^ {2}} \cos \frac {\pi r}{2 a} \right] \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {a} \\ = 2 a ^ {2} c (\beta - \alpha) \left(\frac {1}{\pi} - \frac {2}{\pi^ {2}}\right) = \frac {2 a ^ {2} c (\beta - \alpha) (\pi - 2)}{\pi^ {2}}. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4020】 $z = x^{2} + y^{2}, z = x + y.$

提示 注意两曲面的交线在 $Oxy$ 平面上的投影域的围线为圆

$$
x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} = x + y \quad {\text {或}} \quad \left(x - {\frac {1}{2}}\right) ^ {2} + \left(y - {\frac {1}{2}}\right) ^ {2} = {\frac {1}{2}}.
$$

故令 $x = \frac{1}{2} + r\cos \varphi, y = \frac{1}{2} + r\sin \varphi$ ，则曲面方程化为

$$
z = r ^ {2} + \frac {1}{2} + r (\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi) \quad \text {及} \quad z = 1 + r (\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi) \quad (0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant 2 \pi ,   0 \leqslant r \leqslant \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}}).
$$

解 立体的投影域的围线为 $x^{2} + y^{2} = x + y$ 或 $\left(x - \frac{1}{2}\right)^{2} + \left(y - \frac{1}{2}\right)^{2} = \frac{1}{2}$ . 若引用代换 $x = \frac{1}{2} + r\cos \varphi, y = \frac{1}{2} + r\sin \varphi$ , 则有

$$
z = r ^ {2} + \frac {1}{2} + r (\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi), \quad z = 1 + r (\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi) (0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant 2 \pi , 0 \leqslant r \leqslant \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}}).
$$

于是，所求的体积为

$$
V = \iint_ {\left(x - \frac {1}{2}\right) ^ {2} - \left(y - \frac {1}{2}\right) ^ {2} \leqslant \frac {1}{2}} \left[ (x + y) - \left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}\right) \right] d x d y
$$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {1}{\sqrt {2}}} \left\{\left[ 1 + r (\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi) \right] - \left[ r ^ {2} + \frac {1}{2} + r (\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi) \right] \right\} r d r \\ = \int_ {0} ^ {3 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {1}{\sqrt {2}}} \left(\frac {1}{2} - r ^ {2}\right) r d r = \frac {\pi}{8}. \\ \end{array}
$$

求下列曲面所围区域的体积（假定参数是正的）：

【4021】 $\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2} +\frac{z^2}{c^2} = 1,\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2} = \frac{z^2}{c^2}$ （ $z > 0$ ）

提示 注意两曲面的交线在 $Oxy$ 平面上的投影域的围线为椭圆 $\frac{x^2}{a^2} + \frac{y^2}{b^2} = \frac{1}{2}$ ，故令 $x = a\cos \varphi, y = b\sin \varphi$ ，则曲面方程化为

$$
z = c \sqrt {1 - r ^ {2}} \quad \text {及} \quad z = c r \quad (0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant 2 \pi , 0 \leqslant r \leqslant \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}}).
$$

解两曲面的交线在 $Oxy$ 平面上的投影为椭圆 $\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2} = \frac{1}{2}$ 令 $x = ar\cos \varphi ,y = br\sin \varphi$ ，则方程化为

$$
z = c \sqrt {1 - r ^ {2}} \quad \text {及} \quad z = c r \quad (0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant 2 \pi , 0 \leqslant r \leqslant \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}}).
$$

于是，曲面所围区域的体积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = \iint_ {a} \left[ c \sqrt {1 - \left(\frac {x ^ {2}}{a ^ {2}} + \frac {y ^ {2}}{b ^ {2}}\right)} - c \sqrt {\frac {x ^ {2}}{a ^ {2}} + \frac {y ^ {2}}{b ^ {2}}} \right] d x d y = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {1}{\sqrt {2}}} a b r (c \sqrt {1 - r ^ {2}} - c r) d r \\ = a b c \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {1}{\sqrt {2}}} (r \sqrt {1 - r ^ {2}} - r ^ {2}) d r = - \frac {1}{3} a b c \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} \left[ r ^ {3} + (1 - r ^ {2}) ^ {\frac {3}{2}} \right] \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {\frac {1}{\sqrt {2}}} d \varphi \\ = \frac {1}{3} \pi a b c (2 - \sqrt {2}). \\ \end{array}
$$

【4022】 $\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2} -\frac{z^2}{c^2} = -1,\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2} = 1.$

提示 令 $x = \arccos \varphi, y = brsin\varphi$ ，则曲面方程化为

$$
z = \pm c \sqrt {1 + r ^ {2}} \quad (0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant 2 \pi , 0 \leqslant r \leqslant 1).
$$

解 若令 $x = \arccos \varphi, y = b r \sin \varphi$ ，则曲面方程化为

$$
z = \pm c \sqrt {1 + r ^ {2}} \quad (0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant 2 \pi , 0 \leqslant r \leqslant 1).
$$

于是，曲面所围区域的体积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = \iint_ {\frac {x ^ {2}}{a ^ {2}} + \frac {y ^ {2}}{b ^ {2}} \leqslant 1} 2 c \sqrt {1 + \frac {x ^ {2}}{a ^ {2}} + \frac {y ^ {2}}{b ^ {2}}} d x d y = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {1} 2 a b c r \sqrt {1 + r ^ {2}} d r = 2 a b c \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \int_ {0} ^ {1} r \sqrt {1 + r ^ {2}} d r \\ = \frac {4 \pi}{3} a b c (2 \sqrt {2} - 1). \\ \end{array}
$$

【4023】 $\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2} = \frac{z}{c},\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2} = \frac{x}{a} +\frac{y}{b},z = 0.$

提示 注意立体在 $Oxy$ 平面上的投影域的围线为椭圆

$$
\frac {x ^ {2}}{a ^ {2}} + \frac {y ^ {2}}{b ^ {2}} = \frac {x}{a} + \frac {y}{b} \quad \text {或} \quad \left(\frac {x}{a} - \frac {1}{2}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {y}{b} - \frac {1}{2}\right) ^ {2} = \frac {1}{2},
$$

故令 $\frac{x}{a} = \frac{1}{2} + r\cos \varphi, \frac{y}{b} = \frac{1}{2} + r\sin \varphi,$ 则曲面方程化为

$$
z = c \left[ \frac {1}{2} + r (\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi) + r ^ {2} \right] \quad (0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant 2 \pi , 0 \leqslant r \leqslant \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}}).
$$

解 立体在 $Oxy$ 平面上的投影域的围线为椭圆 $\frac{x^2}{a^2} + \frac{y^2}{b^2} = \frac{x}{a} + \frac{y}{b}$ ，即 $\left(\frac{x}{a} - \frac{1}{2}\right)^2 + \left(\frac{y}{b} - \frac{1}{2}\right)^2 = \frac{1}{2}$ .

若令 $\frac{x}{u} = \frac{1}{2} + r\cos \varphi, \frac{y}{b} = \frac{1}{2} + r\sin \varphi$ ，则曲面方程化为

$$
z = c \left[ \frac {1}{2} + r (\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi) + r ^ {2} \right] \quad (0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant 2 \pi , 0 \leqslant r \leqslant \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}}).
$$

于是，曲面所围区域的体积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = \iint_ {\left(\frac {x}{a} + \frac {1}{2}\right) ^ {2} \cdot \left(\frac {y}{b} - \frac {1}{2}\right) ^ {2} \leqslant \frac {1}{2}} c \left(\frac {x ^ {2}}{a ^ {2}} + \frac {y ^ {2}}{b ^ {2}}\right) d x d y = a b c \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {n} ^ {\frac {1}{\sqrt {2}}} r \left[ \frac {1}{2} + r (\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi) + r ^ {2} \right] d r \\ = a b c \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} \left[ \frac {1}{8} + \frac {1}{6 \sqrt {2}} (\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi) + \frac {1}{1 6} \right] d \varphi = a b c \frac {3 \cdot 2 \pi}{1 6} = \frac {3}{8} \pi a b c. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4024】 $\left(\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2}\right)^2 +\frac{z}{c} = 1,z = 0.$

提示 令 $x = \arccos \varphi, y = b r \sin \varphi$ ，则曲面方程化为

$$
z = c (1 - r ^ {4}) \quad (0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant 2 \pi , 0 \leqslant r \leqslant 1).
$$

解 若令 $x = \arccos \varphi, y = b r \sin \varphi$ ，则曲面方程化为

$$
z = c (1 - r ^ {1}) \quad (0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant 2 \pi , 0 \leqslant r \leqslant 1).
$$

于是，曲面所围区域的体积为

$$
V = \iint_ {\frac {r ^ {2}}{a ^ {2}} \cdot \frac {v ^ {2}}{b ^ {2}} \leqslant 1} c \left[ 1 - \left(\frac {x ^ {2}}{a ^ {2}} + \frac {y ^ {2}}{b ^ {2}}\right) \right] d x d y = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {1} a b c r (1 - r ^ {3}) d r = \frac {2}{3} \pi a b c.
$$

【4025】 $\left(\frac{x}{a} +\frac{y}{b}\right)^2 +\frac{z^2}{c^2} = 1,x = 0,y = 0,z = 0.$

提示 计算位于第一卦限（即 $x \geq 0, y \geq 0, z \geq 0$ ）部分的体积。令 $x = a r \cos^2 \varphi, y = b r \sin^2 \varphi$ ，则曲面方程化为

$$
z = c \sqrt {1 - r ^ {2}} \quad (0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, 0 \leqslant r \leqslant 1).
$$

解下面计算位于第一卦限部分的体积.令 $x = a r\cos^2\varphi$ ， $y = b r\sin^2\varphi$ ，则曲面方程化为

$$
z = c \sqrt {1 - r ^ {2}} \quad (0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, 0 \leqslant r \leqslant 1).
$$

于是，曲面所围区域的体积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = \iint_ {\Omega} c \sqrt {1 - \left(\frac {x}{a} + \frac {y}{b}\right) ^ {2}} d x d y = \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {1} a b c \sin 2 \varphi \sqrt {1 - r ^ {2}} r d r \\ = a b c \left(\int_ {L} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \sin 2 \varphi d \varphi\right) \left(\int_ {0} ^ {1} r \sqrt {1 - r ^ {2}} d r\right) = \frac {a b c}{3}. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4026】 $\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2} +\frac{z^2}{c^2} = 1,\quad \left(\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2}\right)^2 = \frac{x^2}{a^2} -\frac{y^2}{b^2}.$

解 令 $x = \arccos \varphi, y = brsin\varphi$ ，则方程化为

$$
z = \pm c \sqrt {1 - r ^ {2}}, \quad r ^ {2} = \cos^ {2} \varphi - \sin^ {2} \varphi = \cos 2 \varphi
$$

（因 $r^2 = \cos 2\varphi \geqslant 0$ ，故 $-\frac{\pi}{4} \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac{\pi}{4}, \frac{3\pi}{4} \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac{5\pi}{4})$ .于是，利用对称性知，曲面所围区域的体积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = 8 c \iint_ {\Omega} \sqrt {1 - \frac {r ^ {2}}{a ^ {2}} - \frac {y ^ {2}}{b ^ {2}}} d x d y = 8 a b c \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt {\cos 2 \varphi}} \sqrt {1 - r ^ {2}} r d r d \varphi \\ = 8 a b c \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} \frac {1}{3} (1 - \sqrt {8} \sin^ {3} \varphi) d \varphi = \frac {8 a b c}{3} \left(\varphi + \sqrt {8} \cos \varphi - \frac {\sqrt {8}}{3} \cos^ {3} \varphi\right) \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} \\ = \frac {8 a b c}{3} \left(\frac {\pi}{4} + \frac {5}{3} - \frac {4 \sqrt {2}}{3}\right) = \frac {2 a b c}{9} (3 \pi + 2 0 - 1 6 \sqrt {2}). \\ \end{array}
$$

【4027】 $z^2 = xy, x + y = a, x + y = b (0 < a < b)$

解 由于 $z = \pm \sqrt{xy}$ ，又所界立体在 $Oxy$ 平面上的投影域 $\Omega$ 由直线 $x + y = a, x + y = b, x = 0$ 及 $y = 0$ 围成。利用对称性知，曲面所围区域的体积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = 2 \iint_ {\Omega} \sqrt {x y} d x d y = 2 \left(\int_ {0} ^ {a} d x \int_ {a - x} ^ {b - r} \sqrt {x y} d y + \int_ {a} ^ {b} d x \int_ {0} ^ {b - x} \sqrt {x y} d y\right) \\ = \frac {4}{3} \int_ {0} ^ {a} \left[ \sqrt {x (b - x) ^ {3}} - \sqrt {x (a - x) ^ {3}} \right] d x + \frac {4}{3} \int_ {a} ^ {b} \sqrt {x (b - x) ^ {3}} d x \\ = \frac {4}{3} \int_ {0} ^ {b} (b - x) \sqrt {x (b - x)} d x - \frac {4}{3} \int_ {0} ^ {a} (a - x) \sqrt {a (a - x)} d x. \\ \end{array}
$$

令 $x = b\sin^2 t$ ，可得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int_ {0} ^ {b} (b - x) \sqrt {x (b - x)} d x = 2 b ^ {3} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {4} t \sin^ {2} t d t \\ = 2 b ^ {3} \left(\int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {4} t d t - \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {6} t d t\right) = 2 b ^ {3} \left(\frac {3 \cdot 1}{4 \cdot 2} - \frac {5 \cdot 3 \cdot 1}{6 \cdot 4 \cdot 2}\right) \frac {\pi}{2} = \frac {1}{1 6} \pi b ^ {3}; \\ \end{array}
$$

同理，有 $\int_0^a (a - x)\sqrt{x(a - x)}\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{16}\pi a^3.$

于是，所求的体积为 $V = \frac{4}{3}\left(\frac{\pi b^3}{16} -\frac{\pi a^3}{16}\right) = \frac{\pi}{12} (b^3 -a^3).$

【4028】 $z = x^{2} + y^{2},xy = a^{2},xy = 2a^{2},y = \frac{x}{2},y = 2x,z = 0.$

提示 注意曲面所围区域的立体在 $(xy)$ 平面上的投影域由曲线 $xy = a^2$ ， $xy = 2a^2$ 及直线 $y = \frac{x}{2}$ ， $y = 2x$ 围成，故令 $xy = ua^2$ ， $y = vx$ ，则积分域变为长方形域

$$
1 \leqslant u \leqslant 2, \frac {1}{2} \leqslant v \leqslant 2, \text {且} | I | = \frac {a ^ {2}}{2 v}, z = x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} = a ^ {2} (\frac {u}{v} + u v).
$$

再利用对称性，

解 曲面所界的立体在 $Oxy$ 平面上的投影域 $\Omega$ 由曲线 $xy = a^2$ ， $xy = 2a^2$ 和直线 $y = \frac{x}{2}$ ， $y = 2x$ 围成。利用对称性知，曲面所围区域的体积为 $V = 2\iint_{\Omega} z \, \mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y = 2\iint_{\Omega} (x^2 + y^2) \, \mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y.$

作变量代换 $xy = ua^2, y = vx$ ，则积分域变为长方形域 $1 \leqslant u \leqslant 2, \frac{1}{2} \leqslant v \leqslant 2$ ，且 $|I| = \frac{a^2}{2v}, z = x^2 + y^2 = a^2\left(\frac{u}{v} + uv\right)$ 。

于是，所求的体积为

$$
V = 2 \iint_ {\Omega} (x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}) \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y = 2 \iint_ {\substack {1 \leq u \leq 2 \\ \frac{1}{2} \leq v \leq 2}} a ^ {2} \left(\frac{u}{v} + u v\right) \frac{a ^ {2}}{2 v} \mathrm {d} u \mathrm {d} v = a ^ {4} \int_ {1} ^ {2} u \mathrm {d} u \int_ {\frac{1}{2}} ^ {2} \left(1 + \frac{1}{v^{2}}\right) \mathrm {d} v = \frac{9}{2} a ^ {4}.
$$

【4029】 $z = xy, x^2 = y, x^2 = 2y, y^2 = x, y^2 = 2x, z = 0.$

提示仿4028题，令 $x = uy^2$ ， $y = vx^2$ ，则积分域 $\Omega$ 变为正方形域 $\frac{1}{2} \leq u \leq 1, \frac{1}{2} \leq v \leq 1$ ，且 $|I| = \frac{1}{3} u^{2}v^{2}$

解曲面所围区域的立体在 $Oxy$ 平面上的投影域 $\Omega$ 由曲线 $x^{2} = y, x^{2} = 2y, y^{2} = x$ 及 $y^{2} = 2x$ 围成.我们有

$$
V = \iint_ {\Omega} z d x d y = \iint_ {\Omega} x y d x d y.
$$

作变量代换

$$
x = u y ^ {2}, \quad y = v x ^ {2}, \quad \text {或} x = u ^ {- \frac {1}{3}} v ^ {- \frac {2}{3}}, \quad y = u ^ {- \frac {2}{3}} v ^ {- \frac {1}{3}},
$$

则积分域 $\Omega$ 变为正方形域 $\frac{1}{2} \leq u \leq 1, \frac{1}{2} \leq v \leq 1$ ，且 $|I| = \frac{1}{3} u^{2}v^{-2}$ 。于是，曲面所围区域的体积为

$$
V = \iint_ {\Omega} x y \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y = \frac {1}{3} \int_ {\frac {1}{2}} ^ {1} \int_ {\frac {1}{2}} ^ {1} u ^ {- 3} v ^ {- 3} \mathrm {d} u \mathrm {d} v = \frac {1}{3} \left(\int_ {\frac {1}{2}} ^ {1} u ^ {- 3} \mathrm {d} u\right) ^ {2} = \frac {1}{3} \cdot \frac {9}{4} = \frac {3}{4}.
$$

【4030】 $z = c\sin \frac{\pi x y}{a^2}, z = 0, x y = a^2, y = \alpha x, y = \beta x (0 < \alpha < \beta; x > 0)$ .

解 曲面所界的立体在 $Oxy$ 平面上的投影域 $\Omega$ 由曲线 $xy = a^2$ 和直线 $y = \alpha x, y = \beta x (x > 0)$ 围成. 于是，曲面所围区域的体积为

$$
V = \iint_ {\Omega} z d x d y = c \iint_ {\Omega} \sin \frac {\pi x y}{a ^ {2}} d x d y.
$$

作变量代换 $x = \arccos \varphi, y = \arcsin \varphi$ ，则 $|I| = a^2 r.$ 于是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = \iint_ {\Omega} z d x d y = c \iint_ {\Omega} \sin \frac {\pi x y}{a ^ {2}} d x d y = a ^ {2} c \int_ {\arctan \alpha} ^ {\arctan \beta} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {1}{\sqrt {\sin \varphi \cos \varphi}}} \sin (\pi r ^ {2} \sin \varphi \cos \varphi) r d r d \varphi \\ = \frac {a ^ {2} c}{\pi} \int_ {\arctan \alpha} ^ {\arctan \beta} \frac {1}{\sin \varphi \cos \varphi} d \varphi = \frac {a ^ {2} c}{\pi} \ln \tan \varphi \left| _ {\arctan \alpha} ^ {\arctan \beta} = \frac {a ^ {2} c}{\pi} \ln \frac {\beta}{\alpha}. \right. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4031】 $z = x^{\frac{3}{2}} + y^{\frac{3}{2}}, z = 0, x + y = 1, x = 0, y = 0.$

解曲面所界的立体在 $Oxy$ 平面上的投影域 $\Omega$ 由直线 $x + y = 1, x = 0, y = 0$ 围成.于是，曲面所围区域的体积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = \iint_ {\Omega} z d x d y = \iint_ {\Omega} \left(x ^ {\frac {3}{2}} + y ^ {\frac {3}{2}}\right) d x d y = \int_ {0} ^ {1} \int_ {0} ^ {1 - r} \left(x ^ {\frac {3}{2}} + y ^ {\frac {3}{2}}\right) d x d y = \int_ {0} ^ {1} \left[ x ^ {\frac {3}{2}} (1 - x) + \frac {2}{5} (1 - x) ^ {\frac {5}{2}} \right] d x \\ = \frac {5}{2} x ^ {\frac {5}{2}} \left| _ {0} ^ {1} - \frac {7}{2} x ^ {\frac {7}{2}} \right| _ {0} ^ {1} - \frac {4}{3 5} (1 - x) ^ {\frac {7}{2}} \left| _ {0} ^ {1} = \frac {2}{5} - \frac {2}{7} + \frac {4}{3 5} = \frac {8}{3 5}. \right. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4032】 $\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2} +\frac{z}{c} = 1,\left(\frac{x}{a}\right)^{\frac{2}{3}} + \left(\frac{y}{b}\right)^{\frac{2}{3}} = 1,z = 0.$

提示 令 $x = \arccos^3\varphi, y = brsin^3\varphi$ ，则曲面方程化为

$$
z = c \left[ 1 - r ^ {2} \left(\cos^ {6} \varphi + \sin^ {6} \varphi\right) \right], r = 1 \quad (0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant 2 \pi , 0 \leqslant r \leqslant 1),
$$

注意对称性，并利用3856题的结果，

解 令 $x = \arccos^3\varphi, y = brsin^3\varphi$ ，则方程化为

$$
z = c \left[ 1 - r ^ {2} \left(\cos^ {6} \varphi + \sin^ {6} \varphi\right) \right], \quad r = 1 \quad (0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant 2 \pi , 0 \leqslant r \leqslant 1).
$$

于是，利用对称性知，曲面所围区域的体积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = 4 \iint_ {\Omega} z d x d y = 1 2 a b c \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \int_ {0} ^ {1} [ 1 - r ^ {2} (\cos^ {6} \varphi + \sin^ {6} \varphi) ] r \cos^ {2} \varphi \sin^ {2} \varphi d r d \varphi \\ = 1 2 a b c \left(\int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \frac {1}{2} \cos^ {2} \varphi \sin^ {2} \varphi d \varphi - \frac {1}{4} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} (\cos^ {6} \varphi + \sin^ {6} \varphi) \cos^ {2} \varphi \sin^ {2} \varphi d \varphi\right) \\ = 6 a b c \left(\int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {2} \varphi \sin^ {2} \varphi d \varphi - \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {6} \varphi \cos^ {2} \varphi \sin^ {2} \varphi d \varphi\right) \\ = 6 a b c \left[ \frac {\pi}{4} \left(1 - \frac {3}{4}\right) - \frac {1}{1 0} \cdot \frac {7 \cdot 5 \cdot 3 \cdot 1}{8 \cdot 6 \cdot 4 \cdot 2} \frac {\pi}{2} \right] \\ = \frac {3 \pi a b c}{2} \left(\frac {1}{4} - \frac {1 0 5}{1 9 2 0}\right) = \frac {7 5}{2 5 6} \pi a b c. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4033】 $z = \arctan{\frac{y}{x}}, z = 0, \sqrt{x^2 + y^2} = a\arctan{\frac{y}{x}} (y \geqslant 0).$

解 令 $x = r\cos \varphi, y = r\sin \varphi$ ，则方程化为 $z = c\varphi, r = a\varphi (0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac{\pi}{2})$ ，于是，曲面所围区域的体积为

$$
V = \iint_ {\Omega} z \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y = \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \int_ {0} ^ {a _ {\varphi}} c \varphi r \mathrm {d} r \mathrm {d} \varphi = \frac {a ^ {2} c}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \varphi^ {3} \mathrm {d} \varphi = \frac {a ^ {2} c}{8} \varphi^ {4} \left| _ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} = \frac {\pi^ {4} a ^ {2} c}{1 2 8}. \right.
$$

【4034】 $\frac{x^n}{a^n} +\frac{y^n}{b^n} +\frac{z^n}{c^n} = 1,x = 0,y = 0,z = 0(n > 0)$

提示 令 $x = a r \cos^{\frac{2}{n}} \varphi, y = b r \sin^{\frac{2}{n}} \varphi (0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac{\pi}{2})$ ，则曲面方程化为

$$
z = c \sqrt [ n ]{1 - r ^ {n}} \quad (0 \leqslant r \leqslant 1).
$$

在求体积 $V$ 的过程中，先后令 $r^n = t$ 及 $\sin^2\varphi = z$ ，并利用B函数的定义及计算公式.

解 曲面方程可表示为

$$
z = c \sqrt [ n ]{1 - \left(\frac {x ^ {n}}{a ^ {n}} + \frac {y ^ {n}}{b ^ {n}}\right)}.
$$

若令 $x = a r \cos^{\frac{2}{n}} \varphi, y = b r \sin^{\frac{2}{n}} \varphi (0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac{\pi}{2})$ ，则曲所围区域的体积为

$$
V = c \iint_ {\Omega} \sqrt [ n ]{1 - \left(\frac {x ^ {n}}{a ^ {n}} + \frac {y ^ {n}}{b ^ {n}}\right)} d x d y = \frac {2 a b c}{n} \int_ {0} ^ {1} \sqrt [ n ]{1 - r ^ {n}} r d r \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {\frac {2 - n}{n}} \varphi \sin^ {\frac {2 - n}{n}} \varphi d \varphi .
$$

若令 $r^{\prime \prime} = t$ 可得

$$
\int_ {0} ^ {1} \sqrt [ n ]{1 - r ^ {n}} r d r = \int_ {0} ^ {1} (1 - t) ^ {\frac {1}{n}} t ^ {\frac {2}{n} - 1} d t = B \left(\frac {1}{n} + 1, \frac {2}{n}\right) = \frac {\Gamma \left(\frac {1}{n} + 1\right) \Gamma \left(\frac {2}{n}\right)}{\Gamma \left(1 + \frac {3}{n}\right)} = \frac {\Gamma \left(\frac {1}{n}\right) \Gamma \left(\frac {2}{n}\right)}{3 \Gamma \left(\frac {3}{n}\right)};
$$

令 $\sin^2\varphi = t$ 可得

$$
\int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {\frac {2 - n}{n}} \varphi \sin^ {\frac {2 - n}{n}} \varphi d \varphi = \frac {1}{2 n} \int_ {0} ^ {1} (1 - t) ^ {\frac {1}{n} - 1} t ^ {\frac {1}{n}} d t = \frac {1}{2 n} B \left(\frac {1}{n}, \frac {1}{n}\right) = \frac {1}{2 n} \frac {\Gamma^ {2} \left(\frac {1}{n}\right)}{\Gamma \left(\frac {2}{n}\right)}.
$$

于是，所求的体积为 $V = \frac{abc}{n^2}\frac{\Gamma\left(\frac{1}{n}\right)\Gamma\left(\frac{2}{n}\right)}{3\Gamma\left(\frac{3}{n}\right)}\frac{\Gamma^2\left(\frac{1}{n}\right)}{\Gamma\left(\frac{2}{n}\right)} = \frac{abc}{3n^2}\frac{\Gamma^3\left(\frac{1}{n}\right)}{\Gamma\left(\frac{3}{n}\right)}.$

【4035】 $\left(\frac{x}{a} +\frac{y}{b}\right)^n +\left(\frac{z}{c}\right)^m = 1,x = 0,y = 0,z = 0(n > 0,m > 0).$

提示 令 $x = \arccos^2\varphi, y = brsin^2\varphi (0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac{\pi}{2})$

解 令 $x = \arccos^2\varphi, y = brsin^2\varphi (0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac{\pi}{2})$ ，则曲面所围区域的体积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = c \iint_ {\Omega} \sqrt [ m ]{1 - \left(\frac {x}{a} + \frac {y}{b}\right) ^ {n}} d x d y = 2 a b c \int_ {0} ^ {1} \sqrt [ m ]{1 - r ^ {n}} r d r \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos \varphi \sin \varphi d \varphi = a b c \int_ {0} ^ {1} \sqrt [ m ]{1 - r ^ {n}} r d r \\ = \frac {a b c}{n} B \left(\frac {1}{m} + 1, \frac {2}{n}\right) = \frac {a b c}{n} \frac {\Gamma \left(\frac {1}{m} + 1\right) \Gamma \left(\frac {2}{n}\right)}{\Gamma \left(\frac {1}{m} + \frac {2}{n} + 1\right)} = \frac {a b c}{n + 2 m} \frac {\Gamma \left(\frac {1}{m}\right) \Gamma \left(\frac {2}{n}\right)}{\Gamma \left(\frac {1}{m} + \frac {2}{n}\right)}. \\ \end{array}
$$

# § 4. 曲面面积的计算法

$1^{\circ}$ 曲面由显函数给出的情形光滑曲面 $z = z(x,y)$ 的面积由以下积分表示：

$$
S = \iint_ {\Omega} \sqrt {1 + \left(\frac {\partial z}{\partial x}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\partial z}{\partial y}\right) ^ {2}} d x d y,
$$

其中 $\Omega$ 为该曲面在 $Oxy$ 平面上的投影

$2^{\circ}$ 曲面由参数方程给出的情形 若曲面是由参数方程给出的：

$$
x = x (u, v), y = y (u, v), z = z (u, v),
$$

其中 $(u, v) \in \Omega, \Omega$ 为封闭可求积的有限区域，且函数 $x, y$ 和 $z$ 在区域 $\Omega$ 内连续可微，则对于曲面的面积有公式

$$
S = \iint_ {\Omega} \sqrt {E G - F ^ {2}} d u d v,
$$

其中

$$
E = \left(\frac {\partial x}{\partial u}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\partial y}{\partial u}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\partial z}{\partial u}\right) ^ {2}, \quad G = \left(\frac {\partial x}{\partial v}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\partial y}{\partial v}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\partial z}{\partial v}\right) ^ {2}, \quad F = \frac {\partial x}{\partial u} \frac {\partial x}{\partial v} + \frac {\partial y}{\partial u} \frac {\partial y}{\partial v} + \frac {\partial z}{\partial u} \frac {\partial z}{\partial v}.
$$

【4036】求曲面 $a z = x y$ 包含在圆柱 $x^{2} + y^{2} = a^{2}$ 内那部分的面积.

解 所求的面积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} S = \iint_ {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} \leqslant a ^ {2}} \sqrt {1 + \left(\frac {y}{a}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {x}{a}\right) ^ {2}} d x d y = \iint_ {r ^ {2} + y ^ {2} \leqslant r ^ {2}} \sqrt {\frac {a ^ {2} + (x ^ {2} + y ^ {2})}{a ^ {2}}} d x d y \\ = \frac {1}{a} \iint_ {r ^ {2} - y ^ {2} \leqslant a ^ {2}} \sqrt {a ^ {2} + (x ^ {2} + y ^ {2})} d x d y = \frac {4}{a} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {a} r \sqrt {a ^ {2} + r ^ {2}} d r = \frac {2 \pi a ^ {2}}{3} (2 \sqrt {2} - 1). \\ \end{array}
$$

【4037】求以曲面 $x^{2} + z^{2} = a^{2}$ 和 $y^{2} + z^{2} = a^{2}$ 为界的物体的表面积.

解如图8.48所示，两曲面的交线在 $Oyz$ 平面上的投影为圆 $y^{2} + z^{2} = a^{2},x = 0.$

![](images/40c948d35dcea27dabece8f0aa2ceeac2281b151c1da408ce838c85e8c7c6864.jpg)  
图8.48

于是，利用对称性知，所求的面积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} S = 4 \iint_ {z ^ {2} + y ^ {2} \leqslant a ^ {2}} \sqrt {1 + \left(\frac {\partial x}{\partial y}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\partial x}{\partial z}\right) ^ {2}} d y d z = 4 \cdot 4 \int_ {0} ^ {a} d z \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt {a ^ {2} - z ^ {2}}} \sqrt {1 + 0 ^ {2} + \left(- \frac {z}{x}\right) ^ {2}} d y \\ = 1 6 \int_ {0} ^ {a} d z \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt {a ^ {2} - z ^ {2}}} \sqrt {\frac {x ^ {2} + z ^ {2}}{x ^ {2}}} d y = 1 6 a \int_ {0} ^ {a} d z \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt {a ^ {2} - z ^ {2}}} \frac {d y}{\sqrt {a ^ {2} - z ^ {2}}} \\ = 1 6 a \int_ {0} ^ {a} \frac {1}{\sqrt {a ^ {2} - z ^ {2}}} \sqrt {a ^ {2} - z ^ {2}} d z = 1 6 a ^ {2}. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4038】求球面 $x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2} = a^{2}$ 包含在柱面 $\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2} = 1(b\leqslant a)$ 内那部分的面积.

解 因为 $\sqrt{1 + \left(\frac{\partial z}{\partial x}\right)^2 + \left(\frac{\partial z}{\partial y}\right)^2} = \sqrt{1 + \frac{x^2}{z^2} + \frac{y^2}{z^2}} = \sqrt{\frac{x^2 + y^2 + z^2}{z^2}} = \frac{a}{\sqrt{a^2 - x^2 - y^2}},$

又积分域 $\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2}\leqslant 1$ 位于第一象限部分为

$$
0 \leqslant x \leqslant a, \quad 0 \leqslant y \leqslant \frac {b}{a} \sqrt {a ^ {2} - x ^ {2}}.
$$

于是，利用对称性知，所求的面积为

$$
S = 2 \cdot 4 \int_ {0} ^ {a} d x \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {b}{a} \sqrt {a ^ {2} - x ^ {2}}} \frac {a}{\sqrt {a ^ {2} - x ^ {2} - y ^ {2}}} d y = 8 a \int_ {0} ^ {a} \arcsin \frac {y}{\sqrt {a ^ {2} - x ^ {2}}} \left| \begin{array}{l} \frac {b}{a} \sqrt {a ^ {2} - x ^ {2}} \\ \end{array} \right. d x = 8 a ^ {2} \arcsin \frac {b}{a}.
$$

【4039】求曲面 $z^2 = 2xy$ 被平面 $x + y = 1, x = 0, y = 0$ 所截部分的面积.

解因为

$$
\sqrt {1 + \left(\frac {\partial z}{\partial x}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\partial z}{\partial y}\right) ^ {2}} = \sqrt {1 + \frac {y ^ {2}}{z ^ {2}} + \frac {x ^ {2}}{z ^ {2}}} = \sqrt {\frac {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} + z ^ {2}}{z ^ {2}}} = \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \sqrt {\frac {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} + 2 x y}{x y}} = \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \frac {x + y}{\sqrt {x y}},
$$

于是，所求的面积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} S = \frac {2}{\sqrt {2}} \int_ {0} ^ {1} d x \int_ {0} ^ {1 - x} \frac {x + y}{\sqrt {x y}} d y = \frac {2}{\sqrt {2}} \int_ {0} ^ {1} [ 2 \sqrt {x (1 - x)} + \frac {2}{3 \sqrt {x}} (1 - x) \sqrt {1 - x} ] d x \\ = \sqrt {2} \int_ {0} ^ {1} \frac {2 \sqrt {1 - x} (1 + 2 x)}{3 \sqrt {x}} d x = \frac {4 \sqrt {2}}{3} \int_ {0} ^ {1} \sqrt {1 - x} (1 + 2 x) d (\sqrt {x}) \\ = \frac {4 \sqrt {2}}{3} \int_ {0} ^ {1} \sqrt {1 - t ^ {2}} (1 + 2 t ^ {2}) d t = \frac {4 \sqrt {2}}{3} \left(\frac {\pi}{4} + \frac {\pi}{8}\right) = \frac {\pi}{\sqrt {2}}. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4040】求曲面 $x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2} = a^{2}$ 在圆柱 $x^{2} + y^{2} = \pm ax$ 内那部分的面积（维维亚尼问题）.

解 只须求出球面被圆柱面割出部分的面积. 因为

$$
\sqrt {1 + \left(\frac {\partial z}{\partial x}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\partial z}{\partial y}\right) ^ {2}} = \sqrt {1 + \frac {x ^ {2}}{z ^ {2}} + \frac {y ^ {2}}{z ^ {2}}} = \frac {a}{\sqrt {a ^ {2} - x ^ {2} - y ^ {2}}},
$$

于是，利用对称性知，割出部分的面积为

$$
S = 8 \iint_ {\Omega} \frac {a}{\sqrt {a ^ {2} - x ^ {2} - y ^ {2}}} d x d y = 8 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {a \cos \varphi} \frac {a r}{\sqrt {a ^ {2} - r ^ {2}}} d r = 8 a ^ {2} \left(\frac {\pi}{2} - 1\right).
$$

于是，所求的面积为 $A = 4\pi a^2 - S = 4\pi a^2 - 8a^2 \left(\frac{\pi}{2} - 1\right) = 8a^2.$

【4041】求曲面 $z = \sqrt{x^2 + y^2}$ 包含在圆柱 $x^{2} + y^{2} = 2x$ 内那部分的面积.

解 注意到 $\sqrt{1 + \left(\frac{\partial z}{\partial x}\right)^2 + \left(\frac{\partial z}{\partial y}\right)^2} = \sqrt{1 + \left(\frac{x}{\sqrt{x^2 + y^2}}\right)^2 + \left(\frac{y}{\sqrt{x^2 + y^2}}\right)^2} = \sqrt{2},$

又积分域为： $-\frac{\pi}{2}\leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac{\pi}{2},0\leqslant r\leqslant 2\cos \varphi .$ 于是，所求的面积为

$$
S = \iint_ {\Omega} \sqrt {2} d x d y = \int_ {- \frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {2 \cos \varphi} \sqrt {2} r d r = 2 \sqrt {2} \int_ {- \frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {2} \varphi d \varphi = \sqrt {2} \pi .
$$

【4042】求曲面 $z = \sqrt{x^2 - y^2}$ 包含在柱面 $(x^{2} + y^{2})^{2} = a^{2}(x^{2} - y^{2})$ 内那部分的面积.

解 注意到 $\sqrt{1 + \left(\frac{\partial z}{\partial x}\right)^2 + \left(\frac{\partial z}{\partial y}\right)^2} = \sqrt{1 + \left(\frac{x}{\sqrt{x^2 - y^2}}\right)^2 + \left(\frac{-y}{\sqrt{x^2 - y^2}}\right)^2} = \frac{\sqrt{2}x}{\sqrt{x^2 - y^2}},$

又积分域由双纽线 $r^2 = a^2\cos 2\varphi$ 所围成.于是，利用对称性知，所求的面积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} S = \iint_ {\Omega} \frac {\sqrt {2} x}{\sqrt {x ^ {2} - y ^ {2}}} d x d y = 4 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {a \sqrt {\cos 2 \varphi}} \sqrt {2} r \frac {r \cos \varphi}{r \sqrt {\cos 2 \varphi}} d r = 2 \sqrt {2} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} a ^ {2} \cos \varphi \sqrt {\cos 2 \varphi} d \varphi \\ = 2 a ^ {2} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} \sqrt {1 - 2 \sin^ {2} \varphi} d (\sqrt {2} \sin \varphi) = 2 a ^ {2} \left[ \frac {\sqrt {2} \sin \varphi}{2} \sqrt {1 - 2 \sin^ {2} \varphi} + \frac {1}{2} \arcsin (\sqrt {2} \sin \varphi) \right] \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} = \frac {\pi a ^ {2}}{2}. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4043】求曲面 $z = \frac{1}{2} (x^2 - y^2)$ 被平面 $x - y = \pm 1, x + y = \pm 1$ 所截部分的面积.

解 因为 $\sqrt{1 + \left(\frac{\partial z}{\partial x}\right)^2 + \left(\frac{\partial z}{\partial y}\right)^2} = \sqrt{1 + x^2 + y^2}$ ，故所求的面积为

$$
S = \iint_ {\Omega} \sqrt {1 + x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}} d x d y,
$$

其中 $\Omega$ 为由直线 $x - y = \pm 1, x + y = \pm 1$ 围成的正方形域. 为便于计算，作变换

$$
x = \frac {\sqrt {2}}{2} u - \frac {\sqrt {2}}{2} v, \quad y = \frac {\sqrt {2}}{2} u + \frac {\sqrt {2}}{2} v,
$$

从而积分域变为由方程 $u = \pm \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}, v = \pm \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}$ 围成的正方形，且 $I = 1$ 。于是，注意利用对称性，即得所求的面

积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} S = \iint_ {\Omega} \sqrt {1 + x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}} d x d y = 4 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\sqrt {2}}{2}} d u \int_ {- u} ^ {u} \sqrt {1 + u ^ {2} + v ^ {2}} d v \\ = 4 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\sqrt {2}}{2}} \left\{u \sqrt {1 + 2 u ^ {2}} + \frac {1 + u ^ {2}}{2} \left[ \ln \left(\sqrt {1 + 2 u ^ {2}} + u\right) - \ln \left(\sqrt {1 + 2 u ^ {2}} - u\right) \right] \right\} d u \\ = \frac {2}{3} (1 + 2 u ^ {2}) ^ {\frac {3}{2}} \left| _ {0} ^ {\frac {\sqrt {2}}{2}} + 2 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\sqrt {2}}{2}} \left[ \ln \left(\sqrt {1 + 2 u ^ {2}} + u\right) - \ln \left(\sqrt {1 + 2 u ^ {2}} - u\right) \right] d \left(u + \frac {u ^ {3}}{3}\right) \right. \\ = \frac {4 \sqrt {2}}{3} - \frac {2}{3} + \frac {7 \sqrt {2}}{6} \ln 3 - \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\sqrt {2}}{2}} 4 \left(u + \frac {u ^ {3}}{3}\right) \frac {\mathrm {d} u}{\sqrt {1 + 2 u ^ {2}} (1 + u ^ {2})} \\ = \frac {4 \sqrt {2}}{3} - \frac {2}{3} + \frac {7 \sqrt {2}}{6} \ln 3 - \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\sqrt {2}}{2}} \frac {1 + \frac {u ^ {3}}{3}}{1 + u ^ {2}} \frac {\mathrm {d} (1 + 2 u ^ {2})}{\sqrt {1 + 2 u ^ {2}}} = \frac {4 \sqrt {2}}{3} - \frac {2}{3} + \frac {7 \sqrt {2}}{6} \ln 3 - \frac {2}{3} \int_ {1} ^ {\sqrt {2}} \frac {t ^ {2} + 5}{t ^ {2} + 1} \mathrm {d} t \\ = \frac {4 \sqrt {2}}{3} - \frac {2}{3} + \frac {7 \sqrt {2}}{6} \ln 3 - \frac {2}{3} (\sqrt {2} - 1) - \frac {8}{3} \int_ {1} ^ {\sqrt {2}} \frac {\mathrm {d} t}{t ^ {2} + 1} = \frac {2 \sqrt {2}}{3} \left(1 + \frac {7}{4} \ln 3\right) + \frac {2 \pi}{3} - \frac {8}{3} \arctan \sqrt {2} \\ = - \frac {2 \pi}{3} + \frac {2 \sqrt {2}}{3} \left(1 + \frac {7 \ln 3}{4}\right) + \frac {8}{3} \arctan \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}}. \\ \end{array}
$$

\*) 作代换 $1 + 2u^{2} = t^{2}$

【4044】求曲面 $x^{2} + y^{2} = 2az$ 包含在柱面 $(x^{2} + y^{2})^{2} = 2a^{2}xy$ 内那部分的面积

解 注意到 $\sqrt{1 + \left(\frac{\partial z}{\partial x}\right)^2 + \left(\frac{\partial z}{\partial y}\right)^2} = \sqrt{1 + \left(\frac{x}{a}\right)^2 + \left(\frac{y}{a}\right)^2} = \frac{1}{a}\sqrt{a^2 + (x^2 + y^2)}$

又积分域由双纽线 $r^2 = a^2\sin 2\varphi$ 围成.于是，利用对称性，即得所求的面积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} S = \iint_ {a} \frac {1}{a} \sqrt {a ^ {2} + (x ^ {2} + y ^ {2})} d x d y = 4 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {a \sqrt {\sin 2 \varphi}} \frac {1}{a} \sqrt {a ^ {2} + r ^ {2}} r d r \\ = \frac {4}{3 a} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} \left[ a ^ {3} (1 + \sin 2 \varphi) ^ {\frac {3}{2}} - a ^ {3} \right] d \varphi = \frac {4 a ^ {2}}{3} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} (1 + \sin 2 \varphi) ^ {\frac {3}{2}} d \varphi - \frac {\pi a ^ {2}}{3}. \\ \end{array}
$$

由于

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} (1 + \sin 2 \varphi) ^ {\frac {3}{2}} d \varphi = \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} [ 1 + \cos 2 (\frac {\pi}{4} - \varphi) ] ^ {\frac {3}{2}} d \varphi = 2 \sqrt {2} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} \cos^ {3} (\frac {\pi}{4} - \varphi) d \varphi \\ = 2 \sqrt {2} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} \cos^ {3} t d t = 2 \sqrt {2} \left(\sin t - \frac {\sin^ {3} t}{3}\right) \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} = \frac {5}{3}, \\ \end{array}
$$

故最后得 $S = \frac{4a^2}{3} \cdot \frac{5}{3} - \frac{\pi a^2}{3} = \frac{a^2}{9} (20 - 3\pi).$

【4045】求曲面 $x^{2} + y^{2} = a^{2}$ 被平面 $x + z = 0, x - z = 0 (x > 0, y > 0)$ 所截部分的面积.
