解 因为 $\sqrt{1 + \left(\frac{\partial y}{\partial x}\right)^2 + \left(\frac{\partial y}{\partial z}\right)^2} = \sqrt{1 + \left(\frac{x}{y}\right)^2} = \frac{a}{\sqrt{a^2 - x^2}}$

于是，所求的面积为 $S = \iint_{\Omega} \frac{a}{\sqrt{a^2 - x^2}} \mathrm{d}x \mathrm{~d}z = \int_{0}^{a} \mathrm{~d}x \int_{x}^{x'} \frac{a}{\sqrt{a^2 - x^2}} \mathrm{~d}z = \int_{0}^{a} \frac{2ax}{\sqrt{a^2 - x^2}} \mathrm{~d}x = 2a^2.$

【4046】求以曲面 $x^{2} + y^{2} = \frac{1}{3} z^{2}$ 和 $x + y + z = 2a(a > 0)$ 为界的物体的表面积和体积.

解 曲面的交线在 $Oxy$ 平面上的投影为

$$
3 x ^ {2} + 3 y ^ {2} = (2 a - x - y) ^ {2},
$$

即 $x^{2} + y^{2} - xy + 2a(x + y) = 2a^{2}.$

令 $x = \frac{x' - y'}{\sqrt{2}}$ ， $y = \frac{x' + y'}{\sqrt{2}}$ ，则方程变为 $\frac{\left(x' + \frac{4a}{\sqrt{2}}\right)^2}{(2\sqrt{3}a)^2} + \frac{y'^2}{(2a)^2} = 1.$

由此可见，曲面所界的物体在 $Oxy$ 平面上的投影域为以 $2a$ 为短半轴、 $2\sqrt{3}a$ 为长半轴的椭圆。

物体的表面积由截面和截出的锥面两部分组成. 对于 $z = 2a - x - y$ ， $z = \sqrt{3x^2 + 3y^2}$ 分别有

$$
\sqrt {1 + \left(\frac {\partial z}{\partial x}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\partial z}{\partial y}\right) ^ {2}} = \sqrt {3}, \quad \sqrt {1 + \left(\frac {\partial z}{\partial x}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\partial z}{\partial y}\right) ^ {2}} = 2.
$$

于是，物体的表面积 $S = \iint_{\Omega} \sqrt{3} \, \mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y + \iint_{\Omega} 2 \, \mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y = (\sqrt{3} + 2) \cdot \pi \cdot 2a \cdot 2\sqrt{3} a = 4\pi (3 + 2\sqrt{3}) a^2.$

又所截圆锥之高为 $H = \left|\frac{-2a}{\sqrt{1^2 + 1^2 + 1^2}}\right| = \frac{2a}{\sqrt{3}}$

（即坐标原点到平面 $x + y + z = 2a$ 的距离).于是，物体的体积为

$$
V = \frac {1}{3} \cdot A \cdot \frac {2 a}{\sqrt {3}},
$$

其中 $A$ 为截圆锥的底面积： $A = \iint_{a}\sqrt{3} \mathrm{d}x \mathrm{d}y = \sqrt{3} \cdot \pi \cdot 2a \cdot 2\sqrt{3} a = 12\pi a^2.$

因此，所求物体的体积为 $V = \frac{1}{3} \cdot 12\pi a^2 \cdot \frac{2a}{\sqrt{3}} = \frac{8}{\sqrt{3}}\pi a^3.$

【4047】求球面在两条纬线和两条经线之间那部分的面积.

解题思路 球面的参数方程为

$$
x = R \cos \varphi \cos \psi , \quad y = R \sin \varphi \cos \psi , \quad z = R \sin \psi ,
$$

其中 $R$ 为球的半径. $\sqrt{EG - F^2} = R^2\cos \psi$ ，又 $\varphi_1 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \varphi_2, \psi_1 \leqslant \psi \leqslant \psi_2$ ，其中 $\varphi_1$ 及 $\varphi_2$ 为经线的经度， $\psi_1$ 及 $\psi_2$ 为纬线的纬度.

解球面的参数方程为 $x = R\cos \varphi \cos \psi ,y = R\sin \varphi \cos \psi ,z = R\sin \psi ,$

其中 $R$ 为球的半径.因为

$$
E = \left(\frac {\partial x}{\partial \varphi}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\partial y}{\partial \varphi}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\partial z}{\partial \varphi}\right) ^ {2} = R ^ {2} \sin^ {2} \varphi \cos^ {2} \psi + R ^ {2} \cos^ {2} \varphi \cos^ {2} \psi = R ^ {2} \cos^ {2} \psi ,
$$

$$
G = \left(\frac {\partial x}{\partial \psi}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\partial y}{\partial \psi}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\partial z}{\partial \psi}\right) ^ {2} = R ^ {2} \cos^ {2} \varphi \sin^ {2} \psi + R ^ {2} \sin^ {2} \varphi \sin^ {2} \psi + R ^ {2} \cos^ {2} \psi = R ^ {2},
$$

$$
F = \frac {\partial x}{\partial \varphi} \frac {\partial x}{\partial \psi} + \frac {\partial y}{\partial \varphi} \frac {\partial y}{\partial \psi} + \frac {\partial z}{\partial \varphi} \frac {\partial z}{\partial \psi} = R ^ {2} \sin \varphi \cos \psi \cos \varphi \sin \psi - R ^ {2} \sin \varphi \cos \varphi \sin \psi \cos \psi + 0 = 0,
$$

故 $\sqrt{EG - F^2} = R^2\cos \psi.$ 于是，所求的面积为

$$
S = \int_ {\varphi_ {1}} ^ {\varphi_ {2}} d \varphi \int_ {\psi_ {1}} ^ {\psi_ {2}} R ^ {2} \cos \psi d \psi = (\varphi_ {2} - \varphi_ {1}) (\sin \psi_ {2} - \sin \psi_ {1}) R ^ {2},
$$

其中 $\varphi_{1}$ 及 $\varphi_{2}$ 为经线的经度， $\psi_{1}$ 及 $\psi_{2}$ 为纬线的纬度.

【4048】求螺旋面 $x = r\cos \varphi, y = r\sin \varphi, z = h\varphi$ 在 $0 < r < a, 0 < \varphi < 2\pi$ 那部分的面积.

解因为

$$
E = \left(\frac {\partial x}{\partial r}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\partial y}{\partial r}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\partial z}{\partial r}\right) ^ {2} = 1, \quad G = \left(\frac {\partial x}{\partial \varphi}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\partial y}{\partial \varphi}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\partial z}{\partial \varphi}\right) ^ {2} = r ^ {2} + h ^ {2},
$$

$$
F = \frac {\partial x}{\partial r} \frac {\partial x}{\partial \varphi} + \frac {\partial y}{\partial r} \frac {\partial y}{\partial \varphi} + \frac {\partial z}{\partial r} \frac {\partial z}{\partial \varphi} = 0,
$$

故 $\sqrt{EG - F^2} = \sqrt{r^2 + h^2}$ . 于是，所求的面积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} S = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} \mathrm {d} \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {a} \sqrt {r ^ {2} + h ^ {2}} \mathrm {d} r = 2 \pi \left[ \frac {r}{2} \sqrt {r ^ {2} + h ^ {2}} + \frac {h ^ {2}}{2} \ln (r + \sqrt {r ^ {2} + h ^ {2}}) \right] \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {a} \\ = \pi a \sqrt {a ^ {2} + h ^ {2}} + \pi h ^ {2} \ln \frac {a + \sqrt {a ^ {2} + h ^ {2}}}{h}. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4049】求环面 $x = (b + a\cos \psi)\cos \varphi ,\quad y = (b + a\cos \psi)\sin \varphi ,\quad z = a\sin \psi (0 <   a\leqslant b)$

在两条经线 $\varphi = \varphi_{1}$ ， $\varphi = \varphi_{2}$ 和两条纬线 $\psi = \psi_{1}$ ， $\psi = \psi_{2}$ 之间那部分的面积.整个环的表面积等于什么？

解因为

$$
E = \left(\frac {\partial x}{\partial \varphi}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\partial y}{\partial \varphi}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\partial z}{\partial \varphi}\right) ^ {2} = (b + a \cos \psi) ^ {2},
$$

$$
G = \left(\frac {\partial x}{\partial \psi}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\partial y}{\partial \psi}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\partial z}{\partial \psi}\right) ^ {2} = a ^ {2}, \quad F = \frac {\partial x}{\partial \varphi} \frac {\partial x}{\partial \psi} + \frac {\partial y}{\partial \varphi} \frac {\partial y}{\partial \psi} + \frac {\partial z}{\partial \varphi} \frac {\partial z}{\partial \psi} = 0
$$

故 $\sqrt{EG - F^2} = a(b + a\cos \psi)$ 于是，所求的面积为

$$
S = \int_ {\varphi_ {1}} ^ {\varphi_ {2}} d \varphi \int_ {\psi_ {1}} ^ {\psi_ {2}} a (b + a \cos \psi) d \psi = a (\varphi_ {2} - \varphi_ {1}) [ b (\psi_ {2} - \psi_ {1}) + a (\sin \psi_ {2} - \sin \psi_ {1}) ].
$$

整个环的表面积为 $A = \int_{0}^{2\pi}\mathrm{d}\varphi \int_{-\pi}^{\pi}a(b + a\cos \psi)\mathrm{d}\psi = 4\pi^{2}ab.$

【4050】求矩形 $x = a > 0, 0 \leqslant y \leqslant b, 0 \leqslant z \leqslant c$ 对坐标原点的立体角 $\omega$ . 若 $a$ 很大, 推出 $\omega$ 的近似公式.

解 以原点为球心作单位球，则 $\omega$ 即为该球面含于四面体 $O - ABCD$ 内的面积，其中 $ABCD$ 是以 $b, c$ 为边长的矩形（图8.49）.

取球坐标系，由4047题知： $\sqrt{EG - F^2} = \cos \psi$

又 $\varphi$ 和 $\psi$ 的变化域为

$$
0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \arcsin \frac {b}{\sqrt {a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}}}, \quad 0 \leqslant \psi \leqslant \arcsin \frac {c \cos \varphi}{\sqrt {a ^ {2} + c ^ {2} \cos^ {2} \varphi}}.
$$

![](images/41c353036d92f43010f09233542ec0b4283a9cc427c298c28ec0dbee8943574a.jpg)  
图8.49

于是，立体角

$$
\begin{array}{l} \omega = \int_ {0} ^ {\arcsin \frac {b}{\sqrt {a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}}}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\arcsin \frac {c \cos \varphi}{\sqrt {a ^ {2} + c ^ {2} \cos^ {2} \varphi}}} \cos \psi d \psi = \int_ {0} ^ {\arcsin \frac {b}{\sqrt {a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}}}} \frac {c \cos \varphi}{\sqrt {a ^ {2} + c ^ {2} \cos^ {2} \varphi}} d \varphi \\ = \int_ {0} ^ {\arcsin \frac {b}{\sqrt {a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}}}} \frac {\mathrm {d} \left(\frac {c}{\sqrt {a ^ {2} + c ^ {2}}} \sin \varphi\right)}{\sqrt {1 - \left(\frac {c}{\sqrt {a ^ {2} + c ^ {2}}} \sin \varphi\right) ^ {2}}} \\ = \arcsin \left(\frac {c}{\sqrt {a ^ {2} + c ^ {2}}} \sin \arcsin \frac {b}{\sqrt {a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}}}\right) = \arcsin \frac {b c}{\sqrt {\left(a ^ {2} + c ^ {2}\right) \left(a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}\right)}}. \\ \end{array}
$$

当 $a$ 很大时，有 $\frac{bc}{\sqrt{(a^2 + c^2)(a^2 + b^2)}} = \frac{bc}{a^2\sqrt{\left(1 + \frac{c^2}{a^2}\right)\left(1 + \frac{b^2}{a^2}\right)}} \approx \frac{bc}{a^2},$

于是，得 $\omega$ 的近似公式 $\omega \approx \frac{bc}{a^2}$

# § 5. 二重积分在力学上的应用

$1^{\circ}$ 质心 若薄板 $\Omega$ 位于平面 $Oxy$ 内， $x_0, y_0$ 为其质心坐标， $\rho = \rho(x, y)$ 为其面密度，则

$$
x _ {0} = \frac {1}{M} \iint_ {\Omega} \rho x \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y, \quad y _ {0} = \frac {1}{M} \iint_ {\Omega} \rho y \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y, \tag {1}
$$

其中 $M = \iint_{\Omega} \rho \mathrm{d}x \mathrm{d}y$ 为薄板的质量.

若薄板是均质的，则在公式(1)中应令 $\rho = 1$

$2^{\circ}$ 转动惯量 $I_{x}$ 和 $I_{y}$ 分别为平面 $Oxy$ 内薄板 $\Omega$ 对坐标轴 $Ox$ 和 $Oy$ 的转动惯量，可表示为以下公式：

$$
I _ {x} = \iint_ {\Omega} \rho y ^ {2} d x d y, \quad I _ {y} = \iint_ {\Omega} \rho x ^ {2} d x d y, \tag {2}
$$

其中 $\rho = \rho (x,y)$ 为薄板的面密度.

还可研究惯性积 $I_{xy} = \iint_{\Omega}\rho xy\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y.$

在公式(2)中取 $\rho = 1$ ，我们就得到平面图形的几何转动惯量.

【4051】求边长为 $a$ 的正方形薄板的质量，设薄板上每一点的面密度与该点到正方形顶点之一的距离成正比，且在正方形的中心等于 $\rho_0$

解取坐标系如图8.50所示，则面密度 $\rho = k\sqrt{x^2 + y^2}$ 由于

$$
\rho_ {0} = k \sqrt {\left(\frac {a}{2}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {a}{2}\right) ^ {2}},
$$

故 $k = \frac{\rho_0}{a}\sqrt{2}$ 从而， $\rho = \frac{\rho_0\sqrt{2}}{a}\sqrt{x^2 + y^2}.$

若引用极坐标，即得质量

$$
\begin{array}{l} M = \iint_ {\Omega} \frac {\rho_ {0} \sqrt {2}}{a} \sqrt {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}} d x d y = \frac {\rho_ {0}}{a} \sqrt {2} \left[ \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {a}{\cos \varphi}} r ^ {2} d r + \int_ {\frac {\pi}{4}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {a}{\sin \varphi}} r ^ {2} d r \right] \\ = \frac {\rho_ {0} a ^ {2}}{3} \sqrt {2} \left[ \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} \frac {\mathrm {d} \varphi}{\cos^ {3} \varphi} + \int_ {\frac {\pi}{4}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \frac {\mathrm {d} \varphi}{\sin^ {3} \varphi} \right] = \frac {\rho_ {0} a ^ {2}}{3} 2 \sqrt {2} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} \frac {\mathrm {d} \varphi}{\cos^ {3} \varphi} \\ = \frac {\rho_ {0} a ^ {2}}{3} 2 \sqrt {2} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} \sqrt {1 + \tan^ {2} \varphi} d (\tan \varphi) \\ = \frac {\rho_ {0} a ^ {2}}{3} 2 \sqrt {2} \left[ \frac {\tan \varphi}{2} \sqrt {1 + \tan^ {2} \varphi} + \frac {1}{2} \ln \left| \tan \varphi + \sqrt {1 + \tan^ {2} \varphi} \right| \right] \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} = \frac {\rho_ {0} a ^ {2}}{3} [ 2 + \sqrt {2} \ln (1 + \sqrt {2}) ]. \\ \end{array}
$$

![](images/40a0a2851f5df611260c882ed39b7c2fa062ac5422c8d5f911aa605a0bf85434.jpg)  
图8.50

求以下列曲线为界的均匀薄板的质心坐标：

【4052】 $ay = x^2$ ， $x + y = 2a(a > 0)$

解 面密度 $\rho$ 为常数. 积分域如图8.51所示. 质量

$$
M = \rho \int_ {- 2 a} ^ {a} d x \int_ {\frac {x ^ {2}}{a}} ^ {2 a - x} d y = \frac {9}{2} \rho a ^ {2}.
$$

对于坐标轴的一次矩为

$$
M _ {y} = \rho \int_ {- 2 x} ^ {a} x d x \int_ {\frac {x ^ {2}}{a}} ^ {2 a - x} d y = - \frac {9}{4} \rho a ^ {3},
$$

$$
M _ {x} = \rho \int_ {- 2 a} ^ {a} d x \int_ {\frac {x ^ {2}}{a}} ^ {2 a - x} y d y = \frac {3 6}{5} \rho a ^ {3}.
$$

于是，质心 $(x_0, y_0)$ 为

$$
x _ {0} = \frac {M _ {\mathrm {y}}}{M} = - \frac {a}{2}, \quad y _ {0} = \frac {M _ {r}}{M} = \frac {8}{5} a.
$$

![](images/4329d04da8bfb28bd6781ea0b3fd3f2c10de04027f171399609cc2099ca0b71d.jpg)  
图8.51

【4053】 $\sqrt{x} +\sqrt{y} = \sqrt{a},x = 0,y = 0.$

解 质量和对 $Oy$ 轴的一次矩分别为

$$
M = \rho \int_ {0} ^ {a} \mathrm {d} x \int_ {0} ^ {(\sqrt {a} - \sqrt {x}) ^ {2}} \mathrm {d} y = \frac {1}{6} \rho a ^ {2}, \quad M _ {y} = \rho \int_ {0} ^ {a} x \mathrm {d} x \int_ {0} ^ {(\sqrt {a} - \sqrt {x}) ^ {2}} \mathrm {d} y = \frac {1}{3 0} \rho a ^ {3}.
$$

于是，质心的横坐标为 $x_0 = \frac{M_v}{M} = \frac{a}{5}$

由关于直线 $y = x$ 的对称性知， $x_0 = y_0 = \frac{a}{5}$

【4054】 $x^{\frac{2}{3}} + y^{\frac{2}{3}} = a^{\frac{2}{3}} \quad (x > 0, y > 0)$ .

解 质量和对 $Oy$ 轴的一次矩分别为

$$
\begin{array}{l} M = \rho \int_ {0} ^ {a} d x \int_ {0} ^ {\left(a ^ {\frac {2}{3}} - x ^ {\frac {2}{3}}\right) ^ {\frac {3}{2}}} d y = \rho \int_ {0} ^ {a} \left(a ^ {\frac {2}{3}} - x ^ {\frac {2}{3}}\right) ^ {\frac {3}{2}} d x = 3 a ^ {2} \rho \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \sin^ {4} t \cos^ {2} t d t ^ {*}) = 3 a ^ {2} \rho \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} (\sin^ {4} t - \sin^ {6} t) d t \\ = 3 a ^ {2} \rho \left(\frac {3}{4} \cdot \frac {1}{2} - \frac {5}{6} \cdot \frac {3}{4} \cdot \frac {1}{2}\right) \frac {\pi}{2} = \frac {3 \pi a ^ {2} \rho}{3 2}, \\ \end{array}
$$

$$
M _ {y} = \rho \int_ {0} ^ {a} x \mathrm {d} x \int_ {0} ^ {\left(a ^ {\frac {2}{3}} - x ^ {\frac {2}{3}}\right) \frac {3}{2}} \mathrm {d} y = \rho \int_ {0} ^ {a} x \left(a ^ {\frac {2}{3}} - x ^ {\frac {2}{3}}\right) ^ {\frac {3}{2}} \mathrm {d} x = 3 a ^ {3} \rho \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \sin^ {4} t \cos^ {5} t \mathrm {d} t = \frac {8 a ^ {3} \rho}{1 0 5}.
$$

于是，质心的横坐标为 $x_0 = \frac{M_y}{M} = \frac{256a}{315\pi}.$

由关于直线 $y = x$ 的对称性知， $x_0 = y_0 = \frac{256a}{315\pi}$

\*）作代换 $x = a\cos^3 t$

【4055】 $\left(\frac{x}{a} +\frac{y}{b}\right)^3 = \frac{xy}{c^2}$ （线圈）.

解此曲线在第一象限部分是一封闭曲线，围成一图形 $\Omega$ 作变量代换

$$
x = \frac {a ^ {2} b}{c ^ {2}} r \cos^ {4} \theta \sin^ {2} \theta , \quad y = \frac {a b ^ {2}}{c ^ {2}} r \cos^ {2} \theta \sin^ {4} \theta , \quad (0 \leqslant \theta \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2})
$$

则原曲线方程变为 $r = 1$ 又容易算得

$$
\frac {D (x , y)}{D (r , \theta)} = \frac {2 a ^ {3} b ^ {3}}{c ^ {4}} r (\sin^ {5} \theta \cos^ {7} \theta + \sin^ {7} \theta \cos^ {5} \theta),
$$

故（利用3856题的结果）

$$
\begin{array}{l} M = \iint_ {\Omega} \rho d x d y = \frac {2 a ^ {3} b ^ {3}}{c ^ {4}} \rho \int_ {0} ^ {1} r d r \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} (\sin^ {5} \theta \cos^ {7} \theta + \sin^ {7} \theta \cos^ {5} \theta) d \theta = \frac {a ^ {3} b ^ {3}}{c ^ {4}} \rho \left[ \frac {1}{2} B (3, 4) + \frac {1}{2} B (4, 3) \right] = \frac {a ^ {3} b ^ {3}}{c ^ {4}} \rho B (3, 4), \\ M _ {y} = \iint_ {\Omega} \rho x \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y = \frac {2 a ^ {5} b ^ {4}}{c ^ {6}} \rho \int_ {0} ^ {1} r ^ {2} \mathrm {d} r \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {4} \theta \sin^ {2} \theta (\sin^ {5} \theta \cos^ {7} \theta + \sin^ {7} \theta \cos^ {5} \theta) \mathrm {d} \theta \\ = \frac {2}{3} \cdot \frac {a ^ {5} b ^ {4}}{c ^ {6}} \rho \left(\int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \sin^ {7} \theta \cos^ {1 1} \theta + \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \sin^ {9} \theta \cos^ {9} \theta d \theta\right) = \frac {1}{3} \cdot \frac {a ^ {5} b ^ {4}}{c ^ {6}} \rho [ B (4, 6) + B (5, 5) ]. \\ \end{array}
$$

于是， $x_0 = \frac{M_y}{M} = \frac{a^2b}{3c^2}\frac{\mathrm{B}(4,6) + \mathrm{B}(5,5)}{\mathrm{B}(3,4)}.$

由于 $\mathrm{B}(4,6) = \frac{\Gamma(4)\Gamma(6)}{\Gamma(10)} = \frac{3!\cdot 5!}{9!},\quad \mathrm{B}(5,5) = \frac{[\Gamma(5)]^2}{\Gamma(10)} = \frac{(4!)^2}{9!},\quad \mathrm{B}(3,4) = \frac{\Gamma(3)\Gamma(4)}{\Gamma(7)} = \frac{2!\cdot 3!}{6!},$

代入，化简得 $x_0 = \frac{a^2b}{3c^2} \cdot \frac{6! [3! \cdot 5! + (4!)^2]}{2! \cdot 3! \cdot 9!} = \frac{a^2b}{14c^2}$ .

同理，可求得质心的纵坐标为 $y_0 = \frac{M_x}{M} = \frac{\iint_{\rho y} \mathrm{d}x \mathrm{d}y}{\iint_{\rho} \mathrm{d}x \mathrm{d}y} = \frac{ab^2}{14c^2}$ .

【4056】 $(x^{2} + y^{2})^{2} = 2a^{2}xy$ （ $x > 0,y > 0)$

解曲线的极坐标方程为 $r^2 = a^2\sin 2\varphi$ ，质量和对 $Oy$ 轴的一次矩分别为

$$
M = \iint_ {\Omega} \rho d x d y = \rho \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {a \sqrt {\sin 2 \varphi}} r d r = \frac {\rho a ^ {2}}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \sin 2 \varphi d \varphi = \frac {\rho a ^ {2}}{2},
$$

$$
\begin{array}{l} M _ {y} = \iint_ {\Omega} \rho x d x d y = \rho \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {a \sqrt {\sin 2 \varphi}} r \cdot r \cos \varphi d r = \frac {\rho a ^ {3}}{3} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos \varphi \sin^ {\frac {3}{2}} 2 \varphi d \varphi = \frac {2 \sqrt {2}}{3} \rho a ^ {3} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {\frac {5}{2}} \varphi \sin^ {\frac {3}{2}} \varphi d \varphi \\ = \frac {2 \sqrt {2}}{3} \rho a ^ {3} \cdot \frac {1}{2} B \left(\frac {7}{4}, \frac {5}{4}\right) ^ {\prime \prime} = \frac {2 \sqrt {2}}{3} \rho a ^ {3} \frac {\Gamma \left(\frac {7}{4}\right) \Gamma \left(\frac {5}{4}\right)}{2 \Gamma (3)} = \frac {2 \sqrt {2}}{3} \rho a ^ {3} \frac {\frac {3}{4} \Gamma \left(\frac {3}{4}\right) \cdot \frac {1}{4} \Gamma \left(\frac {1}{4}\right)}{2 \cdot 2} \\ = \frac {1}{8 \sqrt {2}} \rho a ^ {3} \frac {\pi}{2 \sin \frac {\pi}{4}} = \frac {1}{1 6} \pi \rho a ^ {3}. \\ \end{array}
$$

于是，质心的横坐标为 $x_0 = \frac{M_y}{M} = \frac{\pi a}{8}$ 由关于直线 $y = x$ 的对称性知， $x_0 = y_0 = \frac{\pi a}{8}$ .

\*）利用3856题的结果.

【4057】 $r = a(1 + \cos \varphi),\varphi = 0.$

解 质量和对 $Oy$ 轴、 $Ox$ 轴的一次矩分别为

$$
M = \rho \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} \mathrm {d} \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {a (1 + \cos \varphi)} r \mathrm {d} r = \frac {1}{2} \rho a ^ {2} \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} (1 + \cos \varphi) ^ {2} \mathrm {d} \varphi = \frac {3}{4} \pi \rho a ^ {2},
$$

$$
\begin{array}{l} M _ {y} = \rho \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {a (1 - \cos \varphi)} r \cdot r \cos \varphi d r = \frac {\rho a ^ {3}}{3} \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} (1 + \cos \varphi) ^ {3} \cos \varphi d \varphi = \frac {\rho a ^ {3}}{3} \left[ \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} (1 + \cos \varphi) ^ {3} d \varphi - \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} (1 + \cos \varphi) ^ {3} d \varphi \right] \\ = \frac {\rho a ^ {3}}{3} \left[ 3 2 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {8} t d t - 1 6 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {6} t d t \right] = \frac {\rho a ^ {3}}{3} \left[ 3 2 \cdot \frac {7 \cdot 5 \cdot 3 \cdot 1}{8 \cdot 6 \cdot 4 \cdot 2} \cdot \frac {\pi}{2} - 1 6 \cdot \frac {5 \cdot 3 \cdot 1}{6 \cdot 4 \cdot 2} \cdot \frac {\pi}{2} \right] \\ = \frac {5 \pi \rho a ^ {3}}{8}, \\ \end{array}
$$

$$
M _ {x} = \rho \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {a (1 + \cos \varphi)} r \cdot r \sin \varphi d r = \frac {\rho a ^ {3}}{3} \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} (1 + \cos \varphi) ^ {3} \sin \varphi d \varphi = - \frac {\rho a ^ {3}}{3} \cdot \frac {(1 + \cos \varphi) ^ {3}}{4} \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {\pi} = \frac {4 \rho a ^ {3}}{3}.
$$

于是，质心的坐标为 $x_0 = \frac{M_y}{M} = \frac{5}{6} a,$ $y_{0} = \frac{M_{x}}{M} = \frac{16}{9\pi} a.$

【4058】 $x = a(t - \sin t),y = a(1 - \cos t)(0\leqslant t\leqslant 2\pi),y = 0.$

解 质量和对 $Ox$ 轴的一次矩分别为

$$
\begin{array}{l} M = \rho \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi a} d x \int_ {0} ^ {y} d y = \rho \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} a ^ {2} (1 - \cos t) ^ {2} d t = 3 \pi \rho a ^ {2}, \\ M _ {x} = \rho \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi a} d x \int_ {0} ^ {y} y d y = \frac {1}{2} \rho \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi a} y ^ {2} d x = \frac {1}{2} \rho a ^ {3} \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} (1 - \cos t) ^ {3} d t = \frac {5}{2} \pi \rho a ^ {3}. \\ \end{array}
$$

于是，质心的纵坐标为 $y_0 = \frac{M_x}{M} = \frac{5}{6} a.$

由对称性知， $x_0 = \pi a$

【4059】求圆形薄板 $x^{2} + y^{2}\leqslant a^{2}$ 的质心坐标.设它在点 $M(x,y)$ 的面密度与点 $M$ 到点 $A(a,0)$ 的距离成正比.

解 按题设，面密度 $\rho = k\sqrt{(x - a)^2 + y^2}$ （ $k$ 为常数）.于是，质量为

$$
\begin{array}{l} M = \int_ {- a} ^ {a} d x \int_ {- \sqrt {a ^ {2} - x ^ {2}}} ^ {\sqrt {a ^ {2} - x ^ {2}}} k \sqrt {(x - a) ^ {2} + y ^ {2}} d y \\ = k \int_ {- a} ^ {a} \left[ y \sqrt {(x - a) ^ {2} + y ^ {2}} + (x - a) ^ {2} \ln \left(y + \sqrt {(x - a) ^ {2} + y ^ {2}}\right) \right] \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {\sqrt {a ^ {2} - x ^ {2}}} d x \\ = k \int_ {- a} ^ {a} \sqrt {2 a} (a - x) \sqrt {a + x} d x - k \int_ {- a} ^ {a} \left[ \frac {1}{2} \ln (a - x) \right] (a - x) ^ {2} d x + k \int_ {- a} ^ {a} (a - x) ^ {2} \ln (\sqrt {a + x} + \sqrt {2 a}) d x \\ = I _ {1} - I _ {2} + I _ {3}. \\ \end{array}
$$

由于

$$
I _ {1} = k \int_ {- a} ^ {a} \sqrt {2 a} \left[ - (a + x) ^ {\frac {3}{2}} + 2 a (x + a) ^ {\frac {1}{2}} \right] d x = \sqrt {2 a} k \left[ - \frac {2}{5} (a + x) ^ {\frac {5}{2}} + \frac {4 a}{3} (x + a) ^ {\frac {3}{2}} \right] \Bigg | _ {- a} ^ {a} = \frac {3 2}{1 5} k a ^ {3},
$$

$$
I _ {2} = \frac {k}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {2 a} t ^ {2} \ln t \mathrm {d} t = \frac {k}{6} t ^ {3} \ln t \left| _ {0} ^ {2 a} - \frac {k}{6} \int_ {0} ^ {2 a} t ^ {3} \cdot \frac {1}{t} \mathrm {d} t = \frac {4}{3} k a ^ {3} \ln 2 a - \frac {4}{9} k a ^ {3}, \right.
$$

$$
\begin{array}{l} I _ {3} = k \cdot 2 \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt {2 a}} t (2 a - t ^ {2}) ^ {2} \ln (t + \sqrt {2 a}) d t = 8 a ^ {2} k \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt {2 a}} t \ln (t + \sqrt {2 a}) d t - 8 k a \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt {2 a}} t ^ {3} \ln (t + \sqrt {2 a}) d t \\ + 2 k \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt {2 a}} t ^ {5} \ln (t + \sqrt {2 a}) d t = 8 k a ^ {2} \left(\frac {a}{2} + a \ln \sqrt {2 a}\right) - 8 k a \left(\frac {7}{1 2} a ^ {2} + a ^ {2} \ln \sqrt {2 a}\right) \\ + 2 k \left(\frac {3 7}{4 5} a ^ {3} + \frac {4}{3} a ^ {3} \ln \sqrt {2 a}\right) = \frac {4 4}{4 5} k a ^ {3} + \frac {8}{3} k a ^ {3} \ln \sqrt {2 a} = \frac {4 4}{4 5} k a ^ {3} + \frac {4}{3} k a ^ {3} \ln 2 a. \\ \end{array}
$$

因而最后得 $M = \frac{32}{15} ka^3 -\left(\frac{4}{3} ka^3\ln 2a - \frac{4}{9} ka^3\right) + \left(\frac{44}{45} ka^3 +\frac{4}{3} ka^3\ln 2a\right) = \frac{32}{9} ka^3.$

仿照上述方法可求得一次矩 $M_y = \int_{-a}^a\mathrm{d}x\int_{-\sqrt{a^2 - x^2}}^{\sqrt{a^2 - x^2}}kx\sqrt{(x - a)^2 + y^2}\mathrm{d}y = -\frac{32}{45} ka^4.$

而由对称性得： $M_{x} = 0$ .于是，质心的坐标为

$$
x _ {0} = \frac {M _ {y}}{M} = - \frac {a}{5}, \quad y _ {0} = \frac {M _ {x}}{M} = 0.
$$

【4060】求曲线 $y = \sqrt{2px}$ ， $y = 0$ ， $x = X$ 所围图形的质心在参数 $X$ 变化时所描绘的曲线.

解 变动面积的质量为 $M = \rho \int_{0}^{X}\mathrm{d}x\int_{0}^{\sqrt{2\rho x}}\mathrm{d}y = \rho \frac{2\sqrt{2p}}{3} X^{\frac{3}{2}},$

而一次矩 $M_{y} = \rho \int_{0}^{X} x \, \mathrm{d}x \int_{0}^{\sqrt{2px}} \, \mathrm{d}y = \rho \frac{2\sqrt{2p}}{5} X^{\frac{5}{2}}, \quad M_{r} = \rho \int_{0}^{X} \, \mathrm{d}x \int_{0}^{\sqrt{2px}} y \, \mathrm{d}y = \rho \frac{1}{2} pX^{2}$ .

于是，变动面积的质心为 $x_0 = \frac{M_y}{M} = \frac{3}{5} X,$ $y_{0} = \frac{M_{r}}{M} = \frac{3\sqrt{pX}}{4\sqrt{2}}.$

因此，质心的轨迹方程为 $y_0 = \frac{3}{4\sqrt{2}}\sqrt{p \cdot \frac{5}{3}x_0} = \frac{1}{8}\sqrt{30px_0},$

此即所求的曲线方程，其图形是抛物线的一半.

求由下列曲线所围的面积 $(\rho = 1)$ 对坐标轴 $Ox$ 和 $Oy$ 的转动惯量 $I_{x}$ 和 $I_{y}$

【4061】 $\frac{x}{b_1} +\frac{y}{h} = 1,\frac{x}{b_2} +\frac{y}{h} = 1,y = 0(b_1 > 0,b_2 > 0,h > 0).$

解 若设 $b_{2} > b_{1}$ ，则

$$
I _ {x} = \int_ {0} ^ {h} y ^ {2} d y \int_ {(1 - \frac {y}{h}) b _ {1}} ^ {(1 - \frac {y}{h}) h _ {0}} d x = (b _ {2} - b _ {1}) \int_ {0} ^ {h} y ^ {2} \left(1 - \frac {y}{h}\right) d y = \frac {\left(b _ {2} - b _ {1}\right) h ^ {3}}{1 2},
$$

$$
I _ {y} = \int_ {0} ^ {h} d y \int_ {(1 - \frac {x}{h}) b _ {1}} ^ {(1 - \frac {x}{h}) b _ {2}} x ^ {2} d x = \frac {b _ {2} ^ {3} - b _ {1} ^ {3}}{3} \int_ {0} ^ {h} \left(1 - \frac {y}{h}\right) ^ {3} d y = \frac {h \left(b _ {2} ^ {3} - b _ {1} ^ {3}\right)}{1 2};
$$

若设 $b_{1} > b_{2}$ ，则 $I_{x} = \frac{(b_{1} - b_{2})h^{3}}{12},\qquad I_{y} = \frac{h(b_{1}^{3} - b_{2}^{3})}{12}.$

【4062】 $(x - a)^{2} + (y - a)^{2} = a^{2}, x = 0, y = 0 (0 \leqslant x \leqslant a)$ .

解 $I_{x} = \int_{0}^{a}\mathrm{d}x\int_{0}^{a - \sqrt{2ar - x^2}}y^2\mathrm{d}y$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {1}{3} \int_ {0} ^ {a} \left[ a ^ {3} - 3 a ^ {2} \sqrt {2 a x - x ^ {2}} + 3 a (2 a x - x ^ {2}) - (2 a x - x ^ {2}) ^ {\frac {3}{2}} \right] d x \\ = \frac {1}{3} \left[ a ^ {3} x - 3 a ^ {2} \left(\frac {x - a}{2} \sqrt {2 a x - x ^ {2}} + \frac {a ^ {2}}{2} \arcsin \frac {x - a}{2}\right) + 3 a ^ {2} x ^ {2} - a x ^ {3} \right] \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {a} - \frac {1}{3} \int_ {0} ^ {a} (2 a x - x ^ {2}) ^ {\frac {3}{2}} d x \\ = a ^ {4} \left(1 - \frac {\pi}{4}\right) - \frac {1}{3} \int_ {- \frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {0} a ^ {4} \cos^ {4} t d t ^ {\cdot 1} = a ^ {4} \left(1 - \frac {\pi}{4}\right) - \frac {1}{3} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} a ^ {4} \cos^ {4} t d t \\ = a ^ {4} \left(1 - \frac {\pi}{4}\right) - \frac {a ^ {1}}{3} \cdot \frac {3}{4} \cdot \frac {1}{2} \cdot \frac {\pi}{2} = \frac {a ^ {1}}{1 6} (1 6 - 5 \pi). \\ \end{array}
$$

利用图形的对称性，即得 $I_{y} = I_{x} = \frac{a^{3}}{16} (16 - 5\pi)$

\*）作代换 $x - a = a\sin t$

【4063】 $r = a(1 + \cos \varphi)$

解曲线所围的平面域可表示为 $-\pi \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \pi, 0 \leqslant r \leqslant a(1 + \cos \varphi)$ .

于是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} I _ {r} = \int_ {- \pi} ^ {\pi} \int_ {0} ^ {a (1 + \cos \varphi)} r ^ {2} \sin^ {2} \varphi \cdot r d r d \varphi = \int_ {- \pi} ^ {\pi} \frac {1}{4} a ^ {4} (1 + \cos \varphi) ^ {4} \sin^ {2} \varphi d \varphi \\ = 2 \cdot \frac {1}{4} a ^ {4} \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} (1 + 4 \cos \varphi + 6 \cos^ {2} \varphi + 4 \cos^ {3} \varphi + \cos^ {4} \varphi) \sin^ {2} \varphi d \varphi = \frac {1}{2} \pi a ^ {4} \cdot \frac {2 1}{1 6} = \frac {2 1}{3 2} \pi a ^ {4}, \\ \end{array}
$$

$$
\begin{array}{l} I _ {y} = \int_ {\pi} ^ {\pi} \int_ {0} ^ {u (1 + \cos \varphi)} r ^ {2} \cos^ {2} \varphi \cdot r d r d \varphi = \frac {1}{2} a ^ {4} \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} (1 + \cos \varphi) ^ {1} \cos^ {2} \varphi d \varphi \\ = \frac {1}{2} a ^ {4} \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} (\cos^ {2} \varphi + 4 \cos^ {3} \varphi + 6 \cos^ {3} \varphi + 4 \cos^ {5} \varphi + \cos^ {5} \varphi) d \varphi = \frac {4 9}{3 2} \pi a ^ {4}. \\ \end{array}
$$

$\int_{0}^{\pi}\cos^{n}\varphi \mathrm{d}\varphi = \left\{ \begin{array}{ll}2\int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}\cos^{n}\varphi \mathrm{d}\varphi , & n\text{为偶数};\\ 0, & n\text{为奇数.} \end{array} \right.$ （204

为算出 $I_{x}, I_{y}$ 的值，也可变换被积函数的形式，直接用换元法计算，这样较简单。事实上，我们有

$$
\begin{array}{l} I _ {r} = \frac {a ^ {4}}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} (1 + \cos \varphi) ^ {4} \sin^ {2} \varphi d \varphi = 2 ^ {6} a ^ {4} \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} \cos^ {1 0} \frac {\varphi}{2} \sin^ {2} \frac {\varphi}{2} d \left(\frac {\varphi}{2}\right) \\ = 2 ^ {6} a ^ {4} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {1 0} x (1 - \cos^ {2} x) d x = 2 ^ {6} a ^ {4} \frac {9 \cdot 7 \cdot 5 \cdot 3 \cdot 1}{1 0 \cdot 8 \cdot 6 \cdot 4 \cdot 2} \left(1 - \frac {1 1}{1 2}\right) \frac {\pi}{2} = \frac {2 1}{3 2} \pi a ^ {4}. \\ \end{array}
$$

$$
\begin{array}{l} I _ {y} = \frac {a ^ {4}}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} (1 + \cos \varphi) ^ {4} \cos^ {2} \varphi d \varphi = \frac {a ^ {4}}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} (1 + \cos \varphi) ^ {4} d \varphi - \frac {2 1}{3 2} \pi a ^ {4} \\ = 2 ^ {4} a ^ {4} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {8} x \mathrm {d} x - \frac {2 1}{3 2} \pi a ^ {4} = \frac {7 0}{3 2} \pi a ^ {4} - \frac {2 1}{3 2} \pi a ^ {4} = \frac {4 9}{3 2} \pi a ^ {4}. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4064】 $x^4 + y^4 = a^2 (x^2 + y^2)$

解曲线的图像关于两坐标轴和直线 $y = x$ 是对称的，参看1542题的图像.曲线的极坐标方程为

$$
r ^ {2} = \frac {a ^ {2}}{\cos^ {4} \varphi + \sin^ {4} \varphi} \quad (0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant 2 \pi).
$$

根据对称性，只要算出从 $\varphi = 0$ 到 $\varphi = \frac{\pi}{4}$ 那部分面积的转动惯量再八倍起来即得结果，并且显然有 $I_{x} = I_{y}$ 。于是，我们有

$$
\begin{array}{l} I _ {x} = I _ {y} = 4 \iint_ {0} (x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}) d x d y = 4 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt {\frac {a ^ {2}}{\cos^ {4} \varphi + \sin^ {4} \varphi}}} r ^ {3} d r = \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} \frac {a ^ {4} d \varphi}{(\cos^ {4} \varphi + \sin^ {4} \varphi) ^ {2}} = \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} \frac {a ^ {4} d \varphi}{(1 - 2 \sin^ {2} \varphi \cos^ {2} \varphi) ^ {2}} \\ = \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} \frac {a ^ {4} \mathrm {d} \varphi}{\left(\frac {3}{4} + \frac {1}{4} \cos 4 \varphi\right) ^ {2}} = 1 6 a ^ {4} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} \frac {\mathrm {d} \varphi}{(3 + \cos 4 \varphi) ^ {2}} = \frac {4 a ^ {4}}{9} \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\left(1 + \frac {1}{3} \cos x\right) ^ {2}} \\ = \frac {4 a ^ {4}}{9} \left[ - \frac {\frac {1}{3} \sin x}{\left(1 - \frac {1}{9}\right) \left(1 + \frac {1}{3} \cos x\right)} + \frac {2}{\left(1 - \frac {1}{9}\right) ^ {\frac {3}{2}}} \arctan \left(\sqrt {\frac {1 - \frac {1}{3}}{1 + \frac {1}{3}}} \tan \frac {x}{2}\right) \right] \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {x ^ {* *})} \\ = \frac {4 a ^ {4}}{9} \cdot 2 \left(\frac {9}{8}\right) ^ {\frac {3}{2}} \frac {\pi}{2} = \frac {3 \pi a ^ {4}}{4 \sqrt {2}}. \\ \end{array}
$$

\*）作代换 $x = 4\varphi$

\*\*）利用2063题的结果.

【4065】 $xy = a^2, xy = 2a^2, x = 2y, 2x = y (x > 0, y > 0)$ .

解 作代换 $xy = u, \frac{y}{x} = v$ ，则 $x = \sqrt{\frac{u}{v}}, y = \sqrt{uv}$ ，且雅可比行列式的绝对值 $|I| = \frac{1}{2v}$ ，曲线所围的面积即积分域变为

$$
a ^ {2} \leqslant u \leqslant 2 a ^ {2}, \quad \frac {1}{2} \leqslant v \leqslant 2.
$$

于是， $I_{x} = \iint_{\Omega} y^{2} \, \mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y = \int_{\frac{1}{2}}^{2} \, \mathrm{d}v \int_{a^{2}}^{2a^{2}} \frac{uv}{2v} \, \mathrm{d}u = \frac{9a^{4}}{8},$ $I_{y} = \iint_{\Omega} x^{2} \, \mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y = \int_{\frac{1}{2}}^{2} \, \mathrm{d}v \int_{a^{2}}^{2a^{2}} \frac{u}{2v^{2}} \, \mathrm{d}u = \frac{9a^{4}}{8}.$

【4066】求曲线 $(x^{2} + y^{2})^{2} = a^{2}(x^{2} - y^{2})$ 所围区域 $S$ 的极转动惯量

$$
I _ {0} = \iint_ {S} (x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}) \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y.
$$

解引用极坐标，则图形 $S$ 的界线的极坐标方程为

$$
r ^ {2} = a ^ {2} \cos 2 \varphi ,
$$

这是双纽线.利用对称性，得 $I_0 = \iint \limits_{S}(x^2 +y^2)\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y = 4\int \limits_0^{\frac{\pi}{4}}\mathrm{d}\varphi \int \limits_0^{a\sqrt{\cos 2\varphi}}r^3\mathrm{d}r = \int \limits_0^{\frac{\pi}{4}}a^4\cos^2 2\varphi \mathrm{d}\varphi = \frac{\pi a^4}{8}.$

【4067】证明公式： $I_{t} = I_{t_{0}} + Sd^{2}$

其中 $I_{l}, I_{l_{0}}$ 是图形 $S$ 对于二平行轴 $l$ 和 $l_{0}$ 的转动惯量，其中 $l_{0}$ 是通过图形的质心，而 $d$ 为两轴间的距离。

证明思路 取 $l_{0}$ 轴为 $Ox$ 轴，图形 $S$ 的质心为坐标原点，则 $I_{l} = \iint \limits_{S}(y - d)^{2}\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y.$ 由题设即易获证.

证取 $l_{0}$ 轴为 $Ox$ 轴，图形的质心为坐标原点，则

$$
I _ {l} = \iint_ {S} (y - d) ^ {2} \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y = \iint_ {S} y ^ {2} \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y - 2 d \iint_ {S} y \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y + d ^ {2} \iint_ {S} \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y.
$$

因为 $l_{0}$ 通过图形 $S$ 的质心，故 $y_{0} = \frac{1}{S}\iint \limits_{S}y\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y = 0$ ，即 $\iint \limits_{S}y\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y = 0.$

又 $\iint_{S} y^{2} \mathrm{d}x \mathrm{d}y = I_{t_{0}}$ , $\iint_{S} \mathrm{d}x \mathrm{d}y = S$ ,

于是， $I_{t} = I_{t_{0}} + Sd^{2}$

【4068】证明：平面图形 $S$ 对通过其质心 $O(0,0)$ 并与 $Ox$ 轴成 $\alpha$ 角的直线的转动惯量等于

$$
I = I _ {x} \cos^ {2} \alpha - 2 I _ {x y} \sin \alpha \cos \alpha + I _ {y} \sin^ {2} \alpha ,
$$

其中 $I_{x}$ 和 $I_{y}$ 为图形 $S$ 对于 $Ox$ 轴和 $Oy$ 轴的转动惯量及 $I_{xy}$ 为惯性积：

$$
I _ {x y} = \iint_ {5} \rho x y d x d y.
$$

证明思路 取直角坐标系 $Ox^{\prime}y^{\prime}$ ，使 $Ox^{\prime}$ 轴与 $Ox$ 轴的夹角为 $\alpha$ ，则有

$$
x ^ {\prime} = x \mathrm {c o s} \alpha + y \mathrm {s i n} \alpha , \quad y ^ {\prime} = - x \mathrm {s i n} \alpha + y \mathrm {c o s} \alpha . \quad \text {且} \quad | I | = \left| \frac {D (x ^ {\prime} , y ^ {\prime})}{D (x , y)} \right| = 1.
$$

于是，所求的转动惯量为 $I = \iint_{S} y'^2 \rho \mathrm{d}x' \mathrm{d}y'$ . 由题设即易获证.

证今取直角坐标系 $Ox^{\prime}y^{\prime}$ ，使 $Ox^{\prime}$ 轴与 $Ox$ 轴的夹角为 $\alpha$ ，则有

$$
x ^ {\prime} = x \cos \alpha + y \sin \alpha , \quad y ^ {\prime} = - x \sin \alpha + y \cos \alpha .
$$

这就是旋转变换，雅可比行列式的绝对值 $|I| = \left|\frac{D(x',y')}{D(x,y)}\right| = 1.$

于是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} I = \iint_ {S} y ^ {\prime 2} \rho d x ^ {\prime} d y ^ {\prime} = \iint_ {S} (- x \sin \alpha + y \cos \alpha) ^ {2} \rho d x d y \\ = \cos^ {2} \alpha \iint_ {S} \rho y ^ {2} d x d y - 2 \sin \alpha \cos \alpha \iint_ {S} \rho x y d x d y + \sin^ {2} \alpha \iint_ {S} \rho x ^ {2} d x d y \\ = I _ {x} \cos^ {2} \alpha - 2 I _ {x y} \sin \alpha \cos \alpha + I _ {y} \sin^ {2} \alpha . \\ \end{array}
$$

【4069】求以 $a$ 为边的正三角形对通过三角形质心并与它的高成 $\alpha$ 角的直线的转动惯量.

解利用4068题的结果，取质心为坐标原点.不妨取 $Ox$ 轴平行于三角形的一条边，则过质心与高成 $\alpha$ 角的直线，即为过坐标原点与 $Ox$ 轴成 $\alpha$ 角的直线.于是，所求的转动惯量为

$$
I _ {\alpha} = I _ {x} \cos^ {2} \alpha - 2 I _ {x y} \sin \alpha \cos \alpha + I _ {y} \sin^ {2} \alpha .
$$

由于三角形三边所在的直线方程分别为

$$
y = - \frac {a}{2 \sqrt {3}}, \quad y = - \sqrt {3} x + \frac {a}{\sqrt {3}}, \quad y = \sqrt {3} x + \frac {a}{\sqrt {3}},
$$

所以，根据对称性知：

$$
\begin{array}{l} I _ {x} = 2 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {a}{2}} d x \int_ {- \frac {a}{2 \sqrt {3}}} ^ {- \sqrt {3} x + \frac {a}{\sqrt {3}}} y ^ {2} d y = 2 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {a}{2}} \frac {1}{3} \left[ \left(- \sqrt {3} x + \frac {a}{\sqrt {3}}\right) ^ {3} - \left(- \frac {a}{2 \sqrt {3}}\right) ^ {3} \right] d x \\ = 2 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {a}{2}} \left(- \sqrt {3} x ^ {3} + \sqrt {3} a x ^ {2} - \frac {\sqrt {3}}{3} a ^ {2} x + \frac {\sqrt {3}}{2 4} a ^ {3}\right) d x = 2 \sqrt {3} a ^ {4} \left(\frac {1}{4 8} - \frac {1}{6 4}\right) = \frac {a ^ {4}}{3 2 \sqrt {3}}; \\ \end{array}
$$

$$
\begin{array}{l} I _ {x y} = \iint_ {S} x y \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y = 0; \\ I _ {y} = 2 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {a}{2}} \mathrm {d} x \int_ {\frac {a}{2 \sqrt {3}}} ^ {\sqrt {3} x + \frac {a}{\sqrt {3}}} x ^ {2} \mathrm {d} y = 2 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {a}{2}} x ^ {2} \left[ \left(- \sqrt {3} x + \frac {a}{\sqrt {3}}\right) + \frac {a}{2 \sqrt {3}} \right] \mathrm {d} x \\ \end{array}
$$

$$
= 2 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {a}{2}} \left(- \sqrt {3} x ^ {3} + \frac {\sqrt {3} a}{2} x ^ {2}\right) d x = \sqrt {3} a ^ {4} \left(\frac {1}{2 4} - \frac {1}{3 2}\right) = \frac {a ^ {4}}{3 2 \sqrt {3}}.
$$

于是， $I_{\alpha} = \frac{a^4}{32\sqrt{3}}\cos^2\alpha +\frac{a^4}{32\sqrt{3}}\sin^2\alpha = \frac{a^4}{32\sqrt{3}}.$

【4070】设圆柱形容器 $x^{2} + y^{2} = a^{2},z = 0$ 内盛有水，水平面为 $z = h$ ，求水对容器侧壁 $x\geqslant 0$ 的压力.

解 用 $X$ 和 $Y$ 分别表示压力在 $Ox$ 与 $Oy$ 轴上的投影. 由对称性, 显然有 $Y = 0$ . 下面求 $X$ . 由于 $\mathrm{d}S = a \mathrm{~d}\theta \mathrm{d}z\left(-\frac{\pi}{2} \leqslant \theta \leqslant \frac{\pi}{2}\right)$ , 而在面元 $\mathrm{d}S$ 上的压力在 $Ox$ 轴上的投影 $\mathrm{d}X$ 为 $(z \mathrm{~d}S) \cos \theta$ . 于是,

$$
X = \iint_ {S} z \cos \theta d S = \iint_ {S} a z \cos \theta d \theta d z = a \left(\int_ {- \frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos \theta d \theta\right) \left(\int_ {0} ^ {h} z d z\right) = a h ^ {2}.
$$

【4071】半径为 $a$ 的球体沉入密度为 $\delta$ 的液体中深度为 $h$ （由球心算起）的地方，这里 $h \geq a$ . 求液体对球的上表面和下表面的压力.

解设球面方程为 $x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2} = a^{2}$ ，则在球面上的点 $(x,y,z)$ 处沉入液体的深度 $d$ 为

$$
d = h - z \quad (- a \leqslant z \leqslant h).
$$

于是，上半球面 $S_{1}$ 的点和下半球面 $S_{2}$ 的点的深度分别为

$$
d = h - \sqrt {a ^ {2} - \left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}\right)}, \quad d = h + \sqrt {a ^ {2} - \left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}\right)}.
$$

根据对称性知，压力在 $Ox$ 轴上和 $Oy$ 轴的投影均为零，故只要计算压力在 $Oz$ 轴上的投影，液体作用于球的上表面和下表面的压力分别记以 $p_1$ 和 $p_2$ ，并设 $\gamma$ 为球上各点处压力的方向（即内法线方向）与 $Oz$ 轴正向的夹角，则

$$
\begin{array}{l} p _ {1} = \iint_ {S _ {1}} d \delta \cos \gamma \mathrm {d} S = - \iint_ {r ^ {2} + y ^ {2} \leqslant a ^ {2}} \delta [ h - \sqrt {a ^ {2} - (x ^ {2} + y ^ {2})} ] \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y = - h \pi a ^ {2} \delta + \delta \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} \mathrm {d} \theta \int_ {0} ^ {a} \sqrt {a ^ {2} - r ^ {2}} r \mathrm {d} r \\ = - h \pi a ^ {2} \delta + \left[ \frac {- 2 \pi \delta}{3} \sqrt {\left(a ^ {2} - r ^ {2}\right) ^ {3}} \right] \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {a} = - \pi a ^ {2} \delta \left(h - \frac {2 a}{3}\right) \quad (p _ {1} <   0 \text {表 示 压 力 向 下}). \\ \end{array}
$$

同理，我们有

$$
p _ {2} = \iint_ {S _ {2}} d \delta \cos \gamma \mathrm {d} S = \iint_ {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} <   a ^ {2}} \delta \left[ h + \sqrt {a ^ {2} - \left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}\right)} \right] \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y = \pi a ^ {2} \delta \left(h + \frac {2 a}{3}\right) \quad (p _ {2} > 0 \text {表 示 压 力 向 上}).
$$

【4072】底半径为 $a$ 高为 $b$ 的直圆柱体完全沉入密度为 $\delta$ 的液体中，其中心在液面下的深度为 $h$ ，而圆柱的轴与竖直方向成 $\alpha$ 角，求液体对圆柱上底和下底的压力.

解取圆柱的中心为坐标原点，取 $Oxy$ 平面是水平的，再取圆柱的轴（朝上的方向）在 $Oxy$ 平面上的投影所在的方向为 $Ox$ 轴，取 $Oz$ 轴垂直向上，最后取 $Oy$ 轴使 $Ox$ 轴、 $Oy$ 轴和 $Oz$ 轴构成右手系.

于是，液面方程为 $z = h$ 设圆柱上底为 $S_{1}$ ，下底为 $S_{2}$ ，则 $S_{1}$ 所在平面的方程为

$$
x \sin \alpha + z \cos \alpha = \frac {b}{2}, \tag {1}
$$

$S_{2}$ 所在平面的方程为

$$
x \sin \alpha + z \cos \alpha = - \frac {b}{2}. \tag {2}
$$

在点 $(x, y, z)$ 处 $(z \leqslant h)$ 液体的深度为 $h - z$ . 用 $X_{1}, Y_{1}$ 和 $Z_{1}$ 分别表示液体在圆柱上底 $S_{1}$ 上的压力在 $Ox$ 轴、 $Oy$ 轴和 $Oz$ 轴上的投影. 同样，用 $X_{2}, Y_{2}$ 和 $Z_{2}$ 分别表示在 $S_{2}$ 上的压力在 $Ox$ 轴、 $Oy$ 轴和 $Oz$ 轴上的投影. 显然， $Y_{1} = Y_{2} = 0$ . 我们有

$$
X _ {1} = - \iint_ {S _ {1}} \delta (h - z) \sin \alpha d S = - \delta \sin \alpha \iint_ {S _ {1}} (h - z) d S, \tag {3}
$$

$$
Z _ {1} = - \iint_ {S _ {1}} \delta (h - z) \cos \alpha d S = - \delta \cos \alpha \iint_ {S _ {1}} (h - z) d S. \tag {4}
$$

由(1)式知，在 $S_{1}$ 上有 $z = \frac{1}{\cos\alpha}\left(\frac{b}{2} -x\sin \alpha\right)$ . 于是，注意到 $S_{1}$ 的面积为 $\pi a^2$ ，可知

$$
\begin{array}{l} \iint_ {S _ {1}} (h - z) d S = \iint_ {S _ {1}} \left[ h - \frac {1}{\cos \alpha} \left(\frac {b}{2} - x \sin \alpha\right) \right] d S = \left(h - \frac {b}{2} \frac {1}{\cos \alpha}\right) \iint_ {S _ {1}} d S + \frac {\sin \alpha}{\cos \alpha} \iint_ {S _ {1}} x d S \\ = \left(h - \frac {b}{2} \frac {1}{\cos \alpha}\right) \pi a ^ {2} + \frac {\sin \alpha}{\cos \alpha} \iint_ {S _ {1}} x d S. \\ \end{array}
$$

由于 $\frac{1}{\pi a^2}\iint_{S_1}x\mathrm{d}S$ 是 $S_{1}$ 的质心的 $x$ 坐标，也即 $\frac{b}{2}\sin \alpha$ ，故 $\iint_{S_1}x\mathrm{d}S = \frac{1}{2}\pi a^2 b\sin \alpha .$ 代人即得

$$
\iint_ {S _ {1}} (h - z) \mathrm {d} S = \left(h - \frac {b}{2 \cos \alpha}\right) \pi a ^ {2} + \frac {1}{2} \pi a ^ {2} b \frac {\sin^ {2} \alpha}{\cos \alpha} = \left(h - \frac {b}{2} \cos \alpha\right) \pi a ^ {2},
$$

以此代入(3)式与(4)式，得 $X_{1} = -\pi a^{2}\delta \left(h - \frac{b}{2}\cos \alpha\right)\sin \alpha, Z_{1} = -\pi a^{2}\delta \left(h - \frac{b}{2}\cos \alpha\right)\cos \alpha,$

同理，我们有 $X_{2} = \iint_{S_{2}}\delta (h - z)\sin \alpha \mathrm{d}S = \delta \sin \alpha \iint_{S_{2}}(h - z)\mathrm{d}S,\quad Z_{2} = \iint_{S_{2}}\delta (h - z)\cos \alpha \mathrm{d}S = \delta \cos \alpha \iint_{S_{2}}(h - z)\mathrm{d}S.$

再注意到（2）式，类似地可计算得

$$
\iint_ {S _ {2}} (h - z) d S = \iint_ {S _ {2}} \left[ h + \frac {1}{\cos \alpha} \left(\frac {b}{2} + x \sin \alpha\right) \right] d S = \left(h + \frac {b}{2} \cos \alpha\right) \pi a ^ {2}.
$$

于是， $X_{2} = \pi a^{2}\delta \left(h + \frac{b}{2}\cos \alpha\right)\sin \alpha ,Z_{2} = \pi a^{2}\delta \left(h + \frac{b}{2}\cos \alpha\right)\cos \alpha .$

【4073】求均匀的圆柱体 $x^{2} + y^{2}\leqslant a^{2},0\leqslant z\leqslant h$ 对质点 $P(0,0,b)$ 的引力，设圆柱的质量等于 $M$ ，而质点的质量等于 $m$

解 根据对称性知，引力在 $Ox$ 轴和 $Oy$ 轴上的投影等于零，故只要计算引力在 $Oz$ 轴上的投影 $F_{z}$ 。今取圆环，其体积为

$$
\mathrm {d} V = 2 \pi r \mathrm {d} r \mathrm {d} z,
$$

则相应的质量为 $\mathrm{d}M = \frac{2\pi r M \mathrm{d}r \mathrm{d}z}{\pi a^2 h} = \frac{2Mr}{a^2 h} \mathrm{d}r \mathrm{d}z,$

吸引质点 $P$ 的引力 $\mathrm{d}F_{z} = -\frac{2krmM(b - z)}{a^{2}h\sqrt{\left[r^{2} + (b - z)^{2}\right]^{3}}}\mathrm{d}r\mathrm{d}z.$

于是，所求的引力为

$$
\begin{array}{l} F _ {z} = - \frac {2 k m M}{a ^ {2} h} \int_ {0} ^ {h} \int_ {0} ^ {a} \frac {r (b - z)}{\sqrt {\left[ r ^ {2} + (b - z) ^ {2} \right] ^ {3}}} d r d z = - \frac {2 k m M}{a ^ {2} h} \left[ \int_ {0} ^ {h} \operatorname {s g n} (b - z) d z - \int_ {0} ^ {h} \frac {b - z}{\sqrt {a ^ {2} + (b - z) ^ {2}}} d z \right] \\ = - \frac {2 k m M}{a ^ {2} h} \left[ | b | - | b - h | + \sqrt {a ^ {2} + (b - h) ^ {2}} - \sqrt {a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}} \right], \\ \end{array}
$$

其中 $k$ 为引力常数.

【4074】 物体对挤压面 $\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2}\leqslant 1$

的压强分布由公式 $p = p_0\left(1 - \frac{x^2}{a^2} -\frac{y^2}{b^2}\right)$

给出.求物体对此面的平均压强

解 物体在椭圆面上的平均压强为

$$
p _ {i p} = \frac {1}{\pi a b} \iint_ {\frac {x ^ {2}}{a ^ {2}} \cdot \frac {y ^ {2}}{b ^ {2}} \leq 1} p _ {0} \left(1 - \frac {x ^ {2}}{a ^ {2}} - \frac {y ^ {2}}{b ^ {2}}\right) d x d y = \frac {4}{\pi a b} \int_ {a} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \theta \int_ {a} ^ {1} p _ {0} (1 - r ^ {2}) a b r d r = \frac {4}{\pi a b} \cdot \frac {\pi}{2} \cdot \frac {p _ {0} a b}{4} = \frac {p _ {0}}{2}.
$$

【4075】以 $a$ 和 $b$ 为边的矩形草地上均匀地覆盖有已收割的干草，其面密度为 $p$ 。若运送质量为 $M$ 的货物到距离为 $r$ 的地方所需的功为 $kMr(0 < k < 1)$ ，则为了把所有的干草集中在草地的中心，至少应消耗多少功？

解 不妨将坐标原点取在矩形的中心， $Ox$ 轴平行于 $a$ 边， $Oy$ 轴平行于 $b$ 边. 由于将面积 $\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y$ 上的干草移到中心要消耗的功为 $\mathrm{d}W = kp\sqrt{x^2 + y^2}\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y$ ，并利用对称性，即知所要求的功为

$$
\begin{array}{l} W = 1 k p \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {b}{2}} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {a}{2}} \sqrt {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}} d x d y = 4 k p \left[ \int_ {0} ^ {\arctan \frac {b}{a}} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {a}{2 \cos \varphi}} r ^ {2} d r d \varphi + \int_ {\arctan \frac {b}{a}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {b}{2 \sin \varphi}} r ^ {2} d r d \varphi \right] \\ = \frac {k p}{6} \left[ a ^ {3} \int_ {0} ^ {\arctan \frac {h}{a}} \frac {1}{\cos^ {3} \varphi} d \varphi + b ^ {3} \int_ {\arctan \frac {h}{a}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \frac {1}{\sin^ {3} \varphi} d \varphi \right]. \\ \end{array}
$$

但是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int_ {0} ^ {\arctan \frac {b}{a}} \frac {1}{\cos^ {3} \varphi} d \varphi = \left[ \frac {\sin \varphi}{2 \cos^ {2} \varphi} + \frac {1}{2} \ln \left| \tan \left(\frac {\varphi}{2} + \frac {\pi}{4}\right) \right| \right] \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {\arctan \frac {b}{a} \cdot 1} = \frac {b \sqrt {a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}}}{2 a ^ {2}} + \frac {1}{2} \ln \frac {b + \sqrt {a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}}}{a}, \\ \int_ {\arctan \frac {b}{a}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \frac {1}{\sin^ {3} \varphi} d \varphi = \left[ - \frac {\cos \varphi}{2 \sin^ {2} \varphi} + \frac {1}{2} \ln \left| \tan \frac {\varphi}{2} \right| \right] \left| _ {\arctan \frac {b}{a}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2} * *} = \frac {a \sqrt {a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}}}{2 b ^ {2}} + \frac {1}{2} \ln \frac {a + \sqrt {a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}}}{b}, \right. \\ \end{array}
$$

于是，我们有 $W = \frac{kp}{12}\left(2ab\sqrt{a^2 + b^2} + a^3\ln \frac{b + \sqrt{a^2 + b^2}}{a} + b^3\ln \frac{a + \sqrt{a^2 + b^2}}{b}\right).$

\*) 利用2000题的结果.

$\star \star$ ）利用1999题的结果.

# §6. 三重积分

1° 三重积分的直接计算法 函数 $f(x,y,z)$ 是连续的，且有界区域 $V$ 由下列不等式给出：

$$
x _ {1} \leqslant x \leqslant x _ {2}, \quad y _ {1} (x) \leqslant y \leqslant y _ {2} (x), \quad z _ {1} (x, y) \leqslant z \leqslant z _ {2} (x, y),
$$

其中 $y_{1}(x), y_{2}(x), z_{1}(x, y), z_{2}(x, y)$ 皆为连续函数，则函数 $f(x, y, z)$ 在区域 $V$ 内的三重积分可按公式

$$
\iiint_ {V} f (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y \mathrm {d} z = \int_ {x _ {1}} ^ {x _ {2}} \mathrm {d} x \int_ {y _ {1} (x)} ^ {y _ {2} (x)} \mathrm {d} y \int_ {z _ {1} (x, y)} ^ {z _ {2} (x, y)} f (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} z
$$

来计算. 有时采用下面的公式也很方便：

$$
\iiint_ {V} f (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y \mathrm {d} z = \int_ {x _ {1}} ^ {x _ {2}} \mathrm {d} x \iint_ {S (x)} f (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} y \mathrm {d} z,
$$

其中 $S(x)$ 是用平面 $x =$ 常数截区域 $V$ 所得的截面

$2^{\circ}$ 三重积分中的变量代换 若连续可微函数

$$
r = x (u, v, w), \quad y = y (u, v, w), \quad z = z (u, v, w)
$$

给出 $Oxyz$ 空间的有界可求积的三维闭区域 $V$ 与 $O'uvw$ 空间的区域 $V'$ 之间的——映射，并且当 $(u, v, w) \in V'$ 时，

$$
I = \frac {D (x , y , z)}{D (u , v , w)} \neq 0,
$$

则成立公式

$$
\iiint_ {V} f (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y \mathrm {d} z = \iiint_ {V} f [ x (u, v, w), y (u, v, w), z (u, v, w) ] | I | \mathrm {d} u \mathrm {d} v \mathrm {d} w.
$$

在特殊情况下，有：1）圆柱坐标系 $\varphi, r, h$ ，其中

$$
x = r \cos \varphi , \quad y = r \sin \varphi , \quad z = h, \quad \frac {D (x , y , z)}{D (\varphi , r , h)} = r.
$$

2）球坐标系 $\varphi, \psi, r$ ，其中

$$
x = r \cos \varphi \cos \psi , \quad y = r \sin \varphi \cos \psi , \quad z = r \sin \psi , \quad \frac {D (x , y , z)}{D (\varphi , \psi , r)} = r ^ {2} \cos \psi .
$$

# 计算下列三重积分：

【4076】 $\iiint_{V} xy^{2} z^{3} \, \mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y \, \mathrm{d}z$ ，其中 $V$ 是曲面 $z = xy, y = x, x = 1, z = 0$ 所围的区域。

解 $\iiint_{V} xy^{2}z^{3} \mathrm{d}x \mathrm{d}y \mathrm{d}z = \int_{0}^{1} x \mathrm{~d}x \int_{0}^{x} y^{2} \mathrm{~d}y \int_{0}^{xy} z^{3} \mathrm{~d}z = \frac{1}{364}$ .

【4077】 $\iiint_{V} \frac{\mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y \, \mathrm{d}z}{(1 + x + y + z)^3}$ ，其中 $V$ 是曲面 $x + y + z = 1, x = 0, y = 0, z = 0$ 所围的区域.

解 $\iiint_{V} \frac{\mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y \, \mathrm{d}z}{(1 + x + y + z)^3} = \int_0^1 \mathrm{d}x \int_0^1 x \, \mathrm{d}y \int_0^{1 - x - y} \frac{\mathrm{d}z}{(1 + x + y + z)^3}$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \int_ {0} ^ {1} d x \int_ {0} ^ {1 - x} \left[ - \frac {1}{2 (1 + x + y + z) ^ {2}} \right] \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {1 - x - y} d y = \int_ {0} ^ {1} d x \int_ {0} ^ {1 - x} \left[ - \frac {1}{8} + \frac {1}{2 (1 + x + y) ^ {2}} \right] d y \\ = \int_ {0} ^ {1} \left[ - \frac {1}{8} y - \frac {1}{2 (1 + x + y)} \right] \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {1} d x = \int_ {0} ^ {1} \left[ - \frac {3}{8} + \frac {x}{8} + \frac {1}{2 (1 + x)} \right] d x \\ = \left[ - \frac {3}{8} x + \frac {1}{1 6} x ^ {2} + \frac {1}{2} \ln (1 + x) \right] \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {1} = \frac {1}{2} \ln 2 - \frac {5}{1 6}. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4078】 $\iiint_{V} xyz \, \mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y \, \mathrm{d}z$ ，其中 $V$ 是曲面 $x^2 + y^2 + z^2 = 1, x = 0, y = 0, z = 0$ 所围的区域.

解 $\iiint_{V} xyz \, \mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y \, \mathrm{d}z = \int_{0}^{1} x \, \mathrm{d}x \int_{0}^{\sqrt{1 - x^2}} y \, \mathrm{d}y \int_{0}^{\sqrt{1 - x^2 - y^2}} z \, \mathrm{d}z = \frac{1}{2} \int_{0}^{1} x \, \mathrm{d}x \int_{0}^{\sqrt{1 - x^2}} y (1 - x^2 - y^2) \, \mathrm{d}y$

$$
= \frac {1}{8} \int_ {0} ^ {1} x (1 - x ^ {2}) ^ {2} d x = \frac {1}{4 8}.
$$

【4079】 $\iiint_{V}\left(\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2} +\frac{z^2}{c^2}\right)\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y\mathrm{d}z$ ，其中 $V$ 是曲面

$$
\frac {x ^ {2}}{a ^ {2}} + \frac {y ^ {2}}{b ^ {2}} + \frac {z ^ {2}}{c ^ {2}} = 1
$$

所围的区域.

解题思路 设 $P_x, Q_y, R_z$ 分别表示区域 $V$ 与平面 $x =$ 常数， $y =$ 常数， $z =$ 常数所截部分在 $Oyz, Ozx, Oxy$ 平面上的投影，则有

$$
\text {原 式} = \int_ {a} ^ {a} \frac {x ^ {2}}{a ^ {2}} \mathrm {d} x \iint_ {P _ {r}} \mathrm {d} y \mathrm {d} z + \int_ {b} ^ {b} \frac {y ^ {2}}{b ^ {2}} \mathrm {d} y \iint_ {Q _ {y}} \mathrm {d} z \mathrm {d} x + \int_ {c} ^ {c} \frac {z ^ {2}}{c ^ {2}} \mathrm {d} z \iint_ {R _ {z}} \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y.
$$

解设 $P_{x}, Q_{y}, R_{z}$ 分别表示区域 $V$ 与平面 $x =$ 常数， $y =$ 常数， $z =$ 常数所截部分在 $Oyz, Ozx, Oxy$ 平面上的投影，则有

$$
\begin{array}{l} \iiint_ {V} \left(\frac {x ^ {2}}{a ^ {2}} + \frac {y ^ {2}}{b ^ {2}} + \frac {z ^ {2}}{c ^ {2}}\right) d x d y d z = \int_ {- a} ^ {a} \frac {x ^ {2}}{a ^ {2}} d x \iint_ {P _ {x}} d y d z + \int_ {- b} ^ {b} \frac {y ^ {2}}{b ^ {2}} d y \iint_ {\tilde {Q} _ {y}} d z d x + \int_ {- c} ^ {c} \frac {z ^ {2}}{c ^ {2}} d z \iint_ {R _ {z}} d x d y \\ = \frac {\pi b c}{a ^ {2}} \int_ {a} ^ {a} x ^ {2} \left(1 - \frac {x ^ {2}}{a ^ {2}}\right) d x ^ {*}) + \frac {\pi a c}{b ^ {2}} \int_ {- b} ^ {b} y ^ {2} \left(1 - \frac {y ^ {2}}{b ^ {2}}\right) d y + \frac {\pi a b}{c ^ {2}} \int_ {c} ^ {c} z ^ {2} \left(1 - \frac {z ^ {2}}{c ^ {2}}\right) d z = 3 \cdot \frac {4 \pi a b c}{1 5} = \frac {4 \pi a b c}{5}. \\ \end{array}
$$

\*) $P_{r}$ 在平面 $x =$ 常数上的方程为

$$
\frac {y ^ {2}}{b ^ {2} \left(1 - \frac {x ^ {2}}{a ^ {2}}\right)} + \frac {z ^ {2}}{c ^ {2} \left(1 - \frac {x ^ {2}}{a ^ {2}}\right)} = 1,
$$

故其面积为 $\pi b\sqrt{1 - \frac{x^2}{a^2}}\cdot c\sqrt{1 - \frac{x^2}{a^2}} = \pi bc\left(1 - \frac{x^2}{a^2}\right).$

$Q_{y}$ 及 $R_{z}$ 的面积类推.

【4080】 $\iiint_{V} \sqrt{x^2 + y^2} \, \mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y \, \mathrm{d}z$ ，其中 $V$ 是曲面 $x^2 + y^2 = z^2, z = 1$ 所围的区域.

解题思路 注意曲面在 $(xy)$ 平面上的投影 $Q$ 为圆盘 $x^{2} + y^{2} \leqslant 1$ . 则有

$$
\text {原 式} = \iint_ {Q} \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y \int_ {\sqrt {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}}} ^ {1} \sqrt {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}} \mathrm {d} z.
$$

解曲面在 $Oxy$ 平面上的投影 $Q$ 为圆盘 $x^{2} + y^{2}\leqslant 1.$ 于是，

$$
\iiint_ {V} \sqrt {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}} d x d y d z = \iint_ {\Omega} d x d y \int_ {\sqrt {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}}} ^ {1} \sqrt {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}} d z = \iint_ {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} \leqslant 1} [ \sqrt {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}} - (x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}) ] d x d y
$$

$$
= \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {1} (r - r ^ {2}) r d r = \frac {\pi}{6}.
$$

在下列三重积分内，用不同方法配置积分的上下限：

【4081】 $\int_{0}^{1}\mathrm{d}x\int_{0}^{1 - x}\mathrm{d}y\int_{0}^{x + y}f(x,y,z)\mathrm{d}z.$

解 有界区域 $V$ 如图8.52所示，

![](images/74b198edad1049fd87e105d827e1e67be47f4c4f4183b1d33bc50947aa2bbdda.jpg)  
图8.52

![](images/0e7e4bf333d9e278cbef3585496798a46d5517411375f3eaef24be9a39b42468.jpg)  
图8.53

如果先对 $y$ 积分，再对 $z, x$ 积分，如图8.53所示，则积分域在 $Oyz$ 平面上的投影域由诸直线

$$
z = 0, \quad z = x + y, \quad y = 0, \quad y = 1 - x \quad (x \text {固 定})
$$

围成.于是，我们有

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int_ {0} ^ {1} \mathrm {d} x \int_ {0} ^ {1 - x} \mathrm {d} y \int_ {0} ^ {x + y} f (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} z \\ = \int_ {0} ^ {1} d x \left\{\int_ {0} ^ {x} d z \int_ {0} ^ {1 - x} f (x, y, z) d y + \int_ {x} ^ {1} d z \int_ {z} ^ {1} f (x, y, z) d y \right\} ^ {\cdot 1}, \\ \end{array}
$$

如果先对 $x$ 积分，再对 $y, z$ 积分，如图8.54所示，则有

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int_ {0} ^ {1} \mathrm {d} x \int_ {0} ^ {1 - x} \mathrm {d} y \int_ {0} ^ {x - y} f (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} z \\ = \int_ {0} ^ {1} \mathrm {d} z \left\{\int_ {0} ^ {z} \mathrm {d} y \int_ {z - y} ^ {1 - y} f (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} x + \int_ {z} ^ {1} \mathrm {d} y \int_ {0} ^ {1 - y} f (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} x \right\}. \\ \end{array}
$$

$\star$ ）这里用的公式为

$$
\iiint_ {V} f (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y \mathrm {d} z = \int_ {a} ^ {b} \mathrm {d} x \iint_ {S (x)} f (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} y \mathrm {d} z.
$$

【4082】 $\int_{-1}^{1}\mathrm{d}x\int_{-\sqrt{1 - x^2}}^{\sqrt{1 - x^2}}\mathrm{d}y\int_{\sqrt{x^2 + y^2}}^{1}f(x,y,z)\mathrm{d}z.$

解 有界区域 $V$ 如图8.55所示，

如果先对 $y$ 积分，再对 $z, x$ 积分，如图8.56所示，则积分域在 $Oyz$ 平面上的投影域由不等式

$$
| x | \leqslant z \leqslant 1, - \sqrt {z ^ {2} - x ^ {2}} \leqslant y \leqslant \sqrt {z ^ {2} - x ^ {2}},
$$

$(x$ 固定)给出.于是，我们有

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int_ {1} ^ {1} \mathrm {d} x \int_ {- \sqrt {1 - x ^ {2}}} ^ {\sqrt {1 - x ^ {2}}} \mathrm {d} y \int_ {\sqrt {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}}} ^ {1} f (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} z \\ = \int_ {1} ^ {1} \mathrm {d} x \int_ {r} ^ {1} \mathrm {d} z \int_ {\sqrt {z ^ {2} - x ^ {2}}} ^ {\sqrt {z ^ {2} - x ^ {2}}} f (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} y. \\ \end{array}
$$

如果先对 $x$ 积分，再对 $y, z$ 积分，如图8.57所示，则有

$$
\int_ {- 1} ^ {1} \mathrm {d} x \int_ {- \sqrt {1 - x ^ {2}}} ^ {\sqrt {1 - x ^ {2}}} \mathrm {d} y \int_ {\sqrt {x ^ {2} - y ^ {2}}} ^ {1} f (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} z = \int_ {0} ^ {1} \mathrm {d} z \int_ {- z} ^ {z} \mathrm {d} y \int_ {- \sqrt {z ^ {2} - y ^ {2}}} ^ {\sqrt {z ^ {2} - y ^ {2}}} f (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} r.
$$

![](images/b7c585ff2dad68779c133ff4e7cbab6de8cc6f4556fcfd3b12dcb91e7fb7554e.jpg)

【4083】 $\int_0^1\mathrm{d}x\int_0^1\mathrm{d}y\int_0^{x^2 +y^2}f(x,y,z)\mathrm{d}z.$

解如果先对 $y$ 积分，再对 $z, x$ 积分，则积分域在 $Oxy$ 平面上的投影域由方程

$$
x = 1, z = 0, z = x ^ {2} \quad \text {及} \quad x = 0, r = 1, z = x ^ {2}, z = x ^ {2} + 1
$$

所表示的曲线围成.于是，我们有

$$
\int_ {0} ^ {1} \mathrm {d} x \int_ {0} ^ {1} \mathrm {d} y \int_ {0} ^ {x ^ {2} - y ^ {2}} f (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} z = \int_ {0} ^ {1} \mathrm {d} x \left[ \int_ {0} ^ {x ^ {2}} \mathrm {d} z \int_ {0} ^ {1} f (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} y + \int_ {z ^ {2}} ^ {x ^ {2} - 1} \mathrm {d} z \int_ {\sqrt {z - x ^ {2}}} ^ {1} f (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} y \right].
$$

如果先对 $x$ 积分，再对 $z, y$ 积分，不难由轮换对称关系得出结果。

如果先对 $x$ 积分，再对 $y, z$ 积分，则积分域在 $Oyz$ 平面上的投影域由方程

$$
y = 1, z = 0, y = \sqrt {z} \quad \text {及} \quad y = 0, y = 1, y = \sqrt {z}, y = \sqrt {z - 1}
$$

所表示的曲线围成.于是，我们有

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int_ {0} ^ {1} \mathrm {d} x \int_ {0} ^ {1} \mathrm {d} y \int_ {0} ^ {x ^ {2} - y ^ {2}} f (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} z \\ = \int_ {0} ^ {1} d z \left[ \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt {\varepsilon}} d y \int_ {\sqrt {z y ^ {2}}} ^ {1} f (x, y, z) d x + \int_ {\sqrt {\varepsilon}} ^ {1} d y \int_ {0} ^ {1} f (x, y, z) d x \right] + \int_ {1} ^ {2} d z \int_ {\sqrt {z - 1}} ^ {1} d y \int_ {\sqrt {z - y ^ {2}}} ^ {1} f (x, y, z) d x. \\ \end{array}
$$

\*）这里采用的投影方式与前两题不同，系用结果

$$
\iiint_ {V} f (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y \mathrm {d} z = \iint_ {S} \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} z \int_ {y _ {1}} ^ {y _ {2}} f (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} y.
$$

以一重积分代替三重积分：

【4084】 $\int_{0}^{x}\mathrm{d}\xi \int_{0}^{\xi}\mathrm{d}\eta \int_{0}^{\eta}f(\zeta)\mathrm{d}\zeta$

解 $\int_{0}^{x}\mathrm{d}\xi \int_{0}^{\xi}\mathrm{d}\eta \int_{0}^{\eta}f(\zeta)\mathrm{d}\zeta = \int_{0}^{x}\mathrm{d}\xi \int_{0}^{\xi}\mathrm{d}\zeta \int_{\zeta}^{\xi}f(\zeta)\mathrm{d}\eta = \int_{0}^{x}\mathrm{d}\xi \int_{0}^{\xi}f(\zeta)(\xi -\zeta)\mathrm{d}\zeta = \int_{0}^{x}\mathrm{d}\zeta \int_{\zeta}^{x}f(\zeta)(\xi -\zeta)\mathrm{d}\xi$

$$
= \frac {1}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {x} f (\zeta) (x - \zeta) ^ {2} d \zeta .
$$

【4085】 $\int_{0}^{1}\mathrm{d}x\int_{0}^{1}\mathrm{d}y\int_{0}^{x - y}f(z)\mathrm{d}z.$

解化为先对 $y$ 积分，再对 $x, z$ 积分，可将原积分表示成如下两部分：

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int_ {0} ^ {1} \mathrm {d} z \left[ \int_ {\tau} ^ {1} \mathrm {d} x \int_ {0} ^ {1} f (z) \mathrm {d} y + \int_ {0} ^ {\tau} \mathrm {d} x \int_ {z - \tau} ^ {1} f (z) \mathrm {d} y \right] = \int_ {0} ^ {1} \mathrm {d} z \int_ {z} ^ {1} f (z) \mathrm {d} x + \int_ {0} ^ {1} \mathrm {d} z \int_ {0} ^ {z} f (z) (1 - z + x) \mathrm {d} x \\ = \int_ {0} ^ {1} f (z) (1 - z) d z + \int_ {0} ^ {1} f (z) (1 - z) z d z + \frac {1}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {1} f (z) z ^ {2} d z \\ = \int_ {0} ^ {1} f (z) \left(1 - \frac {z ^ {2}}{2}\right) d z = \frac {1}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {1} f (z) \left(2 - z ^ {2}\right) d z; \\ \int_ {1} ^ {2} \mathrm {d} z \int_ {z - 1} ^ {1} \mathrm {d} x \int_ {z - x} ^ {1} f (z) \mathrm {d} y = \int_ {1} ^ {2} \mathrm {d} z \int_ {z - 1} ^ {1} f (z) (1 - z + x) \mathrm {d} x = \int_ {1} ^ {2} \left[ f (z) (1 - z) x + \frac {1}{2} f (z) x ^ {2} \right] \Bigg | _ {z - 1} ^ {1} \mathrm {d} z \\ = \int_ {1} ^ {2} f (z) \left[ 1 - z + (z - 1) ^ {2} + \frac {1}{2} - \frac {1}{2} (z - 1) ^ {2} \right] d z = \frac {1}{2} \int_ {1} ^ {2} f (z) (z - 2) ^ {2} d z, \\ \end{array}
$$

于是， $\int_{0}^{1}\mathrm{d}x\int_{0}^{1}\mathrm{d}y\int_{0}^{1 + y}f(z)\mathrm{d}z = \frac{1}{2}\int_{0}^{1}f(z)(2 - z^2)\mathrm{d}z + \frac{1}{2}\int_{1}^{2}f(z)(2 - z)^2\mathrm{d}z.$

【4086】设 $f(x,y,z) = F_{xyz}^{\prime \prime}(x,y,z)$ ，且 $a,b,c,A,B,C$ 为常数，求

$$
\int_ {a} ^ {A} \mathrm {d} x \int_ {b} ^ {B} \mathrm {d} y \int_ {c} ^ {C} f (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} z.
$$

解 $\int_{a}^{A}\mathrm{d}x\int_{b}^{B}\mathrm{d}y\int_{c}^{C}f(x,y,z)\mathrm{d}z = \int_{a}^{A}\mathrm{d}x\int_{b}^{B}\left[F^{\prime \prime}_{xy}(x,y,C) - F^{\prime \prime}_{xy}(x,y,c)\right]\mathrm{d}y$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \int_ {a} ^ {A} \left[ F _ {x} ^ {\prime} (x, B, C) - F _ {r} ^ {\prime} (x, b, C) - F _ {x} ^ {\prime} (x, B, c) + F _ {x} ^ {\prime} (x, b, c) \right] d x \\ = F (A, B, C) - F (a, B, C) - F (A, b, C) + F (a, b, C) - F (A, B, c) + F (a, B, c) + F (A, b, c) - F (a, b, c). \\ \end{array}
$$

变换为球坐标，计算积分：

【4087】 $\iiint_{V} \sqrt{x^2 + y^2 + z^2} \, \mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y \, \mathrm{d}z$ ，其中 $V$ 是曲面 $x^2 + y^2 + z^2 = z$ 所围的区域。

提示 注意积分域 $V$ 为 $0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant 2\pi, 0 \leqslant \psi \leqslant \frac{\pi}{2}, 0 \leqslant r \leqslant \sin \psi$ ，且 $|I| = r^2 \cos \psi$ .

解令 $r = r\cos \varphi \cos \psi ,y = r\sin \varphi \cos \psi ,z = r\sin \psi$ ，则曲面 $x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2} = z$ 化为 $r = \sin \psi .$ 从而，

$$
V: 0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant 2 \pi , 0 \leqslant \psi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, 0 \leqslant r \leqslant \sin \psi , | I | = r ^ {2} \cos \psi .
$$

于是，

$$
\iiint_ {V} \sqrt {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} + z ^ {2}} d x d y d z = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \psi \int_ {0} ^ {\sin \psi} r \cdot r ^ {2} \cos \psi d r = \frac {1}{4} \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \sin^ {1} \psi \cos \psi d \psi = \frac {\pi}{1 0}.
$$

【4088】 $\int_{1}^{1}\mathrm{d}x\int_{1}^{\sqrt{1 - r^2}}\mathrm{d}y\int_{\sqrt{x^2 + y^2}}^{\sqrt{2r^2 + y^2}}z^2\mathrm{d}z.$

提示 注意积分域 $V$ 为 $0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac{\pi}{2}, \frac{\pi}{4} \leqslant \psi \leqslant \frac{\pi}{2}, 0 \leqslant r \leqslant \sqrt{2}$ .

解变换为球坐标，积分域 $V$ 为

$$
0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, \frac {\pi}{4} \leqslant \psi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, 0 \leqslant r \leqslant \sqrt {2}.
$$

于是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int_ {0} ^ {1} d x \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt {1 - r ^ {2}}} d y \int_ {\sqrt {x ^ {2} - y ^ {2}}} ^ {\sqrt {2 - r ^ {2}} z ^ {2}} z ^ {2} d z = \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {\frac {\pi}{4}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \psi \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt {2}} r ^ {2} \cos \psi \cdot r ^ {2} \sin^ {2} \psi d r = \frac {1}{5} 4 \sqrt {2} \cdot \frac {\pi}{2} \int_ {\frac {\pi}{4}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos \psi \sin^ {2} \psi d \psi \\ = \frac {\pi}{5} 2 \sqrt {2} \cdot \frac {1}{3} \sin^ {3} \psi \left| _ {\frac {\pi}{4}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} = \frac {\pi}{1 5} (2 \sqrt {2} - 1) \right. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4089】在积分中变换为球坐标：

$$
\iiint_ {V} f \left(\sqrt {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} + z ^ {2}}\right) d x d y d z,
$$

其中 $V$ 是曲面 $z = x^{2} + y^{2},x = y,x = 1,y = 0,z = 0$ 所围的区域

解引用球坐标，由 $x = y$ ， $x = 1$ ， $y = 0$ 知： $0\leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac{\pi}{4}$

（图8.58）

又从原点引半射线，由曲面 $z = x^{2} + y^{2}$ 穿进，平面 $x = 1$ 穿出，于是，得 $r$ 的下限为 $r = \frac{\sin\psi}{\cos^2\psi}, r$ 的上限为 $r = \frac{1}{\cos\varphi\cos\psi}$ . 而 $\psi$ 的变化域由 $z = 0$ 到 $z = x^{2} + y^{2}, x = 1$ 所决定，即

$$
0 \leqslant \psi \leqslant \arctan \frac {1}{\cos \varphi}.
$$

于是，

![](images/97492d9512f64f63fb42e072f09e140dc8171c83ceb5e690af29b3e00c020f84.jpg)  
图8.58

$$
\iiint_ {V} f \left(\sqrt {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} + z ^ {2}}\right) d x d y d z = \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\arctan \frac {1}{\cos \varphi}} \cos \psi d \psi \int_ {\frac {\sin \psi}{\cos^ {2} \psi}} ^ {\frac {1}{\cos \varphi \cos \psi}} r ^ {2} f (r) d r.
$$

\*）因为 $x = 1$ 对应 $r = \frac{1}{\cos\varphi\cos\psi},z = x^2 +y^2$ 对应 $r = \frac{\sin\psi}{\cos^2\psi}$ 故 $\frac{1}{\cos\varphi\cos\psi} = \frac{\sin\psi}{\cos^2\psi}$ 即 $\psi = \arctan \frac{1}{\cos\varphi}$

【4090】进行适当的变量代换，计算三重积分

$$
\iiint_ {S} \sqrt {1 - \frac {x ^ {2}}{a ^ {2}} - \frac {y ^ {2}}{b ^ {2}} - \frac {z ^ {2}}{c ^ {2}}} d x d y d z,
$$

其中 $V$ 为椭球 $\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2} +\frac{z^2}{c^2} = 1.$

解题思路 作变量代换 $x = \arccos \varphi \cos \psi, y = b r \sin \varphi \cos \psi, z = c r \sin \psi,$

则有 $|I| = abc r^2 \cos \psi$ ，且对于 $V$ 的 $\frac{1}{8}$ 部分（第一卦限）有 $0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac{\pi}{2}$ ， $0 \leqslant \psi \leqslant \frac{\pi}{2}$ ， $0 \leqslant r \leqslant 1$ .

解 作变量代换 $x = \arccos \varphi \cos \psi, y = b r \sin \varphi \cos \psi, z = c r \sin \psi,$

则有 $|I| = abc r^2 \cos \psi$ ，且对于 $V$ 的 $\frac{1}{8}$ 部分有

$$
0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, \quad 0 \leqslant \psi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, \quad 0 \leqslant r \leqslant 1.
$$

于是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} \iiint_ {V} \sqrt {1 - \frac {x ^ {2}}{a ^ {2}} - \frac {y ^ {2}}{b ^ {2}} - \frac {z ^ {2}}{c ^ {2}}} d x d y d z = 8 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \psi \int_ {0} ^ {1} a b c r ^ {2} \cos \psi \sqrt {1 - r ^ {2}} d r = 4 \pi \int_ {0} ^ {1} a b c r ^ {2} \sqrt {1 - r ^ {2}} d r \\ = 4 \pi a b c \int_ {1 1} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \sin^ {2} t \cos^ {2} t d t = \frac {\pi a b c}{2} \int_ {1 1} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} (1 - \cos 4 t) d t = \frac {\pi^ {2} a b c}{4}. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4091】变换为圆柱坐标，计算积分 $\iint_{V} (x^2 + y^2) \, \mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y \, \mathrm{d}z$ ，其中 $V$ 是曲面 $x^2 + y^2 = 2z, z = 2$ 所围的区域.

提示 注意积分域 $V$ 为 $0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant 2\pi, 0 \leqslant r \leqslant 2, \frac{r^2}{2} \leqslant z \leqslant 2$ ，且 $|I| = r$ 。

解 令 $x = r\cos \varphi, y = r\sin \varphi, z = z$ ，则 $x^2 + y^2 = 2z$ 化为 $r^2 = 2z$ 。积分域

$$
V: 0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant 2 \pi , 0 \leqslant r \leqslant 2, \frac {r ^ {2}}{2} \leqslant z \leqslant 2. \quad | I | = r.
$$

于是，

【4092】 计算积分 $\iiint_{V} x^{2} \, \mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y \, \mathrm{d}z$

其中 $V$ 是曲面 $z = ay^{2}, z = by^{2}, y > 0 (0 < a < b), z = \alpha x, z = \beta x (0 < \alpha < \beta), x = h (h > 0)$ 所围的区域.

解题思路 作变量代换 $\frac{z}{y^2} = u, \frac{z}{x} = v, z = w$ ，则有 $x = \frac{w}{v}, y = \sqrt{\frac{w}{u}}, z = w$ 及 $|I| = \frac{w\sqrt{w}}{2u\sqrt{uv^2}}$ ，且区域 $V$ 为 $a \leqslant u \leqslant b, \alpha \leqslant v \leqslant \beta, 0 \leqslant w \leqslant h$ ，且 $|I| = \frac{\omega\sqrt{\omega}}{2u\sqrt{uv^2}}$ .

解 作变换 $\frac{z}{y^2} = u, \frac{z}{x} = v, z = w$ ，则 $x = \frac{w}{v}, y = \sqrt{\frac{w}{u}}, z = w.$ 从而，积分域变为

$$
V: a \leqslant u \leqslant b, \alpha \leqslant v \leqslant \beta , 0 \leqslant w \leqslant h,
$$

且雅可比行列式

$$
I = \left| \begin{array}{c c c} 0 & - \frac {w}{v ^ {2}} & \frac {1}{v} \\ \frac {- \sqrt {w}}{2 u \sqrt {u}} & 0 & \frac {1}{2 \sqrt {u w}} \\ 0 & 0 & 1 \end{array} \right| = \frac {- w \sqrt {w}}{2 u \sqrt {u} v ^ {2}}.
$$

于是， $\iiint_{V} x^{2} \mathrm{d}x \mathrm{d}y \mathrm{d}z = \int_{0}^{h} w^{\frac{7}{2}} \mathrm{d}w \int_{a}^{\beta} \frac{1}{v^{4}} \mathrm{d}v \int_{a}^{b} \frac{1}{2u\sqrt{u}} \mathrm{d}u = \frac{2}{27}\left(\frac{1}{\alpha^{3}} - \frac{1}{\beta^{3}}\right)\left(\frac{1}{\sqrt{a}} - \frac{1}{\sqrt{b}}\right)h^{4}\sqrt{h}.$

【4093】求积分 $\iiint_{V} xyz \, \mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y \, \mathrm{d}z,$

其中 $V$ 位于 $x > 0, y > 0, z > 0$ 这一卦限内且由下列曲面围成：

$$
z = \frac {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}}{m}, z = \frac {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}}{n}, x y = a ^ {2}, x y = b ^ {2}, y = \alpha x, y = \beta x (0 <   a <   b, 0 <   \alpha <   \beta , 0 <   m <   n).
$$

解题思路 作变量代换 $\frac{z}{x^2 + y^2} = u, xy = v, \frac{y}{x} = w$ ，则有 $x = \sqrt{\frac{v}{w}}, y = \sqrt{vw}, z = uv(w + \frac{1}{w})$ 及 $|I| = \frac{v}{2w}\left(w + \frac{1}{w}\right)$ ，且区域 $V$ 变为 $\frac{1}{n} \leqslant u \leqslant \frac{1}{m}, a^2 \leqslant v \leqslant b^2, \alpha \leqslant w \leqslant \beta.$

解 作变换 $\frac{z}{x^2 + y^2} = u, xy = v, \frac{y}{x} = w$ ，则 $x = \sqrt{\frac{v}{w}}, y = \sqrt{vw}, z = uv\left(w + \frac{1}{w}\right)$ ，且

$$
I = \left| \begin{array}{c c c} 0 & \frac {1}{2 \sqrt {v w}} & - \frac {\sqrt {v}}{2 w \sqrt {w}} \\ 0 & \frac {\sqrt {w}}{2 \sqrt {v}} & \frac {\sqrt {v}}{2 \sqrt {w}} \\ v \left(w + \frac {1}{w}\right) & u \left(w + \frac {1}{w}\right) & u v \left(1 - \frac {1}{w ^ {2}}\right) \end{array} \right| = \frac {v}{2 w} \left(w + \frac {1}{w}\right),
$$

$$
V: \frac {1}{n} \leqslant u \leqslant \frac {1}{m}, a ^ {2} \leqslant v \leqslant b ^ {2}, \alpha \leqslant w \leqslant \beta .
$$

于是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} \iiint_ {V} x y z \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y \mathrm {d} z = \int_ {\frac {1}{n}} ^ {\frac {1}{m}} \frac {u}{2} \mathrm {d} u \int_ {a ^ {2}} ^ {b ^ {2}} v ^ {3} \mathrm {d} v \int_ {a} ^ {\beta} \left(w + \frac {1}{w ^ {3}} + \frac {2}{w}\right) \mathrm {d} w \\ = \frac {1}{3 2} \left(\frac {1}{m ^ {2}} - \frac {1}{n ^ {2}}\right) (b ^ {8} - a ^ {8}) \left[ (\beta^ {2} - \alpha^ {2}) \left(1 + \frac {1}{\alpha^ {2} \beta^ {2}}\right) + 4 \ln \frac {\beta}{\alpha} \right]. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4094】求函数 $f(x, y, z) = x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2}$ 在区域 $x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2} \leqslant x + y + z$ 内的平均值.

解 区域 $x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2} \leqslant x + y + z$ 即

$$
\left(x - \frac {1}{2}\right) ^ {2} + \left(y - \frac {1}{2}\right) ^ {2} + \left(z - \frac {1}{2}\right) ^ {2} \leqslant \frac {3}{4},
$$

其体积 $V = \frac{4}{3}\pi \left(\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\right)^{3} = \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\pi .$ 作变换： $x = r\cos \varphi \cos \psi +\frac{1}{2},y = r\sin \varphi \cos \psi +\frac{1}{2},z = \frac{1}{2} +r\sin \psi ,$

则有 $f_{\text{平均}} = \frac{1}{V} \iiint_{V} (x^2 + y^2 + z^2) \, \mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y \, \mathrm{d}z$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {1}{V} \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {- \frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \psi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\sqrt {3}}{2}} r ^ {2} \cos \psi \left(\frac {3}{4} + r ^ {2} + r \sin \psi + r \cos \varphi \cos \psi + r \sin \varphi \cos \psi\right) d r \\ = \frac {1}{V} \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {- \frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \psi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\sqrt {3}}{2}} r ^ {2} \cos \psi \left(\frac {3}{4} + r ^ {2}\right) d r = \frac {1}{V} \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {- \frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \frac {3 \sqrt {3}}{2 0} \cos \psi d \psi = \frac {1}{V} \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} \frac {3 \sqrt {3}}{2 0} d \varphi \\ = \frac {1}{V} \cdot \frac {3 \sqrt {3}}{5} \pi = \frac {2}{\sqrt {3} \pi} \cdot \frac {3 \sqrt {3} \pi}{5} = \frac {6}{5}. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4095】求函数 $f(x, y, z) = \mathrm{e}^{\sqrt{\frac{x^2}{a^2} + \frac{y^2}{b^2} + \frac{z^2}{c^2}}}$ 在区域 $\frac{x^2}{a^2} + \frac{y^2}{b^2} + \frac{z^2}{c^2} \leq 1$ 内的平均值.

解 由于区域 $V: \frac{x^2}{a^2} + \frac{y^2}{b^2} + \frac{z^2}{c^2} \leqslant 1$ 为椭球，其体积等于 $\frac{4}{3}\pi abc$ ，故平均值为

$$
f _ {\text {平 均}} = \frac {3}{4 \pi a b c} \iiint_ {V} \mathrm {e} \sqrt {\frac {x ^ {2}}{a ^ {2}} + \frac {y ^ {2}}{b ^ {2}} + \frac {z ^ {2}}{c ^ {2}}} \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y \mathrm {d} z.
$$

若作变换 $x = \arccos \varphi \cos \psi, y = brs\sin \varphi \cos \psi, z = cr\sin \psi$ ，并利用对称性，则有

$$
f _ {\text {平 均}} = \frac {3}{4 \pi a b c} \cdot 8 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \mathrm {d} \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \mathrm {d} \psi \int_ {0} ^ {1} a b c e ^ {r} r ^ {2} \cos \psi \mathrm {d} r = 3 \left(\int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos \psi \mathrm {d} \psi\right) \left(\int_ {0} ^ {1} r ^ {2} e ^ {r} \mathrm {d} r\right) = 3 (\mathrm {e} - 2).
$$

【4096】 利用中值定理，估计积分

$$
u = \iiint_ {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} + z ^ {2} \leqslant R ^ {2}} \frac {\mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y \mathrm {d} z}{\sqrt {(x - a) ^ {2} + (y - b) ^ {2} + (z - c) ^ {2}}},
$$

其中 $a^2 + b^2 + c^2 > R^2$ .

解 由积分中值定理，有

$$
u = \iiint_ {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} + z ^ {2} \leqslant R ^ {2}} \frac {\mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y \mathrm {d} z}{\sqrt {(x - a) ^ {2} + (y - b) ^ {2} + (z - c) ^ {2}}} = \frac {1}{\sqrt {(\xi - a) ^ {2} + (\eta - b) ^ {2} + (\zeta - c) ^ {2}}} \cdot \frac {4}{3} \pi R ^ {3}, \tag {1}
$$

其中 $\xi^2 +\eta^2 +\zeta^2\leqslant R^2$ .由于函数

$$
\sqrt {(x - a) ^ {2} + (y - b) ^ {2} + (z - c) ^ {2}}
$$

代表点 $(x, y, z)$ 与点 $(a, b, c)$ 之间的距离，显然在区域 $x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2} \leqslant R^{2}$ 中此距离的最小值是 $\sqrt{a^{2} + b^{2} + c^{2}} - R$ 最大值是 $\sqrt{a^{2} + b^{2} + c^{2}} + R$ ，并且只在一个点达到最小值，也只在一个点达到最大值. 因此，函数

$$
\frac {1}{\sqrt {(x - a) ^ {2} + (y - b) ^ {2} + (z - c) ^ {2}}}
$$

在区域 $x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2}\leqslant R^{2}$ 中的最大值是 $\frac{1}{\sqrt{a^2 + b^2 + c^2} - R}$ ，最小值是 $\frac{1}{\sqrt{a^2 + b^2 + c^2} + R}$ 并且只在一个点达到最大值，也只在一个点达到最小值.我们证明(1)式中的中值不可能是函数的最大值，也不可能是函数的最小值.事实上，例如，若是最大值，即

则由（1）式知

$$
\frac {1}{\sqrt {(\xi - a) ^ {2} + (\eta - b) ^ {2} + (\zeta - c) ^ {2}}} = \frac {1}{\sqrt {a ^ {2} + b ^ {2} + c ^ {2}} - R},
$$

$$
\iiint_ {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} + z ^ {2} \leqslant R ^ {2}} f (x, y, z) d x d y d z = 0, \tag {2}
$$

其中

$$
f (x, y, z) = \frac {1}{\sqrt {a ^ {2} + b ^ {2} + c ^ {2}} - R} - \frac {1}{\sqrt {(x - a) ^ {2} + (y - b) ^ {2} + (z - c) ^ {2}}}.
$$

显然，在区域 $x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2}\leqslant R^{2}$ 上 $f(x,y,z)\geqslant 0$ 且 $f(x,y,z)$ 为连续函数.于是，由(2)式知在区域 $x^{2} + y^{2}+$ $z^2\leqslant R^2$ 上必有 $f(x,y,z)\equiv 0$ ，这显然是不可能的.因此，

即 $\sqrt{a^2 + b^2 + c^2} - R < \sqrt{(\xi - a)^2 + (\eta - b)^2 + (\zeta - c)^2} < \sqrt{a^2 + b^2 + c^2} + R,$

故 $\sqrt{(\xi - a)^2 + (\eta - b)^2 + (\zeta - c)^2} = \sqrt{a^2 + b^2 + c^2} +\theta R,$

其中 $|\theta| < 1$ . 于是，由(1)式得 $u = \frac{4\pi}{3} \frac{R^3}{\sqrt{a^2 + b^2 + c^2} + \theta R}$ .

【4097】证明：若函数 $f(x,y,z)$ 在区域 $V$ 内是连续的，且对于任何区域 $\omega \subset V$ 有

$$
\iiint_ {\omega} f (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y \mathrm {d} z = 0,
$$

则当 $(x,y,z)\in V$ 时， $f(x,y,z)\equiv 0.$

提示 用反证法及积分中值定理，

证 用反证法. 若当 $(x, y, z) \in V$ 时， $f(x, y, z) \neq 0$ . 不失一般性，设对于 $V$ 的某内点 $(x_0, y_0, z_0)$ ，有 $f(x_0, y_0, z_0) > 0$ ，则由于 $f(x, y, z)$ 的连续性，故存在点 $(x_0, y_0, z_0)$ 的某个闭邻域 $\omega' \subset V$ ，使当 $(x, y, z) \in \omega'$ 时， $f(x, y, z) > 0$ . 这样一来，利用中值定理，即有

$$
\iiint_ {\omega} f (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y \mathrm {d} z = f (\xi , \eta , \zeta) \cdot V _ {\omega^ {\prime}} > 0,
$$

其中 $(\xi, \eta, \zeta) \in \omega' \subset V.$ 这与假设 $\iiint_{\omega} f(x, y, z) \mathrm{d}x \mathrm{d}y \mathrm{d}z \equiv 0$ 矛盾. 因此，当 $(x, y, z) \in V$ 时， $f(x, y, z) \equiv 0$

【4098】求 $F^{\prime}(t)$ ，设：

(1) $F(t) = \iiint_{\substack{r^2 - y^2 + z^2 \leqslant t^2}} f(x^2 + y^2 + z^2) \, \mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y \, \mathrm{d}z$ ，其中 $f$ 为可微函数；  
(2） $F(t) = \iiint_{\substack{0\leqslant x\leqslant t\\ 0\leqslant y\leqslant t\\ 0\leqslant z\leqslant t}}f(xyz)\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y\mathrm{d}z$ ，其中 $f$ 为可微函数.

提示 (1) 作球坐标变换；(2) 作变量代换 $x = t\xi, y = t\eta, z = t\zeta$

解（1）作球坐标变换得

$$
F (t) = \iiint_ {r ^ {2} \cdot y ^ {2} \cdot z ^ {2} \leqslant t ^ {2}} f \left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} + z ^ {2}\right) d x d y d z = 8 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos \psi d \psi \int_ {0} ^ {t} f \left(r ^ {2}\right) r ^ {2} d r = 4 \pi \int_ {0} ^ {t} f \left(r ^ {2}\right) r ^ {2} d r,
$$

于是， $F^{\prime}(t) = 4\pi t^{2}f(t^{2}).$

(2) 作变换 $x = t\xi, y = t\eta, z = t\zeta$ 得

$$
F (t) = \iiint_ {0 \leqslant x \leqslant t} f (x y z) \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y \mathrm {d} z = \iiint_ {0 \leqslant x \leqslant 1} f (t ^ {3} \xi \eta \zeta) t ^ {3} \mathrm {d} \xi \mathrm {d} \eta \mathrm {d} \zeta ,
$$

于是，

$$
F ^ {\prime} (t) = 3 \iiint_ {0 \leqslant \xi \leqslant 1} t ^ {2} f (t ^ {3} \xi \eta \zeta) d \xi d \eta d \zeta + 3 \iiint_ {0 \leqslant \xi \leqslant 1} f ^ {\prime} (t ^ {3} \xi \eta \zeta) t ^ {5} \xi \eta \zeta d \xi d \eta d \zeta = \frac {3}{t} \left[ F (t) + \iiint_ {0 \leqslant x \leqslant t} f ^ {\prime} (x y z) x y z d x d y d z \right].
$$

【4099】求 $\iiint_{x^2 + y^2 + z^2 \leqslant 1} x^m y^n z^p \, \mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y \, \mathrm{d}z$ ，其中 $m, n, p$ 为非负整数.

解 分两种情况：

（1）设 $m, n, p$ 中至少有一个是奇数。例如，设 $p$ 为奇数。于是，

$$
I = \iiint_ {r ^ {2} \cdot y ^ {2} \cdot z ^ {2} \leqslant 1} x ^ {m} y ^ {n} z ^ {p} d x d y d z = \iiint_ {r ^ {2} \cdot y ^ {2} + z ^ {2} \leqslant 1} x ^ {m} y ^ {n} z ^ {p} d x d y d z + \iiint_ {r ^ {2} + y ^ {2} + z ^ {2} \leqslant 1} x ^ {m} y ^ {n} z ^ {p} d x d y d z = I _ {1} + I _ {2}.
$$

今在积分 $I_{2}$ 中作变量代换 $x = u, y = v, z = -w$ ，则 $\frac{D(x, y, z)}{D(u, v, w)} = -1$ ，从而，注意到 $p$ 为奇数，可知

$$
I _ {2} = - \iiint_ {\substack {u ^ {2} + v ^ {2} + w ^ {2} \leqslant 1 \\ w \geqslant 0}} u ^ {m} v ^ {n} w ^ {p} \mathrm {d} u \mathrm {d} v \mathrm {d} w = - I _ {1},
$$

于是， $I = I_{1} - I_{1} = 0$

（2）设 $m, n, p$ 均为偶数. 此时被积函数 $x^{m}y^{n}z^{p}$ 关于三个坐标平面皆对称. 于是，

$$
I = \iiint_ {r ^ {2} - y ^ {2} - z ^ {2} \leqslant 1} x ^ {m} y ^ {n} z ^ {p} d x d y d z = 8 \iiint_ {\substack {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} - z ^ {2} \leqslant 1 \\ x \geqslant 0, y \geqslant 0, z \geqslant 0}} x ^ {m} y ^ {n} z ^ {p} d x d y d z.
$$

引用球坐标， $x = r\cos \varphi \cos \psi ,y = r\sin \varphi \cos \psi ,z = r\sin \psi$ ，得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \iiint_ { \begin{array}{l} r ^ {2} - y ^ {2} + z ^ {2} \leq 1 \\ r \geqslant 0, y \geqslant 0, z \geqslant 0 \end{array} } x ^ {m} y ^ {n} z ^ {p} d x d y d z = \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {m} \varphi \sin^ {n} \varphi d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {m + n + 1} \psi \sin^ {p} \psi d \psi \int_ {0} ^ {1} r ^ {m + n + p + 2} d r \\ = \frac {1}{m + n + p + 3} \cdot \frac {1}{2} \cdot \frac {\Gamma (\frac {m + 1}{2}) \Gamma (\frac {n + 1}{2})}{\Gamma (\frac {m + n + 2}{2})} \cdot \frac {1}{2} \cdot \frac {\Gamma (\frac {m + n + 2}{2}) \Gamma (\frac {p + 1}{2}) ^ {*}}{\Gamma (\frac {m + n + p + 3}{2})} \\ = \frac {1}{4 (m + n + p + 3)} \cdot \frac {\Gamma (\frac {m + 1}{2}) \Gamma (\frac {n + 1}{2}) \Gamma (\frac {p + 1}{2})}{\Gamma (\frac {m + n + p + 3}{2})} \\ \end{array}
$$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {1}{4 (m + n + p + 3)} \cdot \frac {\frac {(m - 1) ! !}{2 ^ {\frac {m}{2}}} \cdot \frac {(n - 1) ! !}{2 ^ {\frac {n}{2}}} \cdot \frac {(p - 1) ! !}{2 ^ {\frac {p}{2}}} \cdot \pi \sqrt {\pi}}{\frac {(m + n + p + 1) ! !}{2 ^ {\frac {m - n - p - 2}{2}}} \cdot \sqrt {\pi}} \\ = \frac {\pi}{2 (m + n + p + 3)} \cdot \frac {(m - 1) ! ! (n - 1) ! ! (p - 1) ! !}{(m + n + p + 1) ! !}, \\ \end{array}
$$

故 $I = \iiint_{x^2 + y^2 - z^2 \leqslant 1} x^m y^n z^p \, \mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y \, \mathrm{d}z = \frac{4\pi}{m + n + p + 3} \cdot \frac{(m - 1)!! (n - 1)!! (p - 1)!!}{(m + n + p + 1)!!}$ .

\*) 利用3856题的结果.

【4100】令 $x + y + z = \xi, y + z = \xi \eta, z = \xi \eta \zeta$ ，计算狄利克雷积分

$$
\iiint_ {V} x ^ {p} y ^ {q} z ^ {r} (1 - x - y - z) ^ {s} \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y \mathrm {d} z \quad (p > 0, q > 0, r > 0, s > 0),
$$

其中 $V$ 是平面 $x + y + z = 1, x = 0, y = 0, z = 0$ 所围的区域.

解 由假设知 $x = \xi (1 - \eta),\quad y = \xi \eta (1 - \zeta),\quad z = \xi \eta \zeta .$

在此变换下可求得 $|I| = \xi^2\eta$ ，并且积分域 $V$ 变为：

$$
0 <   \xi <   1, 0 <   \eta <   1, 0 <   \zeta <   1.
$$

于是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} \iiint_ {V} x ^ {p} y ^ {q} z ^ {r} (1 - x - y - z) ^ {3} \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y \mathrm {d} z = \int_ {0} ^ {1} \xi^ {p - q + r + 2} (1 - \xi) ^ {3} \mathrm {d} \xi \int_ {0} ^ {1} \eta^ {q - r - 1} (1 - \eta) ^ {p} \mathrm {d} \eta \int_ {0} ^ {1} \zeta^ {r} (1 - \zeta) ^ {q} \mathrm {d} \zeta \\ = B (p + q + r + 3, s + 1) B (q + r + 2, p + 1) B (r + 1, q + 1) \\ = \frac {\Gamma (p + q + r + 3) \Gamma (s + 1) \Gamma (q + r + 2) \Gamma (p + 1) \Gamma (r + 1) \Gamma (q + 1)}{\Gamma (p + q + r + s + 4) \Gamma (p + q + r + 3) \Gamma (q + r + 2)} \\ = \frac {\Gamma (p + 1) \Gamma (q + 1) \Gamma (s + 1) \Gamma (r + 1)}{\Gamma (p + q + r + s + 4)}. \\ \end{array}
$$

# § 7. 利用三重积分计算体积

区域的体积 $V$ 可表示为以下公式： $V = \iiint_{V} \mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y \, \mathrm{d}z.$

求以下列曲面为界的物体的体积：

【4101】 $z = x^{2} + y^{2}, z = 2x^{2} + 2y^{2}, y = x, y = x^{2}$

解区域V为 $0\leqslant x\leqslant 1,x^{2}\leqslant y\leqslant x,x^{2} + y^{2}\leqslant z\leqslant 2x^{2} + 2y^{2},$

故体积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = \int_ {0} ^ {1} d x \int_ {x ^ {2}} ^ {x} d y \int_ {x ^ {2} \cdot y ^ {2}} ^ {2 x ^ {2} \cdot 2 y ^ {2}} d z = \int_ {0} ^ {1} d x \int_ {x ^ {2}} ^ {x} (x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}) d y = \int_ {0} ^ {1} \left(\frac {4}{3} x ^ {3} - x ^ {4} - \frac {1}{3} x ^ {6}\right) d x \\ = \left(\frac {1}{3} x ^ {4} - \frac {1}{5} x ^ {5} - \frac {1}{2 1} x ^ {7}\right) \Big | _ {0} ^ {1} = \frac {3}{3 5}. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4102】 $z = x + y, z = xy, x + y = 1, x = 0, y = 0.$

解区域V为 $0\leqslant x\leqslant 1,0\leqslant y\leqslant 1 - x,xy\leqslant z\leqslant x + y^{*},$

故体积为 $V = \int_{0}^{1}\mathrm{d}x\int_{0}^{1 - x}\mathrm{d}y\int_{x,y}^{x + y}\mathrm{d}z = \int_{0}^{1}\mathrm{d}x\int_{0}^{1 - x}(x + y - xy)\mathrm{d}y = \int_{0}^{1}\left[x(1 - x) + \frac{(1 - x)^{3}}{2}\right]\mathrm{d}x = \frac{7}{24}.$

\*) 因为 $0 \leqslant y \leqslant 1$ ，故有 $xy \leqslant z \leqslant x + y$ .

【4103】 $x^{2} + z^{2} = a^{2}, x + y = \pm a, x - y = \pm a.$

解 $V = 8\int_{0}^{a}\mathrm{d}x\int_{0}^{a - x}\mathrm{d}y\int_{0}^{\sqrt{a^2 - x^2}}\mathrm{d}z = 8\int_{0}^{a}(a - x)\sqrt{a^2 - x^2}\mathrm{d}x$

$$
= 8 a \left[ \frac {x}{2} \sqrt {a ^ {2} - x ^ {2}} + \frac {a ^ {2}}{2} \arcsin \frac {x}{a} \right] \left| _ {0} ^ {a} + \frac {8}{3} (a ^ {2} - x ^ {2}) ^ {\frac {3}{2}} \right| _ {0} ^ {a} = \frac {2 a ^ {3}}{3} (3 \pi - 4).
$$

【4104】 $a z = x^{2} + y^{2},z = \sqrt{x^{2} + y^{2}} (a > 0).$

解 对区域 $V$ 在 $Oxy$ 平面上的投影作极坐标变换

$$
x = r \cos \varphi , \quad y = r \sin \varphi ,
$$

则区域 $V$ 为

且有 $|I| = r.$ 于是，体积为

$$
V = \iint_ {r ^ {2} + y ^ {2} \leqslant a ^ {2}} d x d y \int_ {\frac {r ^ {2} + y ^ {2}}{a}} ^ {\sqrt {r ^ {2} - y ^ {2}}} d z = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {a} r d r \int_ {\frac {r ^ {2}}{a}} ^ {r} d z = 2 \pi \int_ {0} ^ {a} \left(r ^ {2} - \frac {r ^ {3}}{a}\right) d r = \frac {\pi a ^ {3}}{6}.
$$

【4105】 $az = a^2 - x^2 - y^2, z = a - x - y, x = 0, y = 0, z = 0 (a > 0)$

解由 $a z = a^{2} - x^{2} - y^{2},x = 0,y = 0,z = 0$ 为界的物体体积为

$$
V _ {1} = \iint_ {\substack {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} \leqslant a ^ {2} \\ x \geqslant 0, y \geqslant 0}} \left(\int_ {0} ^ {\frac {a ^ {2} - x ^ {2} - y ^ {2}}{a}} d z\right) d x d y = \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {a} \frac {a ^ {2} - r ^ {2}}{a} r d r = \frac {\pi a ^ {3}}{8}.
$$

由 $z = a - x - y, x = 0, y = 0, z = 0$ 为界的物体体积为

$$
V _ {2} = \iiint_ {\substack {x + y + z \leqslant a \\ x \geqslant 0, y \geqslant 0, z \geqslant 0}} d x d y d z = \int_ {0} ^ {a} d x \int_ {0} ^ {a - x} d y \int_ {0} ^ {a} \int_ {0} ^ {x} d z = \frac {a ^ {3}}{6}.
$$

于是，所求的体积为 $V = V_{1} - V_{2} = \frac{a^{3}}{24} (3\pi - 4)$

【4106】 $z = 6 - x^{2} - y^{2}, z = \sqrt{x^{2} + y^{2}}.$

提示 利用圆柱坐标，则区域 $V$ 为 $0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant 2\pi, 0 \leqslant r \leqslant 2, r \leqslant z \leqslant 6 - r^2$

解引用圆柱坐标，则区域 $V$ 为 $0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant 2\pi, 0 \leqslant r \leqslant 2, r \leqslant z \leqslant 6 - r^2.$

于是，体积为 $V = \int_{0}^{2\pi}\mathrm{d}\varphi \int_{0}^{2}r\mathrm{d}r\int_{r}^{6 - r^2}\mathrm{d}z = 2\pi \int_{0}^{2}(6r - r^3 -r^2)\mathrm{d}r = \frac{32\pi}{3}.$

# 变换为球坐标或圆柱坐标，计算以下曲面所围的体积：

【4107】 $x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2} = 2az, x^{2} + y^{2} \leqslant z^{2}$

解题思路 变换为圆柱坐标，则有

$$
r ^ {2} + z ^ {2} = 2 a z \quad \text {及} \quad r ^ {2} \leqslant z ^ {2},
$$

且区域 $V$ 为

这里要注意，球面方程应该是 $z = a \pm \sqrt{a^2 - r^2}$ ，但因体积 $V$ 的一部分为球 $x^2 + y^2 + z^2 = 2az$ 的上半部，故取 $z = a + \sqrt{a^2 - r^2}$ 。

解变换为圆柱坐标，则有 $r^2 +z^2 = 2az$ 及 $r^2\leqslant z^2$

因而区域 $V$ 为

于是，体积为

$$
V = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {a} r d r \int_ {r} ^ {a + \sqrt {a ^ {2} - r ^ {2}}} d z = 2 \pi \int_ {0} ^ {a} r (a + \sqrt {a ^ {2} - r ^ {2}} - r) d r = 2 \pi \left[ \frac {a r ^ {2}}{2} - \frac {1}{3} (a ^ {2} - r ^ {2}) ^ {\frac {3}{2}} - \frac {r ^ {3}}{3} \right] \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {a} = \pi a ^ {3}.
$$

\*) 球面的方程应该是 $z = a \pm \sqrt{a^2 - r^2}$ , 但因体积 $V$ 的一部分为球 $x^2 + y^2 + z^2 = 2az$ 的上半部, 故取 $z = a + \sqrt{a^2 - r^2}$ .

【4108】 $(x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2})^{2} = a^{2}(x^{2} + y^{2} - z^{2}).$

提示 变换为球坐标，则区域 $V$ 的 $\frac{1}{8}$ 部分（第一卦限内）为

$$
0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, 0 \leqslant \psi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{4}, 0 \leqslant r \leqslant a \sqrt {\cos 2 \psi}.
$$

解变换为球坐标，则区域 $V$ 的 $\frac{1}{8}$ 部分为

$$
0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, 0 \leqslant \psi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{1}, 0 \leqslant r \leqslant a \sqrt {\cos 2 \psi}.
$$

于是，体积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = 8 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} d \psi \int_ {0} ^ {u \sqrt {\cos^ {2} \psi}} r ^ {2} \cos \psi d r = \frac {4 \pi a ^ {3}}{3} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} \cos \psi (\cos 2 \psi) ^ {\frac {3}{2}} d \psi = \frac {4 \pi a ^ {3}}{3} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} (1 - 2 \sin^ {2} \psi) ^ {\frac {3}{2}} d (\sin \psi) \\ = \frac {4 \pi a ^ {3}}{3} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {1}{2}} (1 - 2 x ^ {2}) ^ {\frac {3}{2}} d x = \frac {4 \pi a ^ {3}}{3} \cdot \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {4} t d t ^ {\cdot 1} = \frac {4 \pi a ^ {3}}{3 \sqrt {2}} \cdot \frac {3}{4} \cdot \frac {1}{2} \cdot \frac {\pi}{2} = \frac {\pi^ {2} a ^ {3}}{4 \sqrt {2}}. \\ \end{array}
$$

\*） 作代换 $\sqrt{2} x = \sin t.$

【4109】 $(x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2})^{3} = 3xyz.$

解 立体在第一，第三，第六及第八卦限内，对于这些卦限分别有：

$$
r \geqslant 0, y \geqslant 0, z \geqslant 0; \quad x \leqslant 0, y \leqslant 0, z \geqslant 0; \quad x \leqslant 0, y \geqslant 0, z \leqslant 0; \quad x \geqslant 0, y \leqslant 0, z \leqslant 0.
$$

立体在这四个卦限内的各部分，一对一对地对称于坐标轴之一。这是因为左端及右端当 $x, y, z$ 中的任何两个同时变号时等号不变。

变换为球坐标，计算得体积

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = 4 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \psi \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt [ 3 ]{3 \cos^ {2} \psi \cos \varphi \sin \varphi \sin \psi}} r ^ {2} \cos \psi d r = 4 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos \varphi \sin \varphi d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {3} \psi \sin \psi d \psi \\ = 4 \left(\frac {\sin^ {2} \varphi}{2} \left| _ {1 1} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}}\right) \left(- \frac {1}{4} \cos^ {4} \psi \right| _ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}}\right) = \frac {1}{2}. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4110】 $x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2} = a^{2}, x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2} = b^{2}, x^{2} + y^{2} = z^{2}(z \geqslant 0)(0 < a < b)$ .

提示 变换为球坐标，则区域 $V$ 为 $0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant 2\pi$ ， $\frac{\pi}{4} \leqslant \psi \leqslant \frac{\pi}{2}$ ， $a \leqslant r \leqslant b$ .

解变换为球坐标，得区域 $V$ 为 $0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant 2\pi, \frac{\pi}{4} \leqslant \psi \leqslant \frac{\pi}{2}, a \leqslant r \leqslant b.$

于是，体积为 $V = \int_{0}^{2\pi}\mathrm{d}\varphi \int_{\frac{\pi}{1}}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}\mathrm{d}\psi \int_{a}^{b}r^{2}\cos \psi \mathrm{d}r = 2\pi \left(\int_{\frac{\pi}{1}}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}\cos \psi \mathrm{d}\psi\right)\left(\int_{a}^{b}r^{2}\mathrm{d}r\right) = \frac{\pi(2 - \sqrt{2})(b^{3} - a^{3})}{3}.$

在下列各题中最好利用广义球坐标 $r, \varphi, \psi (r \geqslant 0; 0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant 2\pi; -\frac{\pi}{2} \leqslant \psi \leqslant \frac{\pi}{2})$ ，它们由以下公式引入：

$$
x = a r \cos^ {\alpha} \varphi \cos^ {\beta} \psi , \quad y = b r \sin^ {\alpha} \varphi \cos^ {\beta} \psi , \quad z = c r \sin^ {\beta} \psi \quad (a, b, c, \alpha , \beta \text {为 常 数}),
$$

并且

$$
\frac {D (x , y , z)}{D (r , \varphi , \psi)} = \alpha \beta a b c r ^ {2} \cos^ {\circ} 1 \varphi \sin^ {\circ} 1 \varphi \cos^ {2 \beta} 1 \psi \sin^ {\beta - 1} \psi .
$$

求以下列曲面为界的物体的体积：

【4111】 $\left(\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2} +\frac{z^2}{c^2}\right)^2 = \frac{x}{h}.$

解令 $x = \arccos \varphi \cos \psi$ ， $y = br\sin \varphi \cos \psi$ ， $z = cr\sin \psi$ ，则区域的 $\frac{1}{4}$ 部分（第一卦限内）为

$$
0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, 0 \leqslant \psi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, 0 \leqslant r \leqslant \sqrt [ 3 ]{\frac {a}{h} \cos \varphi \cos \psi}.
$$

于是，体积为 $V = 4\int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}\mathrm{d}\varphi \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}\mathrm{d}\psi \int_{0}^{\sqrt[3]{\frac{u}{h}\cos\varphi\cos\psi}}abcr^{2}\cos \psi \mathrm{d}r = \frac{4a^{2}bc}{3h}\left(\int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}\cos \varphi \mathrm{d}\varphi\right)\left(\int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}\cos^{2}\psi \mathrm{d}\psi\right) = \frac{\pi a^{2}bc}{3h}.$

【4112】 $\left(\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2} +\frac{z^2}{c^2}\right)^2 = \frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2}.$

解令 $x = \arccos \varphi \cos \psi$ ， $y = br\sin \varphi \cos \psi$ ， $z = cr\sin \psi$ ，并利用对称性，即得体积

$$
