\begin{array}{l} V = 8 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \psi \int_ {0} ^ {\cos \psi} a b c r ^ {2} \cos \psi d r = 8 \cdot \frac {\pi}{2} \cdot \frac {a b c}{3} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {4} \psi d \psi = \frac {4 \pi a b c}{3} \cdot \frac {3}{4} \cdot \frac {1}{2} \cdot \frac {\pi}{2} = \frac {\pi^ {2}}{4} a b c. \\ \text {【 4 1 1 3 】} \quad \frac {x ^ {2}}{a ^ {2}} + \frac {y ^ {2}}{b ^ {2}} + \frac {z ^ {2}}{c ^ {2}} = 1, \frac {x ^ {2}}{a ^ {2}} + \frac {y ^ {2}}{b ^ {2}} = \frac {z}{c}. \\ \end{array}
$$

解 令 $x = \arccos \varphi, y = b r \sin \varphi, z = z$ ，则 $r$ 满足方程 $r^4 + r^2 - 1 = 0$ . 解得 $r = \sqrt{\frac{\sqrt{5} - 1}{2}}$ . 于是，体积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt {\frac {\sqrt {5} - 1}{2}}} a b r d r \int_ {c r ^ {2}} ^ {c \sqrt {1 - r ^ {2}}} d z = 2 \pi a b c \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt {\frac {\sqrt {5} - 1}{2}}} r (\sqrt {1 - r ^ {2}} - r ^ {2}) d r \\ = 2 \pi a b c \left[ - \frac {1}{3} (1 - r ^ {2}) ^ {\frac {3}{2}} - \frac {1}{4} r ^ {4} \right] \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {\sqrt {\frac {\sqrt {5} - 1}{2}}} = \frac {5 \pi a b c (3 - \sqrt {5})}{1 2}. \\ \end{array}
$$

$$
\text {【 4 1 1 4 】} \quad \frac {x ^ {2}}{a ^ {2}} + \frac {y ^ {2}}{b ^ {2}} + \frac {z ^ {4}}{c ^ {4}} = 1.
$$

解 令 $x = \arccos \varphi, y = b r \sin \varphi, z = z$ ，则得体积

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {1} a b r d r \int_ {- c (1 - r ^ {2}) \frac {1}{4}} ^ {c (1 - r ^ {2}) \frac {1}{4}} d z = 4 \pi a b c \int_ {0} ^ {1} r (1 - r ^ {2}) ^ {\frac {1}{4}} d r = 4 \pi a b c \left[ - \frac {2}{5} (1 - r ^ {2}) ^ {\frac {5}{4}} \right] \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {1} = \frac {8}{5} \pi a b c. \\ \left(\frac {x ^ {2}}{a ^ {2}} + \frac {y ^ {2}}{b ^ {2}}\right) ^ {2} + \frac {z ^ {4}}{c ^ {4}} = 1. \tag {4115} \\ \end{array}
$$

解题思路 作变量代换 $x = \arccos \varphi \cos^{\frac{1}{2}}\psi, y = b r \sin \varphi \cos^{\frac{1}{2}}\psi, z = c r \sin^{\frac{1}{2}}\psi,$

则有 $|I| = \frac{1}{2} abcr^2\sin^{-\frac{1}{2}}\psi$ 且 $V$ 的 $\frac{1}{8}$ 部分（第一卦限内）为 $0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac{\pi}{2}, 0 \leqslant \psi \leqslant \frac{\pi}{2}, 0 \leqslant r \leqslant 1$ ，并利用3856题的结果及延拓公式.

解 令 $x = \arccos \varphi \cos^{\frac{1}{2}}\psi, y = brsin\varphi \cos^{\frac{1}{2}}\psi, z = cr\sin^{\frac{1}{2}}\psi$ ，则有 $|I| = \frac{1}{2} abcr^{2}\sin^{-\frac{1}{2}}\psi$ 且 $\frac{1}{8}$ 区域 $V$ （第一卦限内）为

$$
0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, \quad 0 \leqslant \psi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, \quad 0 \leqslant r \leqslant 1.
$$

于是，体积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = 8 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \psi \int_ {0} ^ {1} \frac {1}{2} a b c r ^ {2} \sin^ {- \frac {1}{2}} \psi d r = \frac {2}{3} \pi a b c \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \sin^ {- \frac {1}{2}} \psi d \psi = \frac {2}{3} \pi a b c \cdot \frac {1}{2} B \left(\frac {1}{2}, \frac {1}{4}\right) ^ {*}) \\ = \frac {2}{3} \pi a b c \frac {1}{2} \frac {\Gamma (\frac {1}{2}) \Gamma (\frac {1}{4})}{\Gamma (\frac {3}{4})} = \frac {1}{3} \pi a b c \frac {\sqrt {\pi} \Gamma^ {2} (\frac {1}{4})}{\Gamma (\frac {1}{4}) \Gamma (\frac {3}{4})} = \frac {1}{3} \pi a b c \frac {\sqrt {\pi} \Gamma^ {2} (\frac {1}{4})}{\sqrt {2} \pi} ^ {\dots} \\ = \frac {1}{3} a b c \sqrt {\frac {\pi}{2}} \Gamma^ {2} \left(\frac {1}{4}\right). \\ \end{array}
$$

$\star$ ）利用3856题的结果.  
$\star \star)$ 利用延拓公式： $\Gamma (x)\Gamma (1 - x) = \frac{\pi}{\sin\pi x}.$

利用适当的变量代换，计算以下列曲面为界的物体的体积（假定参数是正的）：

$$
\left(\frac {x}{a} + \frac {y}{b} + \frac {z}{c}\right) ^ {2} = \frac {x}{h} + \frac {y}{k} (x > 0, y > 0, z > 0). \tag {4116}
$$

解题思路 作变量代换 $x = \arccos^2\varphi \cos^2\psi, y = br\sin^2\varphi \cos^2\psi, z = cr\sin^2\psi,$ 则有 $|I| = 4abcr^2\cos\varphi \sin\varphi \cos^3\psi \sin\psi$ ，且区域 $V$ 为

$$
0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, \quad 0 \leqslant \psi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, \quad 0 \leqslant r \leqslant \left(\frac {a}{h} \cos^ {2} \varphi + \frac {b}{k} \sin^ {2} \varphi\right) \cos^ {2} \psi ,
$$

并利用3856题的结果.

解令 $x = a r\cos^2\varphi \cos^2\psi ,y = b r\sin^2\varphi \cos^2\psi ,z = c r\sin^2\psi$ ，则有 $\left|I\right| = 4a b c r^{2}\cos \varphi \sin \varphi \cos^{3}\psi \sin \psi$ ，且区域V为

$$
0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, \quad 0 \leqslant \psi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}. \quad 0 \leqslant r \leqslant \left(\frac {a}{h} \cos^ {2} \varphi + \frac {b}{k} \sin^ {2} \varphi\right) \cos^ {2} \psi .
$$

于是，体积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \psi \int_ {0} ^ {\left(\frac {a}{h} \cos^ {2} \varphi - \frac {b}{k} \sin^ {2} \varphi\right) \cos^ {2} \psi} 4 a b c r ^ {2} \cos \varphi \sin \varphi \cos^ {3} \psi \sin \psi d r \\ = \frac {4}{3} a b c \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos \varphi \sin \varphi \left(\frac {a}{h} \cos^ {2} \varphi + \frac {b}{k} \sin^ {2} \varphi\right) ^ {3} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {9} \psi \sin \psi d \psi \\ = \frac {2}{1 5} a b c \left(\int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \frac {a ^ {3}}{h ^ {3}} \cos^ {7} \varphi \sin \varphi d \varphi + \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \frac {b ^ {3}}{k ^ {3}} \cos \varphi \sin^ {7} \varphi d \varphi + 3 \cdot \frac {a ^ {2} b}{h ^ {2} k} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {5} \varphi \sin^ {3} \varphi d \varphi + 3 \cdot \frac {a b ^ {2}}{h k ^ {2}} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {3} \varphi \sin^ {5} \varphi d \varphi\right) \\ = \frac {2}{1 5} a b c \left(\frac {a ^ {3}}{8 h ^ {3}} + \frac {b ^ {3}}{8 k ^ {3}} + 3 \cdot \frac {a ^ {2} b}{h ^ {2} k} \cdot \frac {1}{2 4} + 3 \cdot \frac {a b ^ {2}}{h k ^ {2}} \cdot \frac {1}{2 4}\right) ^ {- 1} = \frac {1}{6 0} a b c \left(\frac {a}{h} + \frac {b}{k}\right) \left(\frac {a ^ {2}}{h ^ {2}} + \frac {b ^ {2}}{k ^ {2}}\right). \\ \end{array}
$$

\*) 利用3856题的结果.

【4117】 $\left(\frac{x}{a} +\frac{y}{b} +\frac{z}{c}\right)^4 = \frac{xyz}{abc}$ （ $x > 0,y > 0,z > 0)$

提示 仿4116题的解法.

解令 $x = \arccos^2\varphi \cos^2\psi ,y = br\sin^2\varphi \cos^2\psi ,z = cr\sin^2\psi$ ，则有 $|I| = 4abcr^{2}\cos \varphi \sin \varphi \cos^{3}\psi \sin \psi$ ，且区域V为

$$
0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, 0 \leqslant \psi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, 0 \leqslant r \leqslant \cos^ {2} \varphi \sin^ {2} \varphi \cos^ {4} \psi \sin^ {2} \psi
$$

于是，体积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = 4 a b c \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \psi \int_ {0} ^ {\cos^ {2} \varphi \sin^ {2} \varphi \cos^ {4} \psi \sin^ {2} \psi} r ^ {2} \cos \varphi \sin \varphi \cos^ {3} \psi \sin \psi d r = \frac {4}{3} a b c \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {7} \varphi \sin^ {7} \varphi d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {1 5} \psi \sin^ {7} \psi d \psi \\ = \frac {4}{3} a b c \cdot \frac {1}{2} \frac {\Gamma (4) \Gamma (4)}{\Gamma (8)} \cdot \frac {1}{2} \frac {\Gamma (8) \Gamma (4) ^ {*}}{\Gamma (1 2)} = \frac {1}{3} a b c \frac {3 ! 3 !}{7 !} \cdot \frac {7 ! 3 !}{1 1 !} = \frac {a b c}{5 5 4 4 0 0}. \\ \end{array}
$$

\*) 利用3856题的结果.

【4118】 $\left(\frac{x}{a} +\frac{y}{b}\right)^2 +\left(\frac{z}{c}\right)^2 = 1\quad (x > 0,y > 0,z > 0).$

解题思路 作变量代换 $x = \arccos^2\varphi \cos \psi, y = br\sin^2\varphi \cos \psi, z = cr\sin \psi,$

则有 $|I| = 2abcr^2\cos \varphi \sin \varphi \cos \psi$ ，且区域 $V$ 为

$$
0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, \quad 0 \leqslant \psi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, \quad 0 \leqslant r \leqslant 1.
$$

解令 $x = a r\cos^2\varphi \cos \psi ,y = b r\sin^2\varphi \cos \psi ,z = c r\sin \psi$ ，则有 $|I| = 2abcr^{2}\cos \varphi \sin \varphi \cos \psi$ ，且区域V为

$$
0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, \quad 0 \leqslant \psi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, \quad 0 \leqslant r \leqslant 1.
$$

于是，体积为

$$
V = 2 a b c \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \psi \int_ {0} ^ {1} r ^ {2} \cos \varphi \sin \varphi \cos \psi d r = \frac {2}{3} a b c \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos \varphi \sin \varphi d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos \psi d \psi = \frac {1}{3} a b c.
$$

【4119】 $z = x^{2} + y^{2}, z = 2(x^{2} + y^{2}), xy = a^{2}, xy = 2a^{2}, x = 2y, 2x = y (x > 0, y > 0)$ .

解题思路 作变量代换 $z = u(x^{2} + y^{2}),xy = v,x = yw$ ，则

$$
x = \sqrt {v w}, y = \sqrt {\frac {v}{w}}, z = u \left(v w + \frac {v}{w}\right) \quad \text {及} \quad | I | = \frac {v}{2} + \frac {v}{2 w ^ {2}},
$$

且区域 $V$ 为 $1 \leqslant u \leqslant 2, a^{2} \leqslant v \leqslant 2a^{2}, \frac{1}{2} \leqslant w \leqslant 2.$

解令 $z = u(x^{2} + y^{2}),xy = v,x = yw$ ，则

$$
x = \sqrt {v w}, \quad y = \sqrt {\frac {v}{w}}, \quad z = u \left(v w + \frac {v}{w}\right).
$$

变换的雅可比行列式为

$$
I = \left| \begin{array}{c c c} 0 & \frac {\sqrt {w}}{2 \sqrt {v}} & \frac {\sqrt {v}}{2 \sqrt {w}} \\ 0 & \frac {1}{2 \sqrt {v w}} & - \frac {\sqrt {v}}{2 \sqrt {w ^ {3}}} \\ v w + \frac {v}{w} & u \left(w + \frac {1}{w}\right) & u \left(v - \frac {v}{w ^ {2}}\right) \end{array} \right| = - \left(\frac {v}{2} + \frac {v}{2 w ^ {2}}\right),
$$

而区域 $V$ 为

于是，体积为

$$
V = \int_ {1} ^ {2} d u \int_ {u ^ {2}} ^ {2 a ^ {2}} d v \int_ {\frac {1}{2}} ^ {2} \left(\frac {v}{2} + \frac {v}{2 w ^ {2}}\right) d w = \frac {3 a ^ {4}}{4} \int_ {\frac {1}{2}} ^ {2} \left(1 + \frac {1}{w ^ {2}}\right) d w = \frac {9 a ^ {4}}{4}.
$$

【4120】 $x^{2} + z^{2} = a^{2}, x^{2} + z^{2} = b^{2}, x^{2} - y^{2} - z^{2} = 0 (x > 0)$

解 令 $x = r\cos \varphi, y = y, z = r\sin \varphi$ ，则区域 $V$ 为

$$
a \leqslant r \leqslant b, - \frac {\pi}{4} \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{4}, - r \sqrt {\cos 2 \varphi} \leqslant y \leqslant r \sqrt {\cos 2 \varphi}.
$$

于是，体积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = \int_ {a} ^ {b} r \mathrm {d} r \int_ {- \frac {\pi}{4}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} \mathrm {d} \varphi \int_ {- r \sqrt {\cos 2 \varphi}} ^ {r \sqrt {\cos 2 \varphi}} \mathrm {d} y = \frac {4}{3} (b ^ {3} - a ^ {3}) \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} \sqrt {\cos 2 \varphi} \mathrm {d} \varphi = \frac {2}{3} (b ^ {3} - a ^ {3}) \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \sqrt {\cos \varphi} \mathrm {d} \varphi \\ = \frac {1}{3} \left(b ^ {3} - a ^ {3}\right) \frac {\Gamma \left(\frac {1}{2}\right) \Gamma \left(\frac {3}{4}\right)}{\Gamma \left(\frac {5}{4}\right)} = \frac {2}{3} \left(b ^ {3} - a ^ {3}\right) \sqrt {\frac {2}{\pi}} \Gamma^ {2} \left(\frac {3}{4}\right) ^ {* *}). \\ \end{array}
$$

\*）利用3856题的结果.

$\star \star$ ）利用延拓公式有 $\Gamma (\frac{1}{4})\Gamma (\frac{3}{4}) = \sqrt{2}\pi .$

【4121】 $(x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2})^{3} = \frac{a^{6}z^{2}}{x^{2} + y^{2}}.$

解采用球坐标 $x = r\cos \varphi \cos \psi$ ， $y = r\sin \varphi \cos \psi$ ， $z = r\sin \psi$ ，则区域 $V$ 的 $\frac{1}{8}$ 部分（第一卦限内）为

$$
0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, \quad 0 \leqslant \psi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, \quad 0 \leqslant r \leqslant a \tan^ {\frac {1}{3}} \psi .
$$

于是，体积为 $V = 8\int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}\mathrm{d}\varphi \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}\mathrm{d}\psi \int_{0}^{a\tan \frac{1}{3}\psi}r^{2}\cos \psi \mathrm{d}r = \frac{4\pi a^{3}}{3}\int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}\sin \psi \mathrm{d}\psi = \frac{4\pi a^{3}}{3}.$

【4122】 $\left(\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2} +\frac{z^2}{c^2}\right)^2 = \frac{z}{h}\cdot \mathrm{e}^{-\frac{\frac{z^2}{c^2}}{\frac{x^2}{a^2} + \frac{y^2}{b^2} + \frac{z^2}{c^2}}}}.$

解令 $x = \arccos \varphi \cos \psi ,y = br\sin \varphi \cos \psi ,z = cr\sin \psi$ ，则区域 $V$ 的 $\frac{1}{4}$ 部分（第一卦限内）为

$$
0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, \quad 0 \leqslant \psi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, \quad 0 \leqslant r \leqslant \left(\frac {c}{h} \sin \psi e ^ {- \sin^ {2} \psi}\right) ^ {\frac {1}{3}}.
$$

这是由于 $z \geqslant 0$ ，故区域 $V$ 在 $Oxy$ 平面的上方。

于是，体积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = 4 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \psi \int_ {0} ^ {\left(\frac {c}{h} \sin \psi e ^ {- \sin^ {2} \psi}\right) \frac {1}{3}} a b c r ^ {2} \cos \psi d r = \frac {4 c ^ {2} a b}{3 h} \cdot \frac {\pi}{2} \cdot \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \sin \psi \cos \psi e ^ {- \sin^ {2} \psi} d \psi \\ = - \frac {\pi a b c ^ {2}}{3 h} e ^ {- \sin^ {2} \phi} \left| _ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} = \frac {\pi a b c ^ {2}}{3 h} (1 - e ^ {- 1}) \right.. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4123】 $\frac{\frac{x}{a} + \frac{y}{b}}{\frac{x}{a} + \frac{y}{b} + \frac{z}{c}} = \frac{2}{\pi}\arcsin \left(\frac{x}{a} + \frac{y}{b} + \frac{z}{c}\right), \frac{x}{a} + \frac{y}{b} = 1, x = 0, x = a.$

解题思路 作变量代换 $\frac{x}{a} = u, \frac{x}{a} + \frac{y}{b} = v, \frac{x}{a} + \frac{y}{b} + \frac{z}{c} = w,$

则有 $|I| = abc\left(\frac{D(u,v,w)}{D(x,y,z)} = \frac{1}{abc}\right)$ 且区域 $V$ 为 $0 \leqslant u \leqslant 1, -1 \leqslant w \leqslant 1, \frac{2}{\pi} \arcsin w \leqslant v \leqslant 1.$

解 令 $u = \frac{x}{a}, v = \frac{x}{a} + \frac{y}{b}, w = \frac{x}{a} + \frac{y}{b} + \frac{z}{c}$ ，则

$$
\frac {D (u , v , w)}{D (x , y , z)} = \left| \begin{array}{c c c} \frac {1}{a} & 0 & 0 \\ \frac {1}{a} & \frac {1}{b} & 0 \\ \frac {1}{a} & \frac {1}{b} & \frac {1}{c} \end{array} \right| = \frac {1}{a b c},
$$

且区域 $V$ 变为 $0 \leqslant u \leqslant 1, \frac{2}{\pi} u \arcsin u \leqslant v \leqslant 1, -1 \leqslant w \leqslant 1.$

于是， $\frac{D(x,y,z)}{D(u,v,w)} = abc$ ，且体积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = a b c \int_ {0} ^ {1} d u \int_ {- 1} ^ {1} d w \int_ {\frac {2}{\pi} \arcsin u} ^ {1} d v = 2 a b c \int_ {0} ^ {1} \left[ 1 - \frac {2}{\pi} w \arcsin w \right] d w = 2 a b c - \frac {2 a b c}{\pi} \int_ {0} ^ {1} \arcsin w d (w ^ {2}) \\ = a b c + \frac {2 a b c}{\pi} \int_ {0} ^ {1} w ^ {2} (1 - w ^ {2}) ^ {- \frac {1}{2}} d w = a b c + \frac {a b c}{\pi} \int_ {0} ^ {1} t ^ {\frac {1}{2}} (1 - t) ^ {- \frac {1}{2}} d t = a b c + \frac {a b c}{\pi} B \left(\frac {3}{2}, \frac {1}{2}\right) = \frac {3}{2} a b c. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4124】 $\frac{x}{a} +\frac{y}{b} +\frac{z}{c} = \ln \frac{\frac{x}{a} + \frac{y}{b} + \frac{z}{c}}{\frac{x}{a} + \frac{y}{b}},x = 0,z = 0,\frac{y}{b} +\frac{z}{c} = 0,\frac{x}{a} +\frac{y}{b} +\frac{z}{c} = 1.$

提示 仿4123题的解法.

解 令 $u = \frac{x}{a}, v = \frac{x}{a} + \frac{y}{b}, w = \frac{x}{a} + \frac{y}{b} + \frac{z}{c}$ ，则 $\frac{D(u, v, w)}{D(x, y, z)} = \frac{1}{abc}$

且区域 $V$ 变为

$$
0 \leqslant u \leqslant w, \quad w e ^ {u} \leqslant v \leqslant w, \quad 0 \leqslant w \leqslant 1.
$$

于是， $\frac{D(x,y,z)}{D(u,v,w)} = abc$ ，且体积为

$$
V = a b c \int_ {0} ^ {1} d w \int_ {0} ^ {w} d u \int_ {u v ^ {- w}} ^ {w} d v = a b c \int_ {0} ^ {1} \left(w ^ {2} - w ^ {2} e ^ {- w}\right) d w = a b c \left(\frac {1}{3} - 2 + 5 e ^ {- 1}\right) = 5 a b c \left(\frac {1}{e} - \frac {1}{3}\right).
$$

【4125】曲面 $x^{2} + y^{2} + az = 4a^{2}$ 将球 $x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2} = 4az$ 分成两部分，求这两部分的体积之比.

解曲面 $x^{2} + y^{2} + az = 4a^{2}$ 与球面 $x^{2} + y^{2} + (z - 2a)^{2} = 4a^{2}$ 的交线为圆周

$$
\left\{ \begin{array}{l} x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} = 3 a ^ {2} \\ z = a, \end{array} \right.
$$

且有公共的顶点 $(0,0,4a)$ . 球内位于曲面 $x^{2} + y^{2} + az = 4a^{2}$ 下方部分的体积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} V _ {1} = \int_ {0} ^ {u} d z \iint_ {x ^ {2} - y ^ {2} \leqslant 1 a z - z ^ {2}} d x d y + \int_ {a} ^ {1 a} d z \iint_ {x ^ {2} - y ^ {2} \leqslant 1 a ^ {2} - u z} d x d y = \int_ {0} ^ {a} \pi (4 a z - z ^ {2}) d z + \int_ {a} ^ {1 a} \pi (4 a ^ {2} - a z) d z \\ = 2 \pi a ^ {3} - \frac {1}{3} \pi a ^ {3} + 1 2 \pi a ^ {3} - \frac {1 5}{2} \pi a ^ {3} = \frac {3 7}{6} \pi a ^ {3}. \\ \end{array}
$$

从而，另一部分的体积 $V_{2} = \frac{4}{3}\pi (2a)^{3} - \frac{37}{6}\pi a^{3} = \frac{27}{6}\pi a^{3}.$

于是，球被曲面所分的两部分体积之比为 $\frac{V_1}{V_2} = \frac{37}{27}$

【4126】求以曲面 $x^{2} + y^{2} = az$ ， $z = 2a - \sqrt{x^2 + y^2}$ （ $a > 0$ )为界的物体的体积和表面积.

解 两曲面的交线为圆周 $\left\{ \begin{array}{l} x^{2} + y^{2} = a^{2}, \\ z = a, \end{array} \right.$

又曲面 $z = 2a - \sqrt{x^2 + y^2}$ 的顶点为 $(0,0,2a)$ . 于是，体积为

$$
V = \int_ {0} ^ {a} d z \iint_ {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} \leqslant a z} d x d y + \int_ {a} ^ {2 a} d z \iint_ {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} \leqslant (2 a - z) ^ {2}} d x d y = \int_ {0} ^ {a} \pi a z d z + \int_ {a} ^ {2 a} \pi (2 a - z) ^ {2} d z = \frac {\pi a ^ {3}}{2} + \frac {\pi a ^ {3}}{3} = \frac {5 \pi a ^ {3}}{6}.
$$

由两曲面方程分别可得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \frac {\partial z}{\partial x} = \frac {2 x}{a}, \quad \frac {\partial z}{\partial y} = \frac {2 y}{a}, \quad \sqrt {1 + \left(\frac {\partial z}{\partial x}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\partial z}{\partial y}\right) ^ {2}} = \frac {1}{a} \sqrt {a ^ {2} + 4 x ^ {2} + 4 y ^ {2}}; \\ \frac {\partial z}{\partial x} = \frac {- x}{\sqrt {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}}}, \quad \frac {\partial z}{\partial y} = \frac {- y}{\sqrt {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}}}, \quad \sqrt {1 + \left(\frac {\partial z}{\partial x}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\partial z}{\partial y}\right) ^ {2}} = \sqrt {2}. \\ \end{array}
$$

于是，曲面的表面积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} S = \iint_ {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} \leqslant a ^ {2}} \frac {1}{a} \sqrt {a ^ {2} + 4 x ^ {2} + 4 y ^ {2}} d x d y + \iint_ {r ^ {2} + y ^ {2} \leqslant a ^ {2}} \sqrt {2} d x d y = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {1} \sqrt {1 + 4 r ^ {2}} a ^ {2} r d r + \sqrt {2} \pi a ^ {2} \\ = \frac {\pi a ^ {2}}{6} (6 \sqrt {2} + 5 \sqrt {5} - 1). \\ \end{array}
$$

【4127】求以平面 $a_1x + b_1y + c_1z = \pm h_1$ ， $a_2x + b_2y + c_2z = \pm h_2$ ， $a_3x + b_3y + c_3z = \pm h_3$ 为界的平行六面体的体积，设

$$
\Delta = \left| \begin{array}{c c c} a _ {1} & b _ {1} & c _ {1} \\ a _ {2} & b _ {2} & c _ {2} \\ a _ {3} & b _ {3} & c _ {3} \end{array} \right| \neq 0.
$$

解题思路 作变量代换

$$
a _ {1} x + b _ {1} y + c _ {1} z = u, \quad a _ {2} x + b _ {2} y + c _ {2} z = v, \quad a _ {3} x + b _ {3} y + c _ {3} z = w,
$$

则有 $|I| = \frac{1}{|\Delta|}$ ，且区域 $V$ 为 $-h_1 \leq u \leq h_1, -h_2 \leq v \leq h_2, -h_3 \leq w \leq h_3$ .

解令 $a_1x + b_1y + c_1z = u, a_2x + b_2y + c_2z = v, a_3x + b_3y + c_3z = w,$

则有 $\frac{D(u,v,w)}{D(x,y,z)} = \Delta$ 于是 $\frac{D(x,y,z)}{D(u,v,w)} = \frac{1}{\Delta}$ 且体积为

$$
V = \int_ {- h _ {1}} ^ {h _ {1}} d u \int_ {- h _ {2}} ^ {h _ {2}} d v \int_ {- h _ {3}} ^ {h _ {3}} \frac {1}{| \Delta |} d w = \frac {8 h _ {1} h _ {2} h _ {3}}{| \Delta |}.
$$

【4128】求以曲面 $(a_{1}x + b_{1}y + c_{1}z)^{2} + (a_{2}x + b_{2}y + c_{2}z)^{2} + (a_{3}x + b_{3}y + c_{3}z)^{2} = h^{2}$ 为界的物体的体积，设

$$
\Delta = \left| \begin{array}{c c c} a _ {1} & b _ {1} & c _ {1} \\ a _ {2} & b _ {2} & c _ {2} \\ a _ {3} & b _ {3} & c _ {3} \end{array} \right| \neq 0.
$$

提示 仿4127题的解法.

解令 $a_1x + b_1y + c_1z = u, a_2x + b_2y + c_2z = v, a_3x + b_3y + c_3z = w,$

则有 $\frac{D(u,v,w)}{D(x,y,z)} = \Delta$ 于是， $\frac{D(x,y,z)}{D(u,v,w)} = \frac{1}{\Delta}$ ，且体积为

$$
V = \frac {1}{| \Delta |} \iiint_ {u ^ {2} + v ^ {2} + w ^ {2} \leqslant h ^ {2}} d u d v d w = \frac {4 \pi h ^ {3}}{3 | \Delta |}.
$$

【4129】求以曲面 $\left(\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2}\right)^n +\frac{z^{2n}}{c^{2n}} = \frac{z}{h}\left(\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2}\right)^{n - 2}\quad (n > 1)$

为界的物体的体积.

解 令 $x = \arccos \varphi \cos \psi, y = b r \sin \varphi \cos \psi, z = c r \sin \psi$ ，则有 $|I| = a b c r^{2} \cos \psi$ ，且区域 $V$ 的 $\frac{1}{4}$ 为

$$
0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, \quad 0 \leqslant \psi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, \quad 0 \leqslant r \leqslant \sqrt [ 3 ]{\frac {c}{h} \cdot \frac {\sin \psi \cos^ {2 n - 4} \psi}{\cos^ {2 n} \psi + \sin^ {2 n} \psi}}.
$$

于是，体积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = 4 \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \psi \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt {\frac {1}{h} \cdot \frac {\sin \psi \cos^ {2 n - 4} \psi}{\cos^ {2 n} \psi + \sin^ {2 n} \psi}}} a b c r ^ {2} \cos \varphi d r = \frac {2}{3 h} \pi a b c ^ {2} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \frac {\sin \psi \cos^ {2 n - 3} \psi}{\cos^ {2 n} \psi + \sin^ {2 n} \psi} d \varphi \\ = \frac {2}{3 h} \pi a b c ^ {2} \int_ {0} ^ {1} \frac {t ^ {2 n - 3} d t}{t ^ {2 n} + (1 - t ^ {2}) ^ {n}} = - \frac {1}{3 h} \pi a b c ^ {2} \int_ {0} ^ {1} \frac {t ^ {2 n - 1} d (1 - t ^ {2})}{t ^ {2 n} + (1 - t ^ {2}) ^ {n}} \\ = \frac {1}{3 h} \pi a b c ^ {2} \int_ {0} ^ {1} \frac {(1 - x) ^ {n} {} ^ {2} d x}{(1 - x) ^ {n} + x ^ {n}} = \frac {1}{3 h} \pi a b c ^ {2} \int_ {0} ^ {1} \frac {\frac {1}{(1 - x) ^ {2}} d x}{1 + \left(\frac {x}{1 - x}\right) ^ {n}} \\ = \frac {1}{3 h} \pi a b c ^ {2} \int_ {n} ^ {-} \frac {\mathrm {d} t}{1 + t ^ {n}} = \frac {1}{3 h} \pi a b c ^ {2} \frac {\pi}{n \sin \frac {\pi}{n}} = \frac {\pi^ {2}}{3 n \sin \frac {\pi}{n}} \frac {a b c ^ {2}}{h}. \\ \end{array}
$$

\*） 作代换 $t = \frac{x}{1 - x}$

\*) 利用3851题的结果.

【4130】一物体位于正卦限 $Oxyz(x > 0,y > 0,z > 0)$ ，并以曲面

$$
\frac {x ^ {m}}{a ^ {m}} + \frac {y ^ {n}}{b ^ {n}} + \frac {z ^ {p}}{c ^ {p}} = 1 \quad (m > 0, n > 0, p > 0), x = 0, y = 0, z = 0
$$

为界，求其体积.

提示 作变量代换 $x = ar^{\frac{2}{m}}\cos \frac{2}{m}\varphi \cos \frac{2}{m}\psi, y = br^{\frac{2}{n}}\sin \frac{2}{n}\varphi \cos \frac{2}{n}\psi, z = cr^{\frac{2}{p}}\sin \frac{2}{p}\psi$ ，则有

$$
I = \frac {8 a b c}{m n p} r ^ {\frac {2}{m} + \frac {2}{n} + \frac {2}{p} - 1} \cos^ {\frac {2}{m}} ^ {1} \varphi \sin^ {\frac {2}{n} - 1} \varphi \cos^ {\frac {2}{m} + \frac {2}{n}} ^ {1} \psi \sin^ {\frac {2}{p} - 1} \psi .
$$

解令

$$
x = a r ^ {\frac {2}{m}} \cos^ {\frac {2}{m}} \varphi \cos^ {\frac {2}{m}} \psi , \quad y = b r ^ {\frac {2}{n}} \sin^ {\frac {2}{n}} \varphi \cos^ {\frac {2}{n}} \psi , \quad z = c r ^ {\frac {2}{p}} \sin^ {\frac {2}{p}} \psi ,
$$

则

$$
\frac {D (x , y , z)}{D (r , \varphi , \psi)} = \frac {8 a b c}{m n p} r ^ {\frac {2}{m} - \frac {2}{n} - \frac {2}{p} - 1} \cos^ {\frac {2}{m} - 1} \varphi \sin^ {\frac {2}{n}} ^ {1} \varphi \cos^ {\frac {2}{m} + \frac {2}{n} - 1} \psi \sin^ {\frac {2}{p} - 1} \psi .
$$

于是，体积为

$$
\begin{array}{l} V = \frac {8 a b c}{m n p} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {\frac {2}{m}} ^ {- 1} \varphi \sin^ {\frac {2}{n} - 1} \varphi d \varphi \cdot \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {\frac {2}{m}} ^ {- \frac {2}{n} - 1} \psi \sin^ {\frac {2}{p} - 1} \psi d \psi \cdot \int_ {0} ^ {1} r ^ {\frac {2}{m} - \frac {2}{n} - \frac {2}{p} - 1} d r \\ = \frac {8 a b c}{m n p} \cdot \frac {1}{2} B \left(\frac {1}{m}, \frac {1}{n}\right) \cdot \frac {1}{2} B \left(\frac {1}{m} + \frac {1}{n}, \frac {1}{p}\right) \frac {1}{\frac {2}{m} + \frac {2}{n} + \frac {2}{p}} \\ = \frac {8 a b c}{m n p} \cdot \frac {1}{2} \cdot \frac {\Gamma (\frac {1}{m}) \Gamma (\frac {1}{n})}{\Gamma (\frac {1}{m} + \frac {1}{n})} \cdot \frac {1}{2} \cdot \frac {\Gamma (\frac {1}{m} + \frac {1}{n}) \Gamma (\frac {1}{p})}{\Gamma (\frac {1}{m} + \frac {1}{n} + \frac {1}{p})} \frac {m n p}{2 (m n + n p + m p)} \\ = \frac {a b c}{m n + n p + m p} \frac {\Gamma \left(\frac {1}{m}\right) \Gamma \left(\frac {1}{n}\right) \Gamma \left(\frac {1}{p}\right)}{\Gamma \left(\frac {1}{m} + \frac {1}{n} + \frac {1}{p}\right)}. \\ \end{array}
$$

\*) 利用3856题的结果.

# § 8. 三重积分在力学上的应用

$1^{\circ}$ 物体的质量 若一物体占有区域 $V, \rho = \rho(x, y, z)$ 为它在点 $(x, y, z)$ 的密度，则该物体的质量等于

$$
M = \iiint_ {V} \rho \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y \mathrm {d} z. \tag {1}
$$

$2^{\circ}$ 物体的质心物体的质心坐标 $(x_0, y_0, z_0)$ 按下列公式来计算

$$
\left\{ \begin{array}{l} x _ {0} = \frac {1}{M} \iiint_ {V} \rho x d x d y d z, \\ y _ {0} = \frac {1}{M} \iiint_ {V} \rho y d x d y d z, \\ z _ {0} = \frac {1}{M} \iiint_ {V} \rho z d x d y d z. \end{array} \right. \tag {2}
$$

若物体是均匀的，则在公式(1)和(2)中可令 $\rho = 1$

$3^{\circ}$ 转动惯量 积分

$$
I _ {x y} = \iiint_ {V} \rho z ^ {2} d x d y d z, \quad I _ {y z} = \iiint_ {V} \rho x ^ {2} d x d y d z, \quad I _ {z x} = \iiint_ {V} \rho y ^ {2} d x d y d z,
$$

分别称为物体对坐标平面的转动惯量.

积分 $I_{t} = \iiint_{V}\rho r^{2}\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y\mathrm{d}z$

（其中 $r$ 为物体各点 $(x,y,z)$ 与轴 $l$ 的距离）称为物体对于某轴 $l$ 的转动惯量.特别是，对于坐标轴 $Ox,Oy,$ $Oz$ 分别有

$I_{x} = I_{xy} + I_{xz},\quad I_{y} = I_{yx} + I_{yz},\quad I_{z} = I_{zx} + I_{zy}.$ 积分 $I_0 = \iiint_V\rho (x^2 +y^2 +z^2)\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y\mathrm{d}z$

称为物体对坐标原点的转动惯量.

显然有 $I_0 = I_{xy} + I_{yz} + I_{zx}$

4°引力势积分

$$
u (x, y, z) = \iiint_ {V} \rho (\xi , \eta , \zeta) \frac {\mathrm {d} \xi \mathrm {d} \eta \mathrm {d} \zeta}{r}
$$

称为物体在点 $P(x,y,z)$ 的牛顿引力势.式中 $\pmb{V}$ 为物体所占区域， $\rho = \rho (\xi ,\eta ,\zeta)$ 为物体的密度，且

$$
r = \sqrt {(\xi - x) ^ {2} + (\eta - y) ^ {2} + (\zeta - z) ^ {2}}).
$$

质量为 $m$ 的质点吸引物体的力在坐标轴 $Ox, Oy, Oz$ 上的投影 $X, Y, Z$ 分别等于

$$
X = c m \frac {\partial u}{\partial x} = c m \iiint_ {V} \rho \frac {\xi - x}{r ^ {3}} d \xi d \eta d \zeta , \quad Y = c m \frac {\partial u}{\partial y} = c m \iiint_ {V} \rho \frac {\eta - y}{r ^ {3}} d \xi d \eta d \zeta , \quad Z = c m \frac {\partial u}{\partial z} = c m \iiint_ {V} \rho \frac {\zeta - z}{r ^ {3}} d \xi d \eta d \zeta ,
$$

其中 $c$ 为引力常量.

【4131】设物体在点 $M(x, y, z)$ 的密度由公式 $\rho = x + y + z$ 给出，求占有单位体积 $0 \leqslant x \leqslant 1, 0 \leqslant y \leqslant 1, 0 \leqslant z \leqslant 1$ 之物体的质量.

解 质量以 $M$ 表示，则按题设有 $M = \int_{0}^{1}\mathrm{d}x\int_{0}^{1}\mathrm{d}y\int_{0}^{1}(x + y + z)\mathrm{d}z = \frac{3}{2}.$

【4132】若物体的密度按规律 $\rho = \rho_0\mathrm{e}^{-k\sqrt{x^2 + y^2 + z^2}}$ （其中 $\rho_0 > 0$ 及 $k > 0$ 为常数）而变化，求占有无限区域 $x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2}\geqslant 1$ 的物体的质量.

解 若令 $x = r\cos \varphi \cos \psi, y = r\sin \varphi \cos \psi, z = r\sin \psi$ ，则质量为

$$
M = \iiint_ {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} + z ^ {2} \geqslant 1} \rho_ {0} e ^ {- k \sqrt {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} + z ^ {2}}} d x d y d z = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {\frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \psi \int_ {1} ^ {+ \infty} r ^ {2} \rho_ {0} e ^ {- k r} \cos \psi d r = 4 \pi \rho_ {0} \int_ {1} ^ {+ \infty} r ^ {2} e ^ {- k r} d r
$$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = - \frac {4 \pi \rho_ {0}}{k} \int_ {1} ^ {+ \infty} r ^ {2} d e ^ {- k r} = - \frac {4 \pi \rho_ {0}}{k} r ^ {2} e ^ {- k r} \left| _ {1} ^ {+ \infty} + \frac {4 \pi \rho_ {0}}{k} \int_ {1} ^ {+ \infty} 2 r e ^ {- k r} d r = \frac {4 \pi \rho_ {0}}{k} e ^ {- k} - \frac {8 \pi \rho_ {0}}{k ^ {2}} \int_ {1} ^ {+ \infty} r d e ^ {- k r} \right. \\ = \frac {4 \pi \rho_ {0}}{k} e ^ {k} - \frac {8 \pi \rho_ {0}}{k ^ {2}} r e ^ {- k r} \left| _ {1} ^ {+ \infty} + \frac {8 \pi \rho_ {0}}{k ^ {2}} \int_ {1} ^ {+ \infty} e ^ {- k r} d r = 4 \pi \rho_ {0} e ^ {- k} \left(\frac {1}{k} + \frac {2}{k ^ {2}} + \frac {2}{k ^ {3}}\right). \right. \\ \end{array}
$$

求以下列曲面为界的均匀物体的质心坐标：

【4133】 $\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2} = \frac{z^2}{c^2},\quad z = c.$

提示 作变量代换 $x = \arccos \varphi, y = brsin\varphi, z = z$

解 若令 $x = \arccos \varphi, y = b r \sin \varphi, z = z$ ，则质量为

$$
M = a b \int_ {0} ^ {c} d z \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {z}{c}} r d r = \frac {\pi a b c}{3}.
$$

设质心坐标为 $x_0, y_0, z_0$ ，由对称性知 $x_0 = y_0 = 0$ ，而

$$
z _ {0} = \frac {a b}{M} \int_ {0} ^ {c} z d z \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {z}{c}} r d r = \frac {3}{\pi a b c} \cdot \frac {\pi a b c ^ {2}}{4} = \frac {3 c}{4}.
$$

于是，质心为点 $\left(0,0,\frac{3c}{4}\right)$

【4134】 $z = x^{2} + y^{2},x + y = a,x = 0,y = 0,z = 0.$

解 物体的质量为 $M = \int_{0}^{a}\mathrm{d}x\int_{0}^{a - x}\mathrm{d}y\int_{0}^{x^2 +y^2}\mathrm{d}z = \frac{1}{6} a^4.$

质心的横坐标为 $x_0 = \frac{1}{M}\int_0^a x\mathrm{d}x\int_0^{a - x}\mathrm{d}y\int_0^{x^2 +y^2}\mathrm{d}z = \frac{6}{a^4}\cdot \frac{a^5}{15} = \frac{2a}{5},$

同理可求得 $y_0 = \frac{2a}{5}$ 而

$$
\begin{array}{l} z _ {0} = \frac {1}{M} \int_ {0} ^ {a} \mathrm {d} x \int_ {0} ^ {a - x} \mathrm {d} y \int_ {0} ^ {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}} z \mathrm {d} z = \frac {1}{M} \int_ {0} ^ {a} \left(\frac {a ^ {5}}{1 0} - \frac {1}{2} a ^ {4} x + \frac {4}{3} a ^ {3} x ^ {2} - 2 a ^ {2} x ^ {3} + 2 a x ^ {4} - \frac {1 4}{1 5} x ^ {5}\right) \mathrm {d} x \\ = \frac {6}{a ^ {4}} \cdot \frac {7}{1 8 0} a ^ {6} = \frac {7}{3 0} a ^ {2}. \\ \end{array}
$$

于是，质心的坐标为 $x_0 = y_0 = \frac{2}{5} a, z_0 = \frac{7}{30} a^2.$

【4135】 $x^{2} = 2pz, y^{2} = 2px, x = \frac{p}{2}, z = 0.$

解 物体的质量为 $M = \int_{0}^{\frac{p}{2}} \mathrm{d}x \int_{-\sqrt{2px}}^{\sqrt{2px}} \mathrm{d}y \int_{0}^{\frac{x^2}{2p}} \mathrm{d}z = \sqrt{\frac{2}{p}} \int_{0}^{\frac{p}{2}} x^{\frac{5}{2}} \mathrm{d}x = \frac{p^3}{28}$ .

质心的坐标为

$$
x _ {0} = \frac {1}{M} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {p}{2}} x d x \int_ {- \sqrt {2 p x}} ^ {\sqrt {2 p x}} d y \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {x ^ {2}}{2 p}} d z = \frac {p ^ {4}}{7 2} \cdot \frac {2 8}{p ^ {3}} = \frac {7}{1 8} p. \quad y _ {0} = \frac {1}{M} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {p}{2}} d x \int_ {- \sqrt {2 p x}} ^ {\sqrt {2 p x}} y d y \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {x ^ {2}}{2 p}} d z = 0.
$$

$$
z _ {0} = \frac {1}{M} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {p}{2}} \mathrm {d} x \int_ {- \sqrt {2 p x}} ^ {\sqrt {2 p x}} \mathrm {d} y \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {x ^ {2}}{2 p}} z \mathrm {d} z = \frac {p ^ {4}}{7 0 4} \cdot \frac {2 8}{p ^ {3}} = \frac {7}{1 7 6} p.
$$

【4136】 $\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2} +\frac{z^2}{c^2} = 1,x\geqslant 0,y\geqslant 0,z\geqslant 0.$

提示 作变量代换 $x = \arccos \varphi \cos \psi, y = brs\sin \varphi \cos \psi, z = cr\sin \psi$ ，并利用对称性。

解若令 $x = \arccos \varphi \cos \psi ,y = br\sin \varphi \cos \psi ,z = cr\sin \psi ,$

则质量为 $M = \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}\mathrm{d}\varphi \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}\mathrm{d}\psi \int_{0}^{1}abcr^{2}\cos \psi \mathrm{d}r = \frac{1}{6}\pi abc.$

于是，

$$
x _ {0} = \frac {1}{M} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \psi \int_ {0} ^ {1} a b c r ^ {2} \cos \psi \cdot a r \cos \varphi \cos \psi d r = \frac {1}{M} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos \varphi d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {2} \psi d \psi \int_ {0} ^ {1} a ^ {2} b c r ^ {3} d r
$$

$$
= \frac {1}{1 6} \pi a ^ {2} b c \cdot \frac {6}{\pi a b c} = \frac {3}{8} a.
$$

利用对称性知，质心的坐标为 $x_0 = \frac{3}{8} a, y_0 = \frac{3}{8} b, z_0 = \frac{3}{8} c.$

【4137】 $x^{2} + z^{2} = a^{2},y^{2} + z^{2} = a^{2}(z > 0).$

解 物体的质量为 $M = \int_{0}^{a} \mathrm{d}z \int_{\sqrt{a^2 - z^2}}^{\sqrt{a^2 - z^2}} \mathrm{d}y \int_{\sqrt{a^2 - z^2}}^{\sqrt{a^2 - z^2}} \mathrm{d}x = 4 \int_{0}^{a} (a^2 - z^2) \mathrm{d}z = \frac{8a^3}{3}.$

于是， $x_{0} = \frac{1}{M}\int_{0}^{u}\mathrm{d}z\int_{\sqrt{a^{2} - z^{2}}}\sqrt{a^{2} - z^{2}}\mathrm{d}y\int_{\sqrt{a^{2} - z^{2}}}^{\sqrt{a^{2} - z^{2}}}x\mathrm{d}x = 0.$

同理可得 $y_0 = 0$ ，而 $z_0 = \frac{1}{M}\int_0^a z\mathrm{d}z\int_{\sqrt{a^2 - z^2}}^{\sqrt{a^2 - z^2}}\mathrm{d}y\int_{-\sqrt{a^2 - z^2}}^{\sqrt{a^2 - z^2}}\mathrm{d}x = a^4\cdot \frac{3}{8a^3} = \frac{3}{8} a.$

于是，质心的坐标为 $x_0 = y_0 = 0$ ， $z_0 = \frac{3}{8} a$

【4138】 $x^{2} + y^{2} = 2z, x + y = z.$

解由 $x^{2} + y^{2} = 2z$ ， $x + y = z$ 所围成的区域在平面 $z = 0$ 上的投影为圆 $(x - 1)^{2} + (y - 1)^{2} = 2.$

若引用代换 $x = 1 + r\cos \theta ,y = 1 + r\sin \theta ,$

则质量为 $M = \int_{0}^{2\pi}\mathrm{d}\theta \int_{0}^{\sqrt{2}}r\mathrm{d}r\int_{1 - r(\cos \theta +\sin \theta) + \frac{r^2}{2}}^{2 - r(\cos \theta +\sin \theta)}\mathrm{d}z = 2\pi \int_{0}^{\sqrt{2}}(1 - \frac{r^2}{2})r\mathrm{d}r = \pi .$

于是，

$$
x _ {0} = \frac {1}{M} \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \theta \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt {2}} r d r \int_ {1 \cdot r (\cos \theta - \sin \theta) - \frac {r ^ {2}}{2}} ^ {2 \cdot r (\cos \theta - \sin \theta)} (1 + r \cos \theta) d z = \frac {1}{M} \left[ \pi + \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} \cos \theta d \theta \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt {2}} r ^ {2} \left(1 - \frac {r ^ {2}}{2}\right) d r \right] = \frac {\pi}{M} = 1.
$$

同理可得 $y_0 = 1$ ，而

$$
\begin{array}{l} z _ {0} = \frac {1}{M} \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \theta \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt {2}} r d r \int_ {1 + r (\cos \theta + \sin \theta) \cdot \frac {r ^ {2}}{2}} ^ {2 - r (\cos \theta + \sin \theta)} z d z = \frac {1}{2 \pi} \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \theta \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt {2}} \left[ 3 + (\sin \theta + \cos \theta) (2 r - r ^ {3}) - \frac {1}{4} r ^ {4} - r ^ {2} \right] r d r \\ = \frac {1}{2 \pi} \cdot \frac {1 0 \pi}{3} = \frac {5}{3}. \\ \end{array}
$$

于是，质心的坐标为 $x_0 = y_0 = 1, z_0 = \frac{5}{3}$

【4139】 $\left(\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2} +\frac{z^2}{c^2}\right)^2 = \frac{xyz}{abc} (x > 0,y > 0,z > 0).$

解 作代换 $x = \arccos \varphi \cos \psi, y = b r \sin \varphi \cos \psi, z = c r \sin \psi$ ，则物体的质量为

$$
\begin{array}{l} M = \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \psi \int_ {0} ^ {\cos \varphi \sin \varphi \cos^ {2} \psi \sin \psi} a b c r ^ {2} \cos \psi d r = \frac {1}{3} a b c \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {3} \varphi \sin^ {3} \varphi d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {7} \psi \sin^ {3} \psi d \psi \\ = \frac {1}{3} a b c \cdot \frac {1}{2} B (2, 2) \cdot \frac {1}{2} B (4, 2) = \frac {1}{1 2} a b c \cdot \frac {\Gamma (2) \Gamma (2)}{\Gamma (4)} \cdot \frac {\Gamma (4) \Gamma (2)}{\Gamma (6)} = \frac {a b c}{1 4 4 0}. \\ \end{array}
$$

于是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} x _ {0} = \frac {1}{M} a ^ {2} b c \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \psi \int_ {0} ^ {\cos \varphi \sin \varphi \cos^ {2} \psi \sin \psi} r ^ {3} \cos^ {2} \psi \cos \varphi d r = \frac {a ^ {2} b c}{4 M} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {5} \varphi \sin^ {4} \varphi d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {1 0} \psi \sin^ {1} \psi d \psi \\ = \frac {a ^ {2} b c}{4 M} \cdot \frac {1}{4} B \left(3, \frac {5}{2}\right) B \left(\frac {1 1}{2}, \frac {5}{2}\right) = \frac {a ^ {2} b c}{4 M} \cdot \frac {1}{4} \cdot \frac {\Gamma (3) \Gamma \left(\frac {5}{2}\right)}{\Gamma \left(\frac {1 1}{2}\right)} \cdot \frac {\Gamma \left(\frac {1 1}{2}\right) \Gamma \left(\frac {5}{2}\right)}{\Gamma (8)} \\ = \frac {1 8 a ^ {2} b c \pi}{1 6 \cdot 1 6 \cdot 7 !} \cdot \frac {1 4 4 0}{a b c} = \frac {9 \pi}{4 4 8} a. \\ \end{array}
$$

由对称性知，质心的坐标为 $x_0 = \frac{9\pi}{448} a,\quad y_0 = \frac{9\pi}{448} b,\quad z_0 = \frac{9\pi}{448} c.$

【4140】 $z = x^{2} + y^{2}, z = \frac{1}{2} (x^{2} + y^{2}), x + y = \pm 1, x - y = \pm 1.$

解 作代换： $x - y = u$ ， $x + y = v$ ，则有

$$
x = \frac {u + v}{2}, \quad y = \frac {v - u}{2}, \quad z = \frac {u ^ {2} + v ^ {2}}{4} \quad \text {及} \quad z = \frac {u ^ {2} + v ^ {2}}{2},
$$

且 $|I| = \frac{1}{2}$ 及区域 $V$ 为： $-1\leq u\leq 1, - 1\leq v\leq 1,\frac{u^2 + v^2}{4}\leq z\leq \frac{u^2 + v^2}{2}.$ 于是，

$$
M = \frac {1}{2} \int_ {- 1} ^ {1} d u \int_ {- 1} ^ {1} d v \int_ {\frac {u ^ {2} - v ^ {2}}{3}} ^ {\frac {u ^ {2} - v ^ {2}}{2}} d z = \frac {1}{3}.
$$

$$
x _ {0} = \frac {1}{4 M} \int_ {- 1} ^ {1} d u \int_ {1} ^ {1} d v \int_ {\frac {u ^ {2} - v ^ {2}}{3}} ^ {\frac {u ^ {2} - v ^ {2}}{2}} (u + v) d z = 0,
$$

$$
y _ {0} = \frac {1}{4 M} \int_ {1} ^ {1} d u \int_ {1} ^ {1} d v \int_ {\frac {u ^ {2} + v ^ {2}}{4}} ^ {\frac {u ^ {2} + v ^ {2}}{2}} (v - u) d z = 0,
$$

$$
\begin{array}{l} z _ {n} = \frac {1}{2 M} \int_ {1} ^ {1} d u \int_ {1} ^ {1} d v \int_ {\frac {u ^ {2} - v ^ {2}}{4}} ^ {\frac {u ^ {2} - v ^ {2}}{2}} z d z = \frac {3}{6 4} \cdot \frac {1}{M} \int_ {- 1} ^ {1} d u \int_ {- 1} ^ {1} (u ^ {4} + 2 u ^ {2} v ^ {2} + v ^ {4}) d v \\ = \frac {3}{6 4 M} \int_ {- 1} ^ {1} \left(2 u ^ {4} + \frac {4 u ^ {2}}{3} + \frac {2}{5}\right) d u = \frac {7}{2 0}, \\ \end{array}
$$

于是，质心的坐标为 $x_0 = y_0 = 0, z_0 = \frac{7}{20}$

【4141】 $\frac{x^n}{a^n} +\frac{y^n}{b^n} +\frac{z^n}{c^n} = 1,x = 0,y = 0,z = 0(n > 0,x > 0,y > 0,z > 0).$

解 作代换 $x = a r \cos^{\frac{2}{n}} \varphi \cos^{\frac{2}{n}} \psi, y = b r \sin^{\frac{2}{n}} \varphi \cos^{\frac{2}{n}} \psi, z = c r \sin^{\frac{2}{n}} \psi,$

则有 $|I| = \frac{4}{n^2} abcr^2\sin \frac{2}{n}$ $\varphi \cos \frac{2}{n}$ $\varphi \cos \frac{1}{n}$ $\psi \sin \frac{2}{n} - 1$ $\psi_{\bullet}$ 于是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} M = \frac {4}{n ^ {2}} a b c \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \psi \int_ {0} ^ {1} r ^ {2} \sin^ {\frac {2}{n} - 1} \varphi \cos^ {\frac {2}{n} - 1} \varphi \cos^ {\frac {4}{n} - 1} \psi \sin^ {\frac {2}{n} - 1} \psi d r \\ = \frac {4}{n ^ {2}} a b c \cdot \frac {1}{3} \cdot \frac {1}{2} B \left(\frac {1}{n}, \frac {1}{n}\right) \cdot \frac {1}{2} B \left(\frac {2}{n}, \frac {1}{n}\right) = \frac {a b c}{3 n ^ {2}} \cdot \frac {\Gamma^ {3} \left(\frac {1}{n}\right)}{\Gamma \left(\frac {3}{n}\right)}. \\ \end{array}
$$

于是，质心的坐标为

$$
\begin{array}{l} x _ {0} = \frac {1}{M} \cdot \frac {4}{n ^ {2}} a ^ {2} b c \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \psi \int_ {0} ^ {1} r \cos^ {\frac {2}{n}} \varphi \cos^ {\frac {2}{n}} \psi r ^ {2} \sin^ {\frac {2}{n}} 1 \varphi \cos^ {\frac {2}{n} - 1} \varphi \cos^ {\frac {1}{n} - 1} \psi \sin^ {\frac {2}{n}} 1 \psi d r \\ = \frac {1}{M} \cdot \frac {a ^ {2} b c}{n ^ {2}} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \sin^ {\frac {2}{n} - 1} \varphi \cos^ {\frac {4}{n} - 1} \varphi d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {\frac {6}{n} - 1} \psi \sin^ {\frac {2}{n} - 1} \psi d \psi \\ = \frac {1}{M} \cdot \frac {a ^ {2} b c}{n ^ {2}} \cdot \frac {1}{2} B \left(\frac {1}{n}, \frac {2}{n}\right) \cdot \frac {1}{2} B \left(\frac {3}{n}, \frac {1}{n}\right) = \frac {1}{M} \cdot \frac {a ^ {2} b c}{4 n ^ {2}} \cdot \frac {\Gamma^ {2} \left(\frac {1}{n}\right) \Gamma \left(\frac {2}{n}\right)}{\Gamma \left(\frac {4}{n}\right)} \\ = \frac {3 n ^ {2}}{a b c} \cdot \frac {\Gamma \left(\frac {3}{n}\right)}{\Gamma^ {3} \left(\frac {1}{n}\right)} \cdot \frac {a ^ {2} b c}{4 n ^ {2}} \cdot \frac {\Gamma^ {2} \left(\frac {1}{n}\right) \Gamma \left(\frac {2}{n}\right)}{\Gamma \left(\frac {4}{n}\right)} = \frac {3}{4} \cdot \frac {\Gamma \left(\frac {2}{n}\right) \Gamma \left(\frac {3}{n}\right)}{\Gamma \left(\frac {1}{n}\right) \Gamma \left(\frac {4}{n}\right)} a, \\ \end{array}
$$

同理可求得

$$
y _ {0} = \frac {3}{4} \cdot \frac {\Gamma (\frac {2}{n}) \Gamma (\frac {3}{n})}{\Gamma (\frac {1}{n}) \Gamma (\frac {4}{n})} b, \quad z _ {0} = \frac {3}{4} \cdot \frac {\Gamma (\frac {2}{n}) \Gamma (\frac {3}{n})}{\Gamma (\frac {1}{n}) \Gamma (\frac {4}{n})} c.
$$

【4142】求形状为立方体 $0 \leqslant x \leqslant 1, 0 \leqslant y \leqslant 1, 0 \leqslant z \leqslant 1$ 的物体的质心坐标，设此物体在点 $(x, y, z)$ 的密度等于

$$
\rho = x ^ {\frac {2 \beta - 1}{1 - \alpha}} y ^ {\frac {2 \beta - 1}{1 - \beta}} z ^ {\frac {2 \gamma - 1}{1 - \gamma}},
$$

其中 $0 < \alpha < 1, 0 < \beta < 1, 0 < \gamma < 1$ .

解 物体的质量为

$$
\begin{array}{l} M = \int_ {0} ^ {1} x ^ {\frac {2 \alpha - 1}{1 - \alpha}} d x \int_ {0} ^ {1} y ^ {\frac {2 \beta - 1}{1 - \beta}} d y \int_ {0} ^ {1} z ^ {\frac {2 \gamma - 1}{1 - \gamma}} d z = \left. \frac {1 - \alpha}{\alpha} x ^ {\frac {\alpha}{1 - \alpha}} \right| _ {0} ^ {1} \cdot \left. \frac {1 - \beta}{\beta} y ^ {\frac {\beta}{1 - \beta}} \right| _ {0} ^ {1} \cdot \left. \frac {1 - \gamma}{\gamma} z ^ {\frac {\gamma}{1 - \gamma}} \right| _ {0} ^ {1} \\ = \frac {(1 - \alpha) (1 - \beta) (1 - \gamma)}{\alpha \beta \gamma}. \\ \end{array}
$$

于是，质心的坐标为

$$
x _ {1} = \frac {1}{M} \int_ {a} ^ {1} x ^ {\frac {2 a - 1}{1 - a} - 1} d x \int_ {a} ^ {1} y ^ {\frac {2 b - 1}{1 - b}} d y \int_ {b} ^ {1} z ^ {\frac {2 \gamma - 1}{1 - \gamma}} d z = \frac {\alpha \beta \gamma}{(1 - \alpha) (1 - \beta) (1 - \gamma)} (1 - \alpha) \frac {(1 - \beta) (1 - \gamma)}{\beta \gamma} = \alpha .
$$

同理可求得 $y_{11} = \beta, z_{11} = \gamma$ .

求以下列曲面(参变量是正的)为界的均匀物体对于坐标平面的转动惯量：

【4143】 $\frac{x}{a} +\frac{y}{b} +\frac{z}{c} = 1,x = 0,y = 0,z = 0.$

解 $I_{xy} = \int_{a}^{a}\mathrm{d}x\int_{a}^{b(1 - \frac{x}{a})}\mathrm{d}y\int_{a}^{1(1 - \frac{x}{a} +\frac{y}{b})}z^2\mathrm{d}z = \frac{c^3}{3}\int_{a}^{a}\mathrm{d}x\int_{a}^{b(1 - \frac{x}{a})}\left(1 - \frac{x}{a} -\frac{y}{b}\right)^3\mathrm{d}y$

$$
= - \frac {b c ^ {3}}{1 2} \int_ {0} ^ {u} \left(1 - \frac {x}{a} - \frac {y}{b}\right) ^ {4} \left| _ {0} ^ {b (1 - \frac {x}{a})} \right. \mathrm {d} x = \frac {b c ^ {3}}{1 2} \int_ {0} ^ {u} \left(1 - \frac {x}{a}\right) ^ {4} \mathrm {d} x = \frac {a b c ^ {3}}{6 0}.
$$

利用对称性可得 $I_{yz} = \frac{a^3bc}{60}, \quad I_{zx} = \frac{ab^3c}{60}.$

【4144】 $\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2} +\frac{z^2}{c^2} = 1.$

提示 作代换 $x = \arccos \varphi \cos \psi, y = brsin\varphi \cos \psi, z = cr\sin \psi$ ，并利用对称性。

解 若令 $x = \arccos \varphi \cos \psi, y = b r \sin \varphi \cos \psi, z = c r \sin \psi$ ，则有

$$
I _ {r y} = a b c ^ {3} \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {- \frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \psi \int_ {0} ^ {1} r ^ {3} \cos \psi \sin^ {2} \psi d r = \frac {a b c ^ {3}}{5} \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {\frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos \psi \sin^ {2} \psi d \psi = \frac {a b c ^ {3}}{1 5} 2 \pi \sin^ {3} \psi \left| _ {- \frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} = \frac {4}{1 5} \pi a b c ^ {3}. \right.
$$

利用对称性可得 $I_{yz} = \frac{4}{15}\pi a^3 bc,\qquad I_{zx} = \frac{4}{15}\pi ab^3 c.$

【4145】 $\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2} = \frac{z^2}{c^2},z = c.$

解 若令 $x = \arccos \varphi, y = brsin\varphi$ ，则有

$$
I _ {x y} = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {1} a b r d r \int_ {\sigma} ^ {e} z ^ {2} d z = \frac {1}{5} \pi a b c ^ {3},
$$

$$
I _ {y z} = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {1} a b r d r \int_ {\sigma} ^ {c} (a r \cos \varphi) ^ {2} d z = a ^ {3} b c \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} \cos^ {2} \varphi d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {1} (1 - r) r ^ {3} d r = \frac {1}{2 0} \pi a ^ {3} b c.
$$

利用对称性可得 $I_{zr} = \frac{1}{20}\pi ab^3 c.$

【4146】 $\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2} +\frac{z^2}{c^2} = 1,\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2} = \frac{x}{a}.$

解 若令 $x = \arccos \varphi, y = b r \sin \varphi$ ，则得区域 $V$ 为

$$
- \frac {\pi}{2} \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}, \quad 0 \leqslant r \leqslant \cos \varphi , \quad - c \sqrt {1 - r ^ {2}} \leqslant z \leqslant c \sqrt {1 - r ^ {2}}.
$$

于是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} I _ {r y} = \int_ {\frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \mathrm {d} \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\cos \varphi} a b r \mathrm {d} r \int_ {- c \sqrt {1 - r ^ {2}}} ^ {c \sqrt {1 - r ^ {2}}} z ^ {2} \mathrm {d} z = \frac {2}{3} a b c ^ {3} \int_ {- \frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \mathrm {d} \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\cos \varphi} (1 - r ^ {2}) ^ {\frac {3}{2}} r \mathrm {d} r \\ = \frac {2}{1 5} a b c ^ {3} \int_ {- \frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \left[ 1 - \left(\sin^ {2} \varphi\right) ^ {\frac {\bar {s}}{2}} \right] d \varphi = \frac {4}{1 5} a b c ^ {3} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \left(1 - \sin^ {5} \varphi\right) d \varphi \\ = \frac {4}{1 5} a b c ^ {3} \left(\varphi + \cos \varphi - \frac {2}{3} \cos^ {3} \varphi + \frac {1}{5} \cos^ {5} \varphi\right) \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} = \frac {2 a b c ^ {3}}{2 2 5} (1 5 \pi - 1 6). \\ \end{array}
$$

$$
\begin{array}{l} I _ {y z} = \int_ {\frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\cos \varphi} a b r d r \int_ {c \sqrt {1 - r ^ {2}}} ^ {r \sqrt {1 - r ^ {2}}} (a r \cos \varphi) ^ {2} d z = 2 a ^ {3} b c \int_ {- \frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {2} \varphi d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\cos \varphi} \sqrt {1 - r ^ {2}} r ^ {3} d r \\ = 2 a ^ {3} b c \int_ {- \frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {2} \varphi d \varphi \int_ {\varphi} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} | \sin t | \sin t \cos^ {3} t d t = 2 a ^ {3} b c \int_ {\frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {2} \varphi \left\{\int_ {\varphi} ^ {0} | \sin t | \sin t \cos^ {3} t d t \right. \\ + \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} | \sin t | \sin t \cos^ {3} t d t \Bigg \} d \varphi = 2 a ^ {3} b c \int_ {- \frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \left\{\frac {2}{1 5} + \int_ {\varphi} ^ {0} | \sin t | \sin t \cos^ {3} t d t \right\} \cos^ {2} \varphi d \varphi \\ = 2 a ^ {3} b c \left\{\frac {\pi}{1 5} + \int_ {- \frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {0} \left(- \int_ {\varphi} ^ {0} \sin^ {2} t \cos^ {3} t d t\right) \cos^ {2} \varphi d \varphi + \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \left(\int_ {\varphi} ^ {0} \sin^ {2} t \cos^ {3} t d t\right) \cos^ {2} \varphi d \varphi \right\} \\ = 2 a ^ {3} b c \left\{\frac {\pi}{1 5} + \int_ {0} ^ {- \frac {\pi}{2}} \left(\frac {1}{5} \sin^ {5} \varphi - \frac {1}{3} \sin^ {3} \varphi\right) \cos^ {2} \varphi d \varphi + \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \left(\frac {1}{5} \sin^ {5} \varphi - \frac {1}{3} \sin^ {3} \varphi\right) \cos^ {2} \varphi d \varphi \right\} \\ = 2 a ^ {3} b c \left(\frac {\pi}{1 5} - \frac {9 2}{1 5 7 5}\right) = \frac {2 a ^ {3} b c}{1 5 7 5} (1 0 5 \pi - 9 2), \\ \end{array}
$$

$$
\begin{array}{l} I _ {z r} = \int_ {\frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\cos \varphi} a b r d r \int_ {c \sqrt {1 - r ^ {2}}} ^ {c \sqrt {1 - r ^ {2}}} (b r \sin \varphi) ^ {2} d z = 2 a b ^ {3} c \int_ {\frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\cos \varphi} \sqrt {1 - r ^ {2}} r ^ {3} \sin^ {2} \varphi d r \\ = 2 a b ^ {3} c \int_ {- \frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \sin^ {2} \varphi d \varphi \int_ {\varphi} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} | \sin t | \sin t \cos^ {3} t d t = 2 a b ^ {3} c \int_ {- \frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \left\{\frac {2}{1 5} + \int_ {\varphi} ^ {0} | \sin t | \sin t \cos^ {3} t d t \right\} \sin^ {2} \varphi d \varphi \\ = 2 a b ^ {3} c \left\{\frac {\pi}{1 5} + \int_ {0} ^ {- \frac {\pi}{2}} \left(\frac {1}{5} \sin^ {5} \varphi - \frac {1}{3} \sin^ {3} \varphi\right) \sin^ {2} \varphi d \varphi + \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \left(\frac {1}{5} \sin^ {5} \varphi - \frac {1}{3} \sin^ {3} \varphi\right) \sin^ {2} \varphi d \varphi \right\} \\ = 2 a b ^ {3} c \left(\frac {\pi}{1 5} - \frac {2 7 2}{1 5 7 5}\right) = \frac {2 a b ^ {3} c}{1 5 7 5} (1 0 5 \pi - 2 7 2). \\ \end{array}
$$

【4147】 $\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2} = 2\frac{z}{c},\quad \frac{x}{a} +\frac{y}{b} = \frac{z}{c}.$

解两曲面在 $Oxy$ 平面上的投影为 $\frac{x^2}{a^2} +\frac{y^2}{b^2} -2\frac{x}{a} -2\frac{y}{b} = 0$ 即 $\left(\frac{x}{a} -1\right)^2 +\left(\frac{y}{b} -1\right)^2 = 2.$ 若令

$$
\frac {x}{a} = 1 + r \cos \varphi , \quad \frac {y}{b} = 1 + r \sin \varphi ,
$$

则得区域 $V$ 为

$$
0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant 2 \pi , \quad 0 \leqslant r \leqslant \sqrt {2}, \quad c \left[ 1 + \frac {r ^ {2}}{2} + r (\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi) \right] \leqslant z \leqslant c [ 2 + r (\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi) ].
$$

于是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} I _ {r y} = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt {2}} a b r d r \int_ {c [ 1 + \frac {r ^ {2}}{2} + r (\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi) ]} ^ {c [ 2 + r (\cos \varphi - \sin \varphi) ]} z ^ {2} d z = \frac {1}{3} a b c ^ {3} \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt {2}} r \left[ 8 + 1 2 r (\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi) + 6 r ^ {2} (\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi) ^ {2} \right. \\ \left. - \left(1 + \frac {r ^ {2}}{2}\right) ^ {3} - 3 \left(1 + \frac {r ^ {2}}{2}\right) ^ {2} r (\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi) - 3 \left(1 + \frac {r ^ {2}}{2}\right) r ^ {2} (\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi) ^ {2} \right] d r = \frac {7}{2} \pi a b c ^ {3}. \\ \end{array}
$$

$$
\begin{array}{l} I _ {y z} = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt {2}} a ^ {3} b r (1 + r \cos \varphi) ^ {2} d r \int_ {c [ 1 + \frac {r ^ {2}}{2} + r (\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi) ]} ^ {c [ 2 + r (\cos \varphi + \sin \varphi) ]} d z = a ^ {3} b c \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt {2}} r (1 + 2 r \cos \varphi + r ^ {2} \cos^ {2} \varphi) \left(1 - \frac {r ^ {2}}{2}\right) d r \\ = \frac {4}{3} \pi a ^ {3} b c. \\ \end{array}
$$

利用对称性得 $I_{zz} = \frac{4}{3}\pi ab^3 c.$

# 求以下列曲面为界的均匀物体对于 $Oz$ 轴的转动惯量：

【4148】 $z = x^{2} + y^{2},x + y = \pm 1,x - y = \pm 1,z = 0.$

提示 注意 $I_{z} = I_{zx} + I_{xy}$ ，并令 $x + y = u$ ， $x - y = v$

解曲面所界的均匀物体对于 $Oz$ 轴的转动惯量记作 $I_{z}$ ，则 $I_{z} = I_{zx} + I_{zy}$

若令 $x + y = u$ ， $x - y = v$ ，则有 $x = \frac{u + v}{2},y = \frac{u - v}{2},z = \frac{u^2 + v^2}{2}$ 且 $|I| = \frac{1}{2}$ .于是，

$$
I _ {z} = \int_ {- 1} ^ {1} d u \int_ {- 1} ^ {1} d v \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {u ^ {2} - v ^ {2}}{2}} \frac {1}{2} \left\{\left(\frac {u - v}{2}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {u + v}{2}\right) ^ {2} \right\} d z = \int_ {1} ^ {1} d u \int_ {1} ^ {1} \frac {(u ^ {2} + v ^ {2}) ^ {2}}{8} d v = \frac {1 4}{4 5}.
$$

【4149】 $x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2} = 2, x^{2} + y^{2} = z^{2} (z > 0)$

解 若令 $x = r\cos \varphi, y = r\sin \varphi$ ，则有 $0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant 2\pi, 0 \leqslant r \leqslant 1, r \leqslant z \leqslant \sqrt{2 - r^2}$ 。

于是， $I_{z} = \int_{0}^{2\pi}\mathrm{d}\varphi \int_{0}^{1}r\mathrm{d}r\int_{r}^{\sqrt{2 - r^{2}}}r^{2}\mathrm{d}z = \int_{0}^{2\pi}\mathrm{d}\varphi \int_{0}^{1}(r^{3}\sqrt{2 - r^{2}} -r^{4})\mathrm{d}r = \int_{0}^{2\pi}\left(\frac{8\sqrt{2} - 7}{15} -\frac{1}{5}\right)\mathrm{d}\varphi^{*}$

$$
= \frac {4 \pi}{1 5} (4 \sqrt {2} - 5).
$$

\*）作代换 $r = \sqrt{2}\sin t$

【4150】求质量为 $M$ 的非均匀球体 $x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2} \leqslant R^{2}$ 对于其直径的转动惯量. 设球内各点 $P(x, y, z)$ 的密度与该点至球心距离成正比.

解 不失一般性，取 $Oz$ 轴在球内的一段作为直径.若令

$$
x = r \cos \varphi \cos \psi , y = r \sin \varphi \cos \psi , z = r \sin \psi ,
$$

则质量为 $M = \int_{0}^{2\pi}\mathrm{d}\varphi \int_{\frac{\pi}{2}}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}\mathrm{d}\psi \int_{0}^{R}r^{2}\cos \psi \cdot kr\mathrm{d}r = k\pi R^{4},$

由此得 $k = \frac{M}{\pi R^4}$ . 从而, 密度 $\rho = \frac{Mr}{\pi R^4}$ . 于是, 所求的转动惯量为

$$
I _ {z} = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {- \frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \psi \int_ {0} ^ {R} r ^ {2} \cos^ {2} \psi \cdot \frac {M r ^ {3}}{\pi R ^ {4}} \cos \psi d r = \frac {2 M}{R ^ {4}} \left(\int_ {- \frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {3} \psi d \psi\right) \left(\int_ {0} ^ {R} r ^ {5} d r\right) = \frac {4 M R ^ {2}}{9}.
$$

【4151】证明等式： $I_{t} = I_{t_{0}} + Md^{2}$

其中 $I_{l}$ 为物体对某轴 $l$ 的转动惯量， $I_{l_0}$ 为对平行于 $l$ 并通过物体质心的轴 $l_0$ 的转动惯量， $d$ 为此二轴之间的距离及 $M$ 为物体的质量。

证取质心为坐标原点 $O, z$ 轴与 $l_{0}$ 重合， $l$ 与 $Oxy$ 平面的交点为 $(\zeta, \eta, 0)$ ，如图8.59所示，则

$$
\begin{array}{l} I _ {i} = \iiint_ {V} \left[ (x - \zeta) ^ {2} + (y - \eta) ^ {2} \right] \rho d v \\ = \iiint_ {V} \left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}\right) \rho d v + \left(\zeta^ {2} + \eta^ {2}\right) \iiint_ {V} \rho d v - 2 \zeta \iiint_ {V} x \rho d v - 2 \eta \iiint_ {V} y \rho d v \tag {1} \\ \end{array}
$$

由于质心在原点，故 $x_0 = y_0 = 0$ ，即

$$
x _ {0} = \frac {1}{M} \iiint_ {V} x \rho \mathrm {d} v = 0 \quad \text {及} \quad y _ {0} = \frac {1}{M} \iiint_ {V} y \rho \mathrm {d} v = 0,
$$

并且 $M = \iiint_{V} \rho \mathrm{d}v, d^2 = \zeta^2 + \eta^2$ ，代入（1）式，最后得

![](images/87d3355d644b7a667405b8411d00c8f4095e51329d719f6684af95011380f058.jpg)  
图8.59

$$
I _ {t} = I _ {t _ {0}} + M d ^ {2}.
$$

【4152】证明：占有区域 $V$ 的物体对过其质心 $O(0,0,0)$ 并与坐标轴成角 $\alpha, \beta, \gamma$ 的轴 $l$ 的转动惯量等于： $I_{l} = I_{x}\cos^{2}\alpha + I_{y}\cos^{2}\beta + I_{z}\cos^{2}\gamma - 2K_{xy}\cos\alpha\cos\beta - 2K_{yz}\cos\beta\cos\gamma - 2K_{zx}\cos\alpha\cos\gamma,$

其中 $I_{r}, I_{y}, I_{z}$ 为物体对坐标轴的转动惯量，而

$$
K _ {r y} = \iiint_ {V} \rho r y d x d y d z, \quad K _ {x z} = \iiint_ {V} \rho r z d x d y d z, \quad K _ {y z} = \iiint_ {V} \rho y z d x d y d z
$$

为惯性积.

证 如图8.60所示. 距离

$$
\begin{array}{l} d = \frac {\mid \overrightarrow {O M} \times \overrightarrow {O M ^ {\prime}} \mid}{\mid \overrightarrow {O M ^ {\prime}} \mid} \\ = \frac {1}{r} \sqrt {\left| \begin{array}{l l} y & z \\ r \cos \beta & r \cos \gamma \end{array} \right| ^ {2} + \left| \begin{array}{l l} z & x \\ r \cos \gamma & r \cos \alpha \end{array} \right| ^ {2} + \left| \begin{array}{l l} x & y \\ r \cos \alpha & r \cos \beta \end{array} \right| ^ {2}} \\ \end{array}
$$

![](images/048491b0a757ba828b505b5b9e961a18f3da67fe91b219eb389c43f20ddeb7d6.jpg)  
图8.60

其中 $r = |\overrightarrow{OM}|$ . 由于 $\cos^2\alpha + \cos^2\beta + \cos^2\gamma = 1$ ，故有

$$
d ^ {2} = \left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}\right) \cos^ {2} \gamma + \left(y ^ {2} + z ^ {2}\right) \cos^ {2} \alpha + \left(z ^ {2} + x ^ {2}\right) \cos^ {2} \beta - 2 x y \cos \alpha \cos \beta - 2 y z \cos \beta \cos \gamma - 2 x z \cos \alpha \cos \gamma .
$$

于是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} I _ {t} = \iiint_ {V} \rho d ^ {2} \cdot \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y \mathrm {d} z \\ = \cos^ {2} \gamma \iiint_ {V} \rho \cdot (x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}) d x d y d z + \cos^ {2} \alpha \iiint_ {V} \rho \cdot (y ^ {2} + z ^ {2}) d x d y d z + \cos^ {2} \beta \iiint_ {V} \rho \cdot (x ^ {2} + z ^ {2}) d x d y d z \\ - 2 \cos \alpha \cos \beta \iiint_ {V} \rho x y d x d y d z - 2 \cos \beta \cos \gamma \iiint_ {V} \rho y z d x d y d z - 2 \cos \gamma \cos \alpha \iiint_ {V} \rho x z d x d y d z \\ = I _ {r} \cos^ {2} \alpha + I _ {y} \cos^ {2} \beta + I _ {z} \cos^ {2} \gamma - 2 K _ {x y} \cos \alpha \cos \beta - 2 K _ {x z} \cos \beta \cos \gamma - 2 K _ {z r} \cos \gamma \cos \alpha . \\ \end{array}
$$

证毕.

【4153】求密度为 $\rho_0$ 的均匀圆柱体 $x^{2} + y^{2}\leqslant a^{2}, - h\leqslant z\leqslant h$ 对直线 $x = y = z$ 的转动惯量.

提示 利用4152题的结果.

解直线 $x = y = z$ 通过圆柱体的质心 $O(0,0,0)$ 且具有方向余弦 $\cos \alpha = \cos \beta = \cos \gamma = \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}.$ 若取极坐标，

则有 $I_{r} = \int_{0}^{2\pi}\mathrm{d}\varphi \int_{0}^{a}r\mathrm{d}r\int_{-h}^{h}\rho_{0}(r^{2}\sin^{2}\varphi +z^{2})\mathrm{d}z = \left(\frac{1}{2}\pi a^{4}h + \frac{2}{3}\pi a^{2}h^{3}\right)\rho_{0},$

$$
I _ {y} = \int_ {1 1} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {1 1} ^ {4} r d r \int_ {h} ^ {h} \rho_ {0} \left(r ^ {2} \cos^ {2} \varphi + z ^ {2}\right) d z = \left(\frac {1}{2} \pi a ^ {1} h + \frac {2}{3} \pi a ^ {2} h ^ {3}\right) \rho_ {0},
$$

$$
I _ {z} = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} \mathrm {d} \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {a} r \mathrm {d} r \int_ {h} ^ {h} \rho_ {0} r ^ {2} \mathrm {d} z = \pi h a ^ {4} \rho_ {0}, \quad K _ {c y} = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} \mathrm {d} \varphi \int_ {1 1} ^ {a} r \mathrm {d} r \int_ {h} ^ {h} \rho_ {0} r ^ {2} \cos \varphi \sin \varphi \mathrm {d} z = 0,
$$

$$
K _ {x z} = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} \mathrm {d} \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {u} r \mathrm {d} r \int_ {h} ^ {h} \rho_ {0} r \sin \varphi z \mathrm {d} z = 0, \quad K _ {z c} = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} \mathrm {d} \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {u} r \mathrm {d} r \int_ {- h} ^ {h} \rho_ {0} r \cos \varphi z \mathrm {d} z = 0,
$$

于是，利用4152题结果即得

$$
\begin{array}{l} I _ {t} = I _ {t} \cos^ {2} \alpha + I _ {y} \cos^ {2} \beta + I _ {z} \cos^ {2} \gamma - 2 K _ {r y} \cos \alpha \cos \beta - 2 K _ {y z} \cos \beta \cos \gamma - 2 K _ {z r} \cos \alpha \cos \gamma \\ = \frac {\rho_ {0}}{3} \left(\frac {1}{2} \pi a ^ {4} h + \frac {2}{3} \pi a ^ {2} h ^ {3} + \frac {1}{2} \pi a ^ {4} h + \frac {2}{3} \pi a ^ {2} h ^ {3} + \pi a ^ {4} h\right) = \frac {2}{3} \pi \rho_ {0} a ^ {2} h \left(a ^ {2} + \frac {2}{3} h ^ {2}\right) = \frac {M}{3} \left(a ^ {2} + \frac {2}{3} h ^ {2}\right), \\ \end{array}
$$

其中 $M = 2\pi \rho_{0}a^{2}h$ 为圆柱体的质量.

【4154】求密度为 $\rho_{\mathrm{a}}$ ，以曲面 $(x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2})^{2} = a^{2}(x^{2} + y^{2})$

为界的均匀物体对坐标原点的转动惯量.

解若令 $x = r\cos \varphi \cos \psi ,y = r\sin \varphi \cos \psi ,z = r\sin \psi$ ，则对坐标原点的转动惯量为

$$
I _ {2} = \int_ {1 1} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {- \frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \psi \int_ {0} ^ {a \cos \psi} \rho_ {n} \cdot r ^ {2} \cdot r ^ {2} \cos \psi d r = \frac {4 \pi \rho_ {0} a ^ {5}}{5} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos^ {6} \psi d \psi = \frac {4 \pi \rho_ {0} a ^ {5}}{5} \cdot \frac {5 \pi}{3 2} ^ {*}) = \frac {\pi^ {2} a ^ {5} \rho_ {0}}{8}.
$$

\*) 利用2282题的结果.

【4155】求密度为 $\rho_{0}$ 的均匀球体 $\xi^{2} + \eta^{2} + \zeta^{2} \leqslant R^{2}$ 在点 $(x, y, z)$ 的牛顿引力势.

提示 取 $(\xi)$ 轴通过点 $P(x, y, z)$ ，即易获解。

解 由对称性显然可知，所求的牛顿引力势与 $\xi, \eta, \zeta$ 轴取的方向无关。今取 $O\zeta$ 轴通过点 $P(x, y, z)$ ，即得牛顿引力势

$$
u (x, y, z) = \iiint_ {\xi^ {2} - \eta^ {2} + \zeta^ {2} \leqslant R ^ {2}} \rho_ {0} \frac {\mathrm {d} \xi \mathrm {d} \eta \mathrm {d} \zeta}{\sqrt {\xi^ {2} + \eta^ {2} + (\zeta - r) ^ {2}}} = \rho_ {0} \int_ {R} ^ {R} \mathrm {d} \zeta \iint_ {\xi^ {2} - \eta^ {2} \leqslant R ^ {2}} \frac {\mathrm {d} \xi \mathrm {d} \eta}{\sqrt {\xi^ {2} + \eta^ {2} + (\zeta - r) ^ {2}}},
$$

其中 $r = \sqrt{x^2 + y^2 + z^2}$ 。积分之，得

$$
u (x, y, z) = 2 \pi \rho_ {0} \int_ {R} ^ {R} (\sqrt {R ^ {2} - 2 r \zeta + r ^ {2}} - | \zeta - r |) d \zeta .
$$

由于 $\int_{R}^{R}\sqrt{R^2 - 2r\zeta + r^2}\mathrm{d}\zeta = \frac{1}{3r} [(R + r)^3 -|R - r|^3 ] = \left\{ \begin{array}{ll} \frac{2}{3} R^3\frac{1}{r} +2rR, & r > R,\\ \frac{2}{3} r^2 +2R^2, & r\leqslant R, \end{array} \right.$

及 $\int_{-R}^{R}|\zeta -r|\mathrm{d}\zeta = \left\{ \begin{array}{ll}2Rr, & r > R,\\ r^2 +R^2, & r\leqslant R. \end{array} \right.$

因而，最后得 $u(x,y,z) = \begin{cases} \frac{4}{3r}\pi R^3\rho_0, & r > R,\\ 2\pi \rho_0\left(R^2 -\frac{1}{3} r^2\right), & r\leqslant R. \end{cases}$

由以上结果可以得到下面两个推论：

(1)在球外一点上的牛顿引力势，与将球的全部质量集中在它的中心处时一样；  
(2)如考察一个内半径为 $R_{1}$ 而外半径为 $R_{2}$ 的空心球，则它在位于其空隙处的一点 $(r < R)$ 上的牛顿引力势可表示成差

$$
u (x, y, z) = u _ {2} (x, y, z) - u _ {1} (x, y, z) = \left(R _ {2} ^ {2} - \frac {1}{3} r ^ {2}\right) 2 \pi \rho_ {0} - \left(R _ {1} ^ {2} - \frac {1}{3} r ^ {2}\right) 2 \pi \rho_ {0} = 2 \pi \left(R _ {2} ^ {2} - R _ {1} ^ {2}\right) \rho_ {0}.
$$

它与 $r$ 无关，故空心球体在其空隙范围内的引力势保持一个常数值。

【4156】求球壳层 $R_1^2 \leqslant \xi^2 + \eta^2 + \zeta^2 \leqslant R_2^2$ 在点 $P(x, y, z)$ 的牛顿引力势. 设密度 $\rho = f(R)$ , 其中 $f$ 为已知函数, 而 $R = \sqrt{\xi^2 + \eta^2 + \zeta^2}$ .

提示 仿4155题.

解取 $O\zeta$ 轴通过点 $P(x,y,z)$ ，即得牛顿引力势

$$
u (x, y, z) = \iiint_ {R _ {1} ^ {2} \leqslant \xi^ {2} + \eta^ {2} + \zeta^ {2} \leqslant R _ {2} ^ {2}} f (\sqrt {\xi^ {2} + \eta^ {2} + \zeta^ {2}}) \frac {\mathrm {d} \xi \mathrm {d} \eta \mathrm {d} \zeta}{\sqrt {\xi^ {2} + \eta^ {2} + (\zeta - r) ^ {2}}},
$$

其中 $r = x^2 + y^2 + z^2$ .

若引入球坐标，即得

$$
\begin{array}{l} u (x, y, z) = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {- \frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \psi \int_ {R _ {1}} ^ {R _ {2}} \rho^ {2} f (\rho) \cos \psi \frac {d \rho}{\sqrt {\rho^ {2} + r ^ {2} - 2 \rho r \sin \psi}} = 2 \pi \int_ {R _ {1}} ^ {R _ {2}} d \rho \int_ {- \frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \rho^ {2} f (\rho) \frac {\cos \psi d \psi}{\sqrt {\rho^ {2} + r ^ {2} - 2 \rho r \sin \psi}} \\ = 2 \pi \int_ {R _ {1}} ^ {R _ {2}} \rho^ {2} f (\rho) \left(- \frac {1}{\rho r} \sqrt {\rho^ {2} + r ^ {2} - 2 \rho r \sin \psi}\right) \Bigg | _ {- \frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} d \rho = 2 \pi \int_ {R _ {1}} ^ {R _ {2}} \rho^ {2} f (\rho) \left\{- \frac {1}{\rho r} [ | \rho - r | - (\rho + r) ] \right\} d \rho \\ = \left\{ \begin{array}{l l} 4 \pi \int_ {R _ {1}} ^ {R _ {2}} \rho f (\rho) d \rho , & \rho > r, \\ 4 \pi \int_ {R _ {1}} ^ {R _ {2}} \frac {\rho^ {2}}{r} f (\rho) d \rho , & \rho \leqslant r. \end{array} \right. \\ \end{array}
$$

合并之，最后得 $u(x,y,z) = 4\pi \int_{R_1}^{R_2}f(\rho)\min \left(\frac{\rho^2}{r},\rho\right)\mathrm{d}\rho .$

【4157】求密度 $\rho_0$ 恒定的圆柱体 $\xi^2 +\eta^2\leqslant a^2,0\leqslant \zeta \leqslant h$ 在点 $P(0,0,z)$ 的牛顿引力势.

解 若引用柱坐标，即得

$$
\begin{array}{l} u (x, y, z) = \rho_ {0} \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {h} d \zeta \int_ {0} ^ {a} \frac {r d r}{\sqrt {r ^ {2} + (\zeta - z) ^ {2}}} = 2 \pi \rho_ {0} \int_ {0} ^ {h} \sqrt {r ^ {2} + (\zeta - z) ^ {2}} \left. \right| _ {0} ^ {a} d \zeta \\ = 2 \pi \rho_ {0} \int_ {0} ^ {h} \left[ \sqrt {a ^ {2} + (\zeta - z) ^ {2}} - | \zeta - z | \right] d \zeta \\ = 2 \pi \rho_ {0} \left[ \frac {\zeta - z}{2} \sqrt {a ^ {2} + (\zeta - z) ^ {2}} + \frac {a ^ {2}}{2} \ln | (\zeta - z) | + \sqrt {a ^ {2} + (\zeta - z) ^ {2}} - \frac {(\zeta - z) | \zeta - z |}{2} \right] \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {h} \\ = \pi \rho_ {0} \left\{(h - z) \sqrt {a ^ {2} + (h - z) ^ {2}} + z \sqrt {a ^ {2} + z ^ {2}} - [ (h - z) | h - z | + z | z | ] + a ^ {2} \ln \left| \frac {h - z + \sqrt {a ^ {2} + (h - z) ^ {2}}}{- z + \sqrt {a ^ {2} + z ^ {2}}} \right| \right\}. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4158】半径为 $R$ 质量为 $M$ 的均匀球体 $\xi^2 +\eta^2 +\zeta^2\leqslant R^2$ 以怎样的力吸引质量为 $m$ 的质点 $P(0,0,a)$ ?

解引力在 $Ox$ 轴和 $Oy$ 轴上的投影为零，即 $X = Y = 0$ ，而在 $Oz$ 轴上的投影为

$$
Z = k \rho_ {0} m \iiint_ {\xi^ {2} + \eta^ {2} + \zeta^ {2} \leqslant R ^ {2}} \frac {(\zeta - a) d \xi d \eta d \zeta}{\left[ \xi^ {2} + \eta^ {2} + (\zeta - a) ^ {2} \right] ^ {\frac {3}{2}}} = k m \rho_ {0} \int_ {- R} ^ {R} (\zeta - a) d \zeta \iint_ {\xi^ {2} + \eta^ {2} \leqslant R ^ {2} - \zeta^ {2}} \frac {d \xi d \eta}{\left[ \xi^ {2} + \eta^ {2} + (\zeta - a) ^ {2} \right] ^ {\frac {3}{2}}}
$$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = k m \rho_ {0} \int_ {R} ^ {R} (\zeta - a) d \zeta \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt {R ^ {2} - \zeta^ {2}}} \frac {r d r}{\left[ r ^ {2} + (\zeta - a) ^ {2} \right] ^ {\frac {3}{2}}} = 2 \pi k m \rho_ {0} \int_ {- R} ^ {R} (\zeta - a) \left(\frac {1}{| \zeta - a |} - \frac {1}{\sqrt {R ^ {2} - 2 a \zeta + a ^ {2}}}\right) d \zeta \\ = 2 \pi k m \rho_ {0} \int_ {R} ^ {R} \operatorname {s g n} (\zeta - a) d \zeta - 2 \pi k m \rho_ {0} \int_ {- R} ^ {R} \frac {(\zeta - a) d \zeta}{\sqrt {R ^ {2} - 2 a \zeta + a ^ {2}}}, \\ \end{array}
$$

其中 $\rho_{0} = \frac{3M}{4\pi R^{3}}$

分别求上述两个积分：

当 $a \geqslant R$ 时， $\int_{-R}^{R} \operatorname{sgn}(\zeta - a) \mathrm{d}\zeta = -\int_{-R}^{R} \mathrm{d}\zeta = -2R,$

当 $a < R$ 时， $\int_{-R}^{R}\operatorname{sgn}(\zeta - a)\mathrm{d}\zeta = -\int_{-R}^{a}\mathrm{d}\zeta + \int_{a}^{R}\mathrm{d}\zeta = -2a;$

而

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int_ {R} ^ {R} \frac {(\zeta - a) d \zeta}{\sqrt {R ^ {2} - 2 a \zeta + a ^ {2}}} = - \frac {1}{2 a} \int_ {R} ^ {R} \frac {R ^ {2} + a ^ {2} - 2 a \zeta - (R ^ {2} + a ^ {2})}{\sqrt {R ^ {2} - 2 a \zeta + a ^ {2}}} d \zeta - a \int_ {- R} ^ {R} \frac {d \zeta}{\sqrt {R ^ {2} - 2 a \zeta + a ^ {2}}} \\ = - \frac {1}{2 a} \int_ {- R} ^ {R} \sqrt {R ^ {2} + a ^ {2} - 2 a \zeta} d \zeta + \left(\frac {R ^ {2} + a ^ {2}}{2 a} - a\right) \int_ {- R} ^ {R} \frac {d \zeta}{\sqrt {R ^ {2} + a ^ {2} - 2 a \zeta}} \\ = - \frac {1}{2 a} \int_ {- R} ^ {R} \sqrt {R ^ {2} + a ^ {2} - 2 a \zeta} d \zeta + \frac {R ^ {2} - a ^ {2}}{2 a} \int_ {- R} ^ {R} \frac {d \zeta}{\sqrt {R ^ {2} + a ^ {2} - 2 a \zeta}}, \\ \end{array}
$$

当 $a \geqslant R$ 时，将上式右端分别积分，得结果：

$$
\begin{array}{l} \left[ \frac {1}{4 a ^ {2}} \left(R ^ {2} + a ^ {2} - 2 a \zeta\right) ^ {\frac {3}{2}} \cdot \frac {2}{3} + \frac {R ^ {2} - a ^ {2}}{2 a} \left(- \frac {1}{2 a}\right) \cdot 2 \sqrt {R ^ {2} + a ^ {2} - 2 a \zeta} \right] \Bigg | _ {- R} ^ {R} \\ = \frac {1}{6 a ^ {2}} \left[ (a - R) ^ {3} - (a + R) ^ {3} \right] - \frac {R ^ {2} - a ^ {2}}{2 a ^ {2}} \left[ (a - R) - (a + R) \right] = \frac {2 R ^ {4}}{3 a ^ {2}} - 2 R; \\ \end{array}
$$

当 $a < R$ 时，积分得结果：

$$
\frac {1}{6 a ^ {2}} \left[ (R - a) ^ {3} - (a + R) ^ {3} \right] - \frac {R ^ {2} - a ^ {2}}{2 a ^ {2}} \left[ (R - a) - (R + a) \right] = - \frac {4 a}{3}.
$$

于是，当 $a \geqslant R$ 时，则 $Z = 2\pi km\rho_0\left(-2R - \frac{2R^3}{3a^2} + 2R\right) = -\frac{4}{3a^2}\pi km\rho_0R^3 = -\frac{kMm}{a^2}$

当 $a < R$ 时，则 $Z = 2\pi km\rho_0\left(-2a + \frac{4a}{3}\right) = -\frac{4}{3}\pi akm\rho_0 = -\frac{kMm}{R^3} a.$

从以上结果可以得到下面两个推论：

（1）位于球外的一点 $(a\geqslant R)$ 因球体而受到的引力相当于将球体的全部质量 $M = \frac{4}{3}\pi R^3\rho_0$ 集中在它的中心处时受到的引力，引力的方向朝向球心；  
（2）对于在球里面的一点 $(a < R)$ 来说，引力与 $R$ 无关，其大小与 $R = a$ 时的情况一样，即在点 $P$ 外面的球壳部分对 $P$ 点的引力为零.

【4159】求密度为 $\rho_{0}$ 的均匀圆柱体 $\xi^{2} + \eta^{2} \leqslant a^{2}, 0 \leqslant \zeta \leqslant h$ 对单位质量质点 $P(0,0,z)$ 的引力.

解 由对称性知，引力在 $Ox$ 轴和 $Oy$ 轴上的投影为零，即 $X = Y = 0$ 。若引用柱坐标，即得引力在 $Oz$ 轴上的投影为

$$
\begin{array}{l} Z = k \rho_ {0} \iint_ {\xi^ {2} - \eta^ {2} <   a ^ {2}} d \xi d \eta \int_ {0} ^ {h} \frac {(\zeta - z) d \zeta}{\left[ \xi^ {2} + \eta^ {2} + (\zeta - z) ^ {2} \right] ^ {\frac {3}{2}}} = k \rho_ {0} \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {0} ^ {a} r d r \int_ {0} ^ {h} \frac {(\zeta - z) d \zeta}{\left[ r ^ {2} + (\zeta - z) ^ {2} \right] ^ {\frac {3}{2}}} \\ = 2 \pi k \rho_ {0} \int_ {1} ^ {a} r \left[ \frac {1}{\sqrt {r ^ {2} + z ^ {2}}} - \frac {1}{\sqrt {r ^ {2} + (h - z) ^ {2}}} \right] d r = 2 \pi k \rho_ {0} \left[ \sqrt {a ^ {2} + z ^ {2}} - \sqrt {a ^ {2} + (h - z) ^ {2}} - | z | + | h - z | \right]. \\ \end{array}
$$

易知，

当 $0 \leqslant z < \frac{h}{2}$ 时， $Z > 0$ ，此时吸引力朝着向上的铅垂线；

当 $\frac{h}{2} < z \leqslant h$ 时， $Z < 0$ ，此时吸引力朝着向下的铅垂线；

当 $z = \frac{h}{2}$ 时， $Z = 0$ ，引力为零。

【4160】求密度为 $\rho_0$ 的均匀球锥体对位于其顶点的单位质量质点的引力，设球面半径为 $R$ ，而轴截面的扇形的角等于 $2\alpha$

解 由对称性知，引力在 $Ox$ 轴和 $Oy$ 轴上的投影为零，即 $X = Y = 0$ 。若引用球坐标，即得引力在 $Oz$ 轴上的投影为

$$
Z = \iiint_ {V} \frac {k \rho_ {0} z}{\sqrt {\left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} + z ^ {2}\right) ^ {3}}} d x d y d z = k \rho_ {0} \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {\frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos \psi \sin \psi d \int_ {0} ^ {k} d r = k \pi R \rho_ {0} \sin^ {2} \alpha .
$$

# § 9. 二重和三重广义积分

1° 无界区域的情形 若二维区域 $\Omega$ 是无界的，函数 $f(x,y)$ 在区域 $\Omega$ 上连续，则定义：

$$
\iint_ {a} f (x, y) \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y = \lim  _ {n \rightarrow \infty} \iint_ {\Omega_ {n}} f (x, y) \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y, \tag {1}
$$

其中 $\Omega_{n}$ 是可求积有界封闭区域，并且它们组成 $\Omega$ 的任意一个竭尽递增序列。若右端的极限存在且与序列 $\Omega_{n}$ 的选择无关，则相应积分称为收敛的；否则称为发散的。

类似地定义出连续函数在无界三维区域上的三重广义积分.

$2^{\circ}$ 不连续函数的情形 若函数 $f(x,y)$ 在有界封闭区域 $\Omega$ 内除了点 $P(a,b)$ 而外处处是连续的，则定义：

$$
\iint_ {\Omega} f (x, y) \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y = \lim  _ {\epsilon \rightarrow 0} \iint_ {\Omega \cup \epsilon} f (x, y) \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y, \tag {2}
$$

其中 $U_{\varepsilon}$ 是包含点 $P$ 的以 $\varepsilon$ 为直径的区域，并且当极限存在时，所研究的积分称为收敛的；否则称为发散的。假定在点 $P(a, b)$ 的邻近有等式

$$
f (x, y) = \frac {\varphi (x , y)}{r ^ {a}},
$$

其中函数 $\varphi (x,y)$ 的绝对值是介于二正数 $m$ 和 $M$ 之间，且

$$
r = \sqrt {(x - a) ^ {2} + (y - b) ^ {2}},
$$

则1)当 $a < 2$ 时，积分(2)收敛；2)当 $a \geqslant 2$ 时，积分(2)发散.

若函数 $f(x,y)$ 有不连续的线，也可类似地定义出厂义积分(2).

不连续函数的广义积分的概念易于引伸到三重积分的情形.

研究下列具有无界积分域的广义积分的收敛性 $(0 < m \leqslant |\varphi(x, y)| \leqslant M)$

【4161】 $\iint_{x^2 + y^2 = 1} \frac{\varphi(x, y)}{(x^2 + y^2)^p} \mathrm{d}x \mathrm{d}y.$

解题思路 注意到广义重积分收敛必绝对收敛.

由题设知，所给积分与积分 $\iint_{r^2 + y^2 > 1} \frac{\mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y}{(x^2 + y^2)^p}$ 同时收敛或同时发散。由于 $\frac{1}{(x^2 + y^2)^p}$ 是正的，从而引用极坐标，即可知所给积分当 $p > 1$ 时收敛，当 $p \leqslant 1$ 时发散。

解 由于 $\frac{m}{(x^2 + y^2)^p} \leqslant \frac{|\varphi(x, y)|}{(x^2 + y^2)^p} \leqslant \frac{M}{(x^2 + y^2)^p}$ .

再注意到广义重积分收敛必绝对收敛，即知积分

$$
\iint_ {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} > 1} \frac {\varphi (x , y)}{(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}) ^ {p}} d x d y
$$

与积分 $\iint_{r^2 + y^2 - 1} \frac{1}{(x^2 + y^2)^p} \mathrm{d}x \mathrm{d}y$ 同时收敛或同时发散. 由于 $\frac{1}{(x^2 + y^2)^p}$ 是正的, 故引用极坐标, 得

$$
\iint_ {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} > 1} \frac {1}{(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}) ^ {p}} d x d y = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {1} ^ {+ \infty} \frac {r}{r ^ {2 p}} d r = \left\{ \begin{array}{l l} \frac {\pi}{p - 1}, & p > 1, \\ + \infty , & p \leqslant 1. \end{array} \right.
$$

由此可知，原积分 $\iint_{x^2 + y^2 > 1} \frac{\varphi(x, y)}{(x^2 + y^2)^p} \mathrm{d}x \mathrm{d}y$ 当 $p > 1$ 时收敛，当 $p \leqslant 1$ 时发散.

【4162】 $\int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}\int_{-\infty}^{\infty}\frac{\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y}{(1 + |x|^p)(1 + |y|^q)}.$

解 由于被积函数是正的，并且关于 $Ox$ 轴和 $Oy$ 轴都对称，故

$$
\int_ {0} ^ {\infty} \int_ {- \infty} ^ {\infty} \frac {\mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y}{(1 + | x | ^ {p}) (1 + | y | ^ {q})} = 4 \int_ {0} ^ {- \infty} \int_ {0} ^ {- \infty} \frac {\mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y}{(1 + | x | ^ {p}) (1 + | y | ^ {q})} = 4 \left(\int_ {0} ^ {+ \infty} \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{1 + x ^ {p}}\right) \left(\int_ {0} ^ {- \infty} \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{1 + y ^ {q}}\right).
$$

由于 $\lim_{x\to 0}x^p\frac{1}{1 + x^p} = 1$ ，故积分 $\int_0^{+\infty}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + x^p}$ 当 $p > 1$ 时收敛， $p <   1$ 时发散， $p = 1$ 时显然也发散 $\left(\int_{0}^{+\infty}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + x} = +\infty\right)$

因此， $\int_{0}^{\infty}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + x^p} = \left\{ \begin{array}{ll}\text{有限数}, & p > 1,\\ +\infty , & p\leqslant 1. \end{array} \right.$

同理有 $\int_{0}^{+\infty}\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{1 + y^q} = \left\{ \begin{array}{ll} \text{有限数}, & q > 1, \\ +\infty, & q \leqslant 1. \end{array} \right.$

由此可知， $\int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}\int_{-\infty}^{+\infty}\frac{\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y}{(1 + |x|^p)(1 + |y|^q)}$ 仅当 $p > 1$ 且 $q > 1$ 时收敛，其他情形均发散.

【4163】 $\iint_{(0)\leqslant y\leqslant 1}\frac{\varphi(x,y)}{(1 + x^2 + y^2)^p}\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y.$

解仿4161题，可知积分 $\iint_{0\leqslant y\leqslant 1}\frac{\varphi(x,y)}{(1 + x^2 + y^2)^p}\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y$ 与积分 $\iint_{0\leqslant y\leqslant 1}\frac{\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y}{(1 + x^2 + y^2)^p}$ 同时收敛或同时发散.由于被积函数是正的，故

$$
\iint_ {| | \leqslant y | | _ {1}} \frac {\mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y}{(1 + x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}) ^ {p}} - \int_ {0} ^ {1} \mathrm {d} y \int_ {- \infty} ^ {- \infty} \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(1 + x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}) ^ {p}} = 2 \int_ {0} ^ {1} \mathrm {d} y \int_ {0} ^ {- \infty} \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(1 + x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}) ^ {p}};
$$

由于，当 $0 \leqslant y \leqslant 1$ 时，有

$$
\int_ {0} ^ {+ \infty} \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(2 + x ^ {2}) ^ {p}} \leqslant \int_ {0} ^ {+ \infty} \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(1 + x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}) ^ {p}} \leqslant \int_ {0} ^ {+ \infty} \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(1 + x ^ {2}) ^ {p}} \quad (\text {若} p \geqslant 0),
$$

$$
\int_ {0} ^ {- \infty} \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(2 + x ^ {2}) ^ {p}} \geqslant \int_ {0} ^ {- \infty} \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(1 + x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}) ^ {p}} \geqslant \int_ {0} ^ {- \infty} \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{(1 + x ^ {2}) ^ {p}} \quad (\text {若} p <   0),
$$

故 $2\int_{0}^{+\infty}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(2 + x^2)^p}\leqslant \iint_{0\leqslant y\leqslant 1}\frac{\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y}{(1 + x^2 + y^2)^p}\leqslant 2\int_{0}^{+\infty}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(1 + x^2)^p}\quad (p\geqslant 0),$

若 $p < 0$ ，则有相反的不等式

对于 $a > 0$ ，由于 $\lim_{x\to +\infty}x^{2p}\frac{1}{(a^2 + x^2)^p} = 1.$

故积分 $\int_{0}^{\infty}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{(a^{2} + x^{2})^{p}}$ 当 $p > \frac{1}{2}$ 时收敛， $p < \frac{1}{2}$ 时发散.实际上，此积分当 $p = \frac{1}{2}$ 时也发散，因为

$$
\int_ {0} ^ {+ \infty} \frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\sqrt {a ^ {2} + x ^ {2}}} = \ln (x + \sqrt {a ^ {2} + x ^ {2}}) \Big | _ {0} ^ {+ \infty} = + \infty .
$$

由此可知：积分 $\iint_{[0 < y \leq 1]}\frac{\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y}{(1 + x^2 + y^2)^p}$ ，从而，积分 $\iint_{[0 < y \leq 1]}\frac{\varphi(x,y)}{(1 + x^2 + y^2)^p}\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y$ 当 $p > \frac{1}{2}$ 时收敛，当 $p \leq \frac{1}{2}$ 时发散.

【4164】 $\iint_{x\neq y\geq 1}\frac{\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y}{|x|^p + |y|^q}\quad (p > 0,q > 0).$

解 由对称性及被积函数的非负性，有

$$
\iint_ {| x | + | y | \geqslant 1} \frac {\mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y}{| x | ^ {p} + | y | ^ {q}} - 4 \iint_ {\substack {x \geqslant 0, y \geqslant 0 \\ r + 1 \geqslant 1}} \frac {\mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y}{x ^ {p} + y ^ {q}} = 4 \iint_ {\Omega_ {1}} \frac {\mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y}{x ^ {p} + y ^ {q}} + 4 \iint_ {\Omega_ {2}} \frac {\mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y}{x ^ {p} + y ^ {q}},
$$

其中 $\Omega_{1} = \left\{(x,y) \mid x \geqslant 0, y \geqslant 0, x + y \geqslant 1, x^{p} + y^{q} \leqslant 2\right\}, \Omega_{2} = \left\{(x,y) \mid x \geqslant 0, y \geqslant 0, x + y \geqslant 1, x^{p} + y^{q} \geqslant 2\right\}$ ，令 $\Omega_{3} = \left\{(x,y) \mid x \geqslant 0, y \geqslant 0, x^{p} + y^{q} \geqslant 2\right\}$ ，易知，当 $x \geqslant 0, y \geqslant 0, x^{p} + y^{q} \geqslant 2$ 时必有 $x + y \geqslant 1$ （因若 $x + y < 1$ ，则必有 $0 \leqslant x < 1, 0 \leqslant y < 1$ ，从而， $0 \leqslant x^{p} < 1, 0 \leqslant y^{q} < 1$ ，这就会得出 $x^{p} + y^{q} < 2$ ），故 $\Omega_{2} = \Omega_{3}$ . 由于 $\Omega_{1}$ 是有界闭区域，故(1)式右端第一个积分为常义积分，因此，广义积分

$$
\iint_ {| x | + | y | \geqslant 1} \frac {\mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y}{| x | ^ {p} + | y | ^ {q}}
$$

的敛散性取决于广义积分 $\iint_{\Omega_3} \frac{\mathrm{d}x \, \mathrm{d}y}{x^p + y^q}$ 的敛散性，在此积分中作变量代换 $x = r^{\frac{2}{p}} \cos^{\frac{2}{p}} \theta$ ， $y = r^{\frac{2}{q}} \sin^{\frac{2}{q}} \theta$

则易知 $\frac{D(x,y)}{D(r,\theta)} = \frac{4}{pq} r^{\frac{2}{p} +\frac{2}{q} -1}\sin^{\frac{2}{q} -1}\theta \cos^{\frac{2}{p} -1}\theta .$

于是，注意到被积函数是非负的，得

$$
\iint_ {\Omega_ {3}} \frac {\mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y}{x ^ {p} + y ^ {q}} = \frac {4}{p q} \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \sin^ {\frac {2}{q} - 1} \theta \cos^ {\frac {2}{p} - 1} \theta \mathrm {d} \theta \int_ {\sqrt {2}} ^ {+ \infty} r ^ {\frac {2}{p} + \frac {2}{q} - 3} \mathrm {d} r.
$$

由3856题的结果知，右端第一个积分

$$
\int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \sin^ {\frac {2}{q} - 1} \theta \cos^ {\frac {2}{p} - 1} \theta d \theta (p > 0, q > 0)
$$

恒收敛，且其值为 $\frac{1}{2}\mathrm{B}\left(\frac{1}{q},\frac{1}{p}\right)$ ；而第二个积分

$$
\int_ {\sqrt {2}} ^ {+ \infty} r ^ {\frac {2}{p} + \frac {2}{q} - 3} d r
$$

当 $\frac{2}{p} + \frac{2}{q} - 3 < -1$ （即 $\frac{1}{p} + \frac{1}{q} < 1$ ）时收敛，当 $\frac{2}{p} + \frac{2}{q} - 3 \geq -1$ （即 $\frac{1}{p} + \frac{1}{q} \geq 1$ ）时发散.

综上所述，可知广义积分 $\iint_{|x|^{-1}|y|\geqslant 1}\frac{\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y}{|x|^p + |y|^q}$ 仅当 $\frac{1}{p} +\frac{1}{q} <  1$ 时收敛.

【4165】 $\iint_{x + y\geqslant 1}\frac{\sin x\sin y}{(x + y)^p}\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y.$

解设此积分收敛，以 $I$ 表其值.先设 $p < 1.$ 令

$$
\Omega_ {n} = \left\{(x, y) \mid 1 \leqslant x + y \leqslant 2 n \pi , - 2 n \pi \leqslant x - y \leqslant 2 n \pi \right\},
$$

$$
\Omega_ {n} ^ {\prime} = \left\{(x, y) \mid 1 \leqslant x + y \leqslant 2 n \pi - \frac {\pi}{4}, - 2 n \pi \leqslant x - y \leqslant 2 n \pi \right\},
$$

$$
\omega_ {n} = \left\{\left(x, y\right) \mid 2 n \pi - \frac {\pi}{4} \leqslant x + y \leqslant 2 n \pi , - 2 n \pi \leqslant x - y \leqslant 2 n \pi \right\},
$$

其中 $n = 1,2,3,\dots$ ，则显然有

$$
\lim  _ {n \rightarrow \infty} \iint_ {\Omega_ {n}} \frac {\sin x \sin y}{(x + y) ^ {p}} d x d y = I, \quad \lim  _ {n \rightarrow \infty} \iint_ {\Omega_ {n}} \frac {\sin x \sin y}{(x + y) ^ {p}} d x d y = I.
$$

从而，

$$
\lim  _ {n \rightarrow \infty} \iint_ {\omega_ {n}} \frac {\sin x \sin y}{(x + y) ^ {p}} d x d y = \lim  _ {n \rightarrow \infty} \left[ \iint_ {\Omega_ {n}} \frac {\sin x \sin y}{(x + y) ^ {p}} d x d y - \iint_ {\Omega_ {n} ^ {\prime}} \frac {\sin x \sin y}{(x + y) ^ {p}} d x d y \right] = I - I = 0. \tag {1}
$$

由于 $\sin x\sin y = \frac{1}{2} [\cos (x - y) - \cos (x + y)]$ ，今在(1)式左端的积分中作变量代换 $x + y = u, x - y = v$ （即 $x = \frac{u + v}{2}, y = \frac{u - v}{2}$ ），并注意到 $\frac{D(x,y)}{D(u,v)} = -\frac{1}{2}$ ，得

$$
\iint_ {w _ {n}} \frac {\sin x \sin y}{(x + y) ^ {p}} d x d y = \frac {1}{4} \int_ {2 n \pi - \frac {\pi}{4}} ^ {2 n \pi} d u \int_ {- 2 n \pi} ^ {2 n \pi} \frac {\cos v - \cos u}{u ^ {p}} d v = - n \pi \int_ {2 n \pi - \frac {\pi}{4}} ^ {2 n \pi} \frac {\cos u}{u ^ {p}} d u;
$$

而 $\int_{2n\pi}^{2n\pi}\frac{\cos u}{u^p}\mathrm{d}u\geqslant \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\int_{2n\pi -\frac{\pi}{4}}^{2n\pi}\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{u^p}\geqslant \left\{ \begin{array}{ll}\frac{\pi}{4\sqrt{2}}\cdot \frac{1}{(2n\pi)^p}, & p > 0,\\ \frac{\pi}{4\sqrt{2}}, & p\leqslant 0. \end{array} \right.$

由此可知（注意前面假定 $p < 1$ ）， $\lim_{n \to \infty} \iint_{\omega_n} \frac{\sin x \sin y}{(x + y)^p} \mathrm{d}x \mathrm{d}y = -\infty,$

此显然与(1)式矛盾.

现设 $p \geqslant 1$ . 令

$$
\omega_ {n} ^ {\prime} = \{(x, y) | 2 n \pi - \frac {\pi}{4} \leqslant x + y \leqslant 2 n \pi , - 2 \pi n ^ {p - 2} \leqslant x - y \leqslant 2 \pi n ^ {p - 2} \},
$$

仿上，应有

$$
\lim  _ {n \rightarrow \infty} \iint_ {\omega_ {n}} \frac {\sin x \sin y}{(x + y) ^ {p}} d x d y = 0. \tag {2}
$$

但另一方面，和上面一样，作代换 $x + y = u, x - y = v$ 后，有

$$
\iint_ {u _ {n}} \frac {\sin x \sin y}{(x + y) ^ {p}} d x d y = - \pi n ^ {[ p ] + 2} \int_ {2 n \pi} ^ {2 n \pi} \frac {\cos u}{u ^ {p}} d u.
$$

同样，由 $\int_{2n\pi -\frac{\pi}{4}}^{2n\pi}\frac{\cos u}{u^p}\mathrm{d}u\geqslant \frac{\pi}{4\sqrt{2}}\cdot \frac{1}{(2n\pi)^p},$

即得 $\lim_{n\to \infty}\iint \limits_{u_n}^{\sin x\sin y}\frac{\sin x\sin y}{(x + y)^p}\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y = -\infty ,$

此显然与(2)式矛盾.

综上所述，可知：不论 $p$ 为何值，积分 $\iint_{x - y \geqslant 1} \frac{\sin x \sin y}{(x + y)^p} \mathrm{d}x \mathrm{d}y$ 都发散.

【4166】证明：若连续函数 $f(x, y)$ 不为负及 $S_{n}(n = 1, 2, \dots)$ 为有界闭区域，并且组成区域 $S$ 的任意一个竭尽递增序列. 则

$$
\iint_ {S} f (x, y) \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y = \lim  _ {n \rightarrow + \infty} \iint_ {S _ {n}} f (x, y) \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y,
$$

这里左端与右端同时有意义或同时无意义

证取定一有界闭区域的序列 $S_{n}^{\prime}(n = 1,2,\dots),S_{1}^{\prime}\subset S_{2}^{\prime}\subset \dots \subset S_{n}^{\prime}\subset \dots \subset S$ ，且 $\bigcup_{n = 1}^{c}S_{n}^{\prime} = S$ 由于 $f(x,y)$ 在 $S$ 上非负，故积分序列 $\iint \limits_{S_n}f(x,y)\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y$ 是递增的，从而，极限

$$
I = \lim  _ {n \rightarrow \infty} \iint_ {S _ {n}} f (x, y) d x d y \tag {1}
$$

存在（是有限数或是 $+\infty$ ）.我们要证 $\lim_{n\to \infty}\iint \limits_{S_n}f(x,y)\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y = I.$ (2)

先设 $I$ 为有限数.任给 $\varepsilon >0$ ，由(1)式知，存在 $N$ ，使当 $n\geqslant N$ 时，恒有

$$
I - \varepsilon <   \iint_ {S _ {n} ^ {\prime}} f (x, y) d x d y <   I + \varepsilon . \tag {3}
$$

又存在 $n_0$ ，使当 $n\geqslant n_0$ 时， $S_{n}\supset S_{N}^{\prime}$ .从而，根据 $f(x,y)$ 的非负性以及(3)式，得

$$
\iint_ {S _ {n}} f (x, y) \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y \geqslant \iint_ {S _ {N}} f (x, y) \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y > I - \epsilon .
$$

另一方面，对每个固定的 $n\geqslant n_0$ 又必存在某个充分大的 $k_{n}(\geqslant N)$ 使 $S_{k_n}^{\prime}\supset S_n$ .于是，再由(3)式得

$$
\iint_ {S _ {n}} f (x, y) \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y \leqslant \iint_ {S _ {n}} f (x, y) \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y <   I + \varepsilon .
$$

由此可知，当 $n\geqslant n_0$ 时，恒有

故（2）式成立.

次设 $I = +\infty$ 任给 $M > 0$ ，由（1）式知，存在 $N_{1}$ ，使

$$
\iint_ {\tilde {S} _ {1}} f (x, y) \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y > M.
$$

又存在 $n_1$ ，使当 $n\geqslant n_1$ 时，恒有 $S_{n}\supset S_{N_{1}}^{\prime}$ ，从而，此时有

$$
\iint_ {S _ {n}} f (x, y) \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y \geqslant \iint_ {S _ {N _ {1}}} f (x, y) \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y > M,
$$

故（2）式成立.证毕

【4167】证明： $\lim_{n\to \infty}\iint \limits_{\substack{x\leqslant n\\ y\leqslant n}}\sin (x^2 +y^2)\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y = \pi ,$

然而 $\lim_{n\to \infty}\iint \limits_{x^2 -y^2\leqslant 2n\pi}\sin (x^2 +y^2)\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y = 0$ （ $n$ 为正整数）.

证 利用极坐标，我们有

$$
\iint_ {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} \leqslant 2 n \pi} \sin (x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}) d x d y = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \theta \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt {2 \pi n}} r \sin r ^ {2} d r = \pi (1 - \cos 2 n \pi) = 0 \quad (n = 1, 2, \dots),
$$

故 $\lim_{n\to \infty}\iint \limits_{x^2 -y^2\leqslant 2n\pi}\sin (x^2 +y^2)\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y = 0.$

但由对称性，有

$$
\begin{array}{l} \iint_ {\substack {| x | \leqslant n \\ | y | \leqslant n}} \sin (x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}) \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y = 4 \iint_ {\substack {| x | \leqslant n \\ | y | \leqslant n}} \sin (x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}) \mathrm {d} x \mathrm {d} y = 4 \int_ {0} ^ {n} \mathrm {d} y \int_ {0} ^ {n} (\sin x ^ {2} \cos y ^ {2} + \cos x ^ {2} \sin y ^ {2}) \mathrm {d} x \\ = 4 \left(\int_ {0} ^ {n} \cos y ^ {2} d y\right) \left(\int_ {0} ^ {n} \sin x ^ {2} d x\right) + 4 \left(\int_ {0} ^ {n} \cos x ^ {2} d x\right) \left(\int_ {0} ^ {n} \sin y ^ {2} d y\right) = 8 \left(\int_ {0} ^ {n} \cos x ^ {2} d x\right) \left(\int_ {0} ^ {n} \sin x ^ {2} d x\right). \\ \end{array}
$$

根据3830题的结果，可知 $\int_{0}^{\infty}\sin x^{2}\mathrm{d}x = \int_{0}^{\infty}\cos x^{2}\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{2}\sqrt{\frac{\pi}{2}},$

故 $\lim_{n\to \infty}\int_{0}^{n}\sin x^{2}\mathrm{d}x = \lim_{n\to \infty}\int_{0}^{n}\cos x^{2}\mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{2}\sqrt{\frac{\pi}{2}}.$

从而，得 $\lim_{n\to \infty}\iint \limits_{\substack{|x|\leqslant n\\ |y|\leqslant n}}\sin (x^2 +y^2)\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y = 8\cdot \frac{1}{2}\sqrt{\frac{\pi}{2}}\cdot \frac{1}{2}\sqrt{\frac{\pi}{2}} = \pi .$

【4168】 证明：尽管累次积分

$$
\int_ {1} ^ {\cdot \cdot \cdot} \mathrm {d} x \int_ {1} ^ {\cdot \cdot \cdot} \frac {x ^ {2} - y ^ {2}}{(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}) ^ {2}} \mathrm {d} y \quad \text {及} \quad \int_ {1} ^ {\cdot \cdot \cdot} \mathrm {d} y \int_ {1} ^ {\cdot \cdot \cdot} \frac {x ^ {2} - y ^ {2}}{(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}) ^ {2}} \mathrm {d} x
$$

收敛，但积分 $\iint_{x\geqslant 1,y\geqslant 1}\frac{x^2 - y^2}{(x^2 + y^2)^2}\mathrm{d}x\mathrm{d}y$

发散.

证 先证两个累次积分收敛. 我们有

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int_ {1} ^ {+ \infty} \frac {x ^ {2} - y ^ {2}}{\left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}\right) ^ {2}} d y = \int_ {1} ^ {+ \infty} \frac {x ^ {2}}{2 y} \cdot \frac {2 y d y}{\left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}\right) ^ {2}} - \int_ {1} ^ {+ \infty} \frac {y}{2} \cdot \frac {2 y d y}{\left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}\right) ^ {2}} \\ = - \frac {x ^ {2}}{2 y \left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}\right)} \left| _ {y = 1} ^ {y = - \infty} - \int_ {1} ^ {- \infty} \frac {x ^ {2} d y}{2 y ^ {2} \left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}\right)} + \frac {y}{2 \left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}\right)} \right| _ {y = 1} ^ {y = - \infty} - \int_ {1} ^ {- \infty} \frac {d y}{2 \left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}\right)} \\ = \frac {x ^ {2}}{2 \left(x ^ {2} + 1\right)} - \frac {1}{2} \int_ {1} ^ {\infty} \left(\frac {1}{y ^ {2}} - \frac {1}{x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}}\right) d y - \frac {1}{2 \left(x ^ {2} + 1\right)} - \frac {1}{2} \int_ {1} ^ {\infty} \frac {d y}{x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}} = \frac {x ^ {2} - 1}{2 \left(x ^ {2} + 1\right)} - \frac {1}{2} = - \frac {1}{x ^ {2} + 1}, \\ \end{array}
$$

故 $\int_{1}^{+\infty}\mathrm{d}x\int_{1}^{+\infty}\frac{x^2 - y^2}{(x^2 + y^2)^2}\mathrm{d}y = -\int_{1}^{+\infty}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x^2 + 1} = -\frac{\pi}{4};$

同理（利用已算得的结果）

$$
\int_ {1} ^ {- \infty} d y \int_ {1} ^ {+ \infty} \frac {x ^ {2} - y ^ {2}}{(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}) ^ {2}} d x = - \int_ {1} ^ {- \infty} d y \int_ {1} ^ {+ \infty} \frac {y ^ {2} - x ^ {2}}{(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}) ^ {2}} d x = - \int_ {1} ^ {+ \infty} \left(- \frac {1}{y ^ {2} + 1}\right) d y = \frac {\pi}{4},
$$

故两个累次积分都收敛.

次证积分

$$
\iint_ {x \geqslant 1, y \geqslant 1} \frac {x ^ {2} - y ^ {2}}{\left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}\right) ^ {2}} d x d y \tag {1}
$$

发散. 为此只要证积分

$$
\iint_ {r \geqslant 1. 1 \leqslant y \leqslant r} \frac {x ^ {2} - y ^ {2}}{\left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}\right) ^ {2}} d. r d y \tag {2}
$$

发散即可（因为如果积分(1)收敛，则绝对值积分

$$
\iint_ {x \geqslant 1, y \geqslant 1} \left| \frac {x ^ {2} - y ^ {2}}{\left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}\right) ^ {2}} \right| d x d y \tag {3}
$$

必收敛. 从而, 在小一点的区域上的积分

$$
