V _ {n} = \iint_ {x _ {1} ^ {2} - x _ {2} ^ {2} + \dots + x _ {n} ^ {n} \leqslant a ^ {2}} \mathrm {d} x _ {1} \mathrm {d} x _ {2} \dots \mathrm {d} x _ {n} = a ^ {n} V _ {n} (1).
$$

其中 $V_{n}(1)$ 表示 $a = 1$ 时的 $n$ 维球体的体积.但是

$$
\begin{array}{l} V _ {n} (1) = \iint_ {\xi_ {1} ^ {2} + \xi_ {2} ^ {2} + \dots + \xi_ {n} ^ {2} \leq 1} \mathrm {d} \xi_ {1} \mathrm {d} \xi_ {2} \dots \mathrm {d} \xi_ {n} = \int_ {- 1} ^ {1} \mathrm {d} \xi_ {n} \iint_ {\xi_ {1} ^ {2} + \dots + \xi_ {n - 1} ^ {2} \leq 1 - \xi_ {n} ^ {2}} \mathrm {d} \xi_ {1} \mathrm {d} \xi_ {2} \dots \mathrm {d} \xi_ {n - 1} \\ = V _ {n - 1} (1) \int_ {- 1} ^ {1} \left(1 - \xi_ {n} ^ {2}\right) ^ {\frac {n - 1}{2}} d \xi_ {n} = 2 V _ {n - 1} (1) \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \sin^ {n} \varphi d \varphi \\ = 2 V _ {n - 1} (1) \cdot \frac {1}{2} \frac {\Gamma \left(\frac {n + 1}{2}\right) \Gamma \left(\frac {1}{2}\right)}{\Gamma \left(\frac {n + 2}{2}\right)} = V _ {n - 1} (1) \sqrt {\pi} \frac {\Gamma \left(\frac {n + 1}{2}\right)}{\Gamma \left(\frac {n + 2}{2}\right)}, \\ \end{array}
$$

因为 $V_{1}(1) = 2$ ，故由上述循环公式可得 $V_{n}(1) = \frac{\pi^{\frac{n}{2}}}{\Gamma\left(\frac{n}{2} + 1\right)}.$

因此，所求的体积为 $V_{n} = \frac{\pi^{\frac{n}{2}}}{\Gamma\left(\frac{n}{2} + 1\right)} a^{n}$

对于 $n$ 为偶数及奇数，分别可得公式

$$
V _ {2 m} = \frac {\pi^ {m}}{m !} a ^ {2 m}, \quad V _ {2 m + 1} = \frac {2 \cdot (2 \pi) ^ {m}}{(2 m + 1) ! !} a ^ {2 m + 1}.
$$

特别是，对于 $V_{1}, V_{2}, V_{3}$ 可求得熟知的值： $2a, \pi a^{2}, \frac{4}{3} \pi a^{3}$ .

【4212】求 $\iint_{\Omega} \cdots \int x_n^2 \, \mathrm{d}x_1 \, \mathrm{d}x_2 \cdots \mathrm{d}x_n$ ，其中区域 $\Omega$ 是由下列不等式确定的：

$$
x _ {1} ^ {2} + x _ {2} ^ {2} + \dots + x _ {n - 1} ^ {2} \leqslant a ^ {2}, \quad - \frac {h}{2} \leqslant x _ {n} \leqslant \frac {h}{2}.
$$

提示 利用4211题的结果.

解 $\iint_{\Omega} \cdots \int x_n^2 \, \mathrm{d}x_1 \, \mathrm{d}x_2 \cdots \mathrm{d}x_n = \int_{\frac{h}{2}}^{\frac{h}{2}} x_n^2 \, \mathrm{d}x_n \iint_{x_1^2 + x_2^2 + \cdots + x_n^2 - 1 \leqslant a^2} \, \mathrm{d}x_1 \, \mathrm{d}x_2 \cdots \mathrm{d}x_n = \frac{h^3}{12} \cdot \frac{\pi^{\frac{n-1}{2}}}{\Gamma\left(\frac{n+1}{2}\right)} a^{n-1}$ .

\*) 利用4211题的结果.

【4213】 计算 $\iint_{x_1^2 + x_2^2 + \dots + x_n^2 \leqslant 1} \frac{\mathrm{d}x_1 \mathrm{~d}x_2 \cdots \mathrm{d}x_n}{\sqrt{1 - x_1^2 - x_2^2 - \cdots - x_n^2}}.$

提示 利用4211题的结果，

解 $\iint_{r_1^2 + r_2^2 + \dots + r_n^2 \leqslant 1} \frac{\mathrm{d}x_1 \mathrm{~d}x_2 \cdots \mathrm{d}x_n}{\sqrt{1 - x_1^2 - x_2^2 - \cdots - x_n^2}}$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \iint_ {x _ {1} ^ {2}, r _ {2} ^ {2}, \dots + r _ {n - 1} ^ {2} \leqslant 1} \mathrm {d} x _ {1} \mathrm {d} x _ {2} \dots \mathrm {d} x _ {n} \int_ {- \sqrt {1 - x _ {1} ^ {2} - \cdots - x _ {n - 1} ^ {2}}} ^ {\sqrt {1 - x _ {1} ^ {2} - \cdots - x _ {n - 1} ^ {2}}} \frac {\mathrm {d} x _ {n}}{\sqrt {1 - x _ {1} ^ {2} - x _ {2} ^ {2} - \cdots - x _ {n} ^ {2}}} \\ = \pi \iint_ {x _ {1} ^ {2} + x _ {2} ^ {2} + \dots + x _ {n - 1} ^ {2} \leqslant 1} \mathrm {d} x _ {1} \mathrm {d} x _ {2} \dots \mathrm {d} x _ {n - 1} = \pi \cdot \frac {\pi^ {\frac {n - 1}{2}}}{\Gamma \left(\frac {n - 1}{2} + 1\right)} = \frac {\pi^ {\frac {n + 1}{2}}}{\Gamma \left(\frac {n + 1}{2}\right)}. \\ \end{array}
$$

\*) 利用4211题的结果.

【4214】证明等式： $\int_0^x\mathrm{d}x_1\int_0^{x_1}\mathrm{d}x_2\dots \int_0^{x_{n - 1}}f(x_n)\mathrm{d}x_n = \int_0^x f(u)\frac{(x - u)^{n - 1}}{(n - 1)!}\mathrm{d}u.$

提示 利用4202题的结果.

证 $\int_0^x\mathrm{d}x_1\int_0^{x_1}\mathrm{d}x_2\dots \int_0^{x_{n - 1}}f(x_n)\mathrm{d}x_n$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \int_ {0} ^ {x} f (x _ {n}) d x _ {n} \int_ {x _ {n}} ^ {x} d x _ {n - 1} \int_ {x _ {n - 1}} ^ {x} d x _ {n - 2} \dots \int_ {x _ {2}} ^ {x} d x _ {1} \cdot) = \int_ {0} ^ {x} f (x _ {n}) d x _ {n} \int_ {x _ {n}} ^ {x} d x _ {n - 1} \int_ {x _ {n - 1}} ^ {x} d x _ {n - 2} \dots \int_ {x _ {3}} ^ {x} (x - x _ {2}) d x _ {2} \\ = \int_ {0} ^ {x} f (x _ {n}) d x _ {n} \int_ {x _ {n}} ^ {x} d x _ {n - 1} \int_ {x _ {n - 1}} ^ {x} d x _ {n - 2} \dots \int_ {x _ {4}} ^ {x} \frac {1}{2} (x - x _ {3}) ^ {2} d x _ {3} \\ = \int_ {0} ^ {x} f (x _ {n}) \mathrm {d} x _ {n} \int_ {x _ {n}} ^ {x} \mathrm {d} x _ {n - 1} \int_ {x _ {n - 1}} ^ {x} \mathrm {d} x _ {n - 2} \dots \int_ {x _ {5}} ^ {x} \frac {1}{2 \cdot 3} (x - x _ {4}) ^ {3} \mathrm {d} x _ {4} \\ = \dots \\ = \int_ {0} ^ {x} f \left(x _ {n}\right) d x _ {n} \int_ {x _ {n}} ^ {x} \frac {1}{(n - 2) !} \left(x - x _ {n - 1}\right) ^ {n - 2} d x _ {n - 1} = \int_ {0} ^ {x} \frac {\left(x - x _ {n}\right) ^ {n - 1}}{(n - 1) !} f \left(x _ {n}\right) d x _ {n}. \\ \end{array}
$$

在上述积分中，将 $x_{n}$ 代之以 $u$ ，不影响积分的值，故得

$$
\int_ {0} ^ {x} \mathrm {d} x _ {1} \int_ {0} ^ {x _ {1}} \mathrm {d} x _ {2} \dots \int_ {0} ^ {x _ {n - 1}} f (x _ {n}) \mathrm {d} x = \int_ {0} ^ {x} f (u) \frac {(x - u) ^ {n - 1}}{(n - 1) !} \mathrm {d} u.
$$

\*) 利用4202题的结果.

【4215】证明等式： $\int_{0}^{x} x_{1} \mathrm{d}x_{1} \int_{0}^{x_{1}} x_{2} \mathrm{d}x_{2} \cdots \int_{0}^{x_{n}} f(x_{n+1}) \mathrm{d}x_{n+1} = \frac{1}{2^{n} n!} \int_{0}^{x} (x^{2} - u^{2})^{n} f(u) \mathrm{d}u.$

证 利用4202题的结果，即得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int_ {0} ^ {x} x _ {1} \mathrm {d} x _ {1} \int_ {0} ^ {x _ {1}} x _ {2} \mathrm {d} x _ {2} \dots \int_ {0} ^ {x _ {n}} f (x _ {n + 1}) \mathrm {d} x _ {n + 1} = \int_ {0} ^ {x} f (x _ {n + 1}) \mathrm {d} x _ {n + 1} \int_ {x _ {n + 1}} ^ {x} x _ {n} \mathrm {d} x _ {n} \int_ {x _ {n}} ^ {x} x _ {n - 1} \mathrm {d} x _ {n - 1} \dots \int_ {x _ {2}} ^ {x} x _ {1} \mathrm {d} x _ {1} \\ = \int_ {0} ^ {x} f \left(x _ {n + 1}\right) d x _ {n + 1} \int_ {x _ {n + 1}} ^ {x} x _ {n} d x _ {n} \int_ {x _ {n}} ^ {x} x _ {n - 1} d x _ {n - 1} \dots \int_ {x _ {3}} ^ {x} \frac {1}{2} \left(x ^ {2} - x _ {2} ^ {2}\right) x _ {2} d x _ {2} \\ = \int_ {0} ^ {x} f \left(x _ {n + 1}\right) \mathrm {d} x _ {n + 1} \int_ {x _ {n + 1}} ^ {x} x _ {n} \mathrm {d} x _ {n} \int_ {x _ {n}} ^ {x} x _ {n - 1} \mathrm {d} x _ {n - 1} \dots \int_ {x _ {4}} ^ {x} \frac {1}{2 ^ {2} \cdot 2} \left(x ^ {2} - x _ {3} ^ {2}\right) ^ {2} x _ {3} \mathrm {d} x _ {3} \\ \end{array}
$$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \dots \\ = \int_ {0} ^ {x} f \left(x _ {n + 1}\right) d x _ {n - 1} \int_ {x _ {n + 1}} ^ {x} \frac {1}{2 ^ {n - 1} (n - 1) !} \left(x ^ {2} - x _ {n} ^ {2}\right) ^ {n - 1} x _ {n} d x _ {n} = \int_ {0} ^ {x} \frac {1}{2 ^ {n} n !} f \left(x _ {n + 1}\right) \left(x ^ {2} - x _ {n + 1} ^ {2}\right) ^ {n} d x _ {n - 1}. \\ \end{array}
$$

在上述积分中，将 $x_{n+1}$ 代之以 $u$ ，不影响积分的值，故得

$$
\int_ {0} ^ {x} x _ {1} \mathrm {d} x _ {1} \int_ {x _ {0}} ^ {x _ {1}} x _ {2} \mathrm {d} x _ {2} \dots \int_ {0} ^ {x _ {n}} f (x _ {n + 1}) \mathrm {d} x _ {n + 1} = \frac {1}{2 ^ {n} n !} \int_ {0} ^ {x} (x ^ {2} - u ^ {2}) ^ {n} f (u) \mathrm {d} u.
$$

【4216】 证明狄利克雷公式：

$$
\iint_ {x _ {1} \cdot x _ {2} \dots \dots c _ {n} \geq 0} ^ {\dots} x _ {1} ^ {p _ {1}} ^ {- 1} x _ {2} ^ {p _ {2}} ^ {- 1} \dots x _ {n} ^ {p _ {n}} ^ {- 1} d x _ {1} d x _ {2} \dots d x _ {n} = \frac {\Gamma (p _ {1}) \Gamma (p _ {2}) \cdots \Gamma (p _ {n})}{\Gamma (p _ {1} + p _ {2} + \cdots + p _ {n} + 1)} \quad (p _ {1}, p _ {2}, \dots , p _ {n} > 0).
$$

提示 用数学归纳法证明.

证 我们应用数学归纳法证明之.

当 $n = 1$ 时，公式显然成立，即 $\int_{0\leqslant x_1\leqslant 1}x_1^{p_1}\mathrm{d}x_1 = \frac{1}{p_1} = \frac{\Gamma(p_1)}{\Gamma(p_1 + 1)}.$

其次，设公式对 $n - 1$ 成立，今证公式对 $\pmb{n}$ 也成立.为此，将公式左端写为

$$
\int_ {1} ^ {1} x _ {n} ^ {p _ {n}} ^ {- 1} \mathrm {d} x _ {n} \iint_ {\substack {x _ {1}, x _ {2}, \dots , x _ {n} \geqslant 0 \\ x _ {1} + x _ {2} + \dots + x _ {n - 1} \leqslant 1 - r _ {n}}} x _ {1} ^ {p _ {1}} ^ {- 1} x _ {2} ^ {p _ {2}} ^ {- 1} \dots x _ {n} ^ {p _ {n}} ^ {- 1} ^ {- 1} \mathrm {d} x _ {1} \mathrm {d} x _ {2} \dots \mathrm {d} x _ {n - 1}.
$$

在里面的 $n - 1$ 重积分中作代换

$$
x _ {1} = \left(1 - x _ {n}\right) \xi_ {1}, x _ {2} = \left(1 - x _ {n}\right) \xi_ {2}, \dots , x _ {n - 1} = \left(1 - x _ {n}\right) \xi_ {n - 1},
$$

即得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \frac {\Gamma \left(p _ {1}\right) \Gamma \left(p _ {2}\right) \cdots \Gamma \left(p _ {n - 1}\right)}{\Gamma \left(p _ {1} + p _ {2} + \cdots + p _ {n - 1} + 1\right)} \int_ {0} ^ {1} x _ {n} ^ {p _ {n} - 1} \left(1 - x _ {n}\right) x ^ {p _ {1} + p _ {2} + \dots + p _ {n - 1}} d x _ {n} \\ = \frac {\Gamma (p _ {1}) \cdots \Gamma (p _ {n - 1})}{\Gamma (p _ {1} + \cdots + p _ {n - 1} + 1)} B (p _ {n}, p _ {1} + \dots + p _ {n - 1} + 1) \\ = \frac {\Gamma \left(p _ {1}\right) \cdots \Gamma \left(p _ {n - 1}\right)}{\Gamma \left(p _ {1} + \cdots + p _ {n - 1} + 1\right)} \cdot \frac {\Gamma \left(p _ {n}\right) \Gamma \left(p _ {1} + \cdots + p _ {n - 1} + 1\right)}{\Gamma \left(p _ {1} + \cdots + p _ {n} + 1\right)} \\ = \frac {\Gamma \left(p _ {1}\right) \Gamma \left(p _ {2}\right) \cdots \Gamma \left(p _ {n}\right)}{\Gamma \left(p _ {1} + p _ {2} + \cdots + p _ {n} + 1\right)}. \\ \end{array}
$$

这样一来，我们得知公式对 $n$ 重积分也正确.从而，对 $n$ 为任意的正整数时，狄利克雷公式均成立

【4217】 证明刘维耳公式：

$$
\begin{array}{l} \iint_ {x _ {1} + x _ {2} + \dots + x _ {n} \geqslant 0} f (x _ {1} + x _ {2} + \dots + x _ {n}) x _ {1} ^ {p _ {1}} x _ {2} ^ {p _ {2}} \dots x _ {n} ^ {p _ {n}} d x _ {1} d x _ {2} \dots d x _ {n} \\ = \frac {\Gamma (p _ {1}) \Gamma (p _ {2}) \cdots \Gamma (p _ {n})}{\Gamma (p _ {1} + p _ {2} + \cdots + p _ {n})} \int_ {0} ^ {1} f (u) u ^ {p _ {1} - p _ {2} + \dots + p _ {n} - 1} d u \quad (p _ {1}, p _ {2}, \dots , p _ {n} > 0), \\ \end{array}
$$

式中 $f(u)$ 为连续函数.

提示 用数学归纳法证明.

证 我们应用数学归纳法证明之.

当 $n = 1$ 时，公式显然成立.当 $n = 2$ 时，公式也成立，即

$$
\iint_ {\substack {x _ {1} \geqslant 0, x _ {2} \geqslant 0 \\ x _ {1} + x _ {2} \leqslant 1}} f (x _ {1} + x _ {2}) x _ {1} ^ {p _ {1} - 1} x _ {2} ^ {p _ {2} - 1} \mathrm {d} x _ {1} \mathrm {d} x _ {2} = \frac {\Gamma (p _ {1}) \Gamma (p _ {2})}{\Gamma (p _ {1} + p _ {2})} \int_ {0} ^ {1} f (u) u ^ {p _ {1} + p _ {2} - 1} \mathrm {d} u.
$$

事实上，令 $\Omega$ 表区域： $x_{1}\geqslant 0,x_{2}\geqslant 0,x_{1} + x_{2}\leqslant 1.$ 作代换 $x_{1} = \xi_{1},x_{1} + x_{2} = \xi_{2}$ ，及 $t = \frac{\xi_1}{\xi_2}$

则有 $\iint_{\Omega} f(x_1 + x_2) x_1^{p_1} \mathrm{~d}x_1 \mathrm{~d}x_2 = \int_{0}^{1} f(\xi_2) \mathrm{d}\xi_2 \int_{0}^{\xi_2} \xi_1^{p_1} \mathrm{~d}(\xi_2 - \xi_1)^{p_2 - 1} \mathrm{~d}\xi_1$

$$
= \int_ {0} ^ {1} f \left(\xi_ {2}\right) d \xi_ {2} \int_ {0} ^ {1} t ^ {p _ {1} - 1} (1 - t) ^ {p _ {2} - 1} \xi_ {2} ^ {p _ {1} - p _ {2} - 1} d t = \frac {\Gamma \left(p _ {1}\right) \Gamma \left(p _ {2}\right)}{\Gamma \left(p _ {1} + p _ {2}\right)} \int_ {0} ^ {1} f \left(\xi_ {2}\right) \xi_ {2} ^ {p _ {1} - p _ {2} - 1} d \xi_ {2}
$$

$$
= \frac {\Gamma (p _ {1}) \Gamma (p _ {2})}{\Gamma (p _ {1} + p _ {2})} \int_ {0} ^ {1} f (u) u ^ {p _ {1} + p _ {2} - 1} d u.
$$

其次，设公式对于 $n - 1$ 成立，今证对于 $n$ 公式也成立.为此，将公式左端写为

$$
\iint_ {x _ {1} + x _ {2} + \dots + x _ {n - 1} \leqslant 1} \dots \int_ {x _ {1} + x _ {2} + \dots + x _ {n - 1}} ^ {\infty} x _ {1} ^ {p _ {1}} ^ {- 1} x _ {2} ^ {p _ {2}} ^ {- 1} \dots x _ {n - 1} ^ {p _ {n - 1} - 1} d x _ {1} d x _ {2} \dots d x _ {n - 1} \int_ {0} ^ {1 - (x _ {1} + x _ {2} + \dots + x _ {n - 1})} f (x _ {1} + x _ {2} + \dots + x _ {n}) x _ {n} ^ {p _ {n} - 1} d x _ {n}.
$$

令 $\psi (t) = \int_{0}^{1}f(t + x_n)x_n^{p_n}\mathrm{d}x_n$

代入上式，并利用公式对 $n - 1$ 成立的假定，得知上式为

$$
\frac {\Gamma \left(p _ {1}\right) \Gamma \left(p _ {2}\right) \cdots \Gamma \left(p _ {n - 1}\right)}{\Gamma \left(p _ {1} + p _ {2} + \cdots + p _ {n - 1}\right)} \int_ {0} ^ {1} \psi (t) t ^ {p _ {1} + p _ {2} + \dots + p _ {n - 1}} d t.
$$

利用上面已证的 $n = 2$ 时的公式，于是即得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \iint_ {x _ {1} + x _ {2} + \dots + x _ {n} \geqslant 0} f (x _ {1} + x _ {2} + \dots + x _ {n}) x _ {1} ^ {p _ {1} - 1} x _ {2} ^ {p _ {2} - 1} \dots x _ {n} ^ {p _ {n} - 1} d x _ {1} d x _ {2} \dots d x _ {n} \\ = \frac {\Gamma (p _ {1}) \Gamma (p _ {2}) \cdots \Gamma (p _ {n - 1})}{\Gamma (p _ {1} + p _ {2} + \cdots + p _ {n - 1})} \int_ {0} ^ {1} d t \int_ {0} ^ {1 - t} f (t + x _ {n}) t ^ {p _ {1} + p _ {2} + \dots + p _ {n - 1} - 1} x _ {n} ^ {p _ {n} - 1} d x _ {n} \\ = \frac {\Gamma (p _ {1}) \Gamma (p _ {2}) \cdots \Gamma (p _ {n - 1})}{\Gamma (p _ {1} + p _ {2} + \cdots + p _ {n - 1})} \iint_ {\substack {t, x _ {n} \geqslant 0 \\ t - r _ {n} \leqslant 1}} f (t + x _ {n}) t ^ {p _ {1} + p _ {2} + \dots + p _ {n - 1} - 1} x _ {n} ^ {p _ {n} - 1} d t d x _ {n} \\ = \frac {\Gamma (p _ {1}) \Gamma (p _ {2}) \cdots \Gamma (p _ {n - 1})}{\Gamma (p _ {1} + p _ {2} + \cdots + p _ {n - 1})} \cdot \frac {\Gamma (p _ {1} + p _ {2} + \cdots + p _ {n - 1}) \Gamma (p _ {n})}{\Gamma (p _ {1} + p _ {2} + \cdots + p _ {n})} \int_ {0} ^ {1} f (u) u ^ {p _ {1} + p _ {2} + \dots + p _ {n}} d u \\ = \frac {\Gamma \left(p _ {1}\right) \Gamma \left(p _ {2}\right) \cdots \Gamma \left(p _ {n}\right)}{\Gamma \left(p _ {1} + p _ {2} + \cdots + p _ {n}\right)} \int_ {0} ^ {1} f (u) u ^ {p _ {1} + p _ {2} + \dots + p _ {n}} d u, \\ \end{array}
$$

即公式对于 $n$ 成立. 从而, 公式对于 $n$ 为任意正整数均成立.

【4218】 将区域 $x_{1}^{2} + x_{2}^{2} + \dots +x_{n}^{2}\leqslant R^{2}$ 上的 $_n$ 重积分 $(n\geqslant 2)$

$$
\iint_ {\Omega} \dots \int f (\sqrt {x _ {1} ^ {2} + x _ {2} ^ {2} + \cdots + x _ {n} ^ {2}}) d x _ {1} d x _ {2} \dots d x _ {n}
$$

化为一重积分，其中 $f(u)$ 为连续函数

解 作代换 $x_{1} = Rr\cos \varphi$

$$
x _ {2} = R r \sin \varphi_ {1} \cos \varphi_ {2},
$$

：

$$
\begin{array}{l} x _ {n - 1} = R r \sin \varphi_ {1} \sin \varphi_ {2} \dots \sin \varphi_ {n - 2} \cos \varphi_ {n - 1}, \\ x _ {n} = R r \sin \varphi_ {1} \sin \varphi_ {2} \dots \sin \varphi_ {n - 2} \sin \varphi_ {n - 1}, \\ \end{array}
$$

则有 $I = R^{n}r^{n - 1}\sin^{n - 2}\varphi_{1}\sin^{n - 3}\varphi_{2}\dots \sin \varphi_{n - 2},$

于是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} \iint_ {\Omega} \dots \int f (\sqrt {x _ {1} ^ {2} + x _ {2} ^ {2} + \cdots + x _ {n} ^ {2}}) d x _ {1} d x _ {2} \dots d x _ {n} \\ = R ^ {n} \int_ {0} ^ {1} r ^ {n - 1} f (R r) d r \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} \sin^ {n - 2} \varphi_ {1} d \varphi_ {1} \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} \sin^ {n - 3} \varphi_ {2} d \varphi_ {2} \dots \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} \sin \varphi_ {n - 2} d \varphi_ {n - 2} \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi_ {n - 1} \\ = 2 \pi R ^ {n} \frac {\Gamma \left(\frac {n - 1}{2}\right) \Gamma \left(\frac {1}{2}\right)}{\Gamma \left(\frac {n}{2}\right)} \cdot \frac {\Gamma \left(\frac {n - 2}{2}\right) \Gamma \left(\frac {1}{2}\right)}{\Gamma \left(\frac {n - 1}{2}\right)} \dots \frac {\Gamma \left(\frac {2}{2}\right) \Gamma \left(\frac {1}{2}\right)}{\Gamma \left(\frac {3}{2}\right)} \int_ {0} ^ {1} r ^ {n - 1} f (R r) d r ^ {*}, \\ = R ^ {n} \frac {2 \pi \cdot \pi^ {\frac {n - 2}{2}}}{\Gamma \left(\frac {n}{2}\right)} \int_ {0} ^ {1} r ^ {n - 1} f (R r) d r = R ^ {n} \frac {\pi^ {\frac {n}{2}}}{\Gamma \left(\frac {n}{2}\right)} \int_ {0} ^ {1} \left(r ^ {2}\right) ^ {\frac {n}{2}} ^ {- 1} f (R r) d \left(r ^ {2}\right) \\ = R ^ {n} \frac {\pi^ {\frac {n}{2}}}{\Gamma \left(\frac {n}{2}\right)} \int_ {0} ^ {1} u ^ {\frac {n}{2}} f (R \sqrt {u}) d u. \\ \end{array}
$$

\*) 参看 4210 题的计算过程.

【4219】计算半径为 $R$ ，密度为 $\rho_0$ 的均质球对自身的引力势，即求积分

$$
u = \frac {\rho_ {0} ^ {2}}{2} \iiint_ {x _ {1} ^ {2} + y _ {1} ^ {2} + z _ {1} ^ {2} \leqslant R ^ {2}} \frac {\mathrm {d} x _ {1} \mathrm {d} y _ {1} \mathrm {d} z _ {1} \mathrm {d} x _ {2} \mathrm {d} y _ {2} \mathrm {d} z _ {2}}{r _ {1 , 2}},
$$

式中 $r_{1,2} = \sqrt{(x_1 - x_2)^2 + (y_1 - y_2)^2 + (z_1 - z_2)^2}$

解 我们有

$$
u = \frac {\rho_ {0} ^ {2}}{2} \iiint_ {x _ {1} ^ {2} + y _ {1} ^ {2} + z _ {1} ^ {2} \leqslant R ^ {2}} d x _ {1} d y _ {1} d z _ {1} \iiint_ {x _ {2} ^ {2} + y _ {2} ^ {2} + z _ {2} ^ {2} \leqslant R ^ {2}} \frac {d x _ {2} d y _ {2} d z _ {2}}{r _ {1 , 2}}.
$$

由4155题的结果可知 $\iint_{x_2^2 + y_2^2 + z_2^2 \leqslant R^2} \frac{\mathrm{d}x_2 \mathrm{d}y_2 \mathrm{d}z_2}{r_{1,2}} = 2\pi R^2 - \frac{2}{3}\pi r_1^2,$

其中 $r_1 = \sqrt{x_1^2 + y_1^2 + z_1^2}$ . 于是（利用球坐标），

$$
\begin{array}{l} u = \frac {\rho_ {0} ^ {2}}{2} \iiint_ {x _ {1} ^ {2} - y _ {1} ^ {2} + z _ {1} ^ {2} \leqslant R ^ {2}} \left(2 \pi R ^ {2} - \frac {2}{3} \pi r _ {1} ^ {2}\right) d x _ {1} d y _ {1} d z _ {1} = \frac {\rho_ {0}}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d \varphi \int_ {\frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \cos \psi d \psi \int_ {0} ^ {R} \left(2 \pi R ^ {2} - \frac {2}{3} \pi r ^ {2}\right) r ^ {2} d r \\ = \frac {1 6}{1 5} \pi^ {2} \rho_ {0} ^ {2} R ^ {5}. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4220】设 $\sum_{i,j=1}^{n} a_{ij} x_i x_j (a_{ij} = a_{ji})$ 为正定二次型，计算 $n$ 重积分

$$
\int_ {x _ {1}} ^ {+ \infty} \int_ {- \infty} ^ {+ \infty} \dots \int_ {- \infty} ^ {+ \infty} e ^ {- \left\{\sum_ {i, j = 1} ^ {n} a _ {i j} x _ {i} x _ {j} + 2 \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {n} b _ {i} x _ {j} + c \right\}} d x _ {1} d x _ {2} \dots d x _ {n}.
$$

解 作变量代换

$$
x _ {i} = y _ {i} + \alpha_ {i} \quad (i = 1, 2, \dots , n), \tag {1}
$$

其中诸常数 $a_{i}$ 以下再确定.于是，易得（注意到 $a_{ij} = a_{ji}$ ）

$$
\begin{array}{l} \sum_ {i, j = 1} ^ {n} a _ {i j} x _ {i} x _ {j} + 2 \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {n} b _ {i} x _ {j} + c \\ = \sum_ {i, j = 1} ^ {n} a _ {i j} y _ {i} y _ {j} + 2 \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {n} \left[ \left(\sum_ {j = 1} ^ {n} a _ {i j} \alpha_ {j}\right) + b _ {i} \right] y _ {i} + \sum_ {i, j = 1} ^ {n} a _ {i j} \alpha_ {i} \alpha_ {j} + 2 \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {n} b _ {i} \alpha_ {i} + c. \\ \end{array}
$$

由于 $\sum_{i,j=1}^{n} a_{ij} x_i x_j$ 是正定形，故必有 $\delta = |a_{ij}| > 0$ ，从而，线性方程组

$$
\sum_ {j = 1} ^ {n} a _ {i j} \alpha_ {j} + b _ {i} = 0 \quad (i = 1, 2, \dots , n) \tag {2}
$$

有唯一的一组解 $\alpha_{1},\dots ,\alpha_{n}$ ，今取变换(1)式中的诸 $\alpha_{i}$ 即为方程组(2)的解.于是，

$$
\sum_ {i, j = 1} ^ {n} a _ {i j} x _ {i} x _ {j} + 2 \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {n} b _ {i} x _ {i} + c = \sum_ {i, j = 1} ^ {n} a _ {i j} y _ {i} y _ {j} + c ^ {\prime}, \tag {3}
$$

其中

$$
c ^ {\prime} = \sum_ {i - 1} ^ {n} \left(\sum_ {j = 1} ^ {n} a _ {i j} \alpha_ {j}\right) \alpha_ {i} + 2 \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {n} b _ {i} \alpha_ {i} + c = - \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {n} b _ {i} \alpha_ {i} + 2 \sum_ {i - 1} ^ {n} b _ {i} \alpha_ {i} + c = \sum_ {i - 1} ^ {n} b _ {i} \alpha_ {i} + c. \tag {4}
$$

下面我们用诸 $a_{ij}$ 和 $b_{i}$ 及 $c$ 来表示 $c^{\prime}$ , 令

$$
\Delta = \left| \begin{array}{c c c} a _ {i j} & \vdots & b _ {i} \\ \dots \dots \dots \dots \\ b _ {j} & \vdots & c \end{array} \right| = \left| \begin{array}{c c c c} a _ {1 1} & \dots & a _ {1 n} & b _ {1} \\ \vdots & & \vdots & \vdots \\ a _ {n 1} & \dots & a _ {m n} & b _ {n} \\ b _ {1} & \dots & b _ {n} & c \end{array} \right|
$$

$(n + 1$ 阶行列式，即 $\left|a_{ij}\right|$ 的加边行列式).将此行列式的第一列乘上 $\alpha_{1}$ ，第二列乘上 $\alpha_{2},\dots ,$ 第 $n$ 列乘上 $\alpha_{n}$ 都加到第 $n + 1$ 列上去，并注意到(2)式与(4)式，得

$$
\Delta = \left| \begin{array}{c c c} a _ {i j} & \vdots & b _ {i} \\ \dots \dots \dots \dots \\ b _ {j} & \vdots & c \end{array} \right| = \left| \begin{array}{c c c} a _ {i j} & \sum_ {j = 1} ^ {n} a _ {i j} \alpha_ {j} + b _ {i} \\ \dots & \dots & \dots \\ b _ {j} & \sum_ {j = 1} ^ {n} b _ {j} \alpha_ {j} + c \end{array} \right| = \left| \begin{array}{c c c} a _ {i j} & \vdots & 0 \\ \dots \dots \dots \dots \\ b _ {j} & \vdots & c ^ {\prime} \end{array} \right| = c ^ {\prime} | a _ {i j} | = c ^ {\prime} \delta ,
$$

故 $c^{\prime} = \frac{\Delta}{\delta}$ (5）

由于 $\sum_{i,j=1}^{n} a_{ij} y_i y_j$ 是正定二次型，故由高等代数中二次型的理论知，存在正交矩阵

$$
P = \left(p _ {i j}\right) = \left[ \begin{array}{c c c} p _ {1 1} & \dots & p _ {1 n} \\ \vdots & & \vdots \\ p _ {n 1} & \dots & p _ {m} \end{array} \right],
$$

使在线性变换

$$
y _ {i} = \sum_ {j = 1} ^ {n} p _ {i j} z _ {j}, \quad (i = 1, 2, \dots , n) \tag {6}
$$

下，二次型变为平方和：

$$
\sum_ {i, j = 1} ^ {n} a _ {i j} y _ {i} y _ {j} = \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {n} \lambda_ {i} z _ {i} ^ {2}, \tag {7}
$$

其中 $\lambda_{i} > 0 (i = 1,2,\dots ,n)$ ；也即

$$
P ^ {- 1} A P = \left[ \begin{array}{l l l} \lambda_ {1} & & 0 \\ & \ddots & \\ 0 & & \lambda_ {n} \end{array} \right], \tag {8}
$$

其中 $A = (a_{ij}) = \begin{bmatrix} a_{11} & \dots & a_{1n}\\ \vdots & & \vdots \\ a_{n1} & \dots & a_{nn} \end{bmatrix}$ .由于 $P$ 为正交矩阵，故 $P^{-1} = P^{\prime}(P^{\prime}$ 表 $P$ 的转置矩阵)，且 $|P| = |p_{ij}| = \pm 1.$

由（8）式又知

$$
\delta = \left| a _ {i j} \right| = \left| P ^ {- 1} \right| \cdot | A | \cdot | P | = \lambda_ {1} \lambda_ {2} \dots \lambda_ {n}. \tag {9}
$$

根据（1）式与（6）式，可知

$$
\frac {D \left(x _ {1} , \cdots , x _ {n}\right)}{D \left(y _ {1} , \cdots , y _ {n}\right)} = 1, \quad \frac {D \left(y _ {1} , \cdots , y _ {n}\right)}{D \left(z _ {1} , \cdots , z _ {n}\right)} = \left| p _ {i j} \right| = | P | = \pm 1.
$$

于是，利用广义 $n$ 重积分的变量代换公式，并注意到被积函数的非负性，得（注意(3)式、（5)式与(7)式）

$$
\begin{array}{l} I = \int_ {- \infty} ^ {+ \infty} \int_ {- \infty} ^ {+ \infty} \dots \int_ {- \infty} ^ {+ \infty} e ^ {- \left\{\sum_ {i, j = 1} ^ {n} a _ {i j} x _ {i} x _ {j} + 2 \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {n} b _ {i} x _ {i} + c \right\}} d x _ {1} d x _ {2} \dots d x _ {n} \\ = \int_ {- \infty} ^ {+ \infty} \int_ {- \infty} ^ {+ \infty} \dots \int_ {- \infty} ^ {+ \infty} e ^ {- \left\{\sum_ {i, j = 1} ^ {n} a _ {i j} y _ {i} y _ {j} + \epsilon^ {\prime} \right\}} \left| \frac {D (x _ {1} , \cdots , x _ {n})}{D (y _ {1} , \cdots , y _ {n})} \right| d y _ {1} d y _ {2} \dots d y _ {n} \\ = \mathrm {e} ^ {- \frac {\Delta}{\delta}} \int_ {- \infty} ^ {+ \infty} \int_ {- \infty} ^ {+ \infty} \dots \int_ {- \infty} ^ {+ \infty} \mathrm {e} ^ {- \left\{\sum_ {i, j = 1} ^ {n} a _ {i j} y _ {i} y _ {j} \right\}} d y _ {1} d y _ {2} \dots d y _ {n} \\ = \mathrm {e} ^ {- \frac {\Delta}{\delta}} \int_ {- \infty} ^ {+ \infty} \int_ {- \infty} ^ {+ \infty} \dots \int_ {- \infty} ^ {+ \infty} \mathrm {e} ^ {- \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {n} \lambda_ {i} z _ {i} ^ {2}} \left| \frac {D (y _ {1} , \cdots , y _ {n})}{D (z _ {1} , \cdots , z _ {n})} \right| d z _ {1} d z _ {2} \dots d z _ {n} \\ = \mathrm {e} ^ {- \frac {\Delta}{\delta}} \int_ {- \infty} ^ {+ \infty} \int_ {- \infty} ^ {+ \infty} \dots \int_ {- \infty} ^ {+ \infty} \mathrm {e} ^ {- \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {n} \lambda_ {i} z _ {i} ^ {2}} d z _ {1} d z _ {2} \dots d z _ {n} \\ = \mathrm {e} ^ {- \frac {\Delta}{\delta}} \left(\int_ {- \infty} ^ {+ \infty} \mathrm {e} ^ {- \lambda_ {1} z _ {1} ^ {2}} \mathrm {d} z _ {1}\right) \left(\int_ {- \infty} ^ {+ \infty} \mathrm {e} ^ {- \lambda_ {2} z _ {2} ^ {2}} \mathrm {d} z _ {2}\right) \dots \left(\int_ {- \infty} ^ {+ \infty} \mathrm {e} ^ {- \lambda_ {n} z _ {n} ^ {2}} \mathrm {d} z _ {n}\right). \\ \end{array}
$$

作代换 $z_{i} = \frac{u}{\sqrt{\lambda_{i}}}$ （i固定），得

$$
\int_ {- \infty} ^ {+ \infty} e ^ {- \lambda_ {i} z _ {i} ^ {2}} d z _ {i} = \frac {1}{\sqrt {\lambda_ {i}}} \int_ {- \infty} ^ {+ \infty} e ^ {- u ^ {2}} d u = \frac {2}{\sqrt {\lambda_ {i}}} \int_ {0} ^ {+ \infty} e ^ {- u ^ {2}} d u = \frac {\sqrt {\pi}}{\sqrt {\lambda_ {i}}} (i = 1, 2, \dots , n).
$$

以此代入上式，并注意到（9）式，最后得

$$
I = \int_ {- \infty} ^ {+ \infty} \int_ {- \infty} ^ {+ \infty} \dots \int_ {- \infty} ^ {+ \infty} e ^ {- \left\{\sum_ {i, j = 1} ^ {n} a _ {i j} x _ {i} x _ {j} + 2 \sum_ {i = 1} ^ {n} b _ {i} x _ {i} + c \right\}} d x _ {1} d x _ {2} \dots d x _ {n} = e ^ {- \frac {\Delta}{\delta}} \frac {\pi^ {\frac {n}{2}}}{\sqrt {\lambda_ {1} \lambda_ {2} \cdots \lambda_ {n}}} = \sqrt {\frac {\pi^ {n}}{\delta}} e ^ {- \frac {\Delta}{\delta}}.
$$

# §11. 曲线积分

$1^{\circ}$ 第一型曲线积分 若函数 $f(x,y,z)$ 在平滑曲线 $C$

$$
x = x (t), \quad y = y (t), \quad z = z (t) (t _ {0} \leqslant t \leqslant T) \tag {1}
$$

的各点上有定义并且连续，ds为弧长的微分，则

$$
\int_ {c} f (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} s = \int_ {t _ {0}} ^ {T} f [ x (t), y (t), z (t) ] \sqrt {x ^ {\prime 2} (t) + y ^ {\prime 2} (t) + z ^ {\prime 2} (t)} \mathrm {d} t.
$$

这个积分的特征在于它与曲线 $C$ 的方向无关

$2^{\circ}$ 第一型曲线积分在力学上的应用 若 $\rho = \rho(x, y, z)$ 为曲线 $C$ 在点 $(x, y, z)$ 的线密度，则曲线 $C$ 的质量等于：

$$
M = \int_ {C} \rho (x, y, z) d s.
$$

此曲线的质心坐标 $(x_0, y_0, z_0)$ 由以下公式来表示：

$$
x _ {0} = \frac {1}{M} \int_ {C} x \rho (x, y, z) d s, \quad y _ {0} = \frac {1}{M} \int_ {C} y \rho (x, y, z) d s, \quad z _ {0} = \frac {1}{M} \int_ {C} z \rho (x, y, z) d s.
$$

$3^{\circ}$ 第二型曲线积分 若函数 $P = P(x,y,z), Q = Q(x,y,z), R = R(x,y,z)$ 在曲线(1)上的各点是连续的，且曲线的方向是使参数 $t$ 增加的方向，则

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int_ {C} P (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} x + Q (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} y + R (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} z \\ = \int_ {t _ {0}} ^ {T} \left\{P [ x (t), y (t), z (t) ] x ^ {\prime} (t) + Q [ x (t), y (t), z (t) ] y ^ {\prime} (t) + R [ x (t), y (t), z (t) ] z ^ {\prime} (t) \right\} d t. \tag {2} \\ \end{array}
$$

当沿曲线 $C$ 的方向变更时，此积分的符号也变更.在力学上积分(2)是当其作用点描绘出曲线 $C$ 时变力 $\{P,Q,R\}$ 所作的功.

4°全微分的情形 若

$$
P (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} x + Q (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} y + R (x, y, z) \mathrm {d} z = \mathrm {d} u,
$$

式中 $u = u(x,y,z)$ 为区域 $V$ 内的单值函数，则积分值与完全位于区域 $V$ 内的曲线 $C$ 的形状无关；

$$
\int_ {C} P \mathrm {d} x + Q \mathrm {d} y + R \mathrm {d} z = u \left(x _ {2}, y _ {2}, z _ {2}\right) - u \left(x _ {1}, y _ {1}, z _ {1}\right),
$$

式中 $(x_{1},y_{1},z_{1})$ 为积分路径的始点， $(x_{2},y_{2},z_{2})$ 为其终点.最简单的情况下，若区域 $V$ 是单联通的，而函数 $P,Q,R$ 有连续的一阶偏导数，则上式成立的充分必要条件为：在区域 $V$ 内，下列条件恒满足：

$$
\frac {\partial P}{\partial y} = \frac {\partial Q}{\partial x}, \quad \frac {\partial Q}{\partial z} = \frac {\partial R}{\partial y}, \quad \frac {\partial R}{\partial x} = \frac {\partial P}{\partial z}.
$$

这时，在区域 $V$ 是标准长方体这种简单情形下，函数 $\pmb{u}$ 可按下面的公式来求得

$$
u (x, y, z) = \int_ {x _ {0}} ^ {x} P (x, y, z) d x + \int_ {y _ {0}} ^ {y} Q (x _ {0}, y, z) d y + \int_ {z _ {0}} ^ {z} R (x _ {0}, y _ {0}, z) d z + c,
$$

其中 $(x_0, y_0, z_0)$ 为区域 $V$ 内某一固定的点，而 $c$ 是任意常数。

# 计算下列第一型曲线积分：

【4221】 $\int_{C} (x + y) \mathrm{d}s$ ，其中 $C$ 为以 $O(0,0), A(1,0)$ 和 $B(0,1)$ 为顶点的三角形围线.

解 $\int_{C}(x + y)\mathrm{d}s = \int_{OA}(x + y)\mathrm{d}s + \int_{AB}(x + y)\mathrm{d}s + \int_{BO}(x + y)\mathrm{d}s$

$$
= \int_ {0} ^ {1} x \mathrm {d} x + \int_ {0} ^ {1} \sqrt {2} \mathrm {d} x + \int_ {0} ^ {1} y \mathrm {d} y = 1 + \sqrt {2}.
$$

【4222】 $\int_{C}y^{2}\mathrm{d}s$ ，其中 $C$ 为摆线 $x = a(t - \sin t),y = a(1 - \cos t)(0\leqslant t\leqslant 2\pi)$ 的一拱.

解 弧长的微分为 $\mathrm{ds} = \sqrt{(\mathrm{dx})^2 + (\mathrm{dy})^2} = \sqrt{a^2(1 - \cos t)^2 + a^2\sin^2t}\mathrm{dt} = 2a\sin \frac{t}{2}\mathrm{dt}.$

于是， $\int_{C}y^{2}\mathrm{d}s = 2a^{3}\int_{0}^{2\pi}\sin {\frac{t}{2}}(1 - \cos t)^{2}\mathrm{d}t = 8a^{3}\int_{0}^{2\pi}\sin^{5}\frac{t}{2}\mathrm{d}t = 32a^{3}\int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}}\sin^{5}u\mathrm{d}u = \frac{256}{15} a^{3}.$

【4223】 $\int_{C} (x^{2} + y^{2}) \mathrm{d}s$ 其中 $C$ 为曲线 $x = a(\cos t + t \sin t), y = a(\sin t - t \cos t) (0 \leqslant t \leqslant 2\pi)$ .

解 弧长的微分为 $\mathrm{ds} = \sqrt{a^2t^2\cos^2t + a^2t^2\sin^2t}\mathrm{dt} = at\mathrm{dt}.$

于是， $\int_{C} (x^2 + y^2) \, \mathrm{d}s = \int_{0}^{2\pi} [a^2 (\cos t + t \sin t)^2 + a^2 (\sin t - t \cos t)^2] at \, \mathrm{d}t = \int_{0}^{2\pi} a^3 t (1 + t^2) \, \mathrm{d}t = 2\pi^2 a^3 (1 + 2\pi^2).$

【4224】 $\int_{C} xy \, \mathrm{d}s$ 其中 $C$ 为双曲线 $x = a \cosh t, y = a \sinh t (0 \leqslant t \leqslant t_0)$ 的弧.

解 弧长的微分为 $\mathrm{ds} = \sqrt{a^2\mathrm{sh}^2t + a^2\mathrm{ch}^2t}\mathrm{dt} = a\sqrt{\mathrm{ch}2t}\mathrm{dt}.$

于是， $\int_{C}xy\mathrm{d}s = a^{3}\int_{0}^{t_{0}}\mathrm{ch}t\mathrm{sh}t\sqrt{\mathrm{ch}2t}\mathrm{d}t = \frac{a^{3}}{2}\int_{0}^{t_{0}}\mathrm{sh}2t\sqrt{\mathrm{ch}2t}\mathrm{d}t = \frac{a^{3}}{4}\int_{0}^{t_{0}}\sqrt{\mathrm{ch}2t}\mathrm{d}(\mathrm{ch}2t) = \frac{a^{3}}{6} (\sqrt{\mathrm{ch}^{3}2t_{0}} -1).$

【4225】 $\int_{C} (x^{\frac{1}{3}} + y^{\frac{1}{3}}) \mathrm{d}s$ ，其中 $C$ 为星形线 $x^{\frac{2}{3}} + y^{\frac{2}{3}} = a^{\frac{2}{3}}$ 的弧.

解解法1：

按直角坐标方程计算，弧长的微分为 $\mathrm{ds} = \sqrt{1 + y'^2}\mathrm{dx} = \frac{a^{\frac{1}{3}}}{x^{\frac{1}{3}}}\mathrm{dx}.$

于是， $\int_{C} (x^{\frac{4}{3}} + y^{\frac{4}{3}}) \mathrm{d}s = 4\int_{0}^{a} [x^{\frac{4}{3}} + (a^{\frac{2}{3}} - x^{\frac{2}{3}})^{2}] \frac{a^{\frac{1}{3}}}{x^{\frac{1}{3}}} \mathrm{d}x = 4a^{\frac{1}{3}}\int_{0}^{a} (2x + a^{\frac{4}{3}}x^{-\frac{1}{3}} - 2a^{\frac{2}{3}}x^{\frac{1}{3}}) \mathrm{d}x = 4a^{\frac{7}{3}}.$

解法2：

按参数方程计算. 若令 $x = a\cos^3 t, y = a\sin^3 t$ ，则

$$
\mathrm {d} s = \sqrt {9 a ^ {2} \cos^ {4} t \sin^ {2} t + 9 a ^ {2} \sin^ {4} t \cos^ {2} t} \mathrm {d} t = 3 a \cos t \sin t \mathrm {d} t \quad (0 \leqslant t \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}).
$$

于是， $\int_{C} (x^{\frac{4}{3}} + y^{\frac{4}{3}}) \mathrm{d}s = 4a^{\frac{4}{3}} \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} (\cos^{4} t + \sin^{4} t) 3a \cos t \sin t \mathrm{d}t = 24a^{\frac{7}{3}} \int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{2}} \sin^{5} t \mathrm{d}(\sin t) = 4a^{\frac{7}{3}}.$

【4226】 $\int_{C} \mathrm{e}^{\sqrt{x^2 + y^2}} \, \mathrm{d}s$ 其中 $C$ 为由曲线 $r = a, \varphi = 0, \varphi = \frac{\pi}{4}$ （ $r$ 和 $\varphi$ 为极坐标）给出的凸围线.

解 凸围线由三段组成，分别是：直线段 $\varphi = 0$ （ $0 \leqslant r \leqslant a$ ）；圆弧段 $r = a$ （ $0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac{\pi}{4}$ ）；直线段 $\varphi = \frac{\pi}{4}$ （ $0 \leqslant r \leqslant a$ ）。弧长的微分相应地是： $\mathrm{ds} = \mathrm{dr}$ ； $\mathrm{ds} = \sqrt{r^2 + r'^2}$ ； $\mathrm{d}\varphi = a\mathrm{d}\varphi$ ； $\mathrm{ds} = \mathrm{dr}$ 。于是，

$$
\int_ {c} \mathrm {e} ^ {\sqrt {r ^ {2} - r ^ {2}}} \mathrm {d} s = \int_ {0} ^ {a} \mathrm {e} ^ {r} \mathrm {d} r + \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{4}} \mathrm {e} ^ {a} a \mathrm {d} \varphi + \int_ {0} ^ {a} \mathrm {e} ^ {r} \mathrm {d} r = 2 (\mathrm {e} ^ {a} - 1) + \frac {\pi a \mathrm {e} ^ {a}}{4}.
$$

【4227】 $\int_{C} |y| \mathrm{d}s$ 其中 $C$ 为双纽线 $(x^{2} + y^{2})^{2} = a^{2}(x^{2} - y^{2})$ 的弧.

解 双纽线的极坐标方程为 $r^2 = a^2\cos 2\varphi$ ，弧长的微分为

$$
\mathrm {d} s = \sqrt {r ^ {2} + r ^ {\prime 2}} \mathrm {d} \varphi = \frac {a}{\sqrt {\cos 2 \varphi}} \mathrm {d} \varphi .
$$

于是， $\int_{C}|y|\mathrm{d}s = 4\int_{0}^{\frac{\pi}{4}}a\sqrt{\cos2\varphi}\sin \varphi \frac{a}{\sqrt{\cos2\varphi}}\mathrm{d}\varphi = 4a^{2}(-\cos \varphi)\left| \begin{array}{l}\frac{\pi}{4}\\ 0 \end{array} \right. = 2a^{2}(2 - \sqrt{2}).$

【4228】 $\int_{C} x \, \mathrm{d}s$ ，其中 $C$ 为对数螺线 $r = a \mathrm{e}^{k\varphi} (k > 0)$ 在圆 $r = a$ 内的部分。

解 弧长的微分为 $\mathrm{ds} = ae^{k\varphi}\sqrt{1 + k^2}\mathrm{d}\varphi (-\infty < \varphi < 0).$

于是， $\int_{C}x\mathrm{d}s = \int_{C}^{0}ae^{k\varphi}\cos \varphi \cdot ae^{k\varsigma}\sqrt{1 + k^2}\mathrm{d}\varphi = a^2\sqrt{1 + k^2}\frac{2k\cos\varphi + \sin\varphi}{1 + 4k^2}\mathrm{e}^{2k\varphi}\Bigg{|}_{-}^{0} = \frac{2ka^2\sqrt{1 + k^2}}{1 + 4k^2}.$

【4229】 $\int_{C} \sqrt{x^2 + y^2} \, \mathrm{d}s$ ，其中 $C$ 为圆周 $x^2 + y^2 = ax$ .

解 对于上半圆周，弧长的微分为

$$
\mathrm {d} s = \sqrt {1 + \left(\frac {a - 2 x}{2 y}\right) ^ {2}} \mathrm {d} x = \frac {a}{2 y} \mathrm {d} x = \frac {a}{2 \sqrt {a x - x ^ {2}}} \mathrm {d} x \cdot (0 \leqslant x \leqslant a).
$$

于是， $\int_{c} \sqrt{x^2 + y^2} \, \mathrm{d}s = 2\int_{a}^{a} \sqrt{ax} \frac{a}{2\sqrt{ax - x^2}} \, \mathrm{d}x = a\sqrt{a}\int_{a}^{a} \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{a - x}} = 2a^2.$

【4230】 $\int_{C} \frac{\mathrm{d}s}{y^2}$ ，其中 $C$ 为悬链线 $y = a \operatorname{ch} \frac{x}{a}$

解 弧长的微分为 $\mathrm{ds} = \sqrt{1 + \mathrm{sh}^2\frac{x}{a}}\mathrm{dx} = \mathrm{ch}\frac{x}{a}\mathrm{dx}.$

于是， $\int_{c} \frac{\mathrm{d}s}{y^2} = \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty} \frac{\operatorname{ch} \frac{x}{a}}{a^2 \operatorname{ch}^2 \frac{x}{a}} \mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{a} \int_{-\infty}^{+\infty} \frac{\operatorname{d}\left(\operatorname{sh} \frac{x}{a}\right)}{1 + \operatorname{sh}^2 \frac{x}{a}} = \frac{1}{a} \arctan \left(\operatorname{sh} \frac{x}{a}\right) \Bigg|_{-\infty}^{+\infty} = \frac{\pi}{a}.$

# 求下列空间曲线的弧长（参数是正的）：

【4231】 $x = 3t, y = 3t^2, z = 2t^3$ ，从 $O(0,0,0)$ 到 $A(3,3,2)$

解弧长的微分为 $\mathrm{ds} = \sqrt{x'^2 + y'^2 + z'^2}\mathrm{dt} = 3(2t^2 +1)\mathrm{dt}.$

于是，弧长为 $s = \int_{0}^{1}3(2t^{2} + 1)\mathrm{d}t = 5.$

【4232】 $r = \mathrm{e}^{-t}\cos t, y = \mathrm{e}^{-t}\sin t, z = \mathrm{e}^{-t}$ ，当 $0 < t < +\infty$

解 弧长的微分为 $\mathrm{ds} = \sqrt{\mathrm{e}^{2t} (\cos t - \sin t)^2 + \mathrm{e}^{-2t} (\cos t + \sin t)^2 + \mathrm{e}^{-2t}} \, \mathrm{dt} = \sqrt{3} \mathrm{e}^t \, \mathrm{dt}$ .

于是，弧长为 $s = \sqrt{3}\int_{0}^{+\infty}\mathrm{e}^{-t}\mathrm{d}t = \sqrt{3}.$

【4233】 $y = a\arcsin \frac{x}{a}, z = \frac{a}{4}\ln \frac{a - x}{a + x}$ 从 $O(0,0,0)$ 到 $A(x_0, y_0, z_0)$ .

解 弧长的微分为 $\mathrm{ds} = \sqrt{1 - \frac{a^2}{a^4 - x^2} + \frac{a^4}{4(a^2 - x^2)^2}} = \frac{3a^2 - 2x^2}{2(a^2 - x^2)}\mathrm{d}x$ （ $|x_0| < a)$

于是，当 $x_0 \geq 0$ 时，有

$$
s = \int_ {0} ^ {x _ {0}} \frac {3 a ^ {2} - 2 x ^ {2}}{2 \left(a ^ {2} - x ^ {2}\right)} d x = \frac {a}{4} \ln \frac {a + x _ {0}}{a - x _ {0}} + x _ {0} = | z _ {0} | + | x _ {0} |;
$$

当 $x_0 < 0$ 时，有

$$
s = \int_ {x _ {0}} ^ {0} \frac {3 a ^ {2} - 2 x ^ {2}}{2 \left(a ^ {2} - x ^ {2}\right)} d x = - \frac {a}{4} \ln \frac {a + x _ {0}}{a - x _ {0}} - x _ {0} = | z _ {0} | + | x _ {0} |.
$$

总之，当 $|x_0| < a$ ，有 $s = |z_0| + |x_0|$

【4234】 $(x - y)^{2} = a(x + y), x^{2} - y^{2} = \frac{9}{8} z^{2}$ ，从 $O(0,0,0)$ 到 $A(x_{0},y_{0},z_{0})$

解 由 $(x - y)^2 = a(x + y), x^2 - y^2 = \frac{9}{8} z^2$ 可解得

$$
x = \frac {1}{2} \left[ \frac {1}{a} \sqrt [ 3 ]{\left(\frac {9 a}{8}\right) ^ {2}} \sqrt [ 3 ]{z ^ {4}} + \sqrt [ 3 ]{\frac {9 a}{8}} \sqrt [ 3 ]{z ^ {2}} \right], \quad y = \frac {1}{2} \left[ \frac {1}{a} \sqrt [ 3 ]{\left(\frac {9 a}{8}\right) ^ {2}} \sqrt [ 3 ]{z ^ {4}} - \sqrt [ 3 ]{\frac {9 a}{8}} \sqrt [ 3 ]{z ^ {2}} \right].
$$

注意到

$$
\left(\frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\mathrm {d} z}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\mathrm {d} y}{\mathrm {d} z}\right) ^ {2} = \frac {8}{9 a ^ {2}} \sqrt [ 3 ]{\left(\frac {9 a}{8}\right) ^ {4}} \sqrt [ 3 ]{z ^ {2}} + \frac {2}{9} \sqrt [ 3 ]{\left(\frac {9 a}{8}\right) ^ {2}} \sqrt [ 3 ]{z ^ {- 2}} = \frac {\sqrt [ 3 ]{9 a}}{2 a} \sqrt [ 3 ]{z ^ {2}} + \frac {\sqrt [ 3 ]{3 a ^ {2}}}{6} \sqrt [ 3 ]{z ^ {- 2}},
$$

于是，弧长为

$$
s = \int_ {0} ^ {z _ {0}} \sqrt {\frac {\sqrt [ 3 ]{9 a}}{2 a} \sqrt [ 3 ]{z ^ {2}} + \frac {\sqrt [ 3 ]{3 a ^ {2}}}{6} \sqrt [ 3 ]{z ^ {- 2}} + 1} d z = \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt [ 3 ]{z _ {0} ^ {2}}} \sqrt {\frac {\sqrt [ 3 ]{9 a}}{2 a} t + \frac {\sqrt [ 3 ]{3 a ^ {2}}}{6} \frac {1}{t} + 1} \frac {3 \sqrt {t}}{2} d t
$$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \frac {3}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt [ 3 ]{z _ {0} ^ {2}}} \sqrt {\frac {\sqrt [ 3 ]{9 a}}{2 a} t ^ {2} + t + \frac {\sqrt [ 3 ]{3 a ^ {2}}}{6}} d t = \frac {3}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {\sqrt [ 3 ]{z _ {0} ^ {2}}} \left(\frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \sqrt [ 3 ]{\frac {3}{a}} t + \frac {1}{\sqrt {2}} \sqrt [ 3 ]{\frac {a}{3}}\right) d t \\ = \frac {3}{4 \sqrt {2}} \left(\sqrt [ 3 ]{\frac {3 z _ {0} ^ {4}}{a}} + 2 \sqrt [ 3 ]{\frac {a z _ {0} ^ {2}}{3}}\right). \\ \end{array}
$$

【4235】 $x^{2} + y^{2} = cz, \frac{y}{x} = \tan \frac{z}{c}$ 从 $O(0,0,0)$ 到 $A(x_{0},y_{0},z_{0})$

提示 取曲线的参数方程为 $x = \sqrt{cz}\cos \frac{z}{c}, y = \sqrt{cz}\sin \frac{z}{c}, z = z.$

解取曲线的参数方程为 $x = \sqrt{cz}\cos \frac{z}{c},y = \sqrt{cz}\sin \frac{z}{c},z = z$ ，则弧长的微分为

$$
\begin{array}{l} \mathrm {d} s = \left[ \left(\frac {\sqrt {c}}{2 \sqrt {z}} \cos \frac {z}{c} - \sqrt {\frac {z}{c}} \sin \frac {z}{c}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\sqrt {c}}{2 \sqrt {z}} \sin \frac {z}{c} - \sqrt {\frac {z}{c}} \cos \frac {z}{c}\right) ^ {2} + 1 \right] ^ {\frac {1}{2}} \mathrm {d} z = \sqrt {\frac {c}{4 z} + \frac {z}{c} + 1} \mathrm {d} z \\ = \frac {2 z + c}{\sqrt {4 c z}} d z. \\ \end{array}
$$

于是，弧长为

$$
s = \int_ {0} ^ {z _ {0}} \frac {2 z + c}{\sqrt {4 c z}} d z = \int_ {0} ^ {z _ {0}} \sqrt {\frac {z}{c}} d z + \int_ {0} ^ {z _ {0}} \frac {\sqrt {c}}{2 \sqrt {z}} d z = \sqrt {c z _ {0}} \left(1 + \frac {2 z _ {0}}{3 c}\right).
$$

【4236】 $x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2} = a^{2},\sqrt{x^{2} + y^{2}}\mathrm{ch}\left(\arctan \frac{y}{x}\right) = a$ ，从点 $(a,0,0)$ 到点 $B(x,y,z)$

解令 $x = \sqrt{a^2 - z^2}\cos \varphi ,y = \sqrt{a^2 - z^2}\sin \varphi$ ，不妨设 $z > 0$ ，则有

$$
z = \sqrt {a ^ {2} - (x ^ {2} + y ^ {2})} = \sqrt {a ^ {2} \left(1 - \frac {1}{\operatorname {c h} ^ {2} \varphi}\right)} = a \operatorname {t h} \varphi .
$$

而 $\sqrt{a^2 - z^2} = \sqrt{a^2(1 - \mathrm{th}^2\varphi)} = \frac{a}{\mathrm{ch}\varphi}$ 故 $x = \frac{a\cos\varphi}{\mathrm{ch}\varphi},y = \frac{a\sin\varphi}{\mathrm{ch}\varphi},z = a\mathrm{th}\varphi$ 为曲线的参数方程，弧长的微分为

$$
\mathrm {d} s = \sqrt {\left(\frac {\mathrm {d} x}{\mathrm {d} \varphi}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\mathrm {d} y}{\mathrm {d} \varphi}\right) ^ {2} + \left(\frac {\mathrm {d} z}{\mathrm {d} \varphi}\right) ^ {2}} \mathrm {d} \varphi = a \sqrt {\frac {\mathrm {c h} ^ {2} \varphi + \mathrm {s h} ^ {2} \varphi + 1}{\mathrm {c h} ^ {4} \varphi}} \mathrm {d} \varphi = \sqrt {2} a \frac {\mathrm {d} \varphi}{\mathrm {c h} \varphi}.
$$

于是，弧长为

$$
\begin{array}{l} s = \int_ {0} ^ {\varphi} \sqrt {2} a \frac {\mathrm {d} \varphi}{\mathrm {c h} \varphi} = \sqrt {2} a \int_ {0} ^ {\varphi} \frac {2}{\mathrm {e} ^ {\varphi} + \mathrm {e} ^ {- \varphi}} \mathrm {d} \varphi = 2 \sqrt {2} a \int_ {0} ^ {\varphi} \frac {1}{1 + (\mathrm {e} ^ {\varphi}) ^ {2}} \mathrm {d} (\mathrm {e} ^ {\varphi}) \\ = 2 \sqrt {2} a \arctan^ {\varphi} \left| _ {0} ^ {\varphi} = 2 \sqrt {2} a \left(\arctan \frac {a + z}{\sqrt {a ^ {2} - z ^ {2}}} - \frac {\pi}{4}\right) ^ {*}\right) = \sqrt {2} a \arctan \frac {z}{\sqrt {a ^ {2} - z ^ {2}}} ^ {* *}) \\ \end{array}
$$

容易推证，当 $z < 0$ 时，弧长为 $s = \sqrt{2} a\arctan \frac{-z}{\sqrt{a^2 - z^2}}.$

总之，最后得 $s = \sqrt{2} a\arctan{\frac{|z|}{\sqrt{a^2 - z^2}}}$

\*）由 $z = a\tan \varphi$ 知： $z(\mathrm{e}^{\varphi} + \mathrm{e}^{-\varphi}) = a(\mathrm{e}^{\varphi} - \mathrm{e}^{-\varphi}),\quad z(\mathrm{e}^{2\varphi} + 1) = a(\mathrm{e}^{2\varphi} - 1),$

从而， $\mathrm{e}^{2\varphi} = \frac{a + z}{a - z}$ 或 $\mathrm{e}^{\varphi} = \frac{a + z}{\sqrt{a^2 - z^2}}.$

$\text{串} \quad \text{串}$ 由于 $\tan \left(\arctan {\frac{a + z}{\sqrt{a^2 - z^2}}} - \frac{\pi}{4}\right) = \frac{a - \sqrt{a^2 - z^2}}{z}, \tan \frac{1}{2}\left(\arctan {\frac{z}{\sqrt{a^2 - z^2}}}\right) = \frac{a - \sqrt{a^2 - z^2}}{z},$

故在主值范围内有 $\arctan \frac{a + z}{\sqrt{a^2 - z^2}} - \frac{\pi}{4} = \frac{1}{2}\arctan \frac{z}{\sqrt{a^2 - z^2}}.$

# 计算沿空间曲线的第一型曲线积分：

【4237】 $\int_{C} (x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2}) \mathrm{d}s$ 其中 $C$ 为螺线 $x = a \cos t, y = a \sin t, z = bt$ （ $0 \leqslant t \leqslant 2\pi$ ）的一段.

解 弧长的微分为 $\mathrm{ds} = \sqrt{a^2 + b^2}\mathrm{dt}$ 于是，

$$
\int_ {C} \left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} + z ^ {2}\right) d s = \sqrt {a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}} \int_ {n} ^ {2 \pi} \left(a ^ {2} + b ^ {2} t ^ {2}\right) d t = \frac {2 \pi}{3} \left(3 a ^ {2} + 4 \pi^ {2} b ^ {2}\right) \sqrt {a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}}.
$$

【4238】 $\int_{C}x^{2}\mathrm{d}s$ ，其中 $C$ 为圆周 $x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2} = a^{2},x + y + z = 0.$

提示 由对称性知： $\int_{C}x^{2}\mathrm{d}s = \int_{C}y^{2}\mathrm{d}s = \int_{C}z^{2}\mathrm{d}s.$

解 解法1：

由对称性知： $\int_{C}x^{2}\mathrm{d}s = \int_{C}y^{2}\mathrm{d}s = \int_{C}z^{2}\mathrm{d}s.$ 于是，

$$
\int_ {C} x ^ {2} \mathrm {d} s = \frac {1}{3} \int_ {C} \left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2} + z ^ {2}\right) \mathrm {d} s = \frac {a ^ {2}}{3} \int_ {C} \mathrm {d} s = \frac {2 \pi a ^ {3}}{3}.
$$

解法2：

作代换 $u = \frac{x - y}{\sqrt{2}}$ ， $v = \frac{x + y - 2z}{\sqrt{6}}$ ， $w = \frac{x + y + z}{\sqrt{3}}$ ，则圆周 $C$ 化为 $u^2 + v^2 + w^2 = a^2$ ， $w = 0$ 。于是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int_ {C} x ^ {2} \mathrm {d} s = \int_ {C} \left(\frac {u}{\sqrt {2}} + \frac {v}{\sqrt {6}} + \frac {w}{\sqrt {3}}\right) ^ {2} \mathrm {d} s = \int_ {C} \left(\frac {u}{\sqrt {2}} + \frac {v}{\sqrt {6}}\right) ^ {2} \mathrm {d} s = \frac {1}{6} \int_ {C} \left(3 u ^ {2} + v ^ {2}\right) \mathrm {d} s + \frac {1}{\sqrt {3}} \int_ {C} u v \mathrm {d} s \\ = \frac {1}{6} \int_ {C} a ^ {2} d s + \frac {1}{3} \int_ {C} u ^ {2} d s + \frac {1}{\sqrt {3}} \int_ {C} u v d s = \frac {1}{3} \pi a ^ {3} + \frac {1}{3} \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} a ^ {3} \cos^ {2} \varphi d \varphi + \frac {1}{\sqrt {3}} \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} a ^ {3} \cos \varphi \sin \varphi d \varphi \\ = \frac {1}{3} \pi a ^ {3} + \frac {1}{3} \pi a ^ {3} = \frac {2}{3} \pi a ^ {3}. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4239】 $\int_{C} z \mathrm{~d}s$ ，其中 $C$ 为圆锥螺旋线 $x = t \cos t, y = t \sin t, z = t (0 \leqslant t \leqslant t_0)$

解 弧长的微分为 $\mathrm{ds} = \sqrt{(\cos t - t\sin t)^2 + (\sin t + t\cos t)^2 + 1}\mathrm{dt} = \sqrt{2 + t^2}\mathrm{dt}.$

于是， $\int_{C}z\mathrm{d}s = \int_{0}^{t_0}t\sqrt{2 + t^2}\mathrm{d}t = \frac{1}{3} [(2 + t_0^2)^{\frac{3}{2}} - 2^{\frac{3}{2}}].$

【4240】 $\int_{C} z \mathrm{~d}s$ ，其中 $C$ 为曲线 $x^{2} + y^{2} = z^{2}, y^{2} = ax$ 上从点 $O(0,0,0)$ 到点 $A(a, a, a\sqrt{2})$ 的弧.

解 由曲线方程得 $z = \sqrt{x^2 + y^2} = \sqrt{\frac{y^4}{a^2} + y^2} = \frac{y}{a}\sqrt{y^2 + a^2},$

从而，曲线的参数方程可取为 $x = \frac{y^2}{a}, y = y, z = \frac{y}{a}\sqrt{y^2 + a^2}.$

弧长的微分为 $\mathrm{ds} = \sqrt{\left(\frac{2y}{a}\right)^{2} + 1 + \left(\frac{2y^{2} + a^{2}}{a\sqrt{y^{2} + a^{2}}}\right)^{2}}\mathrm{dy} = \sqrt{\frac{8y^{4} + 9a^{2}y^{2} + 2a^{4}}{a^{2}(y^{2} + a^{2})}}\mathrm{dy}.$

于是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int_ {C} z \mathrm {d} s = \int_ {0} ^ {a} \frac {y}{a} \sqrt {y ^ {2} + a ^ {2}} \sqrt {\frac {8 y ^ {1} + 9 a ^ {2} y ^ {2} + 2 a ^ {1}}{a ^ {2} (y ^ {2} + a ^ {2})}} \mathrm {d} y = \frac {\sqrt {8}}{a ^ {2}} \int_ {0} ^ {a} y \sqrt {y ^ {1} + \frac {9}{8} a ^ {2} y ^ {2} + \frac {1}{4} a ^ {1}} \mathrm {d} y \\ = \frac {\sqrt {2}}{a ^ {2}} \int_ {0} ^ {a} \sqrt {\left(y ^ {2} + \frac {9 a ^ {2}}{1 6}\right) ^ {2} - \frac {1 7 a ^ {4}}{1 6 ^ {2}}} d \left(y ^ {2} + \frac {9 a ^ {2}}{1 6}\right) \\ = \frac {\sqrt {2}}{a ^ {2}} \left[ \frac {y ^ {2} + \frac {9 a ^ {2}}{1 6}}{2} \sqrt {y ^ {4} + \frac {9}{8} a ^ {2} y ^ {2} + \frac {1}{4} a ^ {4}} - \frac {1 7 a ^ {4}}{2 \cdot 1 6 ^ {2}} \ln \left(y ^ {2} + \frac {9 a ^ {2}}{1 6} + \sqrt {y ^ {4} + \frac {9}{8} a ^ {2} y ^ {2} + \frac {1}{4} a ^ {4}}\right) \right] \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {a} \\ = \frac {\sqrt {2}}{a ^ {2}} \left[ \left(\frac {2 5 a ^ {1}}{6 4} \sqrt {\frac {1 9}{2}} - \frac {1 7 a ^ {1}}{2 \cdot 1 6 ^ {2}} \ln \frac {2 5 a ^ {2} + 8 \sqrt {\frac {1 9}{2}} a ^ {2}}{1 6}\right) - \left(\frac {9 a ^ {1}}{6 4} - \frac {1 7 a ^ {1}}{2 \cdot 1 6 ^ {2}} \ln \frac {1 7 a ^ {2}}{1 6}\right) \right] \\ = \frac {\sqrt {2}}{a ^ {2}} \frac {2 5 a ^ {4} \sqrt {3 8} - 1 8 a ^ {4}}{1 2 8} + \frac {\sqrt {2}}{a ^ {2}} \frac {1 7 a ^ {4}}{2 \cdot 1 6 ^ {2}} \ln \frac {\frac {1 7 a ^ {2}}{1 6}}{\frac {2 5 a ^ {2} + 8 \sqrt {\frac {1 9}{2}} a ^ {2}}{1 6}} \\ \end{array}
$$

$$
= \frac {a ^ {2}}{2 5 6 \sqrt {2}} \left[ 1 0 0 \sqrt {3 8} - 7 2 - 1 7 \ln \frac {2 5 + 4 \sqrt {3 8}}{1 7} \right].
$$

【4241】+ 设曲线 $x = a\cos t, y = b\sin t$ （ $0 \leqslant t \leqslant 2\pi$ ）在点 $(x, y)$ 的线密度等于 $\rho = |y|$ ，求其质量.

解 质量 $M = \int_{C} |y| \, \mathrm{d}s$ ，其中 $C$ 为椭圆 $x = a\cos t, y = b\sin t (0 \leqslant t \leqslant 2\pi)$ .

先设 $a > b$ 这时

$$
\mathrm {d} s = \sqrt {a ^ {2} \sin^ {2} t + b ^ {2} \cos^ {2} t} \mathrm {d} t = a \sqrt {1 - \epsilon^ {2} \cos^ {2} t} \mathrm {d} t
$$

其中 $\varepsilon = \frac{\sqrt{a^2 - b^2}}{a}$ 于是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} M = \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} a b \sin t \sqrt {1 - \varepsilon^ {2} \cos^ {2} t} d t + \int_ {\pi} ^ {2 \pi} a (- b \sin t) \sqrt {1 - \varepsilon^ {2} \cos^ {2} t} d t \\ = - a b \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} \sqrt {1 - \varepsilon^ {2} \cos^ {2} t} d (\cos t) + a b \int_ {\pi} ^ {2 \pi} \sqrt {1 - \varepsilon^ {2} \cos^ {2} t} d (\cos t) \\ = a b \int_ {- 1} ^ {1} \sqrt {1 - \epsilon^ {2} u ^ {2}} d u + a b \int_ {- 1} ^ {1} \sqrt {1 - \epsilon^ {2} u ^ {2}} d u = 1 a b \int_ {0} ^ {1} \sqrt {1 - \epsilon^ {2} u ^ {2}} d u \\ = \frac {4 a b}{\varepsilon} \left[ \frac {1}{2} \varepsilon u \sqrt {1 - \varepsilon^ {2} u ^ {2}} + \frac {1}{2} \arcsin (\varepsilon u) \right] \Bigg | _ {u = 0} ^ {u = 1} = 2 b ^ {2} + 2 a b \frac {\arcsin \varepsilon}{\varepsilon}. \\ \end{array}
$$

次设 $a < b$ 。这时

$$
\mathrm {d} s = \sqrt {a ^ {2} \sin^ {2} t + b ^ {2} \cos^ {2} t} \mathrm {d} t = a \sqrt {1 + \varepsilon_ {1} ^ {2} \cos^ {2} t} \mathrm {d} t,
$$

其中 $\varepsilon_{1} = \frac{\sqrt{b^{2} - a^{2}}}{a}$ 仿前，有

$$
\begin{array}{l} M = \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} a b \sin t \sqrt {1 + \varepsilon_ {1} ^ {2} \cos^ {2} t} d t + \int_ {\pi} ^ {2 \pi} a (- b \sin t) \sqrt {1 + \varepsilon_ {1} ^ {2} \cos^ {2} t} d t = 4 a b \int_ {0} ^ {1} \sqrt {1 + \varepsilon_ {1} ^ {2} u ^ {2}} d u \\ = \frac {4 a b}{\varepsilon_ {1}} \left[ \frac {1}{2} \varepsilon_ {1} u \sqrt {1 + \varepsilon_ {1} ^ {2} u ^ {2}} + \frac {1}{2} \ln \left(\varepsilon_ {1} u + \sqrt {1 + \varepsilon_ {1} ^ {2} u ^ {2}}\right) \right] \Bigg | _ {u = 0} ^ {u - 1} = 2 b ^ {2} + 2 a b \frac {\ln \left(\varepsilon_ {1} + \sqrt {1 + \varepsilon_ {1} ^ {2}}\right)}{\varepsilon_ {1}}. \\ \end{array}
$$

最后，若 $a = b$ ，则椭圆退化成圆，这时 $\mathrm{ds} = a\mathrm{dt}$ ，故

$$
M = \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} a ^ {2} \sin t \mathrm {d} t + \int_ {\pi} ^ {2 \pi} (- a \sin t) a \mathrm {d} t = 4 a ^ {2}.
$$

综上所述，可知：

$$
M = \left\{ \begin{array}{l l} 2 b ^ {2} + 2 a b \frac {\arcsin \varepsilon}{\varepsilon}, & a > b, \\ 2 b ^ {2} + 2 a b \frac {\ln \left(\varepsilon_ {1} + \sqrt {1 + \varepsilon_ {1} ^ {2}}\right)}{\varepsilon_ {1}}, & a <   b, \\ 4 a ^ {2}, & a = b, \end{array} \right.
$$

其中 $\varepsilon = \frac{\sqrt{a^2 - b^2}}{a} (a > b),\quad \varepsilon_1 = \frac{\sqrt{b^2 - a^2}}{a} (a <   b),$

【4242】求曲线 $x = at, y = \frac{a}{2} t^2, z = \frac{a}{3} t^3$ （ $0 \leqslant t \leqslant 1$ ）的弧的质量，其密度按规律 $\rho = \sqrt{\frac{2y}{a}}$ 而变化.

解 弧长的微分为 $\mathrm{ds} = \sqrt{a^2 + a^2t^2 + a^2t^4}\mathrm{dt} = a\sqrt{1 + t^2 + t^4}\mathrm{dt},$

而密度 $\rho = \sqrt{\frac{2y}{a}} = t.$ 于是，质量为（作代换 $u = t^2$ ）

$$
\begin{array}{l} M = \int_ {C} \sqrt {\frac {2 y}{a}} d s = a \int_ {0} ^ {1} t \sqrt {1 + t ^ {2} + t ^ {4}} d t = \frac {a}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {1} \sqrt {1 + u + u ^ {2}} d u \\ = \frac {a}{2} \left[ \frac {u + \frac {1}{2}}{2} \sqrt {1 + u + u ^ {2}} + \frac {3}{8} \ln \left(u + \frac {1}{2} + \sqrt {1 + u + u ^ {2}}\right) \right] \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {1} \\ = \frac {a}{8} \left[ (3 \sqrt {3} - 1) + \frac {3}{2} \ln \frac {3 + 2 \sqrt {3}}{3} \right]. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4243】计算均匀曲线 $y = a \cosh \frac{x}{a}$ 从点 $A(0, a)$ 到点 $B(b, h)$ 的弧的质心的坐标.

解 弧长的微分为 $\mathrm{ds} = \sqrt{1 + \mathrm{sh}^2\frac{x}{a}}\mathrm{dx} = \mathrm{ch}\frac{x}{a}\mathrm{dx}.$

质量为 $M = \rho_{0}\int_{0}^{b}\mathrm{ch}\frac{x}{a}\mathrm{d}x = a\rho_{0}\mathrm{sh}\frac{b}{a} = \rho_{0}\sqrt{h^{2} - a^{2}}.$

于是，质心的坐标为

$$
\begin{array}{l} x _ {0} = \frac {\rho_ {0}}{M} \int_ {0} ^ {b} x \operatorname {c h} \frac {x}{a} \mathrm {d} x = \frac {\rho_ {0}}{M} \left[ a b \operatorname {s h} \frac {b}{a} - a ^ {2} \left(\operatorname {c h} \frac {b}{a} - 1\right) \right] = \frac {1}{\sqrt {h ^ {2} - a ^ {2}}} \left[ b \sqrt {h ^ {2} - a ^ {2}} - a ^ {2} \left(\frac {h}{a} - 1\right) \right] \\ = b - a \sqrt {\frac {h - a}{h + a}}; \\ \end{array}
$$

$$
\begin{array}{l} y _ {0} = \frac {\rho_ {0}}{M} \int_ {0} ^ {b} y \operatorname {c h} \frac {x}{a} d x = \frac {a \rho_ {0}}{M} \int_ {0} ^ {b} \operatorname {c h} ^ {2} \frac {x}{a} d x = \frac {a \rho_ {0}}{M} \int_ {0} ^ {b} \frac {1 + \operatorname {c h} 2 x}{2} d x = \frac {a \rho_ {0}}{M} \left[ \frac {x}{2} + \frac {a}{4} \operatorname {s h} \frac {2 x}{a} \right] \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {b} \\ = \frac {a \rho_ {0}}{M} \left(\frac {b}{2} + \frac {a}{4} \operatorname {s h} \frac {2 b}{a}\right) = \frac {a}{\sqrt {h ^ {2} - a ^ {2}}} \left(\frac {b}{2} + \frac {h}{2} \frac {\sqrt {h ^ {2} - a ^ {2}}}{a}\right) = \frac {h}{2} + \frac {a b}{2 \sqrt {h ^ {2} - a ^ {2}}}. \\ \end{array}
$$

$\star$ 由 $h = a \operatorname{ch} \frac{b}{a}$ 知： $\operatorname{ch} \frac{b}{a} = \frac{h}{a}$ . 从而， $\operatorname{sh} \frac{b}{a} = \sqrt{\operatorname{ch}^2 \frac{b}{a} - 1} = \frac{\sqrt{h^2 - a^2}}{a}$ .

【4244】求摆线 $x = a(t - \sin t)$ ， $y = a(1 - \cos t)(0\leqslant t\leqslant \pi)$ 的弧的质心.

解 弧长的微分为 $\mathrm{ds} = \sqrt{a^2(1 - \cos t)^2 + a^2\sin^2t}\mathrm{dt} = 2a\sin \frac{t}{2}\mathrm{dt}.$

质量为 $M = 2a\rho_{0}\int_{0}^{\pi}\sin \frac{t}{2}\mathrm{d}t = 4a\rho_{0}$ .于是，质心的坐标为

$$
\begin{array}{l} x _ {0} = \frac {1}{M} \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} \rho_ {0} a (t - \sin t) \cdot 2 a \sin \frac {t}{2} d t = \frac {a}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} t \sin \frac {t}{2} d t - \frac {a}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} \sin t \sin \frac {t}{2} d t \\ = - a t \cos \frac {t}{2} \left| _ {0} ^ {\pi} + a \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} \cos \frac {t}{2} d t + \frac {a}{4} \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} \left(\cos \frac {3 t}{2} - \cos \frac {t}{2}\right) d t = \frac {4 a}{3}; \right. \\ \end{array}
$$

$$
y _ {0} = \frac {1}{M} \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} \rho_ {0} a (1 - \cos t) \cdot 2 a \sin \frac {t}{2} d t = \frac {a}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} \sin \frac {t}{2} d t - \frac {a}{4} \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} \left(\sin \frac {3 t}{2} - \sin \frac {t}{2}\right) d t = \frac {4 a}{3}.
$$

【4245】计算球面上的三角形 $x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2} = a^{2}; x \geqslant 0, y \geqslant 0, z \geqslant 0$ 的围线的质心的坐标.

解 作球坐标变换 $x = r\cos \varphi \cos \psi, y = r\sin \varphi \cos \psi, z = r\sin \psi,$

则球面上的三角形三条曲边的方程分别是：

$$
x = a \cos \varphi , y = a \sin \varphi , z = 0; 0 \leqslant \varphi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2};
$$

$$
x = \cos \psi , y = 0, z = a \sin \psi ; 0 \leqslant \psi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2};
$$

$$
x = 0, y = a \cos \psi , z = a \sin \psi ; 0 \leqslant \psi \leqslant \frac {\pi}{2}.
$$

又因围线的周长为 $s = 3 \cdot \frac{\pi a}{2} = \frac{3\pi a}{2}$ . 于是, 质心的坐标为

$$
x _ {0} = \frac {\int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} a \cos \varphi \cdot a d \varphi + \int_ {0} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} a \cos \psi \cdot a d \psi}{\frac {3 \pi a}{2}} = \frac {2 a ^ {2}}{\frac {3 \pi a}{2}} = \frac {4 a}{3 \pi}.
$$

利用对称性知： $x_0 = y_0 = z_0 = \frac{4a}{3\pi}.$

【4246】求均匀的弧 $x = \mathrm{e}^{t}\cos t, y = \mathrm{e}^{t}\sin t, z = \mathrm{e}^{t}(-\infty < t \leqslant 0)$ 的质心的坐标.

解 弧长的微分为 $\mathrm{ds} = \sqrt{\mathrm{e}^{2t}(\cos t - \sin t)^2 + \mathrm{e}^{2t}(\sin t + \cos t)^2 + \mathrm{e}^{2t}}\mathrm{dt} = \sqrt{3}\mathrm{e}^t\mathrm{dt}$ 质量为 $M = \int_{\infty}^{0}\sqrt{3}\mathrm{e}^{t}\mathrm{d}t = \sqrt{3}.$

于是，质心的坐标为

$$
\begin{array}{l} x _ {0} = \frac {1}{M} \int_ {- \infty} ^ {0} e ^ {t} \cos t \cdot \sqrt {3} e ^ {t} d t = \int_ {- \infty} ^ {0} e ^ {2 t} \cos t d t = \frac {2 \cos t + \sin t}{5} e ^ {2 t} \left| _ {- \infty} ^ {0} = \frac {2}{5}. \right. \\ y _ {1 0} = \frac {1}{M} \int_ {- \infty} ^ {0} e ^ {t} \sin t \cdot \sqrt {3} e ^ {t} d t = \int_ {- \infty} ^ {0} e ^ {2 t} \sin t d t = \frac {2 \sin t - \cos t}{5} e ^ {2 t} \left| _ {- \infty} ^ {0} = - \frac {1}{5}. \right. \\ z _ {0} = \frac {1}{M} \int_ {- \infty} ^ {0} e ^ {t} \cdot \sqrt {3} e ^ {t} d t = \int_ {- \infty} ^ {0} e ^ {2 t} d t = \frac {1}{2}. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4247】求螺线 $x = a\cos t, y = a\sin t, z = \frac{h}{2\pi} t$ （ $0 \leqslant t \leqslant 2\pi$ ）的一支对坐标轴的转动惯量.

解 弧长的微分为 $\mathrm{ds} = \sqrt{a^2\sin^2t + a^2\cos^2t + \frac{h^2}{4\pi^2}}\mathrm{dt} = \frac{\sqrt{4\pi^2a^2 + h^2}}{2\pi}\mathrm{dt}.$

于是，转动惯量为

$$
\begin{array}{l} I _ {x} = \int_ {C} (y ^ {2} + z ^ {2}) d s = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} \left(a ^ {2} \sin^ {2} t + \frac {h ^ {2}}{4 \pi^ {2}} t ^ {2}\right) \frac {\sqrt {4 \pi^ {2} a ^ {2} + h ^ {2}}}{2 \pi} d t \\ = \frac {a ^ {2}}{2 \pi} \sqrt {4 \pi^ {2} a ^ {2} + h ^ {2}} \cdot \pi + \frac {h ^ {2}}{4 \pi^ {2}} \cdot \frac {1}{2 \pi} \sqrt {4 \pi^ {2} a ^ {2} + h ^ {2}} \cdot \frac {1}{3} (2 \pi) ^ {3} = \left(\frac {a ^ {2}}{2} + \frac {h ^ {2}}{3}\right) \sqrt {4 \pi^ {2} a ^ {2} + h ^ {2}}. \\ \end{array}
$$

$$
\begin{array}{l} I _ {y} = \int_ {c} (x ^ {2} + z ^ {2}) d s = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} \left(a ^ {2} \cos^ {2} t + \frac {h ^ {2}}{4 \pi^ {2}} t ^ {2}\right) \cdot \frac {1}{2 \pi} \sqrt {4 \pi^ {2} a ^ {2} + h ^ {2}} d t \\ = \frac {a ^ {2}}{2 \pi} \sqrt {4 \pi^ {2} a ^ {2} + h ^ {2}} \cdot \pi + \frac {h ^ {2}}{4 \pi^ {2}} \cdot \frac {1}{2 \pi} \sqrt {4 \pi^ {2} a ^ {2} + h ^ {2}} \cdot \frac {1}{3} (2 \pi) ^ {3} = \left(\frac {a ^ {2}}{2} + \frac {h ^ {2}}{3}\right) \sqrt {4 \pi^ {2} a ^ {2} + h ^ {2}}. \\ \end{array}
$$

$$
I _ {z} = \int_ {c} (x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}) d s = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} a ^ {2} \cdot \frac {1}{2 \pi} \sqrt {4 \pi^ {2} a ^ {2} + h ^ {2}} d t = a ^ {2} \sqrt {4 \pi^ {2} a ^ {2} + h ^ {2}}.
$$

【4248】 计算第二型曲线积分 $\int_{OA}x\mathrm{d}y - y\mathrm{d}x,$

式中（）为坐标原点， $A$ 点的坐标为(1,2)并设：(1)OA为直线段；(2)OA为抛物线，其轴为 $Oy$ ；(3)OA为由 $Ox$ 轴上的线段OB和平行于 $Oy$ 轴的线段BA组成的折线.

解（1)直线段的方程为 $y = 2x$ .于是，

$$
\int_ {O A} x \mathrm {d} y - y \mathrm {d} x = \int_ {0} ^ {1} (2 x - 2 x) \mathrm {d} x = 0.
$$

（2）抛物线段的方程为 $y = 2x^{2}$ .于是，

$$
\int_ {O A} x \mathrm {d} y - y \mathrm {d} x = \int_ {0} ^ {1} (4 x ^ {2} - 2 x ^ {2}) \mathrm {d} x = \frac {2}{3}.
$$

(3) 线段 $OB$ 的方程为 $y = 0, BA$ 的方程为 $x = 1$ . 于是，

$$
\int_ {O A} x \mathrm {d} y - y \mathrm {d} x = \int_ {0} ^ {2} 0 \cdot \mathrm {d} x + \int_ {0} ^ {2} \mathrm {d} y = 2.
$$

【4249】对于上题中所指示的路径(1)，（2），（3），计算

$$
\int_ {O A} x \mathrm {d} y + y \mathrm {d} x.
$$

解 (1) $\int_{OA}x\mathrm{d}y + y\mathrm{d}x = \int_{0}^{1}(2x + 2x)\mathrm{d}x = 2.$

(2) $\int_{\Omega A} x \, \mathrm{d}y + y \, \mathrm{d}x = \int_{0}^{1} (4x^2 + 2x^2) \, \mathrm{d}x = 2.$   
(3) $\int_{\Omega A} x \, \mathrm{d}y + y \, \mathrm{d}x = \int_{0}^{2} \, \mathrm{d}y = 2.$

在参数增加的方向，沿所指示的曲线来计算下列第二型曲线积分：

【4250】 $\int_{C} (x^{2} - 2xy) \, \mathrm{d}x + (y^{2} - 2xy) \, \mathrm{d}y$ ，其中 $C$ 为抛物线 $y = x^{2} (-1 \leqslant x \leqslant 1)$ .

解 由题设 $y = x^2$ ，从而， $\mathrm{dy} = 2x\mathrm{dx}$ 于是，

$$
\int_ {c} (x ^ {2} - 2 x y) \mathrm {d} x + (y ^ {2} - 2 x y) \mathrm {d} y = \int_ {1} ^ {1} \left[ \left(x ^ {2} - 2 x ^ {3}\right) + 2 x \left(x ^ {4} - 2 x ^ {3}\right) \right] \mathrm {d} x = - \frac {1 4}{1 5}.
$$

【4251】 $\int_{C} (x^{2} + y^{2}) \mathrm{d}x + (x^{2} - y^{2}) \mathrm{d}y$ ，其中 $C$ 为曲线 $y = 1 - |1 - x| (0 \leqslant x \leqslant 2)$ 。

解 当 $0 \leqslant x \leqslant 1$ 时, $y = 1 - (1 - x) = x$ , 从而, $\mathrm{dy} = \mathrm{dx}$ ; 当 $1 \leqslant x \leqslant 2$ 时, $y = 1 - (x - 1) = 2 - x$ , 从而, $\mathrm{dy} = -\mathrm{dx}$ . 于是,

$$
\int_ {C} \left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}\right) d x + \left(x ^ {2} - y ^ {2}\right) d y = \int_ {0} ^ {1} 2 x ^ {2} d x + \int_ {1} ^ {2} \left[ x ^ {2} + (2 - x) ^ {2} - x ^ {2} + (2 - x) ^ {2} \right] d x = \frac {4}{3}.
$$

【4252】 $\oint_{C} (x + y) \, \mathrm{d}x + (x - y) \, \mathrm{d}y$ ，其中 $C$ 为依逆时针方向通过的椭圆周 $\frac{x^2}{a^2} + \frac{y^2}{b^2} = 1$ .

解利用椭圆的参数方程 $x = a\cos t$ ， $y = b\sin t$ （ $0\leqslant t\leqslant 2\pi$ )，则有

$$
\begin{array}{l} \oint_ {C} (x + y) \mathrm {d} x + (x - y) \mathrm {d} y = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} \left[ \left(a \cos t + b \sin t\right) (- a \sin t) + \left(a \cos t - b \sin t\right) b \cos t \right] \mathrm {d} t \\ = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} \left(a b \cos 2 t - \frac {a ^ {2} + b ^ {2}}{2} \sin 2 t\right) d t = 0. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4253】 $\int_{C} (2a - y) \mathrm{d}x + x \mathrm{d}y$ ，其中 $C$ 为摆线 $x = a(t - \sin t)$ ， $y = a(1 - \cos t) (0 \leqslant t \leqslant 2\pi)$ 的一拱.

解 由题设知： $\mathrm{dx} = a(1 - \cos t)\mathrm{dt},\mathrm{dy} = a\sin t\mathrm{dt}$ 于是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int_ {c} (2 a - y) \mathrm {d} x + x \mathrm {d} y = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} \left\{\left[ 2 a - a (1 - \cos t) \right] a (1 - \cos t) + a (t - \sin t) a \sin t \right\} \mathrm {d} t \\ = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} a ^ {2} t \sin t d t = - a ^ {2} (t \cos t - \sin t) \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {2 \pi} = - 2 \pi a ^ {2}. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4254】 $\oint_{C} \frac{(x + y) \mathrm{d}x - (x - y) \mathrm{d}y}{x^2 + y^2}$ , 其中 $C$ 为依逆时针方向通过的圆周 $x^2 + y^2 = a^2$ .

解利用圆的参数方程 $x = a\cos t$ ， $y = a\sin t$ （ $0\leqslant t\leqslant 2\pi$ )，则有

$$
\oint_ {C} \frac {(x + y) d x - (x - y) d y}{x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}} = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} \frac {- (a \cos t + a \sin t) a \sin t - (a \cos t - a \sin t) a \cos t}{a ^ {2}} d t = - \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} d t = - 2 \pi .
$$

【4255】 $\oint_{ABCDA} \frac{\mathrm{d}x + \mathrm{d}y}{|x| + |y|}$ ，其中 $ABCDA$ 为以 $A(1,0), B(0,1), C(-1,0), D(0,-1)$ 为顶点的正方形的围线.

提示 注意正方形各边的方程分别为

$$
A B: y = 1 - x; \quad B C: y = 1 + x; \quad C D: y = - 1 - x; \quad D A: y = - 1 + x.
$$

解 正方形各边的方程分别为

$$
A B: y = 1 - x; \quad B C: y = 1 + x; \quad C D: y = - 1 - x; \quad D A: y = - 1 + x.
$$

于是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} \oint_ {A B C D A} \frac {\mathrm {d} x + \mathrm {d} y}{| x | + | y |} = \int_ {A B} \frac {\mathrm {d} x + \mathrm {d} y}{x + y} + \int_ {B C} \frac {\mathrm {d} x + \mathrm {d} y}{- x + y} + \int_ {C D} \frac {\mathrm {d} x + \mathrm {d} y}{- x - y} + \int_ {D A} \frac {\mathrm {d} x + \mathrm {d} y}{x - y} \\ = \int_ {1} ^ {0} (1 - 1) d x + \int_ {0} ^ {- 1} 2 d x + \int_ {- 1} ^ {0} (1 - 1) d x + \int_ {0} ^ {1} 2 d x = 0. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4256】 $\int_{AB}\sin y\mathrm{d}x + \sin x\mathrm{d}y$ ，其中 $AB$ 为介于点 $A(0,\pi)$ 和点 $B(\pi ,0)$ 之间的直线段.

解 $AB$ 的方程为 $y = \pi - x$ . 于是，

$$
\int_ {A B} \sin y d x + \sin x d y = \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} \sin (\pi - x) d x - \sin x d x = \int_ {0} ^ {\pi} (\sin x - \sin x) d x = 0.
$$

注 原题为 $\int_{AB} dx \sin y + dy \sin x$ ，若把它理解为 $\int_{AB} d(x \sin y) + d(y \sin x)$ ，其值仍为零，与原答案也符合.

【4257】 $\oint_{\Omega mA nO}\arctan \frac{y}{x}\mathrm{d}y - \mathrm{d}x$ ，其中 $OmA$ 为抛物线段 $y = x^{2},OnA$ 为直线段 $y = x$

解 如图8.62所示，我们有

$$
\begin{array}{l} \oint_ {(m A n)} \arctan \frac {y}{x} d y - d x = \int_ {(m A} \arctan \frac {y}{x} d y - d x + \int_ {A n O} \arctan \frac {y}{x} d y - d x \\ = \int_ {0} ^ {1} 2 x \arctan x d x - \int_ {0} ^ {1} d x + \int_ {1} ^ {\infty} (\arctan 1 - 1) d x \\ = x ^ {2} \arctan x \left| _ {0} ^ {1} - \int_ {0} ^ {1} \frac {x ^ {2}}{1 + x ^ {2}} d x - 1 + \left(\frac {\pi}{4} - 1\right) x \right| _ {1} ^ {0} \\ = \frac {\pi}{4} - (x - \arctan x) \left| _ {0} ^ {1} - 1 - \left(\frac {\pi}{4} - 1\right) = \frac {\pi}{4} - 1 \right. \\ \end{array}
$$

注 原题为 $\int_{(m, m)} \mathrm{d}y \arctan \frac{y}{x} - \mathrm{d}x$ ，若把它理解为

$$
\int_ {(m A n O)} \mathrm {d} \left(y \arctan \frac {y}{x}\right) - \mathrm {d} x,
$$

则其值为零，与原答案不符.

![](images/705cf64a1eefb410cdf51734ecdfc5ed4114064b22f24c6d1d260b59ec04d2a4.jpg)  
图8.62

验证被积函数为全微分，并计算下列曲线积分：

【4258】 $\int_{(1,2)}^{(2,3)}x\mathrm{d}y + y\mathrm{d}x.$

解 显然， $x\mathrm{d}y + y\mathrm{d}x = \mathrm{d}(xy)$ 是全微分.于是，

$$
\int_ {(1, 2)} ^ {(2, 3)} x \mathrm {d} y + y \mathrm {d} x = \int_ {(1, 2)} ^ {(2, 3)} \mathrm {d} (x y) = x y \Bigg | _ {(- 1, 2)} ^ {(2, 3)} = 8.
$$

【4259】 $\int_{(0,1)}^{(3, - 1)}x\mathrm{d}x + y\mathrm{d}y.$

解 显然， $x\mathrm{d}x + y\mathrm{d}y = \mathrm{d}\left(\frac{x^2 + y^2}{2}\right)$ 是全微分.于是，

$$
\int_ {(0, 1)} ^ {(3, - 4)} x \mathrm {d} x + y \mathrm {d} y = \int_ {(0, 1)} ^ {(3, - 4)} \mathrm {d} \left(\frac {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}}{2}\right) = \frac {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}}{2} \Bigg | _ {(0, 1)} ^ {(3, - 4)} = 1 2.
$$

【4260】 $\int_{(0,1)}^{(2,3)} (x + y) \mathrm{d}x + (x - y) \mathrm{d}y.$

解 显然，我们有

$$
(x + y) \mathrm {d} x + (x - y) \mathrm {d} y = (y \mathrm {d} x + x \mathrm {d} y) + (x \mathrm {d} x - y \mathrm {d} y) = \mathrm {d} (x y) + \mathrm {d} \left(\frac {x ^ {2} - y ^ {2}}{2}\right) = \mathrm {d} \left(x y + \frac {x ^ {2} - y ^ {2}}{2}\right),
$$

即是全微分.于是， $\int_{(0,1)}^{(2,3)}(x + y)\mathrm{d}x + (x - y)\mathrm{d}y = \int_{(0,1)}^{(2,3)}\mathrm{d}\left(xy + \frac{x^2 - y^2}{2}\right) = \left(xy + \frac{x^2 - y^2}{2}\right)\Bigg|_{(0,1)}^{(2,3)} = 4.$

【4261】 $\int_{(1, - 1)}^{(1,1)}(x - y)(dx - dy).$

解 显然， $(x - y)(\mathrm{d}x - \mathrm{d}y) = \mathrm{d}\frac{(x - y)^2}{2}$ 是全微分.于是，

$$
\int_ {(1, - 1)} ^ {(1, 1)} (x - y) (\mathrm {d} x - \mathrm {d} y) = \int_ {(1, 1)} ^ {(1, 1)} \mathrm {d} \frac {(x - y) ^ {2}}{2} = \frac {(x - y) ^ {2}}{2} \left| _ {(1, - 1)} ^ {(1, 1)} = - 2. \right.
$$

【4262】 $\int_{(0,0)}^{(a,b)}f(x + y)(\mathrm{d}x + \mathrm{d}y)$ ，其中 $f(u)$ 为连续函数.

解题思路 令 $F(x, y) = \int_{0}^{x + y} f(u) \mathrm{d}u$ . 注意

$$
F _ {x} ^ {\prime} (x, y) = F _ {y} ^ {\prime} (x, y) = f (x + y), \quad \text {及} \quad \mathrm {d} F (x, y) = f (x + y) (\mathrm {d} x + \mathrm {d} y),
$$

即可获解.

解 令 $F(x, y) = \int_{0}^{x + y} f(u) \mathrm{d}u$ . 由于 $f(u)$ 连续，故

$$
F _ {r} ^ {\prime} (x, y) = f (x + y), \quad F _ {y} ^ {\prime} (x, y) = f (x + y),
$$

并且它们都是 $x, y$ 的连续函数. 因此， $F(x, y)$ 可微，且

$$
\mathrm {d} F (x, y) = F _ {x} ^ {\prime} (x, y) \mathrm {d} x + F _ {y} ^ {\prime} (x, y) \mathrm {d} y = f (x + y) (\mathrm {d} x + \mathrm {d} y),
$$

故 $f(x + y)(\mathrm{d}x + \mathrm{d}y)$ 是全微分，并且

$$
\int_ {(0, 0)} ^ {(a, b)} f (x, y) (\mathrm {d} x + \mathrm {d} y) = F (a, b) - F (0, 0) = \int_ {0} ^ {a + b} f (u) \mathrm {d} u.
$$

【4263】 $\int_{(2,1)}^{(1,2)}\frac{y\mathrm{d}x - x\mathrm{d}y}{x^2}$ 沿着不与 $Oy$ 轴相交的路径.

解 显然，当 $x \neq 0$ 时， $\frac{y \mathrm{d}x - x \mathrm{d}y}{x^2} = \mathrm{d}\left(-\frac{y}{x}\right)$ 是全微分.于是，

$$
\int_ {(2, 1)} ^ {(1, 2)} \frac {y d x - x d y}{x ^ {2}} = \int_ {(2, 1)} ^ {(1, 2)} d \left(- \frac {y}{x}\right) = - \frac {y}{x} \Bigg | _ {(2, 1)} ^ {(1, 2)} = - \frac {3}{2}.
$$

【4264】 $\int_{(1,0)}^{(6,8)}\frac{x\mathrm{d}x + y\mathrm{d}y}{\sqrt{x^2 + y^2}}$ 沿着不通过坐标原点的路径.

解 显然，当 $(x, y) \neq (0, 0)$ 时， $\frac{x \mathrm{d}x + y \mathrm{d}y}{\sqrt{x^2 + y^2}} = \mathrm{d}(\sqrt{x^2 + y^2})$ 是全微分.于是，

$$
\int_ {(1, 0)} ^ {(6, 8)} \frac {x d x + y d y}{\sqrt {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}}} = \int_ {(1, 0)} ^ {(6, 8)} d (\sqrt {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}}) = \sqrt {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}} \left| _ {(1, 0)} ^ {(6, 8)} = 9. \right.
$$

【4265】 $\int_{(x_1,y_1)}^{(x_2,y_2)}\varphi (x)\mathrm{d}x + \psi (y)\mathrm{d}y$ ，其中 $\varphi$ 和 $\psi$ 为连续函数.

解 由于 $\varphi, \psi$ 是连续函数，故显然有

$$
\varphi (x) \mathrm {d} x + \psi (y) \mathrm {d} y = \mathrm {d} F (x) + \mathrm {d} G (y) = \mathrm {d} [ F (x) + G (y) ],
$$

其中 $F(x) = \int_{x_1}^x\varphi (u)\mathrm{d}u,G(y) = \int_{y_1}^y\psi (v)\mathrm{d}v.$ 从而， $\varphi (x)\mathrm{d}x + \psi (y)\mathrm{d}y$ 是函数 $F(x) + G(y)$ 的全微分，于是，

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int_ {(x _ {1}, y _ {1})} ^ {(x _ {2}, y _ {2})} \varphi (x) d x + \psi (y) d y = [ F (x) + G (y) ] \left| _ {(x _ {1}, y _ {1})} ^ {(x _ {2}, y _ {2})} = [ F (x _ {2}) + G (y _ {2}) ] - [ F (x _ {1}) + G (y _ {1}) ] \right. \\ = \int_ {x _ {1}} ^ {x _ {2}} \varphi (u) d u + \int_ {y _ {1}} ^ {y _ {2}} \psi (v) d v. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4266】 $\int_{(-2, - 1)}^{(3,0)}(x^4 +4xy^3)\mathrm{d}x + (6x^2 y^2 -5y^4)\mathrm{d}y.$

解 $P = x^4 + 4xy^3, Q = 6x^2y^2 - 5y^4$ . 显然， $P, Q$ 在全平面上具有连续偏导数，并且

$$
\frac {\partial Q}{\partial x} = 1 2 x y ^ {2} \quad \frac {\partial P}{\partial y} = 1 2 x y ^ {2},
$$

故 $\frac{\partial Q}{\partial x} = \frac{\partial P}{\partial y}$ . 由于全平面是单连通区域, 故在整个平面上表达式 $P \mathrm{~d}x + Q \mathrm{~d}y$ 是某函数 $u(x, y)$ 的全微分, 并且线积分 $\int_{C} P \mathrm{~d}x + Q \mathrm{~d}y$ 与路径无关, 因而, 可按平行于坐标轴的直线段来计算所给积分, 得

$$
\begin{array}{l} \int_ {(- 2, - 1)} ^ {(3, 0)} \left(x ^ {4} + 4 x y ^ {3}\right) d x + \left(6 x ^ {2} y ^ {2} - 5 y ^ {4}\right) d y = \int_ {- 2} ^ {3} \left(x ^ {4} + 4 x \cdot 0 ^ {3}\right) d x + \int_ {- 1} ^ {0} \left[ 6 (- 2) ^ {2} y ^ {2} - 5 y ^ {4} \right] d y \\ = 5 5 + 7 = 6 2. \\ \end{array}
$$

注 也可利用简单的技巧求出函数 $u(x, y)$ 来. 我们有

$$
(x ^ {4} + 4 x y ^ {3}) \mathrm {d} x + (6 x ^ {2} y ^ {2} - 5 y ^ {4}) \mathrm {d} y = \mathrm {d} \left(\frac {x ^ {5}}{5}\right) + 2 y ^ {3} \mathrm {d} \left(x ^ {2}\right) + 2 x ^ {2} \mathrm {d} \left(y ^ {3}\right) - \mathrm {d} \left(y ^ {5}\right) = \mathrm {d} \left(\frac {x ^ {5}}{5} + 2 x ^ {2} y ^ {3} - y ^ {5}\right),
$$

从而， $\int_{(-2, - 1)}^{(3,0)}(x^4 +4xy^3)\mathrm{d}x + (6x^2 y^2 -5y^4)\mathrm{d}y = \left(\frac{x^5}{5} +2x^2 y^3 -y^5\right)\bigg|_{(-2, - 1)}^{(3,0)} = 62.$

【4267】 $\int_{(0, -1)}^{(1, 0)} \frac{x \mathrm{d}y - y \mathrm{d}x}{(x - y)^2}$ 沿着不与直线 $y = x$ 相交的路径.

解 $P = -\frac{y}{(x - y)^2}, Q = \frac{x}{(x - y)^2} (x \neq y)$ . 容易验证：

$$
\frac {\partial Q}{\partial x} = \frac {\partial P}{\partial y} = - \frac {x + y}{(x - y) ^ {3}} \quad (x \neq y).
$$

考虑平面上的区域 $\Omega = \{(x, y) | x > y\}$ . 由于 $\Omega$ 是单连通区域，且在其上 $\frac{\partial Q}{\partial x} = \frac{\partial P}{\partial y}$ ，故在 $\Omega$ 上， $P \mathrm{d}x + Q \mathrm{d}y$ 是某函数 $u = u(x, y)$ 的全微分，从而，在 $\Omega$ 上线积分 $\int_{C} P \mathrm{d}x + Q \mathrm{d}y$ 与路径无关. 因此，可按平行于坐标轴的直线段来计算所给积分，得

$$
\int_ {(0, - 1)} ^ {4 1. 0 0} \frac {x \mathrm {d} y - y \mathrm {d} x}{(x - y) ^ {2}} = \int_ {0} ^ {1} \frac {- (- 1) \mathrm {d} x}{(x + 1) ^ {2}} + \int_ {1} ^ {0} \frac {\mathrm {d} y}{(1 - y) ^ {2}} = \frac {1}{2} + \frac {1}{2} = 1.
$$

注 也可利用简单的技巧求出函数 $u(x, y)$ 来. 我们有

$$
\frac {x \mathrm {d} y - y \mathrm {d} x}{(x - y) ^ {2}} = \frac {(x - y) \mathrm {d} y - y \mathrm {d} (x - y)}{(x - y) ^ {2}} = \mathrm {d} \left(\frac {y}{x - y}\right),
$$

从而， $\int_{(0,1)}^{(1,0)}\frac{x\mathrm{d}y - y\mathrm{d}x}{(x - y)^2} = \frac{y}{x - y}\Big|_{(0,1)}^{(1,0)} = 1.$

【4268】 $\int_{(1,\pi)}^{(2,\pi)}\left(1 - \frac{y^2}{x^2}\cos \frac{y}{x}\right)\mathrm{d}x + \left(\sin \frac{y}{x} +\frac{y}{x}\cos \frac{y}{x}\right)\mathrm{d}y$ 沿着不与 $Oy$ 轴相交的路径.

解当 $x\neq 0$ 时，有

$$
\begin{array}{l} P = 1 - \frac {y ^ {2}}{x ^ {2}} \cos \frac {y}{x}, \quad Q = \sin \frac {y}{x} + \frac {y}{x} \cos \frac {y}{x}, \quad \frac {\partial P}{\partial y} = - \frac {2 y}{x ^ {2}} \cos \frac {y}{x} + \frac {y ^ {3}}{x ^ {3}} \sin \frac {y}{x}, \\ \frac {\partial Q}{\partial x} = - \frac {y}{x ^ {2}} \cos \frac {y}{x} - \frac {y}{x ^ {2}} \cos \frac {y}{x} + \frac {y ^ {2}}{x ^ {3}} \sin \frac {y}{x} = - \frac {2 y}{x ^ {2}} \cos \frac {y}{x} + \frac {y ^ {2}}{x ^ {3}} \sin \frac {y}{x}. \\ \end{array}
$$

考虑右半平面 $\Omega = \{(x,y)|x > 0\}$ . 由于 $\Omega$ 是单连通区域, 且在其上 $\frac{\partial Q}{\partial x} = \frac{\partial P}{\partial y}$ , 故在 $\Omega$ 上必是某函数 $u(x,y)$ 的全微分, 且可取

$$
u (x, y) = \int_ {1} ^ {x} \left(1 - \frac {y ^ {2}}{x ^ {2}} \cos \frac {y}{x}\right) d x + \int_ {\pi} ^ {y} (\sin y + y \cos y) d y = \left(x + y \sin \frac {y}{x}\right) \left| _ {1} ^ {x} + y \sin y \right| _ {n} ^ {y} = x - 1 + y \sin \frac {y}{x}.
$$

于是， $\int_{(1,\pi)}^{(2,\pi)}\left(1 - \frac{y^2}{x^2}\cos \frac{y}{x}\right)\mathrm{d}x + \left(\sin \frac{y}{x} +\frac{y}{x}\cos \frac{y}{x}\right)\mathrm{d}y = \left(x - 1 + y\sin \frac{y}{x}\right)\bigg|_{(1,\pi)}^{(2,\pi)} = \pi +1.$

【4269】 $\int_{(0,0)}^{(a,b)}\mathrm{e}^x (\cos y\mathrm{d}x - \sin y\mathrm{d}y).$

解 显然，有 $\mathrm{e}^r (\cos y\mathrm{d}x - \sin y\mathrm{d}y) = \mathrm{d}(\mathrm{e}^x\cos y)$ ，于是，

$$
\int_ {(0, 0)} ^ {(a, b)} \mathrm {e} ^ {x} (\cos y \mathrm {d} x - \sin y \mathrm {d} y) = \int_ {(0, 0)} ^ {(a, b)} \mathrm {d} (\mathrm {e} ^ {x} \cos y) = (\mathrm {e} ^ {x} \cos y) \left| _ {(0, 0)} ^ {(a, b)} = \mathrm {e} ^ {a} \cos b - 1. \right.
$$

【4270】证明：若 $f(u)$ 为连续函数且 $C$ 为分段光滑的封闭曲线，则

$$
\oint_ {c} f \left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}\right) \left(x d x + y d y\right) = 0.
$$

证明思路 若能求得函数 $F(x,y)$ ，使 $\mathrm{d}F(x,y) = f(x^2 + y^2)(x\mathrm{d}x + y\mathrm{d}y)$ （即 $F'_x(x,y) = xf(x^2 + y^2)$ ， $F'_y(x,y) = yf(x^2 + y^2)$ ），即可证明：

$$
\oint_ {C} f \left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}\right) (x d x + y d y) = F (x, y) \left| \begin{array}{l} \left(x _ {0}, y _ {0}\right) \\ \left(x _ {0}, y _ {0}\right) \end{array} = F \left(x _ {0}, y _ {0}\right) - F \left(x _ {0}, y _ {0}\right) = 0, \right.
$$

其中 $(x_0, y_0)$ 为 $C$ 上任意取定的一点. 经过分析，易知 $F(x, y) = \frac{1}{2} \int_{0}^{x^2 + y^2} f(u) \, \mathrm{d}u$ 就是这样的函数.

证 令 $F(x, y) = \frac{1}{2} \int_{0}^{x^2 + y^2} f(u) \, \mathrm{d}u$ . 由于 $f(u)$ 是连续函数，故

$$
F _ {r} ^ {\prime} (x, y) = x f \left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}\right), \quad F _ {y} ^ {\prime} (x, y) = y f \left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}\right),
$$

并且显然 $F_{x}^{\prime}(x,y), F_{y}^{\prime}(x,y)$ 都是 $x, y$ 的连续函数. 因此， $F(x,y)$ 可微，且

$$
\mathrm {d} F (x, y) = F _ {x} ^ {\prime} (x, y) \mathrm {d} x + F _ {y} ^ {\prime} (x, y) \mathrm {d} y = f \left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}\right) \left(x \mathrm {d} x + y \mathrm {d} y\right).
$$

于是，任取 $C$ 上一点 $(x_0, y_0)$ ，有

$$
\oint_ {C} f \left(x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}\right) \left(x d x + y d y\right) = F (x, y) \left| \begin{array}{l} \left(x _ {0}, y _ {0}\right) \\ \left(x _ {0}, y _ {0}\right) \end{array} = F \left(x _ {0}, y _ {0}\right) - F \left(x _ {0}, y _ {0}\right) = 0. \right.
$$

证毕.

求原函数 $z$ ，设：

【4271】 $\mathrm{dz} = (x^{2} + 2xy - y^{2})\mathrm{dx} + (x^{2} + 2xy - y^{2})\mathrm{dy}.$

解 $z = \int_{0}^{x}(x^{2} + 2xy - y^{2})\mathrm{d}x + \int_{0}^{y}(0 - 0 - y^{2})\mathrm{d}y + C = \frac{x^{3}}{3} +x^{2}y - xy^{2} - \frac{1}{3} y^{2} + C.$

【4272】 $\mathrm{dz} = \frac{y\mathrm{d}x - x\mathrm{d}y}{3x^2 - 2xy + 3y^2}$

解 $z = \int_{0}^{x}\frac{y\mathrm{d}x}{3x^2 - 2xy + 3y^2} +\int_{1}^{y}0\mathrm{d}y + C = \frac{y}{3}\int_{0}^{x}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\left(x - \frac{1}{3}y\right)^2 + \frac{8y^2}{9}} +C$

$$
= \frac {y}{3} \cdot \frac {3}{2 \sqrt {2} y} \arctan \frac {3 \left(x - \frac {y}{3}\right)}{2 \sqrt {2} y} \Bigg | _ {0} ^ {x} + C = \frac {1}{2 \sqrt {2}} \arctan \frac {3 x - y}{2 \sqrt {2} y} + C _ {1}.
$$

【4273】 $\mathrm{dz} = \frac{(x^2 + 2xy + 5y^2)\mathrm{d}x + (x^2 - 2xy + y^2)\mathrm{d}y}{(x + y)^3}$

解 $z = \int_{0}^{x}\frac{x^2 + 2xy + 5y^2}{(x + y)^3}\mathrm{d}x + \int_{1}^{y}\frac{0 - 0 + y^2}{(0 + y)^3}\mathrm{d}y + C = \int_{0}^{x}\frac{(x + y)^2 + 4y^2}{(x + y)^3}\mathrm{d}x + \int_{1}^{y}\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{y} +C$

$$
= \left[ \ln | x + y | \right] \left| _ {0} ^ {x} - \frac {2 y ^ {2}}{(x + y) ^ {2}} \right| _ {0} ^ {x} + \left[ \ln | y | \right] \left| _ {1} ^ {y} + C = \ln | x + y | - \frac {2 y ^ {2}}{(x + y) ^ {2}} + C _ {1}. \right.
$$

【4274】 $\mathrm{dz} = \mathrm{e}^{x}\left[\mathrm{e}^{y}(x - y + 2) + y\right]\mathrm{d}x + \mathrm{e}^{x}\left[\mathrm{e}^{y}(x - y) + 1\right]\mathrm{d}y.$

解 $z = \int_{0}^{x}[(x - y + 2)\mathrm{e}^{x + y} + y\mathrm{e}^{x}]\mathrm{d}x + \int_{0}^{y}(1 - y\mathrm{e}^{y})\mathrm{d}y + C$

$$
= \left[ (x - y + 1) e ^ {x + y} + y e ^ {x} \right] \left| _ {0} ^ {x} + [ y - y e ^ {y} + e ^ {y} ] \right| _ {0} ^ {y} + C = (x - y + 1) e ^ {x + y} + y e ^ {r} + C _ {1}.
$$

【4275】 $\mathrm{d}z = \frac{\partial^{n + m + 1}u}{\partial x^{n + 1}\partial y^m}\mathrm{d}x + \frac{\partial^{n + m + 1}u}{\partial x^n\partial y^{m + 1}}\mathrm{d}y.$

提示 注意 $\mathrm{d}z = \mathrm{d}\left(\frac{\partial^{n + m}u}{\partial x^n\partial y^m}\right)$

解 因为 $\mathrm{d}z = \frac{\partial^{n + m + 1}u}{\partial x^{n + 1}\partial y^m}\mathrm{d}x + \frac{\partial^{n + m + 1}u}{\partial x^n\partial y^{m + 1}}\mathrm{d}y = \mathrm{d}\left(\frac{\partial^{n + m}u}{\partial x^n\partial y^m}\right).$

故有 $z = \frac{\partial^{n + m}u}{\partial x^n\partial y^m} +C.$

【4276】 $\mathrm{d}z = \frac{\partial^{n + m + 1}}{\partial x^{n + 2}\partial y^{m - 1}}\left(\ln \frac{1}{r}\right)\mathrm{d}x - \frac{\partial^{n + m + 1}}{\partial x^{n - 1}\partial y^{m + 2}}\left(\ln \frac{1}{r}\right)\mathrm{d}y$ ，其中 $r = \sqrt{x^2 + y^2}$

解 易知（当 $(x,y)\neq (0,0)$ 时）

$$
\begin{array}{l} \frac {\partial}{\partial x} \left(\ln \frac {1}{r}\right) = - \frac {x}{r ^ {2}}, \quad \frac {\partial}{\partial y} \left(\ln \frac {1}{r}\right) = - \frac {y}{r ^ {2}}, \\ \frac {\partial^ {2}}{\partial x ^ {2}} \left(\ln \frac {1}{r}\right) = - \frac {r ^ {2} - 2 x ^ {2}}{r ^ {4}}, \quad \frac {\partial^ {2}}{\partial y ^ {2}} \left(\ln \frac {1}{r}\right) = - \frac {r ^ {2} - 2 y ^ {2}}{r ^ {4}}, \\ \end{array}
$$

故（当 $(x,y)\neq (0,0)$ 时）

$$
\frac {\partial^ {2}}{\partial x ^ {2}} \left(\ln \frac {1}{r}\right) + \frac {\partial^ {2}}{\partial y ^ {2}} \left(\ln \frac {1}{r}\right) = 0. \tag {1}
$$

令 $P = \frac{\partial^{n + m + 1}}{\partial x^{n + 2}\partial y^{m - 1}}\left(\ln \frac{1}{r}\right), Q = -\frac{\partial^{n + m + 1}}{\partial x^{n - 1}\partial y^{m + 2}}\left(\ln \frac{1}{r}\right),$

则当 $(x,y)\neq (0,0)$ 时，由（1）式知

$$
\frac {\partial P}{\partial y} - \frac {\partial Q}{\partial x} = \frac {\partial^ {n + m}}{\partial x ^ {n} \partial y ^ {m}} \left[ \frac {\partial^ {2}}{\partial x ^ {2}} \left(\ln \frac {1}{r}\right) + \frac {\partial^ {2}}{\partial y ^ {2}} \left(\ln \frac {1}{r}\right) \right] = 0.
$$

因此，在任何不含原点(0,0)的单连通域中， $P\mathrm{d}x + Q\mathrm{d}y$ 都是某函数 $\textbf{z}$ 的全微分，并且对上半平面的点 $(x,y)$ （即 $y > 0$ )，可取

$$
\begin{array}{l} z (x, y) = \int_ {0} ^ {x} P (x, y) d x + \int_ {1} ^ {y} Q (0, y) d y + C \\ = \int_ {0} ^ {x} \frac {\partial^ {n + m - 1}}{\partial x ^ {n + 2} \partial y ^ {m - 1}} \left(\ln \frac {1}{r}\right) d x - \int_ {1} ^ {y} \left[ \frac {\partial^ {n + m + 1}}{\partial x ^ {n - 1} \partial y ^ {m + 2}} \left(\ln \frac {1}{r}\right) \right] \Bigg | _ {x = 0} d y + C \\ = \frac {\partial^ {n + m}}{\partial x ^ {n + 1} \partial y ^ {m - 1}} \left(\ln \frac {1}{r}\right) - \left[ \frac {\partial^ {n + m}}{\partial x ^ {n + 1} \partial y ^ {m - 1}} \left(\ln \frac {1}{r}\right) \right] \Bigg | _ {r = 0} - \left[ \frac {\partial^ {n + m}}{\partial x ^ {n - 1} \partial y ^ {m + 1}} \left(\ln \frac {1}{r}\right) \right] \Bigg | _ {x = 0} \\ + \left[ \frac {\partial^ {n + m}}{\partial x ^ {n - 1} \partial y ^ {n + 1}} \left(\ln \frac {1}{r}\right) \right] \Bigg | _ {\substack {x = 0 \\ y = 1}} + C \\ = \frac {\partial^ {n + m - 1}}{\partial x ^ {n} \partial y ^ {m - 1}} \left(\frac {\partial}{\partial x} \ln \frac {1}{r}\right) - \frac {\partial^ {n + m - 2}}{\partial x ^ {n - 1} \partial y ^ {m - 1}} \left[ \frac {\partial^ {2}}{\partial x ^ {2}} \left(\ln \frac {1}{r}\right) + \frac {\partial^ {2}}{\partial y ^ {2}} \left(\ln \frac {1}{r}\right) \right] \Bigg | _ {r = 0} + C _ {1} \\ = \frac {\partial^ {n + m - 1}}{\partial x ^ {n} \partial y ^ {m - 1}} \left(- \frac {x}{r ^ {2}}\right) + C _ {1} = \frac {\partial^ {n + m - 1}}{\partial x ^ {n} \partial y ^ {m - 1}} \left(\frac {\partial}{\partial y} \arctan \frac {x}{y}\right) + C _ {1} = \frac {\partial^ {n + m}}{\partial x ^ {n} \partial y ^ {m}} \left(\arctan \frac {x}{y}\right) + C _ {1}, \\ \end{array}
$$

其中 $C_1 = \left[\frac{\partial^{n + m}}{\partial x^{n - 1}\partial y^{m + 1}}\left(\ln \frac{1}{r}\right)\right]\Big|_{\substack{x = 0\\ y = 1}} + C$ 是任意常数.

同理，对下半平面上的点 $(x,y)$ （即 $y < 0$ ），可取

$$
z (x, y) = \int_ {0} ^ {x} P (x, y) d x + \int_ {- 1} ^ {y} Q (0, y) d y + C.
$$

经过和前面完全类似的计算，可得 $z(x,y) = \frac{\partial^{n + m}}{\partial x^n\partial y^m}\left(\arctan \frac{x}{y}\right) + C_2$

其中

$$
C _ {2} = \left[ \frac {\partial^ {n + m}}{\partial x ^ {n - 1} \partial y ^ {m + 1}} \left(\ln \frac {1}{r}\right) \right] \Big | _ {\substack {r = 0 \\ y = -1}} + C
$$

也是任意常数.

【4277】证明下面的估计对于曲线积分是正确的：

$$
\left| \int_ {c} P \mathrm {d} x + Q \mathrm {d} y \right| \leqslant L M,
$$

式中 $L$ 为积分路径的长， $M = \max \sqrt{P^2 + Q^2}$ （在弧 $C$ 上）

证明思路 首先注意到

$$
\left| \int_ {c} P \mathrm {d} x + Q \mathrm {d} y \right| = \left| \int_ {c} (P \cos \alpha + Q \sin \alpha) \mathrm {d} s \right| \leqslant \int_ {c} | P \cos \alpha + Q \sin \alpha | \mathrm {d} s,
$$

其次，由 $(P\cos \alpha + Q\sin \alpha)^2 + (P\sin \alpha - Q\cos \alpha)^2 = P^2 + Q^2$ 可知

$$
(P \mathrm {c o s} \alpha + Q \mathrm {s i n} \alpha) ^ {2} \leqslant P ^ {2} + Q ^ {2} \quad \text {或} \quad | P \mathrm {c o s} \alpha + Q \mathrm {s i n} \alpha | \leqslant \sqrt {P ^ {2} + Q ^ {2}} \leqslant M.
$$

从而，命题易获证.

证 由于 $\left|\int_{c}P\mathrm{d}x + Q\mathrm{d}y\right| = \left|\int_{c}(P\cos \alpha +Q\sin \alpha)\mathrm{d}s\right|\leqslant \int_{c}|P\cos \alpha +Q\sin \alpha |\mathrm{d}s,$

又因

$$
(P \cos \alpha + Q \sin \alpha) ^ {2} = P ^ {2} \cos^ {2} \alpha + Q ^ {2} \sin^ {2} \alpha + 2 P Q \sin \alpha \cos \alpha ,
$$

$$
0 \leqslant (P \sin \alpha - Q \cos \alpha) ^ {2} = P ^ {2} \sin^ {2} \alpha + Q ^ {2} \cos^ {2} \alpha - 2 P Q \sin \alpha \cos \alpha ,
$$

故有 $(P\cos \alpha + Q\sin \alpha)^2 \leqslant P^2 + Q^2,$

从而， $|P\cos \alpha +Q\sin \alpha |\leqslant \sqrt{P^2 + Q^2}\leqslant M.$ 于是，

$$
\left| \int_ {c} P \mathrm {d} x + Q \mathrm {d} y \right| \leqslant M \int_ {c} \mathrm {d} s = L M.
$$

【4278】估计积分 $I_{R} = \oint_{x^{2} + y^{2} - R^{2}}\frac{y\mathrm{d}x - x\mathrm{d}y}{(x^{2} + xy + y^{2})^{2}}.$ 证明： $\lim_{R\to \infty}I_R = 0.$

提示 注意在圆 $x^{2} + y^{2} = R^{2}$ 上，有 $P^2 + Q^2 \leqslant \frac{16}{R^6}$ ，及 $M = \max \sqrt{P^2 + Q^2} \leqslant \frac{4}{R^3}$ ，并利用4277题的结果.

解 在圆 $x^{2} + y^{2} = R^{2}$ 上，有

$$
\begin{array}{l} P ^ {2} + Q ^ {2} = \frac {y ^ {2}}{\left(x ^ {2} + x y + y ^ {2}\right) ^ {4}} + \frac {x ^ {2}}{\left(x ^ {2} + x y + y ^ {2}\right) ^ {4}} = \frac {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}}{\left(x ^ {2} + x y + y ^ {2}\right) ^ {4}} \\ = \frac {R ^ {2}}{(R ^ {2} + x y) ^ {4}} \leqslant \frac {R ^ {2}}{(R ^ {2} - | x y |) ^ {4}} \leqslant \frac {R ^ {2}}{\left(R ^ {2} - \frac {x ^ {2} + y ^ {2}}{2}\right) ^ {4}} = \frac {1 6}{R ^ {6}}. \\ \end{array}
$$

于是， $M \leqslant \frac{4}{R^3}$ 利用4277题的结果，即得 $I_{R}$ 的估计式：

$$
\left| I _ {R} \right| \leqslant \frac {4}{R ^ {3}} \cdot 2 \pi R = \frac {8 \pi}{R ^ {2}}.
$$

由此可知： $\lim_{R\to \infty}I_R = 0$

# 计算沿空间曲线的积分（假定坐标系是右手的）：

【4279】 $\int_{C} (y^{2} - z^{2}) \mathrm{d}x + 2yz \mathrm{d}y - x^{2} \mathrm{d}z$ ，式中 $C$ 为曲线 $x = t, y = t^{2}, z = t^{3} (0 \leqslant t \leqslant 1)$ ，以参数增加的方向为正。

解 $\int_{C} (y^{2} - z^{2}) \mathrm{d}x + 2yz \mathrm{d}y - x^{2} \mathrm{d}z = \int_{0}^{1} [(t^{1} - t^{6}) + 2t^{5} \cdot 2t - t^{2} \cdot 3t^{2}] \mathrm{d}t = \int_{0}^{1} (3t^{6} - 2t^{4}) \mathrm{d}t = \frac{1}{35}$ .

【4280】 $\int_{C} y \mathrm{~d} x + z \mathrm{~d} y + x \mathrm{~d} z$ ，式中 $C$ 为纽形螺线 $x = a \cos t, y = a \sin t, z = b t (0 \leqslant t \leqslant 2 \pi)$ ，以参数增加方向为正.

解 $\int_{C} y \mathrm{d}x + z \mathrm{d}y + x \mathrm{d}z = \int_{0}^{2\pi} (-a^{2} \sin t \sin t + abt \cos t + abc \cos t) \mathrm{d}t$

$$
= \left. \left(- \frac {a t ^ {2}}{2} + \frac {a ^ {2} \sin 2 t}{4} + a b t \sin t + a b \cos t + a b \sin t\right) \right| _ {0} ^ {2 \pi} = - \pi a ^ {2}.
$$

【4281】 $\int_{C} (y - z) \mathrm{d}x + (z - x) \mathrm{d}y + (x - y) \mathrm{d}z$ ，式中 $C$ 为圆周 $x^2 + y^2 + z^2 = a^2, y = x \tan \alpha (0 < \alpha < \pi)$ ，若从 $(0)x$ 轴的正向看去，沿逆时针方向为正.

解如图8.63所示.利用球面的参数方程

$$
x = a \cos \varphi \cos \psi , y = a \sin \varphi \cos \psi , z = a \sin \psi ,
$$

在 $\widehat{ABC}$ 上， $\varphi = \alpha$ ，因而，有

$$
\begin{array}{l} x = a \cos \alpha \cos \psi , \quad d x = - a \cos \alpha \sin \psi d \psi , \\ y = a \sin \alpha \cos \psi , \quad d y = - a \sin \alpha \sin \psi d \psi , \\ z = a \sin \psi , \quad \mathrm {d} z = a \cos \psi \mathrm {d} \psi , \\ \end{array}
$$

H. $\int_{\widehat{AB}} (y - z) \mathrm{d}x + (z - x) \mathrm{d}y + (x - y) \mathrm{d}z$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = a ^ {2} \int_ {\frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} \left[ - (\sin \alpha \cos \psi - \sin \psi) \cos \alpha \sin \psi - (\sin \psi - \cos \alpha \cos \psi) \sin \alpha \sin \psi \right. \\ + (\cos \alpha \cos \psi - \sin \alpha \cos \psi) \cos \psi ] d \psi \\ = a ^ {2} \int_ {\frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} (\cos \alpha - \sin \alpha) d \psi = \pi a ^ {2} (\cos \alpha - \sin \alpha) = \sqrt {2} \pi a ^ {2} \sin \left(\frac {\pi}{4} - \alpha\right). \\ \end{array}
$$

在 $\widehat{CDA}$ 上， $\varphi = \alpha +\pi$ 同样可得

$$
\int_ {\widehat {D A}} (y - z) \mathrm {d} x + (z - x) \mathrm {d} y + (x - y) \mathrm {d} z = - a ^ {2} \int_ {\frac {\pi}{2}} ^ {\frac {\pi}{2}} (\sin \alpha - \cos \alpha) \mathrm {d} \psi = \sqrt {2} \pi a ^ {2} \sin \left(\frac {\pi}{4} - \alpha\right).
$$

于是，最后得 $\int_{C} (y - z) dx + (z - x) dy + (x - y) dz = 2\sqrt{2} \pi a^2 \sin \left(\frac{\pi}{4} - \alpha\right).$

【4282】 $\int_{C}y^{2}\mathrm{d}x + z^{2}\mathrm{d}y + x^{2}\mathrm{d}z$ ，式中 $C$ 为维维亚尼曲线 $x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2} = a^{2},x^{2} + y^{2} = ax(z\geqslant 0,a > 0)$

![](images/08d40af0e10bc27551aeda1040bdf1d3b5b9d46307d6455140a12350bd52c6be.jpg)  
图8.63

若从 $Ox$ 轴的正向 $(x > 0)$ 看去，沿逆时针方向为正

解 柱面 $x^{2} + y^{2} = ax$ 可变为 $\left(x - \frac{a}{2}\right)^{2} + y^{2} = \left(\frac{a}{2}\right)^{2},$

故若令 $x - \frac{a}{2} = \frac{a}{2}\cos t, y = \frac{a}{2}\sin t (0 \leqslant t \leqslant 2\pi)$ ，则

$$
z = \sqrt {a ^ {2} - (x ^ {2} + y ^ {2})} = \sqrt {a ^ {2} - \left[ \frac {a ^ {2} (1 + \cos t) ^ {2}}{4} + \frac {a ^ {2} \sin^ {2} t}{4} \right]} = a \sin \frac {t}{2}.
$$

从而，曲线的参数方程为 $x = \frac{a(1 + \cos t)}{2}, y = \frac{a\sin t}{2}, z = a\sin \frac{t}{2} (0 \leqslant t \leqslant 2\pi).$

于是， $\int_{C}y^{2}\mathrm{d}x + z^{2}\mathrm{d}y + x^{2}\mathrm{d}z = \int_{0}^{2\pi}\left(-\frac{a^{3}\sin^{3}t}{8} +\frac{a^{3}\sin^{2}\frac{t}{2}\cos t}{2} +\frac{a^{3}\cos^{3}\frac{t}{2}}{2}\right)\mathrm{d}t$

$$
\begin{array}{l} = \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} \frac {a ^ {3}}{8} (1 - \cos^ {2} t) d (\cos t) + \frac {a ^ {3}}{2} \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} \frac {1 - \cos t}{2} \cos t d t + a ^ {3} \int_ {0} ^ {2 \pi} \left(1 - \sin^ {2} \frac {t}{2}\right) d \left(\sin \frac {t}{2}\right) \\ = \frac {a ^ {3}}{8} \left(\cos t - \frac {1}{3} \cos^ {3} t\right) \left| _ {0} ^ {2 \pi} + \frac {a ^ {3}}{4} \left[ \sin t - \left(\frac {t}{2} + \frac {1}{4} \sin 2 t\right) \right] \right| _ {0} ^ {2 \pi} + a ^ {3} \left(\sin \frac {t}{2} - \frac {1}{3} \sin^ {3} \frac {t}{2}\right) \left| _ {0} ^ {2 \pi} = - \frac {\pi a ^ {3}}{4}. \right. \\ \end{array}
$$

【4283】 $\int_{C} (y^{2} - z^{2}) \mathrm{d}x + (z^{2} - x^{2}) \mathrm{d}y + (x^{2} - y^{2}) \mathrm{d}z$ ，式中 $C$ 为球面的一部分 $x^{2} + y^{2} + z^{2} = 1, x \geqslant 0, y \geqslant 0, z \geqslant 0$ 的边界，当沿着它的正向移动时，这部分球面的外侧面保持在左方.

解 边界在 $Oxy$ 平面部分的方程为

$$
